```md
# Agent Workspace Rules

This project runs on a **development server**. All agents must use `.env.development` files (not `.env`). The original `.env` files have been removed to avoid confusion — do not recreate them.

This repository may intentionally use the live `/home/luanngo/boss/server/prisma/prod.db` SQLite database so `/boss-dev` behaves like a live development server. When `server/.env.development` points at `/home/luanngo/boss/server/prisma/prod.db`, it must also set `BOSS_DEV_ALLOW_PROD_DB=1` so the shared database usage is explicit.

Agents working in this repository must follow the workspace rules in `.agents/rules/db_backup.md` .

Production itself lives in `/home/luanngo/boss`, not `/home/luanngo/boss-dev`. `/boss-dev` is the development/testing checkout where agents have more freedom to run dev servers, tests, and local builds, as long as they do not touch production PM2 processes, production ports, or production URLs without explicit user approval.


## Allowed Work Environments

Agents may work in either of these environments:

1. Live development client/server
   - Development client: port `3021`.
   - Development server/API: port `3030`.
   - `client/.env.development` must use `NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL=http://localhost:3030`.
   - `server/.env.development` must use `PORT=3030`.
   - Prefer `./scripts/dev-servers.sh start|stop|restart|status` for launching the development client/server in the background with `nohup`.
   - This repository may intentionally use the live `/home/luanngo/boss/server/prisma/prod.db` SQLite database so `/boss-dev` behaves like a live development server.
   - When `server/.env.development` points at `/home/luanngo/boss/server/prisma/prod.db`, it must also set `BOSS_DEV_ALLOW_PROD_DB=1` so the shared database usage is explicit.
   - Treat this shared database as production-impacting data even though the API/client are running on development ports.

2. Sandbox or test environment
   - Use sandbox-only env files, sandbox databases, mocked services, or temporary local ports.
   - Sandbox testing must not point at production URLs, production databases, production ports, or production build output.
   - If a sandbox port differs from the development ports above, state the port clearly before testing.

## Debugging

- Server-side errors are logged to `server/logs/server-errors.log`. Always check this file first when investigating server bugs (e.g., 500 errors, API failures).
- AI receptionist debug logs are at `server/logs/receptionist-debug.log`.

## Applying Changes

- Only start or restart development servers if the user explicitly asks.
- `/boss-dev` is the only project where persistent development servers are allowed. If the user asks to start `/boss-dev` dev servers, they may remain running after the task.
- Do not proactively start or restart dev servers after editing source files unless validation requires it or the user asks.
- Agents do not need additional user approval to run local development checks, scripts, API probes, browser smoke tests, unit tests, local `/boss-dev` builds, or other non-production test commands needed to validate their work, as long as they follow the development/sandbox rules in this file and do not run production starts/restarts, production URLs, destructive database writes, migrations, or broad data updates.
- **Do not make changes to `/home/luanngo/boss/server/` without explicit user approval.** This directory belongs to a separate deployment (`/boss`). Any edits, file creation, or command execution inside that path requires prior approval.

## Production Safety Rules

- Never test against production port `3008`, production URLs, or a production Next.js build during development work unless the user explicitly approves that exact action.
- Production database access from `/boss-dev` is allowed only through the explicit live development setup above. Do not assume unrelated production resources are safe to use.
- Local `/boss-dev` build commands such as `npm run build` and `next build` are allowed for validation when they write only inside `/boss-dev`.
- Do not run production start, restart, deploy, or PM2 commands unless the user explicitly approves the exact action first.
- Approval is required for commands such as `npm run start`, `next start`, production server launches, deploy commands, PM2 production process changes, or equivalent start/deploy commands for either `client` or `server`.
- Do not stop, restart, delete, reload, or otherwise change the PM2 `proxy` process unless the user explicitly asks for proxy work in the current task.
- If a command or script would hit the existing production Next.js build, agents must stop, switch to the development or sandbox environment, and report the issue.
- Before browser testing, agents must verify the URL is `http://localhost:3021`, `http://localhost:3030`, or an explicitly declared sandbox URL. Do not browse or test `localhost:3008` unless the user approved production testing for that task.

## Production Restart Procedure

Production runs from `/home/luanngo/boss` on ports **3006** client and **3008** server. It must be managed with PM2 processes named `boss-client` and `boss-server`. The production proxy is PM2 process `proxy`. Treat `boss-client`, `boss-server`, and `proxy` as production-managed processes.

For a stable production client build:

1. Build from `/home/luanngo/boss/client/` with `npm run build`. The build script must clear stale output with `rm -rf dist .next` before `next build`.
2. PWA generation is enabled in the production build unless the user explicitly asks to disable it for debugging.
3. After building, verify the generated home HTML does not reference development chunk paths. It must not contain `react-refresh`, `static/development`, `/_next/static/chunks/main.js`, or `/_next/static/chunks/webpack.js`; it should reference hashed files such as `main-<hash>.js` and `webpack-<hash>.js`.
4. Verify standalone assets exist before restart:
   - `client/dist/standalone/server.js`
   - `client/dist/standalone/dist/routes-manifest.json`
   - `client/dist/standalone/dist/server/pages/index.html`
   - `client/dist/standalone/public/manifest.json`
   - `client/dist/standalone/public/service-worker.js`

When restarting production:

1. Run production restart commands from `/home/luanngo/boss`. Use PM2, not manual `nohup` PID files: `pm2 restart boss-server boss-client --update-env` or restart the one process that changed.
2. Confirm PM2 status with `pm2 list` and inspect recent logs with `pm2 logs boss-client --lines 80 --nostream` and `pm2 logs boss-server --lines 80 --nostream`.
3. Verify the client responds on `http://localhost:3006` and the API responds on `http://localhost:3008`.
4. Verify public `https://worksmrt.ca` HTML references hashed production chunks, not development chunk paths.
5. Verify PWA endpoints respond publicly: `https://worksmrt.ca/manifest.json` and `https://worksmrt.ca/service-worker.js`.

Only clean up stale production processes manually if PM2 cannot recover or ports are held by non-PM2 processes. In that case, identify processes first with `ps aux | grep -E 'node.*server\.js|next-server|next.*start' | grep -v grep | grep -v boss-dev` and `ss -tlnp | grep -E '3006|3008'`, then stop only the offending production process.

## Shared Production Database Rules

- Before changing Prisma schema files, Prisma migrations, generated Prisma client behavior, or code that performs broad database writes, agents must ask the user for explicit permission and explain the production database impact.
- This includes changes under `server/prisma/`, commands such as `prisma migrate`, `prisma db push`, `prisma db execute`, custom backfills, seed scripts, destructive SQL, or any script that updates many rows.
- Before any approved schema migration or broad data write against the shared production database, create or verify a current backup according to `.agents/rules/db_backup.md`.
- Safe read-only inspection is allowed without approval, but agents must avoid long-running queries or queries likely to lock SQLite.
- Normal app testing through `http://localhost:3021` and `http://localhost:3030` is allowed, but agents must remember the data is live and avoid creating test spam in customer-visible records unless the user approved it.

## Development Testing

- Use `/boss-dev` dev ports for normal validation: client `http://localhost:3021`, API `http://localhost:3030`.
- The Playwright config should target `http://localhost:3021`. Start `/boss-dev` dev servers with `./scripts/dev-servers.sh start` before browser tests unless the Playwright command starts its own web server.
- `server/.env.development` may contain `TEST_PERSONAL_TOKEN` for local authenticated smoke tests. This file is ignored; never copy the token into tracked files, chat output, screenshots, or test fixtures.
- For authenticated UI checks, use the local smoke script when it exists: `npm run pw:smoke -- http://localhost:3021/email`. It reads `TEST_PERSONAL_TOKEN` from the environment or `server/.env.development` and seeds browser localStorage for the test user.
- For authenticated API checks, send `Authorization: Bearer $TEST_PERSONAL_TOKEN` only against development or explicitly approved production URLs. Do not print the token.
- If `TEST_PERSONAL_TOKEN` is missing or expired, report that authenticated smoke testing is blocked instead of inventing credentials or changing auth code.

```

FILE: client/middleware.js

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/middleware.js
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

const FRAME_ANCESTORS = [
  "'self'",
  "https://teams.microsoft.com",
  "https://*.teams.microsoft.com",
  "https://*.cloud.microsoft",
  "https://*.office.com",
  "https://outlook.office.com",
  "https://outlook.office365.com",
  "https://*.microsoft365.com",

  // TacoTaco site
  "https://tacotacoto.ca",
  "https://*.tacotacoto.ca",

  // EatTaco site
  "https://eattaco.ca",
  "https://*.eattaco.ca",
].join(" ");

const suspiciousKeywords = [
  '.env', '.bak', '.php', '.yaml', '.git', '.log',
  '.sh', '.sql', '.zip', '.tar.gz', '.json.bak',
  '/debug', '/webhook', '/.aws'
];

export function middleware(request) {
  const url = request.nextUrl.pathname.toLowerCase();

  if (suspiciousKeywords.some(keyword => url.includes(keyword))) {
    return new NextResponse('Forbidden', { status: 403 });
  }

  const response = NextResponse.next();

  response.headers.set(
    "Content-Security-Policy",
    `frame-ancestors ${FRAME_ANCESTORS};`
  );

  response.headers.delete("X-Frame-Options");

  return response;
}

export const config = {
  matcher: '/((?!api|_next/static|_next/image|favicon.ico).*)',
};
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/next.config.js
// Browser PWA support is provided by public/manifest.json and the next-pwa
// generated service worker in production builds.

const withPWA = require('next-pwa')({
  dest: 'public',
  register: false,
  skipWaiting: true,
  disable:
    process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ||
    process.env.DISABLE_NEXT_PWA_PLUGIN === '1',
});

/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */
const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  productionBrowserSourceMaps: false,
  devIndicators: false,
  output: 'standalone',
  distDir: 'dist',

  // Required for cross-origin dev requests (e.g., worksmrt.ca → localhost)
  allowedDevOrigins: [
    'worksmrt.ca',
    '*.worksmrt.ca',
    'localhost',
    '127.0.0.1',
    '147.182.157.136',
    '2.25.204.83',
    'http://localhost:3021',
    'http://127.0.0.1:3021',
    'http://147.182.157.136',
    'http://147.182.157.136:3021',
    'http://2.25.204.83:3021',
  ],

  async rewrites() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/api/server/:path*',
        destination: 'http://localhost:3030/:path*',
      },
    ];
  },

  // Optional: enable future webpack caching stability
  webpack: (config) => {
    config.infrastructureLogging = { level: 'error' };
    return config;
  },
};

module.exports = withPWA(nextConfig);
```

```jsx
  '/settings/members': 'Members & Roles',
  '/settings/security': 'Security',
  '/settings/audit-log': 'Audit Log',
  '/settings/import-export': 'Import & Export',
  '/settings/danger-zone': 'Danger Zone',
  '/settings/email': 'Email Settings',
  '/settings/PushSettings': 'Push Settings',
  '/square/DeviceManagement': 'Square Device Management',
  '/square/manage-devices': 'Manage Square Devices',
  '/tasks': 'Tasks',
  '/tasks/new': 'New Task',
  '/ubereats': 'Uber Eats Integration',
  '/user/profile': 'My Profile',
};

function toTitleCase(segment) {
  return segment
    .split('-')
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((word) => word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1))
    .join(' ');
}

function formatDocumentTitle(pageTitle) {
  return pageTitle === APP_NAME ? APP_NAME : `${pageTitle} | ${APP_NAME}`;
}

function getPageTitle(pathname) {
  const explicitTitle = routeTitles[pathname];
  if (explicitTitle) {
    return formatDocumentTitle(explicitTitle);
  }

  const segments = pathname.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  const lastStaticSegment = [...segments].reverse().find((segment) => !segment.startsWith('['));

  if (!lastStaticSegment) {
    return APP_NAME;
  }

  return formatDocumentTitle(toTitleCase(lastStaticSegment));
}

function AppShell({ Component, pageProps, isStandalone, pageTitle }) {
  const { theme } = useTheme();

  return (
    <div data-theme={theme} className="bg-base-100 text-base-content min-h-screen">
      <Head>
        <title key="title">{pageTitle}</title>
        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
        <meta name="theme-color" content={theme === 'dark' ? '#111827' : '#ffffff'} />
        <link rel="icon" href="/icons/favicon.ico" sizes="any" />
        <link rel="shortcut icon" href="/icons/favicon.ico" />
        <link rel="apple-touch-icon" href="/icons/icon-192x192.png" />
        <link rel="manifest" href="/manifest.json" />
      </Head>
      {isStandalone ? (
        <>
          <NativeIOSRouteGuard />
          <ToastContainer
            theme={theme === 'dark' ? 'dark' : 'light'}
            position="top-right"
            autoClose={3000}
            hideProgressBar={false}
            newestOnTop
            closeOnClick={false}
            pauseOnFocusLoss
            draggable={false}
            pauseOnHover
          />
          <Component {...pageProps} />
          <NativeAppPrompt />
          <DetectedTextActionPopover />
        </>
      ) : (
        <MainAppLayout Component={Component} pageProps={pageProps}>
          <NativeIOSRouteGuard />
          <NativeAppPrompt />
          <DetectedTextActionPopover />
        </MainAppLayout>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function MyApp({ Component, pageProps }) {
  const router = useRouter();

  // For dynamic routes, router.pathname preserves the pattern (e.g., /pos/orders/[orgSlug])
  const isStandalone = standaloneRoutes.has(router.pathname);
  const pageTitle = getPageTitle(router.pathname);

  return (
    // Wrap the entire application in AuthProvider so context is always available.
    <AuthProvider>
      <ThemeProvider>
        <AppShell
          Component={Component}
          pageProps={pageProps}
          isStandalone={isStandalone}
          pageTitle={pageTitle}
        />
      </ThemeProvider>
    </AuthProvider>
  );
}

export default MyApp;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/pages/MainAppLayout.jsx
import React, { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import { IncomingCallProvider } from '@/shared/context/IncomingCallContext';
import { ChatProvider as AIProvider } from '@/shared/context/AIContext';
import { SharedHeaderProvider } from '@/shared/context/SharedHeaderContext';
import { MultitaskProvider } from '@/shared/context/MultitaskContext';
import SharedHeader from '@/shared/components/SharedHeader';
import AppContent from '@/shared/components/AppContent';
import AppSidebar from '@/shared/components/AppSidebar';
import ChatPopupManager from '@/services/chat/components/ChatPopupManager';
import ImportantChatManager from '@/services/chat/components/ImportantChatManager';
import GlobalChatWindow from '@/shared/components/GlobalChatWindow';
import { applyTeamsTheme, initializeTeamsSdk, isTeamsEmbeddedLocation } from '@/shared/utils/teams';

export default function MainAppLayout({ children, Component, pageProps = {} }) {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isTeamsEmbedded, setIsTeamsEmbedded] = useState(false);
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
    setIsTeamsEmbedded(isTeamsEmbeddedLocation(window.location));
  }, [router.asPath]);

  useEffect(() => {
    let isMounted = true;

    if (!isTeamsEmbedded) return undefined;

    (async () => {
      const { isInTeams, context } = await initializeTeamsSdk();

      if (!isMounted || !isInTeams) {
        return;
      }

      applyTeamsTheme(context?.app?.theme || context?.theme);
    })();

    return () => {
      isMounted = false;
    };
  }, [isTeamsEmbedded]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = () => setSidebarOpen((prev) => !prev);
    window.addEventListener('toggleAppSidebar', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('toggleAppSidebar', handler);
  }, []);

  const handleCloseSidebar = useCallback(() => {
    setSidebarOpen(false);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className={`min-h-screen bg-base-200 text-base-content ${isTeamsEmbedded ? 'teams-embedded' : ''}`}>
      <IncomingCallProvider>
        <AIProvider>
          <MultitaskProvider>
            <SharedHeaderProvider>
              <SharedHeader />
              <div className="flex" style={{ minHeight: 'calc(100vh - 4rem)' }}>
                <AppSidebar open={sidebarOpen} onClose={handleCloseSidebar} />
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 flex flex-col">
                  <AppContent Component={Component || (() => children)} pageProps={pageProps} />
                  {Component ? children : null}
                </div>
              </div>
              <ImportantChatManager />
              <ChatPopupManager />
              <GlobalChatWindow />
            </SharedHeaderProvider>
          </MultitaskProvider>
        </AIProvider>
      </IncomingCallProvider>
    </div>
  );
}
```

FILE: client/shared/context/AuthContext.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/context/AuthContext.jsx
import React, { createContext, useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { getOrganizationEmailAccounts } from '@/services/email/utils/api';
import { resolveFetchUrl } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { buildClientPlatformHeaders } from '@/shared/utils/clientPlatform';

export const AuthContext = createContext();

const sessionsKey = 'ws.userSessions';
const activeSessionKeyStorage = 'ws.activeSessionKey';
const legacyTokenStorageKey = 'token';

const getSessionKeyForUser = (user) => `${user.id}:${user.organizationId}`;

const isBrowser = () => typeof window !== 'undefined';

const getCurrentEmbeddedValue = () => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return '';

  try {
    const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const embedded = params.get('embedded');
    return typeof embedded === 'string' ? embedded.trim() : '';
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to read embedded query param', error);
    return '';
  }
};

const appendEmbeddedParam = (path, embeddedValue = getCurrentEmbeddedValue()) => {
  if (!path || !embeddedValue || !isBrowser()) return path;

  try {
    const url = new URL(path, window.location.origin);
    url.searchParams.set('embedded', embeddedValue);
    return `${url.pathname}${url.search}${url.hash}`;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to append embedded query param', error);
    return path;
  }
};

const getServerUrl = () => resolveFetchUrl(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL || '');

const readStoredSessions = () => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return {};

  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(sessionsKey);
    if (!raw) return {};
    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
    return parsed && typeof parsed === 'object' && !Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : {};
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to read stored user sessions', error);
    return {};
  }
};

const writeStoredSessions = (sessions) => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return;

  try {
    localStorage.setItem(sessionsKey, JSON.stringify(sessions || {}));
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to write stored user sessions', error);
  }
};

const syncLegacyActiveToken = (sessionsOverride = null) => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return '';

  try {
    const sessions = sessionsOverride || readStoredSessions();
    const activeKey = localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) || '';
    const activeSession = activeKey ? sessions[activeKey] : null;

    const fallbackSession =
      (activeSession && typeof activeSession.token === 'string' && activeSession.token.trim() ? activeSession : null) ||
      Object.values(sessions).find(
        (session) => session && typeof session.token === 'string' && session.token.trim()
      ) ||
      null;

    const token = fallbackSession?.token?.trim() || '';

    if (fallbackSession?.key && activeKey !== fallbackSession.key) {
      localStorage.setItem(activeSessionKeyStorage, fallbackSession.key);
    }

    if (token) {
      localStorage.setItem(legacyTokenStorageKey, token);
    } else {
      localStorage.removeItem(legacyTokenStorageKey);
    }

    return token;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to sync legacy token', error);
    return '';
  }
};

const removeStoredSession = (key) => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return;

  try {
    const sessions = readStoredSessions();
    if (sessions[key]) {
      delete sessions[key];
      writeStoredSessions(sessions);
      syncLegacyActiveToken(sessions);
    }

    if (localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) === key) {
      localStorage.removeItem(activeSessionKeyStorage);
      syncLegacyActiveToken(sessions);
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to remove stored session', error);
  }
};

const clearStoredSessions = () => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return;

  try {
    localStorage.removeItem(sessionsKey);
    localStorage.removeItem(activeSessionKeyStorage);
    localStorage.removeItem(legacyTokenStorageKey);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to clear stored sessions', error);
  }
};

const upsertUserSession = (sessionData) => {
  if (!isBrowser()) return;

  try {
    if (!sessionData?.user) return;

    const sessionKey = sessionData.key || getSessionKeyForUser(sessionData.user);
    const sessions = readStoredSessions();
    const existing = sessions[sessionKey] || {};

    const nextSession = {
      key: sessionKey,
      token:
        typeof sessionData.token === 'string' && sessionData.token.trim()
          ? sessionData.token.trim()
          : existing.token || '',
      userId: sessionData.user.id,
      username: sessionData.user.username,
      organizationId: sessionData.user.organizationId,
      organizationName: sessionData.user.organizationName,
      organizationSlug: sessionData.user.organizationSlug || '',
      permissions: sessionData.user.permissions || [],
      lastLoginAt: Date.now(),
    };

    sessions[sessionKey] = nextSession;

    writeStoredSessions(sessions);
    localStorage.setItem(activeSessionKeyStorage, sessionKey);
    syncLegacyActiveToken(sessions);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to update user sessions in localStorage', error);
  }
};

export const AuthProvider = ({ children }) => {
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null);
  const [organization, setOrganization] = useState(null);
  const [organizationEmailAccounts, setOrganizationEmailAccounts] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const router = useRouter();

  const PUBLIC_ROUTES = [
    '/',
    '/login',
    '/register',
    '/logout',
    '/recover',
    '/reset-password',
    '/demo',
    '/demo/pos-terminal',
    '/pos/orders/[orgSlug]',
  ];

  const getStoredAuthToken = useCallback(() => {
    if (!isBrowser()) return '';

    try {
      const sessions = readStoredSessions();
      const activeKey = localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) || '';
      const activeSession = activeKey ? sessions[activeKey] : null;

      if (activeSession && typeof activeSession.token === 'string' && activeSession.token.trim()) {
        const token = activeSession.token.trim();
        localStorage.setItem(legacyTokenStorageKey, token);
        return token;
      }

      const fallbackToken = syncLegacyActiveToken(sessions);
      if (fallbackToken) return fallbackToken;

      const legacyToken = localStorage.getItem(legacyTokenStorageKey);
      return typeof legacyToken === 'string' ? legacyToken.trim() : '';
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to get stored auth token', error);
      return '';
    }
  }, []);

  const getAuthHeaders = useCallback((headers = {}, options = {}) => {
    const { includeBearerToken = false } = options;
    const nextHeaders = { ...buildClientPlatformHeaders(), ...(headers || {}) };
    const storedToken = includeBearerToken ? getStoredAuthToken() : '';

    if (storedToken && !nextHeaders.Authorization) {
      nextHeaders.Authorization = `Bearer ${storedToken}`;
    }

    return nextHeaders;
  }, [getStoredAuthToken]);

  const redirectToLogin = useCallback(() => {
    const loginPath = appendEmbeddedParam('/login');
    router.replace(loginPath);
  }, [router]);

  const fetchOrgEmailAccounts = async (organizationId) => {
    if (!organizationId) {
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
      return;
    }

    try {
      const accounts = await getOrganizationEmailAccounts(organizationId);
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts(accounts);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching org email accounts:', error);
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
    }
  };

  const applyAuthenticatedUser = async (authUser) => {
    setUser(authUser);

    const orgData = {
      id: authUser.organizationId,
      name: authUser.organizationName,
      slug: authUser.organizationSlug,
      phoneNumber: authUser.organizationPhoneNumber || null,
      timezone: authUser.organizationTimezone || 'America/Toronto',
    };

    setOrganization(orgData);

    if (orgData.id) {
      await fetchOrgEmailAccounts(orgData.id);
    } else {
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
    }
  };

  const syncCurrentSessionToken = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/session/current`, {
        method: 'GET',
        credentials: 'include',
        headers: getAuthHeaders({}, { includeBearerToken: true }),
      });

      if (!res.ok) return null;

      const data = await res.json();

      if (data?.user && data?.token) {
        const key = getSessionKeyForUser(data.user);
        upsertUserSession({ ...data, key });
        return { ...data, key };
      }

      return null;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to sync current session token', error);
      return null;
    }
  }, [getAuthHeaders]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const isPublicRoute =
      PUBLIC_ROUTES.includes(router.pathname) || router.pathname.startsWith('/pos/orders/');

    if (isPublicRoute) {
      setLoading(false);
      return;
    }

    const fetchUser = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/me`, {
          credentials: 'include',
          headers: getAuthHeaders({}, { includeBearerToken: true }),
        });

        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          await applyAuthenticatedUser(data.user);
          await syncCurrentSessionToken();
        } else if (res.status === 401) {
          setUser(null);
          setOrganization(null);
          setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
          if (!isPublicRoute) {
            redirectToLogin();
          }
        } else {
          setUser(null);
          setOrganization(null);
          setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error fetching user:', error);
        setUser(null);
        setOrganization(null);
        setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchUser();
  }, [router.pathname, syncCurrentSessionToken, getAuthHeaders, redirectToLogin]);

  const hasPermission = useCallback((requiredPermission) => {
    if (!user || !user.permissions) return false;

    const userPermissions = user.permissions;

    if (userPermissions.includes('permission:editAll')) return true;

    if (Array.isArray(requiredPermission)) {
      return requiredPermission.some((permission) => userPermissions.includes(permission));
    }

    return userPermissions.includes(requiredPermission);
  }, [user]);

  const handleAuthSuccess = (data) => {
    const sessionKey = getSessionKeyForUser(data.user);
    upsertUserSession({ ...data, key: sessionKey });

    setUser(data.user);

    const orgData = {
      id: data.user.organizationId,
      name: data.user.organizationName,
      slug: data.user.organizationSlug,
      phoneNumber: data.user.organizationPhoneNumber || null,
    };

    setOrganization(orgData);

    if (orgData.id) {
      fetchOrgEmailAccounts(orgData.id);
    } else {
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
    }

    const hasVisitedKey = `ws.hasVisitedApp.${data.user.id}`;
    const hasVisited = isBrowser() ? localStorage.getItem(hasVisitedKey) : null;

    if (!hasVisited) {
      if (isBrowser()) {
        localStorage.setItem(hasVisitedKey, 'true');
      }
      const welcomeNoteId = '1e01c0ef-bf10-449a-a2b6-14eae857ff89';
      router.push(appendEmbeddedParam(`/notes?selectedNoteId=${welcomeNoteId}`));
    } else {
      router.push(appendEmbeddedParam('/dash'));
    }
  };

  const switchAccount = async (token, key, options = {}) => {
    const { silent = false, reload = true } = options;
    const storedSessions = readStoredSessions();
    const fallbackSession = key ? storedSessions[key] : null;
    const tokenToUse =
      typeof token === 'string' && token.trim()
        ? token.trim()
        : typeof fallbackSession?.token === 'string' && fallbackSession.token.trim()
          ? fallbackSession.token.trim()
          : '';

    if (!tokenToUse) {
      if (key) {
        removeStoredSession(key);
      }
      const error = new Error('That saved account is missing a valid switch token. Please log in to that account again.');
      if (!silent) toast.error(error.message);
      throw error;
    }

    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/session/switch`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getAuthHeaders({ 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }),
        credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ token: tokenToUse }),
      });

      const data = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));

      if (!res.ok) {
        const message = data?.error || 'Failed to switch session on server.';

        if (key && /invalid|expired/i.test(message)) {
          removeStoredSession(key);
        }

        throw new Error(message);
      }

      const nextUser = data?.user;
      const nextToken = data?.token;
      const nextKey = key || (nextUser ? getSessionKeyForUser(nextUser) : '');

      if (nextUser) {
        await applyAuthenticatedUser(nextUser);
      }

      if (nextUser && nextToken) {
        upsertUserSession({
          key: nextKey,
          token: nextToken,
          user: nextUser,
        });
      } else if (nextKey && isBrowser()) {
        localStorage.setItem(activeSessionKeyStorage, nextKey);
        syncLegacyActiveToken(readStoredSessions());
      }

      if (!silent) {
        toast.success('Switched account successfully!');
      }

      if (reload) {
        router.reload();
      }

      return data;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Switch Account Error:', error);
      if (!silent) {
        toast.error(error.message || 'Failed to switch account.');
      }
      throw error;
    }
  };

  const login = async (identifier, password) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/login`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getAuthHeaders({ 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, { includeBearerToken: true }),
        credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ identifier, password }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();

      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Login failed.');
      }

      handleAuthSuccess(data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Login Error:', error);
      toast.error(error.message);
      throw error;
    }
  };

  const register = async (username, email, password, organizationId, options = {}) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/register`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getAuthHeaders({ 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }),
        credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({
          username,
          email,
          password,
          organizationId,
          inviteToken: options.inviteToken || undefined,
        }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();

      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Registration failed.');
      }

      handleAuthSuccess(data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Registration Error:', error);
      toast.error(error.message || 'Registration failed.');
      throw error;
    }
  };

  const registerOrganization = async (username, email, password, organizationName) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/organization/register-initial`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getAuthHeaders({ 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }),
        credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ username, email, password, organizationName }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();

      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Organization registration failed.');
      }

      handleAuthSuccess(data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Organization Registration Error:', error);
      toast.error(error.message || 'Organization registration failed.');
      throw error;
    }
  };

  const logout = async () => {
    try {
      const activeKey = isBrowser() ? localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) : '';
      const sessions = readStoredSessions();

      if (activeKey && sessions[activeKey]) {
        delete sessions[activeKey];
      }

      const remainingSessions = Object.values(sessions).filter(
        (session) => session && typeof session === 'object' && session.key
      );

      if (remainingSessions.length > 0) {
        writeStoredSessions(sessions);
        syncLegacyActiveToken(sessions);

        const nextSession =
          remainingSessions.find(
            (session) => typeof session.token === 'string' && session.token.trim()
          ) || null;

        if (nextSession) {
          await switchAccount(nextSession.token, nextSession.key, { silent: true, reload: true });
          return;
        }
      }

      clearStoredSessions();

      await fetch(`${getServerUrl()}/user/logout`, {
        method: 'POST',
        credentials: 'include',
        headers: getAuthHeaders(),
      });

      setUser(null);
      setOrganization(null);
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
      router.push(appendEmbeddedParam('/login'));
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Logout Error:', error);
      toast.error('An error occurred while logging out.');
      clearStoredSessions();
      setUser(null);
      setOrganization(null);
      setOrganizationEmailAccounts([]);
      router.push(appendEmbeddedParam('/login'));
    }
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider
      value={{
        user,
        permissions: user ? user.permissions : [],
        organization,
        organizationEmailAccounts,
        loading,
        hasPermission,
        login,
        register,
        registerOrganization,
        logout,
        switchAccount,
        handleAuthSuccess,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
};

```

FILE: client/shared/context/SocketContext.jsx

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/context/SocketContext.jsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import io from 'socket.io-client';
import { AuthContext } from './AuthContext';

// FIX: Initialize with a safe default object so destructuring doesn't crash the app
// if the Provider is missing or loading.
const SocketContext = createContext({ socket: null, connected: false });

export const useSocket = () => {
  return useContext(SocketContext);
};

export const SocketProvider = ({ children }) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const [socket, setSocket] = useState(null);
  const [connected, setConnected] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;

    const newSocket = io(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL, {
      auth: {
        token: user.token,
      },
      transports: ['websocket'],
    });

    newSocket.on('connect', () => {
      console.log('Connected to Socket.IO server');
      setConnected(true);
    });

    newSocket.on('disconnect', () => {
      console.log('Disconnected from Socket.IO server');
      setConnected(false);
    });

    newSocket.on('connect_error', (err) => {
      console.error('Socket connection error:', err.message);
    });

    setSocket(newSocket);

    return () => {
      newSocket.disconnect();
    };
  }, [user]);

  return (
    <SocketContext.Provider value={{ socket, connected }}>
      {children}
    </SocketContext.Provider>
  );
};
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket.jsx
// client/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket.js
import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { io } from 'socket.io-client';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';

const sockets = {}; // Keep track of sockets per namespace

export const useGenericSocket = (namespace) => {
  const [socket, setSocket] = useState(null);
  const [connected, setConnected] = useState(false);
  const namespaceRef = useRef(namespace); // Store namespace in ref

  useEffect(() => {
    const currentNamespace = namespaceRef.current; // Use ref value

    // Only initialize if namespace is valid and socket doesn't exist or is disconnected
    if (currentNamespace && (!sockets[currentNamespace] || !sockets[currentNamespace].connected)) {
       // Disconnect previous instance if it exists and is different namespace
       if (socket && socket.nsp !== `/${currentNamespace}`) {
          socket.disconnect();
       }

      console.log(`Initializing socket for namespace: /${currentNamespace}`);
      sockets[currentNamespace] = io(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/${currentNamespace}`, {
        withCredentials: true,
        transports: ['websocket'],
        // Consider adding autoConnect: false and connecting manually if needed
      });

      setSocket(sockets[currentNamespace]); // Update state
    } else if (sockets[currentNamespace]) {
         setSocket(sockets[currentNamespace]); // Use existing socket
         setConnected(sockets[currentNamespace].connected);
    }

    const currentSocket = sockets[currentNamespace];

    if (!currentSocket) return; // Exit if no socket could be established

    const handleConnect = () => {
      setConnected(true);
      console.log(`Connected to /${currentNamespace} namespace`);
    };
    const handleDisconnect = () => {
      setConnected(false);
      console.log(`Disconnected from /${currentNamespace} namespace`);
      // Optionally attempt reconnection or notify user
    };
    const handleConnectError = (err) => {
      console.error(`${currentNamespace} Socket connection error:`, err.message);
      // Avoid toast for every error, maybe only specific ones or after retries fail
      // toast.error(`${currentNamespace} Socket connection error: ${err.message}`);
    };

     // Remove previous listeners before adding new ones
    currentSocket.off('connect', handleConnect);
    currentSocket.off('disconnect', handleDisconnect);
    currentSocket.off('connect_error', handleConnectError);

    currentSocket.on('connect', handleConnect);
    currentSocket.on('disconnect', handleDisconnect);
    currentSocket.on('connect_error', handleConnectError);

     // If socket is already connected when effect runs
    if (currentSocket.connected) {
      handleConnect();
    }

    // Connect if not already connected (useful with autoConnect: false)
    // if (!currentSocket.connected) {
    //   currentSocket.connect();
    // }

    return () => {
      console.log(`Cleaning up socket listeners for /${currentNamespace}`);
      // Only disconnect if the component using this specific instance unmounts
      // Global sockets might be managed differently (e.g., singleton pattern)
      // For simplicity here, we'll keep it, but review if sockets should persist globally
        // currentSocket.off('connect', handleConnect);
        // currentSocket.off('disconnect', handleDisconnect);
        // currentSocket.off('connect_error', handleConnectError);
      // Consider if disconnecting here is always desired.
      // If you want the socket to persist across component mounts/unmounts,
      // you might remove the disconnect() call or manage it globally.
      // currentSocket.disconnect();
      // delete sockets[currentNamespace]; // Clean up if disconnecting
    };
  }, [namespace]); // Depend only on the namespace string

  // Return the current socket instance and connection status
  return { socket, connected };
};
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/utils/axiosInstance.js
// shared/utils/axiosInstance.js
import axios from 'axios';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { buildClientPlatformHeaders } from '@/shared/utils/clientPlatform';

const axiosInstance = axios.create({
  baseURL: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL || 'http://localhost:3007',
  withCredentials: true, // Allows sending cookies if your server uses them
});

axiosInstance.interceptors.request.use((config) => {
  config.headers = {
    ...buildClientPlatformHeaders(),
    ...(config.headers || {}),
  };
  return config;
});

// Response interceptor to handle errors globally
axiosInstance.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => response,
  (error) => {
    if (error.response) {
      // Server responded with a status other than 2xx
      const message = error.response.data.error || 'An error occurred.';
      toast.error(message);
    } else if (error.request) {
      // Request was made but no response received
      toast.error('No response from server. Please try again later.');
    } else {
      // Something else happened while setting up the request
      toast.error('Error: ' + error.message);
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

export default axiosInstance;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/utils/clientPlatform.js
export const CLIENT_PLATFORM_HEADER = 'X-Worksmrt-Client-Platform';
export const NATIVE_IOS_PLATFORM = 'native-ios';

export const getClientPlatform = () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return 'web';

  const nativeBridge = window.WorksmrtNative;
  if (nativeBridge?.isNative && nativeBridge?.platform === 'ios') {
    return NATIVE_IOS_PLATFORM;
  }
  if (nativeBridge?.isNative && nativeBridge?.platform === 'android') {
    return 'native-android';
  }

  const capacitor = window.Capacitor;
  const capacitorPlatform =
    typeof capacitor?.getPlatform === 'function' ? capacitor.getPlatform() : null;
  const isNative =
    typeof capacitor?.isNativePlatform === 'function'
      ? capacitor.isNativePlatform()
      : capacitor?.isNative === true || Boolean(capacitor?.Plugins?.WorksmrtNative);

  if (isNative && capacitorPlatform === 'ios') return NATIVE_IOS_PLATFORM;
  if (isNative && capacitorPlatform === 'android') return 'native-android';

  return 'web';
};

export const isNativeIOS = () => getClientPlatform() === NATIVE_IOS_PLATFORM;

export const buildClientPlatformHeaders = () => ({
  [CLIENT_PLATFORM_HEADER]: getClientPlatform(),
});
```

FILE: client/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth.js
// client/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth.js
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { buildClientPlatformHeaders } from '@/shared/utils/clientPlatform';

const sessionsKey = 'ws.userSessions';
const activeSessionKeyStorage = 'ws.activeSessionKey';
const legacyTokenStorageKey = 'token';

const readStoredSessions = () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return {};

  try {
    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(sessionsKey);
    if (!raw) return {};
    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
    return parsed && typeof parsed === 'object' && !Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : {};
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Failed to read stored user sessions', error);
    return {};
  }
};

const writeTokenToStorage = (token) => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !token || typeof token !== 'string') return;

  const trimmedToken = token.trim();
  if (!trimmedToken) return;

  try {
    const sessions = readStoredSessions();
    const activeKey = window.localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) || '';

    if (activeKey && sessions[activeKey] && typeof sessions[activeKey] === 'object') {
      sessions[activeKey] = {
        ...sessions[activeKey],
        token: trimmedToken,
      };
      window.localStorage.setItem(sessionsKey, JSON.stringify(sessions));
    }

    window.localStorage.setItem(legacyTokenStorageKey, trimmedToken);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Failed to persist refreshed auth token', error);
  }
};

const clearStoredAuthToken = () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;

  try {
    const sessions = readStoredSessions();
    const activeKey = window.localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) || '';

    if (activeKey && sessions[activeKey] && typeof sessions[activeKey] === 'object') {
      delete sessions[activeKey].token;
      window.localStorage.setItem(sessionsKey, JSON.stringify(sessions));
    }

    window.localStorage.removeItem(legacyTokenStorageKey);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Failed to clear stored auth token', error);
  }
};

export const getStoredAuthToken = () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return '';

  try {
    const sessions = readStoredSessions();
    const activeKey = window.localStorage.getItem(activeSessionKeyStorage) || '';
    const activeSession = activeKey ? sessions[activeKey] : null;

    if (activeSession && typeof activeSession.token === 'string' && activeSession.token.trim()) {
      const token = activeSession.token.trim();
      window.localStorage.setItem(legacyTokenStorageKey, token);
      return token;
    }

    const fallbackSession = Object.values(sessions).find(
      (session) => session && typeof session.token === 'string' && session.token.trim()
    );

    if (fallbackSession?.token) {
      const token = fallbackSession.token.trim();
      window.localStorage.setItem(legacyTokenStorageKey, token);
      return token;
    }

    const legacyToken = window.localStorage.getItem(legacyTokenStorageKey);
    return typeof legacyToken === 'string' ? legacyToken.trim() : '';
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Failed to resolve stored auth token', error);
    return '';
  }
};

const buildHeaders = (options = {}, token = '') => {
  const headers = {
    ...buildClientPlatformHeaders(),
    ...(options.headers || {}),
  };

  if (token && !headers.Authorization) {
    headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
  }

  return headers;
};

export const resolveFetchUrl = (url) => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return url;

  const configuredUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL || '';
  if (!configuredUrl) return url;

  try {
    const apiUrl = new URL(configuredUrl, window.location.origin);
    const requestUrl = new URL(String(url), window.location.origin);
    const localApiHosts = ['localhost', '127.0.0.1'];
    const isLocalApi =
      localApiHosts.includes(apiUrl.hostname) && ['3030', '3031'].includes(apiUrl.port);
    const isLocalPage = localApiHosts.includes(window.location.hostname);

    if (!isLocalApi || isLocalPage || requestUrl.origin !== apiUrl.origin) {
      return url;
    }

    const pathname = requestUrl.pathname === '/' ? '' : requestUrl.pathname;
    return `/api/server${pathname}${requestUrl.search}${requestUrl.hash}`;
  } catch {
    return url;
  }
};

const doFetch = async (url, options, headers) => {
  return fetch(resolveFetchUrl(url), {
    ...options,
    credentials: 'include',
    headers,
  });
};

const tryRefreshSessionToken = async () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return '';

  try {
    const baseUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL;
    if (!baseUrl) return '';

    const response = await fetch(resolveFetchUrl(`${baseUrl}/user/session/current`), {
      method: 'GET',
      credentials: 'include',
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      return '';
    }

    const payload = await response.json().catch(() => null);
    const refreshedToken = typeof payload?.token === 'string' ? payload.token.trim() : '';

    if (refreshedToken) {
      writeTokenToStorage(refreshedToken);
    }

    return refreshedToken;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Session refresh failed', error);
    return '';
  }
};

export async function fetchWithAuth(url, options = {}) {
  if (!url) {
    throw new Error('fetchWithAuth requires a URL');
  }

  const { silent = false, ...fetchOptions } = options;
  options = fetchOptions;

  const initialToken = getStoredAuthToken();
  let headers = buildHeaders(options, initialToken);

  try {
    console.log('[fetchWithAuth] Request ->', url, {
      ...options,
      headers,
    });

    let response = await doFetch(url, options, headers);

    if (response.status === 401 && headers.Authorization) {
      const cookieOnlyHeaders = { ...(options.headers || {}) };
      response = await doFetch(url, options, cookieOnlyHeaders);

      if (response.ok) {
        clearStoredAuthToken();
        return response;
      }

      const refreshedToken = await tryRefreshSessionToken();
      if (refreshedToken) {
        headers = buildHeaders(options, refreshedToken);
        response = await doFetch(url, options, headers);
        if (response.ok) {
          return response;
        }
      }
    }

    if (response.status === 401) {
      if (!silent) toast.error('Your session has expired. Please log in again.');
    }

    return response;
  } catch (error) {
    if (error?.name === 'AbortError') {
      const wrappedError = new Error('Request was cancelled.');
      wrappedError.cause = error;
      throw wrappedError;
    }

    const message = `Failed to reach server: ${url}`;
    console.error('[fetchWithAuth] Error:', { url, options, error });
    if (!silent) toast.error(message);

    const wrappedError = new Error(message);
    wrappedError.cause = error;
    throw wrappedError;
  }
}
```

```prisma
  @@index([organizationId, bankTransactionId])

}

  transactionGroupId String?  @unique

  suggestions     AccountingRuleSuggestion[] @relation("ApprovedRuleToSuggestion")

}

model EmailAccountSyncState {
  id              String   @id @default(cuid())
  emailAccountId  String
  emailAccount    EmailAccount @relation(fields: [emailAccountId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  provider        String   // "gmail" | "outlook" | "mailcow"
  scope           String   // "inbox" | "sentitems" | "archive" | "deleteditems" | "drafts"
  cursor          String?  // Gmail historyId, Graph deltaLink, or equivalent
  lastSyncAt      DateTime?
  lastFullSyncAt  DateTime?
  errorCount      Int      @default(0)
  lastErrorAt     DateTime?
  lastErrorMsg    String?
  backoffUntil    DateTime?
  createdAt       DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime @updatedAt

  @@unique([emailAccountId, provider, scope])
  @@index([emailAccountId])
}


// Best-effort updated schema section based on the uploaded note.prisma snippet.
// This version adds list-level categories and item-level categories for lists.

enum NoteSharePermission {
  VIEWER
  EDITOR
}

enum NoteCategoryScope {
  USER
  ORGANIZATION
  GLOBAL
}

enum TaskPriority {
  LOW
  MEDIUM
  HIGH
  URGENT
}

enum ListKind {
  CHECKLIST
  GROCERY
}

enum ListMode {
  SINGLE_USE
  TEMPLATE
}

enum ListShareScope {
  PRIVATE
  ORGANIZATION
  SELECTED_USERS
  ORGANIZATION_LINK
}

model Note {
  id             String        @id @default(uuid())
  title          String
  isOrganization Boolean       @default(false)
  isGlobal       Boolean       @default(false)
  pinned         Boolean       @default(false)
  lastOpenedAt   DateTime?
  userId         String?
  organizationId String?
  categoryId     String?
  projectId      String?

  keywordsJson   String         @default("[]")

  user           User?         @relation("UserNotes", fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organization   Organization? @relation("OrganizationNotes", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])
  category       NoteCategory? @relation("NoteCategoryNotes", fields: [categoryId], references: [id])
  project        Project?      @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id])

  snippets       NoteSnippet[] @relation("NoteSnippets")
  shares         NoteShare[]
  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt

  @@index([userId])
  @@index([organizationId])
  @@index([projectId])
  @@index([pinned])
  @@index([lastOpenedAt])
}

model NoteShare {
  id          String              @id @default(cuid())
  noteId      String
  userId      String
  permission  NoteSharePermission @default(VIEWER)
  createdAt   DateTime            @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime            @updatedAt

  note        Note                @relation(fields: [noteId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  user        User                @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@unique([noteId, userId])
  @@index([noteId])
  @@index([userId])
}

model NoteSnippet {
  id         String   @id @default(uuid())
  content    String
  title      String?
  source     String?
  aiSummary  String?
  userId     String
  orderIndex Int
  noteId     String
  note       Note     @relation("NoteSnippets", fields: [noteId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  createdAt  DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt  DateTime @updatedAt

  @@index([noteId])
}

model Task {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  title          String?
  description    String?
  isCompleted    Boolean       @default(false)
  startDate      DateTime?
  dueDate        DateTime?
  reminderAt     DateTime?
  reminderSentAt DateTime?
  projectId      String?
  userId         String
  assignedUsers  User[]        @relation("TaskAssignedUsers")
  categoryId     String?
  dependencyId   String?
  priority       TaskPriority  @default(MEDIUM)
  position       Int           @default(0)

  user           User          @relation("UserTasks", fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  category       TaskCategory? @relation("TaskCategoryTasks", fields: [categoryId], references: [id])
  project        Project?      @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id])
  dependency     Task?         @relation("TaskDependency", fields: [dependencyId], references: [id])
  dependents     Task[]        @relation("TaskDependency")

  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt

  @@index([userId])
  @@index([projectId])
  @@index([projectId, position])
  @@index([isCompleted, reminderAt])
  @@index([reminderSentAt])
}

model Project {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  name           String
  description    String?
  ownerId        String
  organizationId String?
  tasks          Task[]
  notes          Note[]

  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())

  archived       Boolean       @default(false)
  memberRoles    Json?

  owner          User          @relation("UserProjects", fields: [ownerId], references: [id])
  organization   Organization? @relation("OrganizationProjects", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])
  members        User[]        @relation("ProjectMembers")

  @@index([organizationId, archived])
}

  @@index([scopeType, scopeId])

model TaskCategory {

model List {
  id                String         @id @default(cuid())
  title             String
  description       String?
  categoriesJson    String         @default("[]")
  keywordsJson      String         @default("[]")
  kind              ListKind       @default(CHECKLIST)
  mode              ListMode       @default(SINGLE_USE)
  shareScope        ListShareScope @default(PRIVATE)
  shareToken        String         @unique @default(cuid())
  sharedUserIdsJson String         @default("[]")
  ownerUserId       String
  organizationId    String
  sourceTemplateId  String?
  archived          Boolean        @default(false)
  useHtmlEditor     Boolean        @default(false)
  createdAt         DateTime       @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime       @updatedAt

  owner             User           @relation("UserOwnedLists", fields: [ownerUserId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organization      Organization   @relation("OrganizationLists", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  sourceTemplate    List?          @relation("ListTemplateInstances", fields: [sourceTemplateId], references: [id])
  templateInstances List[]         @relation("ListTemplateInstances")
  items             ListItem[]

  @@index([organizationId, mode, archived])
  @@index([ownerUserId, mode, archived])
  @@index([shareScope, organizationId, archived])
  @@index([sourceTemplateId])
}

  @@index([listId, sortOrder])
  @@index([completedByUserId])
}



model Room {
  id                String       @id @default(cuid())
  name              String       @unique
  
  // Relation to Table: "RoomTables"
  tables            Table[]      @relation("RoomTables")

  // Named relation to Organization
  organization      Organization @relation("OrganizationRooms", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId    String
  
  createdAt         DateTime     @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime     @updatedAt
}

model Table {
  id          String @id @default(cuid())
  number      Int
  seats       Int
  orders      Order[]

  organization Organization @relation("OrganizationTables", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId String

  room       Room    @relation("RoomTables", fields: [roomId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  roomId     String

  positionX  Int     @default(0) 
  positionY  Int     @default(0) 
  width      Int     @default(1) // Width in grid units
  height     Int     @default(1) // Height in grid units

  createdAt  DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt  DateTime @updatedAt

  @@unique([number, organizationId], name: "number_organizationId")
}

model Order {
  id               String      @id @default(cuid())
  table            Table?      @relation(fields: [tableId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  tableId          String?
  seatNumber       Int
  user             User?       @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId           String?
  status           String      @default("ORDERED")
  paymentStatus    Boolean     @default(false)
  paymentMethod    String?
  orderItems       OrderItem[]
  organization     Organization @relation(fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId   String
  createdAt        DateTime    @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime    @updatedAt
  hidden           Boolean     @default(false)
  contactId        String?
  contact          Contact?    @relation("ContactOrderRelation", fields: [contactId], references: [id])
  bookingId        String?
  booking          Booking?    @relation("BookingOrderRelation", fields: [bookingId], references: [id])
  notes            String?
  phoneNumber      String?
  emailAddress     String?
  customerName     String?
  squarePaymentId  String?
  squareOrderId    String?     @unique
  salesTransaction SalesTransaction?
  
  // NEW: Added a dedicated, unique field for the Uber Eats Order ID
  uberEatsOrderId  String?     @unique

  @@index([tableId])
  @@index([bookingId])
}

}

model Receipt {
```

```prisma
enum StatementGroup {
  REVENUE
  COST_OF_GOODS_SOLD
  EXPENSES

  UNMAPPED

  BANK_EXPENSE
  BANK_REVENUE
  TRANSFER
  CREDIT_CARD_PAYMENT
  PAYROLL_PAYMENT

  OWNER_DRAW
  OWNER_CONTRIBUTION
}

  HIGH

  SUPERSEDED

model BankTransaction {
```

```prisma
// server/prisma/schemas/chat.prisma

model ChatRoom {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  name           String
  description    String?
  isPrivate      Boolean       @default(false)
  organization   Organization? @relation("OrganizationChatRooms", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId String?
  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt
  shiftNotify      Boolean      @default(false)
  chats          Chat[]        @relation("ChatRoomChats")
  threads        Thread[]      @relation("ChatRoomThreads")
  participants   User[]        @relation("ChatRoomParticipants") 
  mutedBy        UserMutedChatRoom[]

  @@index([organizationId])
}

model Thread {
  id          String    @id @default(cuid())
  title       String
  chatRoom    ChatRoom  @relation("ChatRoomThreads", fields: [chatRoomId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatRoomId  String
  chats       Chat[]    @relation("ThreadChats")
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime  @updatedAt
}

model Chat {
  id                   String             @id @default(cuid())
  content              String
  sender               User               @relation("SenderChats", fields: [senderId], references: [id],onDelete: Cascade)
  senderId             String
  chatRoom             ChatRoom           @relation("ChatRoomChats", fields: [chatRoomId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatRoomId           String
  thread               Thread             @relation("ThreadChats", fields: [threadId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  threadId             String
  updatedAt            DateTime           @updatedAt
  attachments          ChatAttachment[] 
  requiresConfirmation Boolean            @default(false)
  isImportant          Boolean            @default(false)
  importantExpiresAt   DateTime?
  isPinned             Boolean            @default(false)

  readReceipts         ChatReadReceipt[]
  dismissedBy          UserDismissedChat[]
  taggedUsers          ChatTaggedUser[]
  chatReactions        ChatReaction[]
}

model ChatAttachment {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  url       String
  filename  String
  mimetype  String
  size      Int
  chat      Chat?    @relation(fields: [chatId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatId    String?
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
}

model ChatReadReceipt {
  id               String    @id @default(cuid())
  chat             Chat      @relation(fields: [chatId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatId           String
  user             User      @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId           String
  readAt           DateTime?
  confirmedAt      DateTime?
  popupConfirmedAt DateTime?

  createdAt        DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime  @updatedAt

  @@unique([chatId, userId])
}

model UserDismissedChat {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  user      User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId    String
  chat      Chat     @relation(fields: [chatId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatId    String
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())

  @@unique([userId, chatId])
}

model UserMutedChatRoom {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId      String
  chatRoom    ChatRoom @relation(fields: [chatRoomId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatRoomId  String
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())

  @@unique([userId, chatRoomId])
}

model ChatTaggedUser {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  user      User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId    String
  chat      Chat     @relation(fields: [chatId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatId    String
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())

  @@unique([userId, chatId])
}

model ChatReaction {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  chat      Chat     @relation(fields: [chatId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  chatId    String
  user      User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId    String
  emoji     String
  createdAt DateTime @default(now())

  @@unique([chatId, userId, emoji])
  @@index([chatId])
}
```

```prisma
model EmailAccount {
  id               String         @id @default(cuid())
  accountType      String
  emailAddress     String
  accessToken      String?
  refreshToken     String?
  active           Boolean        @default(true)
  googleId         String?        @unique
  microsoftId      String?        @unique
  userId           String?
  user             User?          @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId   String?
  organization     Organization?  @relation("OrganizationEmailAccounts", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  mailcowMailboxId String?        @unique
  mailcowMailbox   MailcowMailbox? @relation("MailcowMailboxEmailAccount", fields: [mailcowMailboxId], references: [id], onDelete: SetNull)
  mailcowPasswordEncrypted String? @map("mailcowPassword")
  allowedUsers     User[]         @relation("AllowedEmailAccounts")
  tenantId         String?
  emails           Email[]
  backgroundInfo   BackgroundInfo? @relation("EmailAccountBackgroundInfo", fields: [backgroundInfoId], references: [id])
  backgroundInfoId String?         @unique

  tags             Tag[]          @relation("EmailAccountTags")
  syncStates       EmailAccountSyncState[]

  createdAt        DateTime       @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime       @updatedAt

  @@unique([emailAddress, userId, organizationId])
}

  id           String        @id @default(cuid())
  info         String
  emailAccount EmailAccount? @relation("EmailAccountBackgroundInfo")
  createdAt    DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt    DateTime      @updatedAt
}

model Email {
  id                String         @id @default(cuid())
  providerId        String
  subject           String
  sender            String
  recipients        String
  date              DateTime
  account           EmailAccount   @relation(fields: [accountId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  accountId         String
  isRead            Boolean        @default(false)
  hasReplied        Boolean        @default(false)
  isProcessed       Boolean        @default(false)
  threadId          String?
  summary           String?
  content           String?
  isImportant       Boolean        @default(false)
  isPinned          Boolean        @default(false)
  createdAt         DateTime       @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime       @updatedAt
  folder            String         @default("INBOX")
  attachments       Attachment[]   @relation("EmailAttachments")
  tags              Tag[]          @relation("EmailTags")
  requiresReply     Boolean        @default(false)
  unsubscribeType   String?
  unsubscribeLink   String?
  fromHeader        String?
  replyToHeader     String?
  inReplyToHeader   String?
  referencesHeader  String?
  messageIdHeader   String?
  bookingId         String?
  booking           Booking?       @relation("BookingEmails", fields: [bookingId], references: [id])
  contactId         String?
  contact           Contact?       @relation("ContactEmails", fields: [contactId], references: [id])

  @@unique([providerId, accountId])
}

model Attachment {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())

  mimeType  String
  url       String

  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt
}

model Tag {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  name           String
  description    String?
  priority       Int           @default(0)

  emailAccountId String?
  emailAccount   EmailAccount? @relation("EmailAccountTags", fields: [emailAccountId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  emails         Email[]       @relation("EmailTags")

  @@unique([name, emailAccountId])
}

model EmailAccountSyncState {
  id              String   @id @default(cuid())
  emailAccountId  String
  emailAccount    EmailAccount @relation(fields: [emailAccountId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  provider        String   // "gmail" | "outlook" | "mailcow"
  scope           String   // "inbox" | "sentitems" | "archive" | "deleteditems" | "drafts"
  cursor          String?  // Gmail historyId, Graph deltaLink, or equivalent
  lastSyncAt      DateTime?
  lastFullSyncAt  DateTime?
  errorCount      Int      @default(0)
  lastErrorAt     DateTime?
  lastErrorMsg    String?
  backoffUntil    DateTime?
  createdAt       DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime @updatedAt

  @@unique([emailAccountId, provider, scope])
  @@index([emailAccountId])
}
```

```prisma
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/prisma/schemas/note.prisma
// Best-effort updated schema section based on the uploaded note.prisma snippet.
// This version adds list-level categories and item-level categories for lists.

enum NoteSharePermission {
  VIEWER
  EDITOR
}

enum NoteCategoryScope {
  USER
  ORGANIZATION
  GLOBAL
}

enum TaskPriority {
  LOW
  MEDIUM
  HIGH
  URGENT
}

enum ListKind {
  CHECKLIST
  GROCERY
}

enum ListMode {
  SINGLE_USE
  TEMPLATE
}

enum ListShareScope {
  PRIVATE
  ORGANIZATION
  SELECTED_USERS
  ORGANIZATION_LINK
}

model Note {
  id             String        @id @default(uuid())
  title          String
  isOrganization Boolean       @default(false)
  isGlobal       Boolean       @default(false)
  pinned         Boolean       @default(false)
  lastOpenedAt   DateTime?
  userId         String?
  organizationId String?
  categoryId     String?
  projectId      String?

  user           User?         @relation("UserNotes", fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organization   Organization? @relation("OrganizationNotes", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])
  category       NoteCategory? @relation("NoteCategoryNotes", fields: [categoryId], references: [id])
  project        Project?      @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id])

  snippets       NoteSnippet[] @relation("NoteSnippets")
  shares         NoteShare[]
  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt

  @@index([userId])
  @@index([organizationId])
  @@index([projectId])
  @@index([pinned])
  @@index([lastOpenedAt])
}

model NoteShare {
  id          String              @id @default(cuid())
  noteId      String
  userId      String
  permission  NoteSharePermission @default(VIEWER)
  createdAt   DateTime            @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime            @updatedAt

  note        Note                @relation(fields: [noteId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  user        User                @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@unique([noteId, userId])
  @@index([noteId])
  @@index([userId])
}

model NoteSnippet {
  id         String   @id @default(uuid())
  content    String
  title      String?
  source     String?
  aiSummary  String?
  userId     String
  orderIndex Int
  noteId     String
  note       Note     @relation("NoteSnippets", fields: [noteId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  createdAt  DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt  DateTime @updatedAt

  @@index([noteId])
}

model Task {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  title          String?
  description    String?
  isCompleted    Boolean       @default(false)
  startDate      DateTime?
  dueDate        DateTime?
  reminderAt     DateTime?
  reminderSentAt DateTime?
  projectId      String?
  userId         String
  assignedUsers  User[]        @relation("TaskAssignedUsers")
  categoryId     String?
  dependencyId   String?
  priority       TaskPriority  @default(MEDIUM)
  position       Int           @default(0)

  user           User          @relation("UserTasks", fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  category       TaskCategory? @relation("TaskCategoryTasks", fields: [categoryId], references: [id])
  project        Project?      @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id])
  dependency     Task?         @relation("TaskDependency", fields: [dependencyId], references: [id])
  dependents     Task[]        @relation("TaskDependency")

  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt

  @@index([userId])
  @@index([projectId])
  @@index([projectId, position])
  @@index([isCompleted, reminderAt])
  @@index([reminderSentAt])
}

model Project {
  id             String        @id @default(cuid())
  name           String
  description    String?
  ownerId        String
  organizationId String?
  tasks          Task[]
  notes          Note[]

  createdAt      DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime      @updatedAt
  archived       Boolean       @default(false)
  memberRoles    Json?

  owner          User          @relation("UserProjects", fields: [ownerId], references: [id])
  organization   Organization? @relation("OrganizationProjects", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])
  members        User[]        @relation("ProjectMembers")

  @@index([organizationId, archived])
}

model NoteCategory {
  id          String            @id @default(cuid())
  name        String
  scopeType   NoteCategoryScope @default(USER)
  scopeId     String?
  createdById String?
  notes       Note[]            @relation("NoteCategoryNotes")
  createdAt   DateTime          @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime          @updatedAt

  @@unique([name, scopeType, scopeId])
  @@index([scopeType, scopeId])
}

model TaskCategory {
  id             String       @id @default(cuid())

model List {

  @@index([ownerUserId, mode, archived])
```

```prisma
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/prisma/schemas/onboarding.prisma

model PaymentProvider {
  id               String           @id @default(cuid())
  name             String           @unique
  displayName      String
  active           Boolean          @default(true)
  configSchema     Json?            // JSON schema for provider-specific config fields
  merchantAccounts MerchantAccount[]
  createdAt        DateTime         @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime         @updatedAt
}

model MerchantAccount {
  id               String           @id @default(cuid())
  provider         PaymentProvider  @relation(fields: [providerId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  providerId       String
  organization     Organization     @relation(fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId   String
  label            String?          // user-friendly name
  currency         String           @default("USD")
  enabled          Boolean          @default(true)
  isActive         Boolean          @default(false)   // marked active after successful test
  config           Json?            // provider-specific credentials/config (encrypted ideally)
  testPassed       Boolean          @default(false)
  lastTestedAt     DateTime?
  createdAt        DateTime         @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime         @updatedAt

  @@unique([providerId, organizationId])
}

model OnboardingState {
  id               String       @id @default(cuid())
  organization     Organization @relation(fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId   String       @unique

  // Completion flags (computed from actual data)
  roomCreated      Boolean      @default(false)
  tableCreated     Boolean      @default(false)
  tablesArranged   Boolean      @default(false)
  productCreated   Boolean      @default(false)
  orderCreated     Boolean      @default(false)
  posOrderCreated  Boolean      @default(false)
  merchantSetup    Boolean      @default(false)

  // Steps the user explicitly skipped
  skippedSteps     String       @default("[]") // JSON array of step names

  // Overall completion
  completed        Boolean      @default(false)
  completedAt      DateTime?

  createdAt        DateTime     @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime     @updatedAt
}
```
