model Room {
  id                String       @id @default(cuid())
  name              String       @unique
  
  // Relation to Table: "RoomTables"
  tables            Table[]      @relation("RoomTables")

  // Named relation to Organization
  organization      Organization @relation("OrganizationRooms", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId    String
  
  createdAt         DateTime     @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime     @updatedAt
}

model Table {
  id          String @id @default(cuid())
  number      Int
  seats       Int
  orders      Order[]

  organization Organization @relation("OrganizationTables", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId String

  room       Room    @relation("RoomTables", fields: [roomId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  roomId     String

  positionX  Int     @default(0) 
  positionY  Int     @default(0) 
  width      Int     @default(1) // Width in grid units
  height     Int     @default(1) // Height in grid units

  createdAt  DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt  DateTime @updatedAt

  @@unique([number, organizationId], name: "number_organizationId")
}

model Order {
  id               String      @id @default(cuid())
  table            Table?      @relation(fields: [tableId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  tableId          String?
  seatNumber       Int
  user             User?       @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  userId           String?
  status           String      @default("ORDERED")
  paymentStatus    Boolean     @default(false)
  paymentMethod    String?
  orderItems       OrderItem[]
  organization     Organization @relation(fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId   String
  createdAt        DateTime    @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime    @updatedAt
  hidden           Boolean     @default(false)
  contactId        String?
  contact          Contact?    @relation("ContactOrderRelation", fields: [contactId], references: [id])
  bookingId        String?
  booking          Booking?    @relation("BookingOrderRelation", fields: [bookingId], references: [id])
  notes            String?
  phoneNumber      String?
  emailAddress     String?
  customerName     String?
  squarePaymentId  String?
  squareOrderId    String?     @unique
  salesTransaction SalesTransaction?
  
  // NEW: Added a dedicated, unique field for the Uber Eats Order ID
  uberEatsOrderId  String?     @unique

  @@index([tableId])
  @@index([bookingId])
}
model ProductCategory {
  id             String         @id @default(cuid())

  organization   Organization   @relation("OrganizationProductCategories", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  updatedAt      DateTime       @updatedAt

  hiddenOnPOS    Boolean        @default(false)
  hiddenOnPublic Boolean        @default(false)

}

model Product {
  id             String           @id @default(cuid())
  name           String
  sku            String           @unique
  description    String?
  price          Float
  inStock        Boolean          @default(true)
  active         Boolean          @default(true)
  public         Boolean          @default(true)
  canBuyOnline   Boolean          @default(true)
  
  category       ProductCategory  @relation("CategoryProducts", fields: [categoryId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  categoryId     String

  variants       ProductVariant[] @relation("ProductVariants")

  organization   Organization     @relation("OrganizationProducts", fields: [organizationId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  organizationId String

  image          String?
  createdAt      DateTime         @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime         @updatedAt
  orderItems     OrderItem[]

  taxable      Boolean  @default(true)
  tippable     Boolean  @default(true)
  uberEatsId   String? 

  isMultiVariant    Boolean  @default(false)
  variantGroupOrder String   @default("")
  comboRules        Json?

  @@unique([name, categoryId, organizationId])
}

model ProductVariant {
  id                   String                       @id @default(cuid())
  name                 String
  sku                  String                       @unique
  additionalPrice      Float                        @default(0.0)
  inStock              Boolean                      @default(true)
  active               Boolean                      @default(true)
  public               Boolean                      @default(true)
  canBuyOnline         Boolean                      @default(true)
  product              Product                      @relation("ProductVariants", fields: [productId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  productId            String
  description          String?
  image                String?
  createdAt            DateTime                     @default(now())
  updatedAt            DateTime                     @default(now())
  orderItems           OrderItem[]                  @relation("LegacyOrderItemVariant")
  orderItemsSelectedIn OrderItemSelectedVariant[]

  taxable              Boolean                      @default(true)
  tippable             Boolean                      @default(true)
  uberEatsId           String?
  groupName            String?
  isDefault            Boolean                      @default(false)

  @@unique([name, productId])
}

model OrderItem {
  id               String                       @id @default(cuid())
  order            Order                        @relation(fields: [orderId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  orderId          String
  product          Product?                     @relation(fields: [productId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  productId        String?
  variant          ProductVariant?              @relation("LegacyOrderItemVariant", fields: [variantId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  variantId        String?
  customName       String?
  notes            String?
  quantity         Int                          @default(1)
  seatNumber       Int
  price            Float
  taxable          Boolean?
  tippable         Boolean?
  createdAt        DateTime                     @default(now())
  updatedAt        DateTime                     @updatedAt
  status           String                       @default("ACTIVE")
  selectedVariants OrderItemSelectedVariant[]
}

model OrderItemSelectedVariant {
  id          String         @id @default(cuid())
  orderItem   OrderItem      @relation(fields: [orderItemId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  orderItemId String
  variant     ProductVariant @relation(fields: [variantId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  variantId   String

  @@unique([orderItemId, variantId])
}

FILE: server/src/middleware/auth.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/middleware/auth.js
// server/src/middleware/auth.js

import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';
import { extractBearerToken } from '#shared/utils/bearerToken.js';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

const buildRequestUser = (decoded = {}) => {
  const normalizedUserId = decoded.userId || decoded.id || null;

  return {
    ...decoded,
    id: normalizedUserId,
    userId: normalizedUserId,
  };
};

const authenticate = async (req, res, next) => {
  if (req.headers['x-internal-request'] === 'true') {
    // For internal requests, set a minimal user context if none exists
    if (!req.user) {
      req.user = { organizationId: null, id: null, role: 'INTERNAL' };
    }
    return next();
  }

  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
  const hasBearerToken = authHeader && /^Bearer\s+/i.test(authHeader);

  if (hasBearerToken) {
    const token = extractBearerToken(authHeader);

    try {
      if (!process.env.JWT_SECRET) {
        console.error('JWT_SECRET is not defined in environment variables.');
        return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Server Configuration Error' });
      }

      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
      req.user = buildRequestUser(decoded);
      return next();
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn(`[Auth] JWT verification failed, attempting cookie/session fallback: ${err.message}`);
    }
  }

  const session = await getSession(req);
  if (session?.user) {
    req.user = session.user;
    req.session = session;
    return next();
  }

  if (hasBearerToken) {
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Invalid or Expired Token',
      needsReauth: true,
    });
  }

  return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized' });
};

export default authenticate;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/middleware/errorHandler.js
// server/src/middleware/errorHandler.js
import { extractRequestContext, logAndReportError } from '../utils/logError.js';

export const errorHandler = (err, req, res, next) => {
  logAndReportError('Error:', err, extractRequestContext(req));

  if (err.code && err.code.startsWith('P')) {
    switch (err.code) {
      case 'P2002':
        return res.status(409).json({ error: 'Unique constraint failed on the fields: ' + err.meta.target });
      case 'P2003':
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Foreign key constraint failed on the field: ' + err.meta.field_name });
      default:
        return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Database error occurred.' });
    }
  }

  const statusCode = err.status || 500;
  res.status(statusCode).json({
    error: err.message || 'Internal Server Error',
  });
};

export const sendErrorResponse = (res, error, context = null) => {
  logAndReportError('Error:', error, context);
  const statusCode = error.status || 500;
  res.status(statusCode).json({
    error: error.message || 'Internal Server Error',
  });
};

import { performance, PerformanceObserver } from 'perf_hooks';
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { logAndReportError } from './utils/logError.js';
import { flushConsoleCaptureWrites, setupConsoleCapture } from './utils/consoleCapture.js';

setupConsoleCapture();

// --- Global Unhandled Error Logging ---
process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason, promise) => {
  logAndReportError('Unhandled Rejection:', reason instanceof Error ? reason : new Error(String(reason)), {
    promise: String(promise),
  })
    .then(async () => {
      await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
      if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') process.exit(1);
    })
    .catch(async (error) => {
      console.error('Failed to log unhandled rejection:', error);
      await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
      if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') process.exit(1);
    });
});

process.on('uncaughtException', (err, origin) => {
  logAndReportError(`Caught exception (origin: ${origin}):`, err, { origin })
    .then(async () => {
      await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
      if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') process.exit(1);
    })
    .catch(async (error) => {
      console.error('Failed to log uncaught exception:', error);
      await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
      if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') process.exit(1);
    });
});

// Load environment variables based on NODE_ENV
const envFile = process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? '.env.development' : '.env';
const envPath = path.resolve(process.cwd(), envFile);
if (fs.existsSync(envPath)) {
  dotenv.config({ path: envPath, override: true });

  dotenv.config();

const registerShutdownHook = (hook) => {
  if (typeof hook === 'function') {
    shutdownHooks.push(hook);
  }
};

const runMaybeAsync = async (fn, label) => {
  try {
    await fn();
    console.log(`${label} completed.`);
  } catch (error) {
    await logAndReportError(`${label} failed:`, error, { label });
  }
};

const registerModuleShutdownHooks = (moduleRef, moduleLabel) => {
  if (!moduleRef) return;

  const candidateFns = [
    { key: 'stop', label: `${moduleLabel}.stop` },
    { key: 'shutdown', label: `${moduleLabel}.shutdown` },
    { key: 'close', label: `${moduleLabel}.close` },
    { key: 'dispose', label: `${moduleLabel}.dispose` },
  ];

  for (const candidate of candidateFns) {
    if (typeof moduleRef[candidate.key] === 'function') {
      registerShutdownHook(async () => {
        await moduleRef[candidate.key]();
        console.log(`${candidate.label} completed.`);
      });
    }
  }

  if (typeof moduleRef.default === 'function') {
    registerShutdownHook(async () => {
      await moduleRef.default();
      console.log(`${moduleLabel}.default completed.`);
    });
  }
};

// --- Load Background Services/Jobs (Dynamic Imports) ---

app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const start = process.hrtime();
  const startMemory = process.memoryUsage().heapUsed;
  console.log(`[${new Date().toISOString()}] --> ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`);

  res.on('finish', () => {
    const diff = process.hrtime(start);
    const duration = (diff[0] * 1000 + diff[1] / 1000000).toFixed(2);
    const endMemory = process.memoryUsage().heapUsed;
    const memoryDiff = ((endMemory - startMemory) / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(3);

    console.log(
      `[${new Date().toISOString()}] <-- ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl} ${res.statusCode} (${duration}ms, Mem: ${memoryDiff}MB)`
    );
  });

  next();
});

// --- Utility Routes ---
performance.mark('before-global-css');
app.get('/global.css', async (req, res) => {
  const clientDir = path.resolve(process.cwd(), '../client');
  const cssDirs = [
    path.join(clientDir, 'dist', 'static', 'css'),
    path.join(clientDir, '.next', 'static', 'css'),
  ];

  try {
    const cssDir = cssDirs.find((dir) => fsExtra.pathExistsSync(dir));

    if (!cssDir) {
      return res.status(404).send('/* CSS directory not found */');
    }

    const files = await fsExtra.readdir(cssDir);
    let combinedCss = '';

    for (const file of files) {
      if (path.extname(file) === '.css') {
        const filePath = path.join(cssDir, file);
        const cssContent = await fsExtra.readFile(filePath, 'utf-8');
        combinedCss += `/* ${file} */\n${cssContent}\n\n`;
      }
    }

    res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/css');
    res.send(combinedCss);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error combining CSS:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to combine CSS files.', details: error.message });
  }
});
performance.mark('after-global-css');
performance.measure('Global CSS Endpoint Setup', 'before-global-css', 'after-global-css');

// --- File serving endpoint by Organization Slug ---
app.get('/uploads/bySlug/:orgSlug/:filePath(*)', async (req, res, next) => {
  const { orgSlug, filePath } = req.params;

  if (!orgSlug || !filePath) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Required params missing.' });
  }

  try {
    const organization = await prisma.organization.findUnique({
      where: { slug: orgSlug },
      select: { id: true },
    });

    if (!organization) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Organization not found.' });
    }

    const organizationId = organization.id;
    const baseUploadsDir = path.resolve(process.cwd(), 'uploads');
    const orgUploadsDir = path.join(baseUploadsDir, organizationId);
    const fullPath = path.join(orgUploadsDir, filePath);
    const normalizedFullPath = path.normalize(fullPath);
    const normalizedOrgDir = path.normalize(orgUploadsDir);

    if (!normalizedFullPath.startsWith(normalizedOrgDir)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access forbidden: Invalid file path.' });
    }

    const fileExists = await fsExtra.pathExists(normalizedFullPath);
    if (!fileExists) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'File not found.' });
    }

    const stats = await fsExtra.stat(normalizedFullPath);
    if (!stats.isFile()) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Not a file.' });
    }

    return res.sendFile(normalizedFullPath, (err) => {
      if (err && !res.headersSent) next(err);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error serving file by slug:', error);
    if (!res.headersSent) {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
    }
  }
});

// --- File serving endpoint by Organization ID ---
app.use('/uploads', async (req, res) => {
  const isInternal = req.headers['x-internal-request'] === 'true';
  let organizationId;

  let relativePath = req.path;
  const segments = relativePath.split('/').filter(Boolean);

  if (segments.length > 0) {
    relativePath = segments.slice(1).join('/');
    organizationId = segments[0];
  }

  if (!relativePath || relativePath === '/') {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'File path is missing.' });
  }

  const baseUploadsDir = path.resolve(process.cwd(), 'uploads');
  let fullPath;

  if (isInternal) {
    fullPath = path.join(baseUploadsDir, organizationId, relativePath);
  } else {
    const orgUploadsDir = path.join(baseUploadsDir, organizationId);
    fullPath = path.join(orgUploadsDir, relativePath);
    const normalizedFullPath = path.normalize(fullPath);
    const normalizedOrgDir = path.normalize(orgUploadsDir);

    if (!normalizedFullPath.startsWith(normalizedOrgDir)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access forbidden.' });
    }
  }

  return res.sendFile(fullPath, (err) => {
    if (err && !res.headersSent) {
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to send file.' });
    }
  });
});

// --- Seed Payment Providers ---
(async () => {
  try {
    const providers = [
      { name: 'square', displayName: 'Square', active: true, configSchema: JSON.stringify({ accessToken: 'string', locationId: 'string', applicationId: 'string' }) },
      { name: 'stripe', displayName: 'Stripe', active: true, configSchema: JSON.stringify({ secretKey: 'string', publishableKey: 'string' }) },
    ];

    for (const provider of providers) {
      await prisma.paymentProvider.upsert({
        where: { name: provider.name },
        create: provider,
        update: { displayName: provider.displayName, active: provider.active, configSchema: provider.configSchema },
      });
    }
    console.log('Payment providers seeded successfully.');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Failed to seed payment providers:', error);
  }
})();

// --- Initialize Socket.IO Namespaces ---
performance.mark('before-sockets');
setupChatSockets();
setupPOSockets();
setupCallSockets();
setupEmailSockets();
setupAISockets();

const audioStreamSocketCleanup = setupAudioStreamSockets(server);
if (typeof audioStreamSocketCleanup === 'function') {
  registerShutdownHook(async () => {
    await audioStreamSocketCleanup();
    console.log('Audio stream sockets cleanup completed.');
  });
} else if (audioStreamSocketCleanup && typeof audioStreamSocketCleanup.close === 'function') {
  registerShutdownHook(async () => {
    await audioStreamSocketCleanup.close();
    console.log('Audio stream sockets close completed.');
  });
}

performance.mark('after-sockets');
performance.measure('Socket Namespaces Setup', 'before-sockets', 'after-sockets');

// --- 404 Handler ---
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({ error: `Endpoint not found: ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}` });
});

app.use(errorHandler);

// --- Start Server ---
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3008;
performance.mark('before-server-listen');
server.listen(PORT, () => {
  performance.mark('server-listen');
  performance.measure('Server Listen Start', 'before-server-listen', 'server-listen');
  performance.measure('Total Initialization Time', 'start', 'server-listen');
  console.log(`🚀 Server is running on port ${PORT} in ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'not set'} mode.`);
});

const closeHttpServer = () =>
  new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    server.close((error) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }

      resolve();
    });
  });

const closeSocketIoServer = () =>
  new Promise((resolve) => {
    io.close(() => {
      resolve();
    });
  });

const destroyOpenSockets = () => {
  for (const socket of openSockets) {
    try {
      socket.destroy();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to destroy socket:', error);
    }
  }
};

const logShutdownState = () => {
  server.getConnections((error, count) => {
    if (error) {
      console.error('Failed to get open HTTP connections:', error);
      return;
    }

    console.log(`Open HTTP connections during shutdown: ${count}`);
  });

  console.log(`Open raw sockets during shutdown: ${openSockets.size}`);
  console.log(`Socket.IO clients during shutdown: ${io.engine.clientsCount}`);
};

const gracefulShutdown = async (signal) => {
  if (isShuttingDown) {
    console.log(`Shutdown already in progress. Ignoring ${signal}.`);
    return;
  }

  isShuttingDown = true;
  console.log(`Signal received (${signal}): closing server...`);
  logShutdownState();

  forceShutdownTimer = setTimeout(async () => {
    console.error('Forced shutdown timeout reached. Destroying lingering sockets.');

    destroyOpenSockets();

    try {
      await prisma.$disconnect();
      console.log('Prisma disconnected during forced shutdown.');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to disconnect Prisma during forced shutdown:', error);
    }

    await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
    process.exit(1);
  }, 10000);

  if (typeof forceShutdownTimer.unref === 'function') {
    forceShutdownTimer.unref();
  }

  try {
    await closeSocketIoServer();
    console.log('Socket.IO server closed');

    await runMaybeAsync(async () => {
      for (const hook of shutdownHooks) {
        await hook();
      }
    }, 'Registered shutdown hooks');

    await closeHttpServer();
    console.log('HTTP server closed');

    destroyOpenSockets();
    obs.disconnect();

    await prisma.$disconnect();
    console.log('Prisma disconnected');

    if (forceShutdownTimer) {
      clearTimeout(forceShutdownTimer);
      forceShutdownTimer = null;
    }

    await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
    process.exit(0);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error during graceful shutdown:', error);

    destroyOpenSockets();

    try {
      await prisma.$disconnect();
      console.log('Prisma disconnected after shutdown error');
    } catch (disconnectError) {
      console.error('Failed to disconnect Prisma after shutdown error:', disconnectError);
    }

    if (forceShutdownTimer) {
      clearTimeout(forceShutdownTimer);
      forceShutdownTimer = null;
    }

    await flushConsoleCaptureWrites();
    process.exit(1);
  }
};

process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  void gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM');
});

process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  void gracefulShutdown('SIGINT');
});

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/shared/utils/asyncHandler.js
//--- File: server/src/shared/utils/asyncHandler.js ---
import { extractRequestContext, logAndReportError } from '../../utils/logError.js';

/**
 * A higher-order function to wrap asynchronous route handlers.
 * It catches any errors and passes them to the next middleware.
 *
 * @param {Function} fn - The asynchronous route handler function.
 * @returns {Function} A new function that wraps the original handler.
 */
const asyncHandler = (fn) => {
    // Ensure that fn is a function
    if (typeof fn !== 'function') {
      throw new TypeError('Expected a function as the argument');
    }
  
    // Return a new function that wraps the original handler
    return function asyncUtilWrap(req, res, next) {
      // Call the handler and catch any errors
      Promise.resolve(fn(req, res, next)).catch((error) => {
        logAndReportError('Async route handler error:', error, extractRequestContext(req));
        next(error);
      });
    };
  };
  
  export default asyncHandler;
  

```

FILE: server/src/shared/utils/auth.js

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/shared/utils/auth.js
import { parse } from 'cookie';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your_jwt_secret_here';

export const getTokenFromRequest = (req) => {
  const cookies = req.headers.cookie ? parse(req.headers.cookie) : {};
  const cookieToken = cookies.token;

  if (cookieToken) {
    return cookieToken;
  }

  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
  if (typeof authHeader === 'string' && authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
    const bearerToken = authHeader.slice('Bearer '.length).trim();
    return bearerToken || null;
  }

  return null;
};

export async function getSession(req) {
  try {
    const token = getTokenFromRequest(req);

    if (!token) {
      console.log('No auth token found in cookies or Authorization header.');
      return null;
    }

    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
    const normalizedUserId = decoded?.userId || decoded?.id || null;

    if (!normalizedUserId) {
      console.warn('Session token missing userId/id.', {
        sessionId: decoded?.sessionId || null,
        username: decoded?.username || null,
      });
      return null;
    }

    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { id: normalizedUserId },
      include: {
        organization: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, phoneNumber: true, slug: true },
        },
        permissions: {
          select: { name: true },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!user) {
      console.log('User not found in database.');
      return null;
    }

    if (user.deletedAt || !user.active) {
      console.log('User account has been deactivated or deleted:', user.id);
      return null;
    }

    if (!user.organization) {
      console.log('Organization not found for user:', user.id);
      return null;
    }

    const sessionUser = {
      ...user,
      id: user.id,
      userId: user.id,
      organizationId: user.organization.id,
      organizationName: user.organization.name,
      organizationSlug: user.organization.slug,
      permissions: user.permissions.map((p) => p.name),
      sessionId: decoded?.sessionId || null,
    };

    return { user: sessionUser };
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Session Error:', error);
    return null;
  }
}

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/shared/utils/bearerToken.js
export function extractBearerToken(authHeader = "") {
  const rawHeader = String(authHeader || "").trim();
  const match = rawHeader.match(/^Bearer\s+([\s\S]+)$/i);
  if (!match) return "";

  let token = match[1].trim();
  token = token.replace(/^["'`]+|["'`]+$/g, "");

  if (token.startsWith("<") && token.endsWith(">")) {
    token = token.slice(1, -1).trim();
  }

  return token;
}

export function isLikelyJwt(value = "") {
  return /^[A-Za-z0-9_-]+\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+$/.test(String(value || "").trim());
}

export const IOS_BLOCKED_ERROR_CODE = 'NEW_ORGANIZATION_NOT_AVAILABLE_ON_IOS';
export const IOS_PURCHASE_BLOCKED_ERROR_CODE = 'PURCHASE_NOT_AVAILABLE_ON_IOS';
export const IOS_UNKNOWN_OAUTH_ERROR_CODE = 'NO_WORKSMRT_ACCOUNT_FOR_OAUTH_ON_IOS';

export const isNativeIOSRequest = (req) => {
  const platform = String(req.headers?.['x-worksmrt-client-platform'] || '').toLowerCase();
  return platform === 'native-ios';
};

export const rejectNativeIOSAction = (req, res, {
  code = IOS_BLOCKED_ERROR_CODE,
  message = 'This action is not available in the WorkSmrt iOS app.',
} = {}) => {
  if (!isNativeIOSRequest(req)) return false;

  res.status(403).json({
    error: message,
    code,
  });
  return true;
};

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/shared/utils/permissionManager.js
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';

export const hasPermission = async (userId, requiredPermission) => {
  if (!userId || !requiredPermission) {
    return false;
  }

  // This query efficiently checks if the user has EITHER the specific permission
  // OR the global 'permission:editAll' override.
  const count = await prisma.user.count({
    where: {
      id: userId,
      permissions: {
        some: {
          name: {
            in: [requiredPermission, 'permission:editAll'],
          },
        },
      },
    },
  });

  return count > 0;
};
```

FILE: server/src/shared/utils/withHandler.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/shared/utils/withHandler.js
import { getSession } from './auth.js';
import { extractBearerToken } from './bearerToken.js';
import { sendErrorResponse } from '#middleware/errorHandler.js';
import { extractRequestContext, logAndReportError } from '../../utils/logError.js';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';

/**
 * Higher-Order Function to handle API route common logic.
 * Updated to support Bearer Token authentication for M2M communication.
 *
 * @param {Object} options - Configuration options.
 * @param {Function} options.handler - The main handler function for the route.
 * @param {Array} options.allowedMethods - List of allowed HTTP methods.
 * @param {Array} [options.requiredRoles=[]] - List of roles required to access the route.
 * @param {Object} [options.schema={}] - Object containing Zod schemas for different methods.
 * @param {Object} [options.requiredBodyParams={}] - Required body parameters per method.
 * @param {Object} [options.requiredQueryParams={}] - Required query parameters per method.
 * @param {Object} [options.requiredBodyParamTypes={}] - Expected types for body parameters per method.
 * @param {Object} [options.requiredQueryParamTypes={}] - Expected types for query parameters per method.
 * @param {boolean} [options.requiresAuth=true] - Whether authentication is required.
 *
 * @returns {Function} - Wrapped API route handler.
 */
const withHandler = ({
  handler,
  allowedMethods = [],
  requiredRoles = [],
  schema = {},
  requiredBodyParams = {},
  requiredQueryParams = {},
  requiredBodyParamTypes = {},
  requiredQueryParamTypes = {},
  requiresAuth = true,
}) => {
  return async (req, res) => {
    try {
      const { method } = req;

      // **1. Method Validation**
      if (!allowedMethods.includes(method)) {
        res.setHeader('Allow', allowedMethods);
        return res.status(405).end(`Method ${method} Not Allowed`);
      }

      // **2. Authentication (Session OR Bearer Token)**
      if (requiresAuth) {
        let user = null;

        // A. Check for Bearer Token (API/M2M Access)
        const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
        if (authHeader && /^Bearer\s+/i.test(authHeader)) {
          const token = extractBearerToken(authHeader);
          try {
            const secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;
            if (!secret) throw new Error('JWT_SECRET not configured');
            
            const decoded = jwt.verify(token, secret);
            const normalizedUserId = decoded?.id || decoded?.userId || null;
            user = {
              ...decoded,
              ...(normalizedUserId ? { id: normalizedUserId, userId: normalizedUserId } : {}),
            };
          } catch (err) {
            console.warn(`[Auth] Invalid Bearer token: ${err.message}`);
            // We continue to check session as a fallback, or fail here.
          }
        }

        // B. Check for Cookie Session (Browser Access)
        if (!user) {
          const session = await getSession(req);
          if (session && session.user) {
            user = session.user;
          }
        }

        // C. Final Auth Check
        if (!user) {
          return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session or token found.' });
        }

        req.user = user;
        
        // Implement permissions check here if needed based on requiredRoles
        if (requiredRoles.length > 0) {
            // Example simple role check
            if (!req.user.role || !requiredRoles.includes(req.user.role)) {
                return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: Insufficient permissions' });
            }
        }
      }

      // **3. Schema Validation with Zod**
      const methodSchema = schema[method];
      if (methodSchema) {
        // Determine which part to validate based on HTTP method
        let validationTarget = method === 'GET' ? req.query : req.body;
        const validation = methodSchema.safeParse(validationTarget);

        if (!validation.success) {
          // Extract and format Zod validation errors
          const errorMessages = validation.error.errors.map(err => ({
            path: err.path.join('.'),
            message: err.message,
          }));
          console.log('Validation Errors:', errorMessages);
          return res.status(400).json({ error: errorMessages });
        }

        // Attach validated data to the request object for use in the handler
        req.validated = validation.data;
      } else {
        // **4. Existing Manual Validation (Legacy support)**
        // Validate required body parameters
        const bodyParams = requiredBodyParams[method] || [];
        if (bodyParams.length > 0) {
          const missingParams = bodyParams.filter(
            (param) => !(param in req.body)
          );
          if (missingParams.length > 0) {
            return res.status(400).json({
              error: `Missing required fields: ${missingParams.join(', ')}`,
            });
          }
        }

        // Validate required query parameters
        const queryParams = requiredQueryParams[method] || [];
        if (queryParams.length > 0) {
          const missingParams = queryParams.filter(
            (param) => !(param in req.query)
          );
          if (missingParams.length > 0) {
            return res.status(400).json({
              error: `Missing required query parameters: ${missingParams.join(
                ', '
              )}`,
            });
          }
        }

        // **Type Validation for Body Params**
        const bodyTypes = requiredBodyParamTypes[method] || {};
        for (const [param, type] of Object.entries(bodyTypes)) {
          if (type === 'string' && typeof req.body[param] !== 'string') {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a string.` });
          }
          if (type === 'number' && typeof req.body[param] !== 'number') {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a number.` });
          }
          if (type === 'boolean' && typeof req.body[param] !== 'boolean') {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a boolean.` });
          }
        }

        // **Type Validation for Query Params**
        const queryTypes = requiredQueryParamTypes[method] || {};
        for (const [param, type] of Object.entries(queryTypes)) {
          if (type === 'string' && typeof req.query[param] !== 'string') {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a string.` });
          }
          if (type === 'number' && isNaN(Number(req.query[param]))) {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a number.` });
          }
          if (type === 'boolean') {
            const val = req.query[param].toLowerCase();
            if (val !== 'true' && val !== 'false') {
              return res.status(400).json({ error: `${param} must be a boolean.` });
            }
          }
        }
      }

      // **5. Execute the Main Handler**
      return handler(req, res);
    } catch (error) {
      logAndReportError('withHandler error:', error, extractRequestContext(req));
      sendErrorResponse(res, error, extractRequestContext(req));
    }
  };
};

export default withHandler;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/camera/CameraPanel.jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import {
  Upload,
  Camera,
  RotateCw,
  Zap,
  Settings,
  Clipboard,
  Mail,
  Image as ImageIcon,
  FileText,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { mutate } from 'swr';
import CustomCamera from './CustomCamera';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { captureNativeReceiptPhoto } from '@/shared/utils/nativeBridge';
import DuplicateReceiptModal from '../DuplicateReceiptModal';
import ImportReceiptFromEmailModal from '../ImportReceiptFromEmailModal';

const IMAGE_SIGNATURES = {
  jpeg: [0xff, 0xd8, 0xff],
  png: [0x89, 0x50, 0x4e, 0x47],
  heicBrands: ['ftypheic', 'ftypheix', 'ftyphevc', 'ftyphevx', 'ftypmif1', 'ftypmsf1'],
};

const blobHasImageSignature = async (blob) => {
  if (!blob || blob.size === 0) return false;

  const bytes = new Uint8Array(await blob.slice(0, 32).arrayBuffer());
  const isJpeg = IMAGE_SIGNATURES.jpeg.every((byte, index) => bytes[index] === byte);
  const isPng = IMAGE_SIGNATURES.png.every((byte, index) => bytes[index] === byte);
  const asciiHeader = Array.from(bytes)
    .map((byte) => (byte >= 32 && byte <= 126 ? String.fromCharCode(byte) : ''))
    .join('');

  return isJpeg || isPng || IMAGE_SIGNATURES.heicBrands.some((brand) => asciiHeader.includes(brand));
};

const buildNativePhotoUrlCandidates = (photo) => {
  if (!photo) return [];

  const candidates = [];
  if (photo.dataUrl) candidates.push(photo.dataUrl);

  const capacitor = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.Capacitor : null;
  [photo.webPath, photo.path].forEach((path) => {
    if (!path) return;

    if (typeof capacitor?.convertFileSrc === 'function' && /^(file|content):\/\//i.test(path)) {
      candidates.push(capacitor.convertFileSrc(path));
    }

    candidates.push(path);
  });

  return Array.from(new Set(candidates));
};

const fetchNativePhotoBlob = async (photo) => {
  const photoUrls = buildNativePhotoUrlCandidates(photo);
  if (photoUrls.length === 0) {
    throw new Error('No captured photo path was returned.');
  }

  let lastError = null;
  for (const photoUrl of photoUrls) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(photoUrl);
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`Unable to read captured photo (${response.status}).`);
      }

      const blob = await response.blob();
      if (!(await blobHasImageSignature(blob))) {
        throw new Error('Captured photo was not returned as a readable image.');
      }

      return {
        blob,
        contentType: response.headers.get('content-type') || '',
      };
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
    }
  }

  throw lastError || new Error('Unable to read captured photo.');
};

const nativePhotoToFile = async (photo, fallbackNamePrefix = 'receipt') => {
  const { blob, contentType } = await fetchNativePhotoBlob(photo);

  const format = photo?.format === 'png' || contentType.includes('png') ? 'png' : 'jpg';
  const mimeType = photo?.mimeType || blob.type || (format === 'png' ? 'image/png' : 'image/jpeg');
  const fileName = photo?.fileName || `${fallbackNamePrefix}_${Date.now()}.${format}`;

  return new File([blob], fileName, { type: mimeType });
};

const CameraPanel = () => {
  const [isCameraOpen, setIsCameraOpen] = useState(false);
  const [uploading, setUploading] = useState(false);
  const cameraRef = useRef(null);
  const galleryInputRef = useRef(null);
  const fileInputRef = useRef(null);
  const cameraUploadInputRef = useRef(null);
  const [availableCameras, setAvailableCameras] = useState([]);
  const [currentCameraIndex, setCurrentCameraIndex] = useState(0);
  const [isTorchOn, setIsTorchOn] = useState(false);
  const [torchSupported, setTorchSupported] = useState(false);
  const [focusSettingsOpen, setFocusSettingsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [showPasteArea, setShowPasteArea] = useState(false);
  const [pastedFiles, setPastedFiles] = useState([]);
  const [pastedText, setPastedText] = useState('');
  const [showDuplicateModal, setShowDuplicateModal] = useState(false);
  const [duplicateReceipt, setDuplicateReceipt] = useState(null);
  const [newReceiptData, setNewReceiptData] = useState(null);
  const [showImportEmailModal, setShowImportEmailModal] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const getCameras = async () => {
      if (typeof navigator !== 'undefined' && navigator.mediaDevices && typeof navigator.mediaDevices.enumerateDevices === 'function') {
        try {
          const devices = await navigator.mediaDevices.enumerateDevices();
          const videoDevices = devices.filter((device) => device.kind === 'videoinput');
          setAvailableCameras(videoDevices);

          const rearIndex = videoDevices.findIndex((device) =>
            device.label.toLowerCase().includes('back') ||
            device.label.toLowerCase().includes('rear') ||
            !device.label.toLowerCase().includes('front')
          );
          setCurrentCameraIndex(rearIndex >= 0 ? rearIndex : 0);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error enumerating devices:', error);
          toast.error('Unable to access camera devices.');
        }
      }
    };

    getCameras();
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (availableCameras.length > 0 && currentCameraIndex >= availableCameras.length) {
      setCurrentCameraIndex(0);
    }
  }, [availableCameras, currentCameraIndex]);

  const uploadFiles = useCallback(async (files) => {
    if (!files || files.length === 0) {
      toast.error('No files to upload.');
      return null;
    }

    setUploading(true);
    const processingToast = toast.loading('Uploading receipt...', {
      position: 'top-right',
      autoClose: false,
      closeButton: false,
    });

    const formData = new FormData();
    Array.from(files).forEach((file) => formData.append('files', file));

    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/upload`, {
        method: 'POST',
        credentials: 'include',
        body: formData,
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to upload receipt.');
      }
      toast.update(processingToast, {
        render: 'Receipt uploaded successfully!',
        type: 'success',
        isLoading: false,
        autoClose: 3000,
        closeButton: true,
      });
      mutate(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/receipt`);
      return data;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error uploading receipt:', error);
      toast.update(processingToast, {
        render: `Error uploading receipt: ${error.message}`,
        type: 'error',
        isLoading: false,
        autoClose: 5000,
        closeButton: true,
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      setUploading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  const checkForDuplicate = useCallback(async (receiptData) => {
    if (!receiptData) return;

    setNewReceiptData(receiptData);
    const dupRes = await fetchWithAuth('/api/receipt/checkDuplicate', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        companyName: receiptData.companyName,
        total: receiptData.total,
        date: receiptData.date,
      }),
    });
    const duplicateData = await dupRes.json();
    if (duplicateData.duplicates && duplicateData.duplicates.length > 0) {
      setDuplicateReceipt(duplicateData.duplicates[0]);
      setShowDuplicateModal(true);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleFileUploadResult = useCallback(async (result) => {
    if (result?.receipts?.length > 0) {
      await checkForDuplicate(result.receipts[0]);
    }
  }, [checkForDuplicate]);

  const handleGalleryChange = useCallback(async (event) => {
    try {
      const result = await uploadFiles(event.target.files);
      event.target.value = '';
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
    }
  }, [uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const handleFileChange = useCallback(async (event) => {
    try {
      const result = await uploadFiles(event.target.files);
      event.target.value = '';
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
    }
  }, [uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const handleCameraUploadChange = useCallback(async (event) => {
    try {
      const result = await uploadFiles(event.target.files);
      event.target.value = '';
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
    }
  }, [uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const handleNativeCameraUpload = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      const nativePhoto = await captureNativeReceiptPhoto();
      if (nativePhoto?.dataUrl || nativePhoto?.webPath || nativePhoto?.path) {
        const file = await nativePhotoToFile(nativePhoto);
        const result = await uploadFiles([file]);
        await handleFileUploadResult(result);
        return;
      }

      const capacitor = window.Capacitor;
      if (!capacitor?.Plugins?.Camera) {
        cameraUploadInputRef.current?.click();
        return;
      }

      const photo = await capacitor.Plugins.Camera.getPhoto({
        quality: 90,
        allowEditing: false,
        resultType: 'Uri',
        source: 'CAMERA',
      });
      if (!photo?.webPath) {
        toast.error('Failed to capture photo.');
        return;
      }
      const file = await nativePhotoToFile(photo);
      const result = await uploadFiles([file]);
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Camera upload error:', error);
      if (error.message?.includes('cancel') || error.code === 'CAMERA_CANCELLED') return;
      toast.error(`Camera upload failed: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }, [uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const handleCapture = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!cameraRef.current) {
      toast.error('Camera not ready.');
      return;
    }

    try {
      const imageSrc = await cameraRef.current.takePhoto('base64url');
      if (!imageSrc) {
        toast.error('Failed to capture image.');
        return;
      }

      const res = await fetch(imageSrc);
      const blob = await res.blob();
      const file = new File([blob], `receipt_${Date.now()}.jpg`, { type: 'image/jpeg' });
      const result = await uploadFiles([file]);
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error uploading receipt:', error);
      toast.error(`Error uploading receipt: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }, [uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const handlePaste = useCallback((event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    const items = event.clipboardData.items;
    let fileAdded = false;

    for (let index = 0; index < items.length; index += 1) {
      const item = items[index];
      if (item.kind === 'file') {
        const blob = item.getAsFile();
        if (blob) {
          const ext = blob.type.split('/')[1] || 'jpg';
          const file = new File([blob], `pasted-receipt-${Date.now()}.${ext}`, { type: blob.type });
          setPastedFiles((prev) => [...prev, file]);
          fileAdded = true;
        }
      }
    }

    if (!fileAdded) {
      const text = event.clipboardData.getData('text');
      setPastedText(text);
    }
  }, []);

  const handleUploadPasted = useCallback(async () => {
    try {
      let result;
      if (pastedFiles.length > 0) {
        result = await uploadFiles(pastedFiles);
      } else if (pastedText.trim()) {
        const textFile = new File([pastedText], `pasted-receipt-${Date.now()}.txt`, { type: 'text/plain' });
        result = await uploadFiles([textFile]);
      } else {
        toast.error('Nothing to upload.');
        return;
      }

      setPastedFiles([]);
      setPastedText('');
      setShowPasteArea(false);
      await handleFileUploadResult(result);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
    }
  }, [pastedFiles, pastedText, uploadFiles, handleFileUploadResult]);

  const toggleTorch = useCallback(async (enable) => {
    if (!cameraRef.current) {
      toast.error('Camera not ready.');
      return;
    }

    try {
      cameraRef.current.toggleTorch();
      setIsTorchOn(enable);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error toggling torch:', error);
      toast.error('Unable to toggle torch.');
    }
  }, []);

  const toggleCamera = useCallback(() => {
    setIsCameraOpen((prev) => !prev);
    if (isCameraOpen && isTorchOn) {
      toggleTorch(false);
    }
  }, [isCameraOpen, isTorchOn, toggleTorch]);

  const handleChangeCamera = useCallback(() => {
    if (availableCameras.length <= 1) {
      toast.info('Only one camera detected.');
      return;
    }
    setCurrentCameraIndex((prevIndex) => (prevIndex + 1) % availableCameras.length);
  }, [availableCameras.length]);

  const switchCameraHandler = useCallback(() => {
    setCurrentCameraIndex((prevIndex) => (prevIndex + 1) % availableCameras.length);
  }, [availableCameras.length]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (cameraRef.current) {
      setTorchSupported(cameraRef.current.torchSupported);
    }
  }, [isCameraOpen]);

  const handleDuplicateConfirm = async () => {
    toast.success('Receipt kept despite duplicate warning.');
    setShowDuplicateModal(false);
    setDuplicateReceipt(null);
    setNewReceiptData(null);
  };

  const handleDuplicateCancel = async () => {
    if (newReceiptData?.id) {
      try {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth('/api/receipt/delete', {
          method: 'DELETE',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ id: newReceiptData.id }),
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          toast.info('Duplicate receipt archived.');
        } else {
          toast.error(data.error || 'Error deleting duplicate receipt.');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Delete error:', error);
        toast.error('Error deleting duplicate receipt.');
      }
    }
    setShowDuplicateModal(false);
    setDuplicateReceipt(null);
    setNewReceiptData(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="card bg-base-100 shadow-lg border border-base-300">
      <div className="card-body p-4 md:p-5 space-y-5">
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 lg:flex-row lg:items-start lg:justify-between">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 p-3">
              <Camera className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-base-content">Upload Receipt</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Use your phone camera, gallery, files, clipboard, or email. Optimized for fast mobile capture.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-base-content/60">
            {uploading && <span className="badge badge-warning">Uploading...</span>}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-6 gap-3">
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={handleNativeCameraUpload}
            className="btn btn-primary min-h-24 flex-col gap-2"
          >
            <Camera className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">Camera Upload</span>
          </button>

          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => galleryInputRef.current?.click()}
            className="btn btn-secondary min-h-24 flex-col gap-2"
            disabled={uploading}
          >
            <ImageIcon className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">Upload from Gallery</span>
          </button>

          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
            className="btn btn-secondary min-h-24 flex-col gap-2"
            disabled={uploading}
          >
            <FileText className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">Upload File</span>
          </button>

          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowPasteArea(true)}
            className="btn btn-accent min-h-24 flex-col gap-2"
            disabled={uploading}
          >
            <Clipboard className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">Paste Receipt</span>
          </button>

          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowImportEmailModal(true)}
            className="btn btn-info min-h-24 flex-col gap-2"
            disabled={uploading}
          >
            <Mail className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">Import from Email</span>
          </button>

          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={toggleCamera}
            className={`btn min-h-24 flex-col gap-2 ${isCameraOpen ? 'btn-success' : 'btn-outline btn-success'}`}
          >
            <Camera className="w-5 h-5" />
            <span className="text-xs font-medium normal-case text-center">{isCameraOpen ? 'Close Live Camera' : 'Open Live Camera'}</span>
          </button>
        </div>

        <input
          ref={galleryInputRef}
          type="file"
          multiple
          accept="image/*"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={handleGalleryChange}
        />
        <input
          ref={fileInputRef}
          type="file"
          multiple
          accept=".jpg,.jpeg,.png,.heic,.heif,.pdf,.txt,.csv,image/jpeg,image/png,image/heic,image/heif,application/pdf,text/plain,text/csv"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={handleFileChange}
        />
        <input
          ref={cameraUploadInputRef}
          type="file"
          accept="image/*"
          capture="environment"
          className="hidden"
          onChange={handleCameraUploadChange}
        />

        {showPasteArea && (
          <div className="rounded-2xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4 space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2">
              <p className="font-semibold text-sm text-base-content">Paste receipt text or image</p>
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowPasteArea(false);
                  setPastedFiles([]);
                  setPastedText('');
                }}
                className="btn btn-xs btn-ghost"
              >
                Close
              </button>
            </div>
            <textarea
              className="textarea textarea-bordered w-full bg-base-100"
              placeholder="Paste receipt text here, or paste an image from your clipboard..."
              onPaste={handlePaste}
              onChange={(event) => setPastedText(event.target.value)}
              value={pastedText}
              rows={4}
            />
            {pastedFiles.length > 0 && (
              <div>
                <p className="text-xs font-medium text-base-content/60 mb-2">Preview</p>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {pastedFiles.map((file, index) => (
                    <img
                      key={`${file.name}-${index}`}
                      src={URL.createObjectURL(file)}
                      alt="Pasted receipt preview"
                      className="max-w-[140px] rounded-xl border border-base-300 bg-base-100"
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              <button type="button" onClick={handleUploadPasted} className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" disabled={uploading}>
                {uploading ? 'Uploading...' : 'Upload Pasted Receipt'}
              </button>
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowPasteArea(false);
                  setPastedFiles([]);
                  setPastedText('');
                }}
                className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm"
              >
                Cancel
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {isCameraOpen && (
          <div className="rounded-3xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-3 sm:p-4 space-y-3">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-2">
              <div>
                <h4 className="font-semibold text-base-content">Live Camera Capture</h4>
                <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Capture directly, then preview and clean it up inside the receipt details modal.</p>
              </div>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                <button type="button" onClick={handleCapture} className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" disabled={uploading}>
                  <Camera className="w-4 h-4" />
                  Capture & Upload
                </button>
                {availableCameras.length > 1 && (
                  <button type="button" onClick={handleChangeCamera} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle" title="Change Camera">
                    <RotateCw className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                )}
                {torchSupported && (
                  <button type="button" onClick={() => toggleTorch(!isTorchOn)} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle" title={isTorchOn ? 'Turn off Torch' : 'Turn on Torch'}>
                    <Zap className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                )}
                {cameraRef.current?.focusSupported && (
                  <button type="button" onClick={() => setFocusSettingsOpen((prev) => !prev)} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle" title="Focus Settings">
                    <Settings className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="relative mx-auto w-full max-w-md rounded-2xl shadow border border-base-300 overflow-hidden bg-base-200/60">
              <CustomCamera
                ref={cameraRef}
                facingMode={
                  availableCameras.length > 0 && availableCameras[currentCameraIndex].label.toLowerCase().includes('front')
                    ? 'user'
                    : 'environment'
                }
                videoSourceDeviceId={availableCameras.length > 0 ? availableCameras[currentCameraIndex].deviceId : undefined}
                aspectRatio="cover"
                onCapture={() => {}}
                onSwitchCamera={switchCameraHandler}
                enableTorch={isTorchOn}
              />
            </div>

            {focusSettingsOpen && cameraRef.current?.focusSupported && (
              <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-base-100 p-4 rounded-2xl shadow border border-base-300 mx-auto">
                <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold mb-3 text-base-content">Focus Settings</h4>
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 text-sm">
                  <label className="form-control gap-1">
                    <span className="text-base-content/70">Focus Mode</span>
                    <select
                      value={cameraRef.current.focusMode || 'auto'}
                      onChange={(event) => {
                        cameraRef.current.setFocusMode(event.target.value);
                      }}
                      className="select select-bordered w-full"
                    >
                      <option value="auto">Auto</option>
                      <option value="continuous">Continuous</option>
                      <option value="manual">Manual</option>
                    </select>
                  </label>
                  {cameraRef.current.focusMode === 'manual' && (
                    <label className="form-control gap-1">
                      <span className="text-base-content/70">Focus Distance (meters)</span>
                      <input
                        type="range"
                        min="0"
                        max="3"
                        step="0.1"
                        value={cameraRef.current.focusDistance || 0}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          cameraRef.current.setFocusDistance(parseFloat(event.target.value));
                        }}
                        className="range range-primary"
                      />
                      <span className="text-base-content/70">{cameraRef.current.focusDistance ? cameraRef.current.focusDistance.toFixed(1) : '0.0'} m</span>
                    </label>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {showDuplicateModal && duplicateReceipt && (
          <DuplicateReceiptModal duplicate={duplicateReceipt} onConfirm={handleDuplicateConfirm} onCancel={handleDuplicateCancel} />
        )}

        {showImportEmailModal && (
          <ImportReceiptFromEmailModal isOpen={showImportEmailModal} onClose={() => setShowImportEmailModal(false)} />
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default CameraPanel;

```

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: client/services/receipt/components/camera/CustomCamera.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/camera/CustomCamera.jsx
import React, {
  useState,
  useEffect,
  useRef,
  useImperativeHandle,
  forwardRef,
} from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { Zap } from 'lucide-react';
import styles from './CustomCamera.module.css';

const CustomCamera = forwardRef((props, ref) => {
  const {
    facingMode = 'environment',
    aspectRatio = 'cover',
    videoSourceDeviceId,
    errorMessages = {
      noCameraAccessible:
        'No camera device accessible. Please connect your camera or try a different browser.',
      permissionDenied:
        'Permission denied. Please refresh and give camera permission.',
      canvas: 'Canvas is not supported.',
    },
    videoReadyCallback,
    onCapture,
    onSwitchCamera,
    enableTorch = false,
  } = props;

  const videoRef = useRef(null);
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  const containerRef = useRef(null);

  const [stream, setStream] = useState(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState('');
  const [torchSupported, setTorchSupported] = useState(false);
  const [torchOn, setTorchOn] = useState(false);
  const [availableCameras, setAvailableCameras] = useState([]);

  // Focus Control States
  const [focusMode, setFocusMode] = useState('continuous'); // 'auto', 'continuous', 'manual'
  const [focusDistance, setFocusDistance] = useState(0); // In meters
  const [focusSupported, setFocusSupported] = useState(false);

  // Tap-to-Focus State
  const [focusArea, setFocusArea] = useState(null); // { x, y, width, height }

  // Fetch available camera devices on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchCameras = async () => {
      // Ensure this code runs only in the browser
      if (typeof navigator !== 'undefined' && navigator.mediaDevices) {
        try {
          const devices = await navigator.mediaDevices.enumerateDevices();
          const videoDevices = devices.filter(
            (device) => device.kind === 'videoinput'
          );
          setAvailableCameras(videoDevices);
        } catch (err) {
          console.error('Error fetching camera devices:', err);
          toast.error(errorMessages.noCameraAccessible);
          setError(''); // Clear internal error state
        }
      } else {
        console.warn('Media Devices API not supported.');
        toast.error('Media Devices API not supported in this browser.');
      }
    };

    fetchCameras();
  }, [errorMessages.noCameraAccessible]);

  // Initialize camera stream
  useEffect(() => {
    const initCamera = async () => {
      if (
        typeof navigator === 'undefined' ||
        !navigator.mediaDevices ||
        !navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia
      ) {
        toast.error(errorMessages.noCameraAccessible);
        setError('');
        return;
      }

      const constraints = {
        audio: false,
        video: {
          deviceId: videoSourceDeviceId
            ? { exact: videoSourceDeviceId }
            : undefined,
          facingMode: facingMode,
          width: { ideal: 1920 },
          height: { ideal: 1080 },
          focusMode: focusMode,
          focusDistance: focusDistance,
        },
      };

      try {
        const mediaStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(
          constraints
        );
        setStream(mediaStream);
        if (videoRef.current) {
          videoRef.current.srcObject = mediaStream;
          videoRef.current.onloadedmetadata = async () => {
            videoRef.current.play();
            if (videoReadyCallback) videoReadyCallback();
            checkFocusSupport(mediaStream);
            
            const track = mediaStream.getVideoTracks()[0];
            if (track) {
              const capabilities = track.getCapabilities();
              if (capabilities.focusMode) {
                try {
                  await track.applyConstraints({
                    advanced: [{ focusMode: focusMode }]
                  });
                } catch (err) {
                  console.error('Error applying focus constraints:', err);
                  toast.error('Unable to apply focus settings.');
                }
              }
            }
          };
        }

        // Check for torch support
        const videoTrack = mediaStream.getVideoTracks()[0];
        const capabilities = videoTrack.getCapabilities();
        if (capabilities.torch) {
          setTorchSupported(true);
        } else {
          setTorchSupported(false);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Error accessing camera:', err);
        if (
          err.name === 'NotAllowedError' ||
          err.name === 'PermissionDeniedError'
        ) {
          toast.error(errorMessages.permissionDenied);
        } else {
          toast.error(errorMessages.noCameraAccessible);
        }
        setError(''); // Clear internal error state
      }
    };

    initCamera();

    return () => {
      if (stream) {
        stream.getTracks().forEach((track) => track.stop());
      }
    };
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [facingMode, videoSourceDeviceId, focusMode, focusDistance]);

  // Function to check focus capabilities
  const checkFocusSupport = (mediaStream) => {
    const videoTrack = mediaStream.getVideoTracks()[0];
    const capabilities = videoTrack.getCapabilities();
    if ('focusMode' in capabilities && 'focusDistance' in capabilities) {
      setFocusSupported(true);
    } else {
      setFocusSupported(false);
      toast.info('Focus control is not supported on this device.');
    }
  };

  // Torch functionality
  useEffect(() => {
    const toggleTorchFunction = async (enable) => {
      if (stream) {
        const videoTrack = stream.getVideoTracks()[0];
        const capabilities = videoTrack.getCapabilities();
        if (capabilities.torch) {
          try {
            await videoTrack.applyConstraints({
              advanced: [{ torch: enable }],
            });
            setTorchOn(enable);
          } catch (err) {
            console.error('Error toggling torch:', err);
            toast.error('Unable to toggle torch.');
          }
        } else {
          toast.error('Torch not supported on this device.');
        }
      }
    };

    if (enableTorch && torchSupported) {
      toggleTorchFunction(torchOn);
    }
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [enableTorch, torchSupported]);

  // Expose methods to parent via ref
  useImperativeHandle(ref, () => ({
    takePhoto: async (type = 'base64url') => {
      if (!stream) {
        throw new Error(errorMessages.noCameraAccessible);
      }

      if ('ImageCapture' in window) {
        try {
          const track = stream.getVideoTracks()[0];
          const imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);
          const blob = await imageCapture.takePhoto();
          if (type === 'imgData') {
            const img = new Image();
            img.src = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            await new Promise(resolve => (img.onload = resolve));
            const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
            canvas.width = img.width;
            canvas.height = img.height;
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
            return ctx.getImageData(0, 0, img.width, img.height);
          } else {
            return URL.createObjectURL(blob);
          }
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Error capturing photo with ImageCapture:', error);
          toast.error('Failed to capture photo with ImageCapture. Falling back to canvas.');
        }
      }
      
      try {
        if (!videoRef.current) {
          throw new Error(errorMessages.noCameraAccessible);
        }

        const video = videoRef.current;
        const canvas = canvasRef.current;
        if (!canvas) {
          throw new Error(errorMessages.canvas);
        }

        const context = canvas.getContext('2d');
        const width = video.videoWidth;
        const height = video.videoHeight;

        canvas.width = width;
        canvas.height = height;
        context.drawImage(video, 0, 0, width, height);

        let imgData;
        if (type === 'imgData') {
          imgData = context.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
        } else {
          imgData = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg');
        }

        if (onCapture) {
          onCapture(imgData);
        }

        return imgData;
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error capturing photo:', error);
        toast.error(error.message);
        return null;
      }
    },
    switchCamera: () => {
      if (availableCameras.length < 2) {
        toast.info('Only one camera is available.');
        return;
      }
      const newFacingMode = facingMode === 'user' ? 'environment' : 'user';
      if (onSwitchCamera) onSwitchCamera(newFacingMode);
    },
    toggleTorch: () => {
      if (torchSupported) {
        setTorchOn((prev) => !prev);
      } else {
        toast.error('Torch is not supported on this device.');
      }
    },
    getNumberOfCameras: () => availableCameras.length,
    torchSupported: torchSupported,
    // Expose focus controls
    setFocusMode: (mode) => setFocusMode(mode),
    setFocusDistance: (distance) => setFocusDistance(distance),
    focusSupported: focusSupported,
    focusMode: focusMode,
    focusDistance: focusDistance,
  }));

  // Handle Torch Toggle Button Click
  const handleTorchToggle = () => {
    if (torchSupported) {
      setTorchOn((prev) => !prev);
    } else {
      toast.error('Torch is not supported on this device.');
    }
  };

  // Handle Focus Mode Change
  const handleFocusModeChange = (e) => {
    setFocusMode(e.target.value);
  };

  // Handle Focus Distance Change
  const handleFocusDistanceChange = (e) => {
    setFocusDistance(parseFloat(e.target.value));
  };

  // Handle Tap-to-Focus
  const handleTapToFocus = async (e) => {
    if (!focusSupported || !stream) return;

    const rect = containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
    const y = e.clientY - rect.top;

    const xPercent = x / rect.width;
    const yPercent = y / rect.height;

    const video = videoRef.current;
    const videoWidth = video.videoWidth;
    const videoHeight = video.videoHeight;

    const focusX = videoWidth * xPercent;
    const focusY = videoHeight * yPercent;

    // Set focus area (e.g., 50x50 pixels)
    setFocusArea({
      x: x - 25,
      y: y - 25,
      width: 50,
      height: 50,
    });

    // Apply focus constraints
    const videoTrack = stream.getVideoTracks()[0];
    try {
      await videoTrack.applyConstraints({
        advanced: [
          {
            focusMode: 'manual',
            focusDistance: focusDistance,
            // Note: Specifying focus area is not widely supported yet
            // This is a placeholder for future enhancements or specialized libraries
          },
        ],
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error setting focus:', err);
      toast.error('Unable to set focus.');
    }

    // Remove focus area after a delay
    setTimeout(() => {
      setFocusArea(null);
    }, 2000);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={styles.container}
      ref={containerRef}
      onClick={handleTapToFocus}
    >
      <video
        ref={videoRef}
        className={styles.video}
        muted
        autoPlay
        playsInline
      />
      <canvas ref={canvasRef} className={styles.canvas} />

      {/* Focus Controls */}
      {focusSupported && (
        <div className={styles.focusControls}>
          <label>
            Focus Mode:
            <select value={focusMode} onChange={handleFocusModeChange}>
              <option value="auto">Auto</option>
              <option value="continuous">Continuous</option>
              <option value="manual">Manual</option>
            </select>
          </label>
          {focusMode === 'manual' && (
            <label>
              Focus Distance (meters):
              <input
                type="range"
                min="0"
                max="3"
                step="0.1"
                value={focusDistance}
                onChange={handleFocusDistanceChange}
              />
              <span>{focusDistance.toFixed(1)}m</span>
            </label>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Visual Indicator for Tap-to-Focus */}
      {focusArea && (
        <div
          className={styles.focusIndicator}
          style={{
            top: focusArea.y,
            left: focusArea.x,
            width: focusArea.width,
            height: focusArea.height,
          }}
        />
      )}

      {/* Torch Toggle Button */}
      {torchSupported && (
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={handleTorchToggle}
          className={`${styles.torchButton} ${
            torchOn ? styles.torchOn : styles.torchOff
          }`}
          aria-label={torchOn ? 'Turn off Torch' : 'Turn on Torch'}
          title={torchOn ? 'Turn off Torch' : 'Turn on Torch'}
        >
          <Zap className="w-4 h-4" />
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
});

CustomCamera.propTypes = {
  facingMode: PropTypes.oneOf(['user', 'environment']),
  aspectRatio: PropTypes.oneOf(['cover', 'contain']),
  videoSourceDeviceId: PropTypes.string,
  errorMessages: PropTypes.shape({
    noCameraAccessible: PropTypes.string,
    permissionDenied: PropTypes.string,
    canvas: PropTypes.string,
  }),
  videoReadyCallback: PropTypes.func,
  onCapture: PropTypes.func,
  onSwitchCamera: PropTypes.func,
  enableTorch: PropTypes.bool,
};

CustomCamera.defaultProps = {
  facingMode: 'environment', // Default to back-facing camera
  aspectRatio: 'cover',
  errorMessages: {
    noCameraAccessible:
      'No camera device accessible. Please connect your camera or try a different browser.',
    permissionDenied:
      'Permission denied. Please refresh and give camera permission.',
    canvas: 'Canvas is not supported.',
  },
  videoReadyCallback: () => {},
  onCapture: () => {},
  onSwitchCamera: () => {},
  enableTorch: false,
};

export default CustomCamera;
```

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/DuplicateReceiptModal.jsx
// client/services/receipt/components/DuplicateReceiptModal.js

import React from 'react';
import { X, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';

const DuplicateReceiptModal = ({ duplicate, onConfirm, onCancel }) => {
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-base-300/70 backdrop-blur-sm flex justify-center items-center z-50">
      <div className="card bg-base-100 shadow-2xl w-11/12 lg:w-[520px] border border-base-300 relative">
        <button
          onClick={onCancel}
          className="btn btn-circle btn-ghost btn-xs absolute top-3 right-3"
          aria-label="Close Modal"
        >
          <X className="w-4 h-4" />
        </button>

        <div className="card-body p-5 md:p-6 space-y-4">
          <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
            <div className="rounded-2xl bg-warning/15 p-3">
              <AlertTriangle className="w-5 h-5 text-warning" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-base-content">Possible duplicate receipt</h3>
              <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60 mt-1">
                A receipt with similar details already exists. Review the match below before keeping the new one.
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="rounded-2xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4 space-y-3">
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">Company</div>
              <div className="mt-1 font-medium text-base-content">{duplicate.companyName}</div>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <div>
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">Date</div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-base-content/80">
                  {new Date(duplicate.date).toLocaleDateString()}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">Amount</div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-base-content/80">${duplicate.total.toFixed(2)}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="rounded-xl bg-base-200/40 border border-base-300 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-base-content/70">
            Keep the new receipt if this is a legitimate repeat purchase. Cancel if this looks like the same receipt uploaded twice.
          </div>

          <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
            <button onClick={onCancel} className="btn btn-ghost">
              Delete new receipt
            </button>
            <button onClick={onConfirm} className="btn btn-primary">
              Keep new receipt
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default DuplicateReceiptModal;

FILE: client/services/receipt/components/DuplicateReceiptsDashboard.jsx
