```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/DuplicateReceiptsDashboard.jsx
import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { Trash } from 'lucide-react';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import ReceiptsDetail from './ReceiptsDetails';

const DuplicateReceiptsDashboard = () => {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [groups, setGroups] = useState([]);
  const [selectedReceipt, setSelectedReceipt] = useState(null);

  const fetchDuplicates = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/findDuplicates`
      );
      const data = await res.json();
      if (res.ok) {
        setGroups(data.groups);
      } else {
        toast.error(data.error || 'Error fetching duplicates');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Reusable deletion function using your endpoint
  const handleDelete = useCallback(
    async (receipt) => {
      if (!window.confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this receipt?')) return;
      try {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(
          `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/delete`,
          {
            method: 'DELETE',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ id: receipt.id, imgName: receipt.imgName }),
          }
        );
        const data = await res.json();
        if (res.ok) {
          toast.success('Receipt deleted successfully');
          fetchDuplicates();
        } else {
          throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to delete receipt.');
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error deleting receipt:', error);
        toast.error(`Error deleting receipt: ${error.message}`);
      }
    },
    []
  );

  // Delete the first receipt of the given group
  const handleDeleteFirst = async (groupIndex) => {
    const group = groups[groupIndex];
    if (!group || !group.receipts || group.receipts.length === 0) return;
    const receiptToDelete = group.receipts[0];
    await handleDelete(receiptToDelete);
  };

  // When a row is clicked, open the receipt details modal
  const handleRowClick = (receipt) => {
    setSelectedReceipt(receipt);
  };

  const handleCloseDetail = () => {
    setSelectedReceipt(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-4">
      <button
        onClick={fetchDuplicates}
        className="btn btn-primary mb-4"
        disabled={loading}
      >
        {loading ? 'Finding duplicates...' : 'Find Duplicate Receipts'}
      </button>

      {groups.length === 0 && !loading && (
        <p>No duplicate receipts found.</p>
      )}

      {groups.map((group, index) => (
        <div
          key={`${group.companyName}-${group.total}`}
          className="card mb-4 p-4 border rounded"
        >
          <h4 className="font-bold mb-2">
            Group {index + 1}: {group.companyName} - ${group.total} (Count: {group.count})
          </h4>
          <table className="min-w-full mb-2 border-collapse">
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 border">Date</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 border">Company Name</th>
                <th className="px-2 py-1 border">Amount</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {group.receipts.map((receipt) => (
                <tr
                  key={receipt.id}
                  className="cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-50"
                  onClick={() => handleRowClick(receipt)}
                >
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 border">
                    {new Date(receipt.date).toLocaleDateString()}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 border">
                    {receipt.companyName || 'N/A'}
                  </td>
                  <td className="px-2 py-1 border">
                    ${receipt.total.toFixed(2)}
                  </td>
                </tr>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
          <button
            onClick={() => handleDeleteFirst(index)}
            className="btn btn-danger"
          >
            Delete First Item
          </button>
        </div>
      ))}

      {/* Receipt Details Modal */}
      {selectedReceipt && (
        <ReceiptsDetail
          receipt={selectedReceipt}
          onClose={handleCloseDetail}
          onUpdate={fetchDuplicates}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default DuplicateReceiptsDashboard;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ImportReceiptFromEmailModal.jsx
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/client/services/receipt/components/ImportReceiptFromEmailModal.js
import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { Search, Mail, Download, Eye } from 'lucide-react';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import ConsolidatedEmailList from '@/services/email/components/ConsolidatedEmailList';
import EmailViewComponent from '@/services/email/components/EmailViewComponent';
import { getEmailAccounts, searchProviderEmails } from '@/services/email/utils/api';

const EmailViewModal = ({ emailId, accountId, onClose }) => {
  return (
    <div
      className="fixed inset-0 bg-base-300/70 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[60]"
      onClick={onClose}
    >
      <div
        className="card bg-base-100 shadow-2xl w-full max-w-5xl max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto border border-base-300"
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <div className="card-body p-4 md:p-6">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 mb-3">
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-base-content">Email preview</h3>
              <p className="text-xs text-base-content/60">
                Review the email before importing its receipt.
              </p>
            </div>
            <button type="button" onClick={onClose} className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost">
              ✕
            </button>
          </div>

          <EmailViewComponent
            emailId={emailId}
            emailAccountId={accountId}
            onClose={onClose}
            onArchive={() => {}}
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

EmailViewModal.propTypes = {
  emailId: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
  accountId: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
  onClose: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
};

const ImportReceiptFromEmailModal = ({
  isOpen,
  onClose,
  onImported,
  initialQuery,
  initialStartDate,
  initialEndDate,
  autoSearchOnOpen,
  modalTitle,
  modalDescription,
  highlightedKeywords,
}) => {
  const [accounts, setAccounts] = useState([]);
  const [selectedAccountId, setSelectedAccountId] = useState('');

  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState(initialQuery || 'has:attachment');
  const [searchResults, setSearchResults] = useState([]);
  const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false);
  const [importing, setImporting] = useState(false);
  const [nextPageTokens, setNextPageTokens] = useState(null);
  const [prevPageTokens, setPrevPageTokens] = useState(null);

  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(initialStartDate || '');
  const [endDate, setEndDate] = useState(initialEndDate || '');

  const [selectedEmailId, setSelectedEmailId] = useState(null);
  const [selectedEmail, setSelectedEmail] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchAccounts = async () => {
      try {
        const accs = await getEmailAccounts();
        setAccounts(accs);
        if (accs.length > 0 && !selectedAccountId) {
          setSelectedAccountId(accs[0].id);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error('Failed to fetch email accounts:', err);
        toast.error(`Error fetching email accounts: ${err.message}`);
      }
    };

    if (isOpen) {
      fetchAccounts();
    }
  }, [isOpen, selectedAccountId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) return;
    setSearchQuery(initialQuery || 'has:attachment');
    setStartDate(initialStartDate || '');
    setEndDate(initialEndDate || '');
    setSearchResults([]);
    setSelectedEmail(null);
    setSelectedEmailId(null);
    setNextPageTokens(null);
    setPrevPageTokens(null);
  }, [autoSearchOnOpen, initialEndDate, initialQuery, initialStartDate, isOpen]);

  const accountLabel = useMemo(() => {
    return accounts.find((acc) => acc.id === selectedAccountId)?.emailAddress || 'Selected account';
  }, [accounts, selectedAccountId]);

  const hasAnySearchPreset = Boolean(initialQuery || initialStartDate || initialEndDate);

  const getAnyNextToken = () => {
    if (!nextPageTokens) return null;
    if (typeof nextPageTokens === 'string') return nextPageTokens;
    return Object.values(nextPageTokens).find((token) => token) || null;
  };

  const getAnyPrevToken = () => {
    if (!prevPageTokens) return null;
    if (typeof prevPageTokens === 'string') return prevPageTokens;
    return Object.values(prevPageTokens).find((token) => token) || null;
  };

  const hasNextPage = !!getAnyNextToken();
  const hasPrevPage = !!getAnyPrevToken();

  const handleSearch = useCallback(
    async (token = null) => {
      if (!searchQuery.trim() && !startDate && !endDate) {
        toast.info('Please enter a search query or specify a date range.');
        return;
      }
      if (!selectedAccountId) {
        toast.info('Please select an email account.');
        return;
      }

      setIsSearching(true);
      try {
        let finalQuery = searchQuery.trim();
        let dateFilter = '';
        if (startDate) {
          dateFilter += ` after:${startDate.replace(/-/g, '/')}`;
        }
        if (endDate) {
          dateFilter += ` before:${endDate.replace(/-/g, '/')}`;
        }
        if (dateFilter) {
          finalQuery = finalQuery ? `${finalQuery}${dateFilter}` : dateFilter.trim();
        }

        const data = await searchProviderEmails({
          accountId: selectedAccountId,
          folder: 'INBOX',
          limit: 20,
          pageToken: token || null,
          query: finalQuery,
          skipAnalysis: true,
        });

        setSearchResults(data.emails || []);
        setNextPageTokens(data.nextPageTokens || null);
        setPrevPageTokens(data.previousPageTokens || null);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error('Search error:', error);
        toast.error(`Search error: ${error.message}`);
      } finally {
        setIsSearching(false);
      }
    },
    [endDate, searchQuery, selectedAccountId, startDate]
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen || !autoSearchOnOpen || !selectedAccountId) return;
    if (!hasAnySearchPreset) return;
    handleSearch();
  }, [autoSearchOnOpen, handleSearch, hasAnySearchPreset, isOpen, selectedAccountId]);

  const handleEmailSelect = (email) => {
    setSelectedEmail(email);
    setSelectedEmailId(email.id);
  };

  const handleImportSelectedEmail = async () => {
    if (!selectedEmail?.id) {
      toast.info('Select an email before importing.');
      return;
    }

    setImporting(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/importFromEmail`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ emailId: selectedEmail.id }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to import receipt from email.');
      }

      toast.success('Receipt imported from email successfully.');
      if (typeof onImported === 'function') {
        onImported(data);
      }
      onClose();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Import from email error:', error);
      toast.error(`Import failed: ${error.message}`);
    } finally {
      setImporting(false);
    }
  };

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  return (
    <>
      <div
        className="fixed inset-0 bg-base-300/70 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-50"
        onClick={onClose}
      >
        <div
          className="card bg-base-100 shadow-2xl w-full max-w-6xl max-h-[92vh] overflow-y-auto border border-base-300"
          onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        >
          <div className="card-body p-4 md:p-6 space-y-5">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 flex-wrap">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-info/10 p-3">
                  <Mail className="w-5 h-5 text-info" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h2 className="text-lg md:text-2xl font-semibold text-base-content">
                    {modalTitle || 'Import receipt from email'}
                  </h2>
                  <p className="text-xs md:text-sm text-base-content/60">
                    {modalDescription || 'Search emails with attachments, preview them, then import the selected receipt.'}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <button type="button" onClick={onClose} className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost">
                ✕
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 xl:grid-cols-[1.1fr_0.9fr] gap-4">
              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4 space-y-4">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-base-content">Search</h3>
                  <p className="text-xs text-base-content/60 mt-1">
                    Tip: keep <code>has:attachment</code> in your query to find receipt emails faster.
                  </p>
                </div>

                {highlightedKeywords?.length ? (
                  <div className="rounded-xl border border-base-300 bg-base-100 p-3 space-y-2">
                    <div className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/60">
                      Suggested keywords from the transaction
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                      {highlightedKeywords.map((keyword) => (
                        <button
                          key={keyword}
                          type="button"
                          className="badge badge-ghost cursor-pointer"
                          onClick={() => setSearchQuery((prev) => {
                            if (prev.includes(keyword)) return prev;
                            return `${prev} ${keyword}`.trim();
                          })}
                        >
                          {keyword}
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ) : null}

                <div>
                  <label className="block mb-1 text-xs font-medium text-base-content/70">
                    Email account
                  </label>
                  <select
                    value={selectedAccountId}
                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedAccountId(e.target.value)}
                    className="select select-bordered w-full bg-base-100"
                  >
                    {accounts.map((acc) => (
                      <option key={acc.id} value={acc.id}>
                        {acc.emailAddress}
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                </div>

                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  <div>
                    <label htmlFor="startDate" className="block text-xs font-medium text-base-content/70 mb-1">
                      Start date
                    </label>
                    <input
                      type="date"
                      id="startDate"
                      value={startDate}
                      onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
                      className="input input-bordered w-full bg-base-100"
                    />
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <label htmlFor="endDate" className="block text-xs font-medium text-base-content/70 mb-1">
                      End date
                    </label>
                    <input
                      type="date"
                      id="endDate"
                      value={endDate}
                      onChange={(e) => setEndDate(e.target.value)}
                      className="input input-bordered w-full bg-base-100"
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  <label className="input input-bordered flex items-center gap-2 w-full bg-base-100">
                    <Search className="w-4 h-4 opacity-70" />
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      value={searchQuery}
                      onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                      className="grow"
                      placeholder="Search emails, e.g. has:attachment receipt OR invoice"
                    />
                  </label>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => handleSearch()}
                    disabled={isSearching}
                    className="btn btn-primary"
                  >
                    {isSearching ? 'Searching...' : 'Search'}
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4 space-y-4">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-base-content">Selected email</h3>
                  <p className="text-xs text-base-content/60 mt-1">
                    Choose an email from the results, preview it, then import the receipt.
                  </p>
                </div>

                {selectedEmail ? (
                  <div className="rounded-xl border border-base-300 bg-base-100 p-4 space-y-3">
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">
                        Account
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-base-content font-medium">{accountLabel}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">
                        Subject
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-base-content font-medium">
                        {selectedEmail.subject || 'No subject'}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">
                        From
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-base-content/80">
                        {selectedEmail.sender || selectedEmail.from || 'Unknown sender'}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    {selectedEmail.snippet && (
                      <div>
                        <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wide text-base-content/50">
                          Preview
                        </div>
                        <div className="text-sm text-base-content/80 line-clamp-3">
                          {selectedEmail.snippet}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 pt-1">
                      <button
                        type="button"
                        onClick={() => setSelectedEmailId(selectedEmail.id)}
                        className="btn btn-sm btn-outline"
                      >
                        <Eye className="w-4 h-4" />
                        Preview email
                      </button>
                      <button
                        type="button"
                        onClick={handleImportSelectedEmail}
                        className="btn btn-sm btn-primary"
                        disabled={importing}
                      >
                        <Download className="w-4 h-4" />
                        {importing ? 'Importing...' : 'Import receipt'}
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="rounded-xl border border-dashed border-base-300 bg-base-100/70 p-6 text-sm text-base-content/60">
                    No email selected yet.
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="rounded-2xl border border-base-300 bg-base-100 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-base-300 bg-base-200/50">
                <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-base-content">Results</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="p-4">
                {searchResults.length > 0 ? (
                  <ConsolidatedEmailList
                    emails={searchResults}
                    onSelect={handleEmailSelect}
                    onArchive={() => {}}
                    onArchiveAll={null}
                    onArchiveAllReplied={null}
                    isArchivingAll={false}
                    emailVisibility={{}}
                    groupBy="date"
                    layout="grid"
                    hasNextPage={hasNextPage}
                    hasPrevPage={hasPrevPage}
                    goToNextPage={() => {
                      const token = getAnyNextToken();
                      if (token) handleSearch(token);
                    }}
                    goToPreviousPage={() => {
                      const token = getAnyPrevToken();
                      if (token) handleSearch(token);
                    }}
                  />
                ) : (
                  <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">
                    {isSearching ? 'Searching...' : 'No emails found yet.'}
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {selectedEmailId && (
        <EmailViewModal
          emailId={selectedEmailId}
          accountId={selectedAccountId}
          onClose={() => setSelectedEmailId(null)}
        />
      )}
    </>
  );
};

ImportReceiptFromEmailModal.propTypes = {
  isOpen: PropTypes.bool.isRequired,
  onClose: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onImported: PropTypes.func,
  initialQuery: PropTypes.string,
  initialStartDate: PropTypes.string,
  initialEndDate: PropTypes.string,
  autoSearchOnOpen: PropTypes.bool,
  modalTitle: PropTypes.string,
  modalDescription: PropTypes.string,
  highlightedKeywords: PropTypes.arrayOf(PropTypes.string),
};

ImportReceiptFromEmailModal.defaultProps = {
  onImported: undefined,
  initialQuery: 'has:attachment',
  initialStartDate: '',
  initialEndDate: '',
  autoSearchOnOpen: false,
  modalTitle: 'Import receipt from email',
  modalDescription: 'Search emails with attachments, preview them, then import the selected receipt.',
  highlightedKeywords: [],
};

export default ImportReceiptFromEmailModal;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/MatchReceiptModal.jsx
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/client/services/receipt/components/MatchReceiptModal.js
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { X, CheckCircle, Banknote, RefreshCw } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';

const formatMoney = (value) => `$${Math.abs(Number(value || 0)).toFixed(2)}`;
const formatPercent = (value) => `${Math.round(Number(value || 0) * 100)}%`;

const scoreValue = (tx, key) => tx?.[key] ?? tx?.scoreBreakdown?.[key] ?? 0;

const MATCH_APPROACHES = [
  { id: 'balanced', label: 'Balanced' },
  { id: 'closest-date', label: 'Closest Date' },
  { id: 'closest-amount', label: 'Closest Amount' },
  { id: 'transaction-details', label: 'Details' },
  { id: 'broad-review', label: 'Broad' },
];

const ScoreBar = ({ label, value }) => (
  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs">
    <span className="w-20 text-base-content/60 truncate">{label}</span>
    <div className="flex-1 bg-base-300 rounded-full h-1.5">
      <div className="bg-primary h-1.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: `${Math.round((value ?? 0) * 100)}%` }} />
    </div>
    <span className="w-8 text-right text-base-content/70">{Math.round((value ?? 0) * 100)}%</span>
  </div>
);

const MatchReceiptModal = ({ receipt, onClose, onMatched }) => {
  const [bankTransactions, setBankTransactions] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [range, setRange] = useState(0.05);
  const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [descFilter, setDescFilter] = useState('');
  const [expandedSearch, setExpandedSearch] = useState(false);
  const [expandedScores, setExpandedScores] = useState({});
  const [matchApproach, setMatchApproach] = useState('balanced');

  useEffect(() => {
    if (receipt?.id) {
      fetchMatchingTransactions();
    }
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [receipt?.id, range, expandedSearch, matchApproach]);

  const fetchMatchingTransactions = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const effectiveRange = expandedSearch ? 0.5 : range;
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match/transactions`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          range: effectiveRange,
          broadSearch: expandedSearch,
          approach: matchApproach,
        }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to fetch matching transactions.');
      }

      setBankTransactions(data.transactions || []);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching matching transactions:', error);
      toast.error(`Failed to fetch matching transactions: ${error.message}`);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const handleMatchToTransaction = async (transactionId) => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          type: 'bank',
          transactionId,
        }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to match receipt.');
      toast.success(data.message || 'Receipt matched successfully');
      onMatched();
      onClose();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error matching receipt:', error);
      toast.error(`Error matching receipt: ${error.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  const handleMarkAsCash = async () => {
    setIsSubmitting(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: receipt.id, type: 'cash' }),
      });

      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to mark as cash.');
      toast.success(data.message || 'Receipt marked as cash');
      onMatched();
      onClose();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error marking receipt as cash:', error);
      toast.error(`Error marking receipt as cash: ${error.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsSubmitting(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-[80] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-end sm:items-center justify-center p-0 sm:p-4" onClick={onClose}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-4xl bg-base-100 border border-base-300 shadow-2xl rounded-t-3xl sm:rounded-3xl max-h-[92vh] overflow-hidden" onClick={(event) => event.stopPropagation()}>
        <div className="sticky top-0 z-10 border-b border-base-300 bg-base-100/95 backdrop-blur px-4 py-3 sm:px-6 sm:py-4 flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-base-content">Match Receipt</h3>
            <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60 mt-1">
              {receipt.companyName || 'Unknown Merchant'} · {formatMoney(receipt.total)} · {receipt.date ? new Date(receipt.date).toLocaleDateString() : 'No date'}
            </p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="btn btn-circle btn-ghost btn-sm" aria-label="Close">
            <X className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="overflow-y-auto max-h-[calc(92vh-72px)] px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 sm:py-5 space-y-5">
          <div className="card border border-base-300 bg-base-100 shadow-sm">
            <div className="card-body p-4 sm:p-5 gap-4">
              <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between">
                <div>
                  <h4 className="text-base font-semibold text-base-content">Matching Tolerance</h4>
                  <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Broaden the amount range to find transactions with slightly different amounts.</p>
                </div>
                <div className="badge badge-ghost">{expandedSearch ? 'Expanded (±50%)' : `±${(range * 100).toFixed(0)}%`}</div>
              </div>

              {!expandedSearch && (
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0.005"
                  max="0.25"
                  step="0.005"
                  value={range}
                  onChange={(event) => setRange(parseFloat(event.target.value) || 0)}
                  className="range range-primary"
                />
              )}

              <label className="flex items-center gap-2 cursor-pointer">
                <input
                  type="checkbox"
                  className="checkbox checkbox-sm checkbox-warning"
                  checked={expandedSearch}
                  onChange={(e) => setExpandedSearch(e.target.checked)}
                />
                <span className="text-sm text-base-content/70">Expanded search</span>
              </label>

              <div className="join flex flex-wrap">
                {MATCH_APPROACHES.map((approach) => (
                  <button
                    key={approach.id}
                    type="button"
                    className={`btn btn-xs join-item ${matchApproach === approach.id ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-outline'}`}
                    onClick={() => setMatchApproach(approach.id)}
                  >
                    {approach.label}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="card border border-base-300 bg-base-100 shadow-sm">
            <div className="card-body p-4 sm:p-5 gap-4">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 flex-wrap">
                <div>
                  <h4 className="text-base font-semibold text-base-content">Suggested Transactions</h4>
                  <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Confidence score and match reasons shown for each suggestion.</p>
                </div>
                {loading && <span className="badge badge-secondary gap-1"><RefreshCw className="w-3 h-3 animate-spin" /> Refreshing</span>}
              </div>

              <input
                type="text"
                className="input input-bordered input-sm w-full"
                placeholder="Filter by description..."
                value={descFilter}
                onChange={(e) => setDescFilter(e.target.value)}
              />

              {loading ? (
                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-base-300 bg-base-200/30 p-6 text-sm text-base-content/60">
                  Loading matching transactions...
                </div>
              ) : bankTransactions.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-base-300 bg-base-200/30 p-6 space-y-3">
                  <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">No matching bank transactions found within ±{expandedSearch ? '50' : `${(range * 100).toFixed(0)}`}% of {formatMoney(receipt.total)}.</p>
                  {!expandedSearch && (
                    <button type="button" className="btn btn-sm btn-outline" onClick={() => setExpandedSearch(true)}>
                      Try expanded search (ignore amount filter)
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="space-y-3">
                  {bankTransactions.filter((tx) => !descFilter || (tx.description || '').toLowerCase().includes(descFilter.toLowerCase())).map((tx) => (
                    <div key={tx.id} className="rounded-xl border border-base-300 bg-base-200/20 p-4 space-y-3">
                      <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between">
                        <div className="min-w-0">
                          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                            <div className="font-semibold text-base-content truncate">{tx.description || 'No description'}</div>
                            <span className="badge badge-outline">{tx.confidenceLabel || 'Match'}</span>
                            <span className="badge badge-ghost">{formatPercent(tx.matchScore)}</span>
                            {tx.matchApproachLabel && <span className="badge badge-ghost">{tx.matchApproachLabel}</span>}
                          </div>
                          <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60 mt-1">
                            {new Date(tx.date).toLocaleDateString()} · {formatMoney(tx.amount)}
                          </div>
                          {Array.isArray(tx.matchReasons) && tx.matchReasons.length ? (
                            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2">
                              {tx.matchReasons.map((reason) => (
                                <span key={reason} className="badge badge-ghost text-xs">{reason}</span>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                          ) : null}
                        </div>
                        <button
                          type="button"
                          onClick={() => handleMatchToTransaction(tx.id)}
                          className="btn btn-success btn-sm gap-2"
                          disabled={isSubmitting}
                        >
                          <CheckCircle className="w-4 h-4" />
                          Match
                        </button>
                      </div>
                      <button
                        type="button"
                        className="text-xs text-primary underline"
                        onClick={() => setExpandedScores((prev) => ({ ...prev, [tx.id]: !prev[tx.id] }))}
                      >
                        {expandedScores[tx.id] ? 'Hide score breakdown' : 'Show score breakdown'}
                      </button>
                      {expandedScores[tx.id] && (
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-x-5 gap-y-1">
                          <ScoreBar label="Amount" value={scoreValue(tx, 'amountScore')} />
                          <ScoreBar label="Date" value={scoreValue(tx, 'dateScore')} />
                          <ScoreBar label="Vendor" value={scoreValue(tx, 'vendorScore')} />
                          <ScoreBar label="Text" value={scoreValue(tx, 'descriptionScore')} />
                          <ScoreBar label="Keywords" value={scoreValue(tx, 'keywordScore')} />
                          <ScoreBar label="HST" value={scoreValue(tx, 'taxScore')} />
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="card border border-base-300 bg-base-100 shadow-sm">
            <div className="card-body p-4 sm:p-5 gap-3">
              <h4 className="text-base font-semibold text-base-content">No Bank Match?</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Mark the receipt as cash if it was not paid from a bank transaction.</p>
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={handleMarkAsCash}
                className="btn btn-warning btn-sm sm:btn-md gap-2 w-full sm:w-auto"
                disabled={isSubmitting}
              >
                <Banknote className="w-4 h-4" />
                Mark as Cash
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default MatchReceiptModal;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptImageEditor.jsx
import React, { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';

const clamp = (value, min, max) => Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max);

const ReceiptImageEditor = ({ isOpen, imageUrl, onClose, onApply }) => {
  const containerRef = useRef(null);
  const imageRef = useRef(null);

  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [dragStart, setDragStart] = useState(null);
  const [selection, setSelection] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) {
      setIsDragging(false);
      setDragStart(null);
      setSelection(null);
    }
  }, [isOpen]);

  const containerRect = useMemo(() => {
    return containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect() || null;
  }, [isOpen, imageUrl, selection]);

  const getPointFromEvent = useCallback((event) => {
    const rect = containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (!rect) return null;

    return {
      x: clamp(event.clientX - rect.left, 0, rect.width),
      y: clamp(event.clientY - rect.top, 0, rect.height),
      rect,
    };
  }, []);

  const handlePointerDown = useCallback((event) => {
    if (!containerRef.current) return;
    event.preventDefault();

    const point = getPointFromEvent(event);
    if (!point) return;

    setIsDragging(true);
    setDragStart({ x: point.x, y: point.y });
    setSelection({
      x: point.x,
      y: point.y,
      width: 0,
      height: 0,
    });
  }, [getPointFromEvent]);

  const handlePointerMove = useCallback((event) => {
    if (!isDragging || !dragStart) return;
    event.preventDefault();

    const point = getPointFromEvent(event);
    if (!point) return;

    const nextX = Math.min(dragStart.x, point.x);
    const nextY = Math.min(dragStart.y, point.y);
    const nextWidth = Math.abs(point.x - dragStart.x);
    const nextHeight = Math.abs(point.y - dragStart.y);

    setSelection({
      x: nextX,
      y: nextY,
      width: nextWidth,
      height: nextHeight,
    });
  }, [dragStart, getPointFromEvent, isDragging]);

  const handlePointerUp = useCallback((event) => {
    if (!isDragging) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    setIsDragging(false);
  }, [isDragging]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) return;

    const handleWindowPointerUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    window.addEventListener('pointerup', handleWindowPointerUp);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('pointerup', handleWindowPointerUp);
    };
  }, [isOpen]);

  const handleApply = useCallback(() => {
    if (!selection || !containerRef.current || !imageRef.current) return;

    const imageEl = imageRef.current;
    const rect = imageEl.getBoundingClientRect();

    if (!rect.width || !rect.height || !imageEl.naturalWidth || !imageEl.naturalHeight) {
      return;
    }

    const scaleX = imageEl.naturalWidth / rect.width;
    const scaleY = imageEl.naturalHeight / rect.height;

    const crop = {
      left: Math.round(selection.x * scaleX),
      top: Math.round(selection.y * scaleY),
      width: Math.round(selection.width * scaleX),
      height: Math.round(selection.height * scaleY),
    };

    if (crop.width < 10 || crop.height < 10) {
      return;
    }

    onApply(crop);
  }, [onApply, selection]);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  return (
    <div
      className="fixed inset-0 z-[70] bg-black/80 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center p-3 md:p-6"
      onClick={onClose}
    >
      <div
        className="w-full max-w-5xl rounded-2xl bg-base-100 shadow-2xl border border-base-300 overflow-hidden"
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 px-4 py-3 border-b border-base-300 bg-base-100">
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-base md:text-lg font-semibold text-base-content">
              Manual Crop
            </h3>
            <p className="text-xs md:text-sm text-base-content/60">
              Drag on the image to select the area you want to keep.
            </p>
          </div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setSelection(null)}
              className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost"
            >
              Clear
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={onClose}
              className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost"
            >
              Cancel
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={handleApply}
              className="btn btn-sm btn-primary"
              disabled={!selection || selection.width < 10 || selection.height < 10}
            >
              Apply Crop
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="p-3 md:p-4 bg-base-200/40">
          <div
            ref={containerRef}
            className="relative mx-auto w-full max-h-[75vh] overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-base-300 bg-black touch-none"
            onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
            onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
            onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
          >
            <img
              ref={imageRef}
              src={imageUrl}
              alt="Receipt crop editor"
              className="block w-full h-auto max-h-[75vh] object-contain select-none pointer-events-none"
              draggable={false}
            />

            {selection && (
              <>
                <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/45 pointer-events-none" />

                <div
                  className="absolute border-2 border-primary bg-primary/15 shadow-[0_0_0_9999px_rgba(0,0,0,0.45)] pointer-events-none"
                  style={{
                    left: `${selection.x}px`,
                    top: `${selection.y}px`,
                    width: `${selection.width}px`,
                    height: `${selection.height}px`,
                  }}
                >
                  <div className="absolute -top-7 left-0 rounded-md bg-base-100/95 px-2 py-1 text-[10px] md:text-xs font-medium text-base-content shadow">
                    {Math.round(selection.width)} × {Math.round(selection.height)}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ReceiptImageEditor;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptsDashboard.jsx
// /home/luan_ngo/boss/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptsDashboard.js
import React, { useContext } from 'react';
import CameraPanel from './camera/CameraPanel';
import ReceiptsTable from './ReceiptsTable';
import DuplicateReceiptsDashboard from './DuplicateReceiptsDashboard';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';

const ReceiptsDashboard = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);

  const hasView =
    user &&
    user.permissions &&
    (user.permissions.includes('receipt:view') || user.permissions.includes('permission:editAll'));

  const hasEdit =
    user &&
    user.permissions &&
    (user.permissions.includes('receipt:edit') || user.permissions.includes('permission:editAll'));

  const hasAddRights =
    user &&
    user.permissions &&
    (user.permissions.includes('receipt:add') || user.permissions.includes('permission:editAll'));

  return (
    <div className="p-6 flex flex-col space-y-6">
      {hasAddRights && (
        <div className="w-full">
          <CameraPanel />
        </div>
      )}

      {hasView ? (
        <>
          <div className="w-full">
            <ReceiptsTable canEdit={hasEdit} />
          </div>
          <DuplicateReceiptsDashboard canEdit={hasEdit} />
        </>
      ) : (
        <p>You do not have sufficient rights to view receipts.</p>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default ReceiptsDashboard;
```
