```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptsDetails.jsx
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptsDetails.js
import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext, useMemo, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import useSWR from 'swr';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import {
  X,
  CheckCircle,
  Banknote,
  RefreshCw,
  Sparkles,
  Download,
  Archive,
  ImageOff,
  Scissors,
  MoreHorizontal,
  GitMerge,
  ChevronDown,
  ChevronUp,
  ZoomIn,
  RotateCw,
  Wand2,
  Copy,
} from 'lucide-react';
import MatchReceiptModal from './MatchReceiptModal';
import ReceiptImageEditor from './ReceiptImageEditor';

const fmt = (v) => `$${Number(v || 0).toFixed(2)}`;
const fmtDate = (v) => {
  if (!v) return '—';
  const d = new Date(v);
  return Number.isNaN(d.getTime()) ? '—' : d.toLocaleDateString('en-CA', { year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: '2-digit' });
};
const getDateIssue = (v) => {
  if (!v) return 'Missing date';
  const d = new Date(v);
  if (Number.isNaN(d.getTime())) return 'Invalid date';
  const year = d.getFullYear();
  const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
  if (year < 2015 || year > currentYear + 1) return 'Review OCR year';
  return '';
};
const fmtBytes = (bytes) => {
  const n = Number(bytes || 0);
  if (n >= 1024 * 1024) return `${(n / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)} MB`;
  if (n >= 1024) return `${(n / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
  return `${n} B`;
};

const CollapsibleSection = ({ title, children, defaultOpen = false }) => {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);
  return (
    <div className="border border-base-300 rounded-box overflow-hidden">
      <button
        type="button"
        className="w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-base-200/50 hover:bg-base-200 text-sm font-medium text-left"
        onClick={() => setOpen((s) => !s)}
      >
        {title}
        {open ? <ChevronUp size={15} className="text-base-content/40" /> : <ChevronDown size={15} className="text-base-content/40" />}
      </button>
      {open && <div className="p-4">{children}</div>}
    </div>
  );
};

const ReceiptImageViewport = ({
  imageUrl,
  zoom,
  rotation,
  onZoomChange,
  onRotationChange,
  compact = false,
}) => {
  const [pan, setPan] = useState({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  const dragRef = useRef(null);

  const updateZoom = useCallback((nextZoom) => {
    onZoomChange(Math.max(0.5, Math.min(5, Number(nextZoom) || 1)));
  }, [onZoomChange]);

  const resetView = useCallback(() => {
    updateZoom(1);
    setPan({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  }, [updateZoom]);

  const handlePointerDown = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    event.currentTarget.setPointerCapture?.(event.pointerId);
    dragRef.current = {
      pointerId: event.pointerId,
      startX: event.clientX,
      startY: event.clientY,
      pan,
    };
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (event) => {
    const drag = dragRef.current;
    if (!drag || drag.pointerId !== event.pointerId) return;
    setPan({
      x: drag.pan.x + event.clientX - drag.startX,
      y: drag.pan.y + event.clientY - drag.startY,
    });
  };

  const handlePointerUp = (event) => {
    if (dragRef.current?.pointerId === event.pointerId) {
      dragRef.current = null;
    }
  };

  const handleWheel = (event) => {
    if (!event.ctrlKey && Math.abs(event.deltaY) < Math.abs(event.deltaX)) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    updateZoom(zoom + (event.deltaY < 0 ? 0.15 : -0.15));
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <div
        className={`rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 overflow-hidden flex items-center justify-center touch-none select-none ${zoom > 1 ? 'cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing' : 'cursor-zoom-in'}`}
        style={{ minHeight: compact ? '200px' : '300px', maxHeight: compact ? '420px' : '560px' }}
        onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
        onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
        onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
        onPointerCancel={handlePointerUp}
        onWheel={handleWheel}
      >
        <img
          src={imageUrl}
          alt="Receipt"
          draggable={false}
          className={`object-contain transition-transform ${compact ? 'max-w-full max-h-full' : 'max-w-full max-h-[540px]'}`}
          style={{
            transform: `translate(${pan.x}px, ${pan.y}px) scale(${zoom}) rotate(${rotation}deg)`,
            transformOrigin: 'center center',
          }}
        />
      </div>
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 justify-center">
        <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => updateZoom(zoom + 0.25)} title="Zoom in"><ZoomIn size={13} /></button>
        <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs" onClick={() => updateZoom(zoom - 0.25)} title="Zoom out">-</button>
        <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs" onClick={resetView} title="Reset view" style={{ fontSize: '11px' }}>{Math.round(zoom * 100)}%</button>
        <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => onRotationChange((r) => (r + 90) % 360)} title="Rotate"><RotateCw size={13} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const MatchStatusHeader = ({ receipt }) => {
  const isMatched = !!receipt.paymentType || (receipt.bankTransactions && receipt.bankTransactions.length > 0);
  const isCash = receipt.paymentType === 'cash';

  if (isCash) {
    return <span className="badge badge-warning badge-sm">Cash payment</span>;
  }
  if (isMatched) {
    return <span className="badge badge-success badge-sm gap-1"><CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3" />Matched</span>;
  }
  return <span className="badge badge-ghost badge-sm">Unmatched</span>;
};

const ReceiptsDetails = ({ receipt, onClose, onUpdate }) => {
  const { organization, user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const canEdit =
    user?.permissions?.includes('receipt:edit') ||
    user?.permissions?.includes('permission:editAll') ||
    false;

  const [receiptId, setReceiptId] = useState(receipt?.id || null);
  const [details, setDetails] = useState(receipt || {});
  const [items, setItems] = useState(receipt?.items || []);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('review');
  const [isUpdating, setIsUpdating] = useState(false);
  const [isRetagging, setIsRetagging] = useState(false);
  const [showMatchModal, setShowMatchModal] = useState(false);
  const [isImageEditing, setIsImageEditing] = useState(false);
  const [previewImgName, setPreviewImgName] = useState(null);
  const [previewImageUrl, setPreviewImageUrl] = useState('');
  const [previewOperation, setPreviewOperation] = useState('');
  const [showCropEditor, setShowCropEditor] = useState(false);
  const [isRunningOcr, setIsRunningOcr] = useState(false);
  const [isExportingImage, setIsExportingImage] = useState(false);
  const [isOptimizing, setIsOptimizing] = useState(false);
  const [optimizationReport, setOptimizationReport] = useState(null);
  const [isPurgingOriginal, setIsPurgingOriginal] = useState(false);
  const [reviewMode, setReviewMode] = useState('ocr-only');
  const [imageZoom, setImageZoom] = useState(1);
  const [imageRotation, setImageRotation] = useState(0);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (receipt?.id) setReceiptId(receipt.id);
  }, [receipt]);

  const fetcher = (url) =>
    fetchWithAuth(url, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, credentials: 'include' })
      .then((res) => {
        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Error: ${res.status} ${res.statusText}`);
        return res.json();
      })
      .catch((err) => {
        toast.error(`Failed to load receipt details: ${err.message}`);
        throw err;
      });

  const { data: updatedReceipt, mutate } = useSWR(
    receiptId ? `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/byId/${receiptId}` : null,
    fetcher,
    { refreshInterval: 0 }
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (updatedReceipt) {
      setDetails(updatedReceipt);
      setItems(updatedReceipt.items || []);
    }
  }, [updatedReceipt]);

  const resolvedImageStatus = details.resolvedImageStatus || details.imageStorageStatus || (details.imgName ? 'ACTIVE' : 'NONE');

  const currentImageUrl = useMemo(() => {
    if (previewImageUrl) return previewImageUrl;
    if (details.imageUrl) {
      return details.imageUrl.startsWith('http') ? details.imageUrl : `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}${details.imageUrl}`;
    }
    if (details.imgName && details.organizationId && resolvedImageStatus !== 'ARCHIVED') {
      return `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/uploads/${encodeURIComponent(details.organizationId)}/receipts/${encodeURIComponent(details.imgName)}`;
    }
    return '';
  }, [details.imageUrl, details.imgName, details.organizationId, previewImageUrl, resolvedImageStatus]);

  const selectedOptimizationCandidate = useMemo(() => optimizationReport?.selected || null, [optimizationReport]);

  const selectedOptimizationUrl = useMemo(() => {
    const url = selectedOptimizationCandidate?.previewUrl;
    if (!url) return '';
    return url.startsWith('http') ? url : `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}${url}`;
  }, [selectedOptimizationCandidate]);

  const isMatched = !!details.paymentType || (details.bankTransactions && details.bankTransactions.length > 0);
  const isTextSource = details.filePath && (details.filePath.endsWith('.pdf') || details.filePath.endsWith('.txt'));
  const isImage = details.imgName && !details.imgName.endsWith('.pdf') && !details.imgName.endsWith('.txt');
  const dateIssue = getDateIssue(details.date);

  // Handlers
  const handleDetailChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    if (name === 'total' || name === 'hst') {
      const parsed = parseFloat(value);
      setDetails((prev) => ({ ...prev, [name]: Number.isNaN(parsed) ? 0 : parsed }));
      return;
    }
    setDetails((prev) => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
  };

  const handleReceiptItemChange = (index, field, value) => {
    const updated = [...items];
    const next = field === 'quantity' ? parseInt(value, 10) || 1 : field === 'price' ? parseFloat(value) || 0 : value;
    updated[index] = { ...updated[index], [field]: next };
    setItems(updated);
  };
  const handleAddReceiptItem = () => setItems((prev) => [...prev, { name: '', quantity: 1, price: 0 }]);
  const handleRemoveReceiptItem = (index) => setItems((prev) => prev.filter((_, i) => i !== index));

  const runImageEdit = useCallback(async (operation, crop = null) => {
    if (!details.id) return;
    setIsImageEditing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/enhance`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, action: 'preview', operation, crop }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to create image preview.');
      setPreviewImgName(data.previewImgName);
      setPreviewImageUrl(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}${data.previewUrl}`);
      setPreviewOperation(operation);
      setShowCropEditor(false);
      toast.success('Image preview created.');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Image edit failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsImageEditing(false);
    }
  }, [details.id]);

  const handleSaveImageEdit = async () => {
    if (!details.id || !previewImgName) return;
    setIsImageEditing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/enhance`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, action: 'save', operation: previewOperation, previewImgName }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to save edited image.');
      setPreviewImgName(null); setPreviewImageUrl(''); setPreviewOperation('');
      await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
      toast.success('Edited image saved.');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Save failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsImageEditing(false);
    }
  };

  const handleDiscardImageEdit = async () => {
    if (!previewImgName) { setPreviewImgName(null); setPreviewImageUrl(''); setPreviewOperation(''); return; }
    setIsImageEditing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/enhance`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, action: 'discard', previewImgName }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to discard preview.');
      setPreviewImgName(null); setPreviewImageUrl(''); setPreviewOperation('');
      toast.info('Preview discarded.');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Discard failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsImageEditing(false);
    }
  };

  const handleRunOcr = async () => {
    if (!details.id) return;
    setIsRunningOcr(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/ocr`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id }),
      });
      if (!res.ok) { const d = await res.json(); throw new Error(d.error || 'Failed to run OCR.'); }
      toast.info('OCR running in background...');
      const id = details.id;
      const poll = async () => {
        for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
          await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 2000));
          try {
            const s = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/ocr/status?receiptId=${id}`);
            const status = await s.json();
            if (!status.isRunning) {
              if (status.lastError) toast.error(`OCR failed: ${status.lastError}`);
              else { toast.success(status.heicConverted ? 'OCR completed. HEIC converted.' : 'OCR completed.'); await mutate(); onUpdate?.(); }
              return;
            }
          } catch { /* ignore poll errors */ }
        }
        toast.warn('OCR is taking longer than expected. Refresh to see results.');
        await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
      };
      poll().catch(() => {});
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`OCR failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsRunningOcr(false);
    }
  };

  const handleRunOptimizationPreview = async () => {
    if (!details.id) return;
    setIsOptimizing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/preview`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, autoCrop: true, maxWidth: 1800, reviewMode }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to create optimization preview.');
      setOptimizationReport(data.report);
      if (data.report?.selected) toast.success('Compression review passed. Preview is ready to approve.');
      else toast.warn('Compression review did not find a clearly safe candidate.');
      await mutate();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Compression review failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsOptimizing(false);
    }
  };

  const handleSaveOptimization = async () => {
    if (!details.id || !selectedOptimizationCandidate?.previewRelativePath) return;
    setIsOptimizing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/save`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, previewRelativePath: selectedOptimizationCandidate.previewRelativePath }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to activate optimized image.');
      setOptimizationReport(null); await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
      toast.success('Optimized image activated. Original was retained.');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Approve failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsOptimizing(false);
    }
  };

  const handleDiscardOptimization = async () => {
    if (!details.id || !selectedOptimizationCandidate?.previewRelativePath) { setOptimizationReport(null); return; }
    setIsOptimizing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/discard`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, previewRelativePath: selectedOptimizationCandidate.previewRelativePath }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to discard optimization preview.');
      setOptimizationReport(null);
      toast.info('Optimization preview discarded.');
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Discard failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsOptimizing(false);
    }
  };

  const handlePurgeOriginal = async () => {
    if (!details.id) return;
    if (!window.confirm('Permanently delete the original pre-optimization image? This cannot be undone.')) return;
    setIsPurgingOriginal(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/purge-original`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to purge original image.');
      toast.success(data.message || 'Original image purged.');
      await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Purge failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsPurgingOriginal(false);
    }
  };

  const handleRerunLlmTag = async () => {
    if (!details.id) return;
    setIsRetagging(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/tagReceipt`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to rerun LLM tagging.');
      toast.success(data.heicConverted ? 'LLM tagging completed. HEIC converted.' : (data.message || 'LLM tagging rerun successfully.'));
      await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Rerun failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsRetagging(false);
    }
  };

  const handleUpdateReceipt = async () => {
    if (!details.id) { toast.error('Invalid receipt ID'); return; }
    setIsUpdating(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/update`, {
        method: 'PUT', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ id: details.id, imgName: details.imgName, filePath: details.filePath, date: details.date, companyName: details.companyName, total: details.total, hst: details.hst, notes: details.notes, items, text: details.text }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to update receipt.');
      toast.success('Receipt updated successfully');
      onUpdate?.(); await mutate();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Error updating receipt: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsUpdating(false);
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteReceipt = async () => {
    if (!details.id) { toast.error('Invalid receipt ID'); return; }
    if (!window.confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this receipt?')) return;
    setIsUpdating(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/delete`, {
        method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ id: details.id, imgName: details.imgName }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to delete receipt.');
      toast.success('Receipt deleted successfully');
      onUpdate?.(); onClose();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Error deleting receipt: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsUpdating(false);
    }
  };

  const handleMarkReceiptAsCash = async () => {
    if (!details.id) { toast.error('Invalid receipt ID'); return; }
    setIsUpdating(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, credentials: 'include',
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: details.id, type: 'cash' }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to mark receipt as cash.');
      toast.success(data.message || 'Receipt marked as cash.');
      onUpdate?.(); await mutate();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Error marking receipt as cash: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsUpdating(false);
    }
  };

  const handleMatchingSuccess = async () => {
    onUpdate?.(); await mutate(); setShowMatchModal(false);
  };

  const handleCopyReceiptId = () => {
    if (details.id) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(details.id); toast.success('Receipt ID copied!'); }
  };

  const triggerBrowserDownload = async (response, fallbackName) => {
    const blob = await response.blob();
    const blobUrl = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const cd = response.headers.get('content-disposition') || '';
    const m = cd.match(/filename="?([^"]+)"?/i);
    const fn = m?.[1] || fallbackName;
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = blobUrl; link.setAttribute('download', fn);
    document.body.appendChild(link); link.click(); link.remove();
    window.URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl);
  };

  const handleDownloadCurrentImage = async () => {
    if (!currentImageUrl || !details.imgName) { toast.error('No receipt image available.'); return; }
    try {
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(currentImageUrl);
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to download.');
      await triggerBrowserDownload(response, details.imgName);
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Download failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handleExportReceiptImage = async (archiveAfterExport = false) => {
    if (!details.id || !details.imgName) { toast.error('No image to export.'); return; }
    setIsExportingImage(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/archive/export`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: [details.id], archiveAfterExport }),
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        let msg = 'Failed to export.';
        try { const d = await response.json(); msg = d.error || msg; } catch { /* ignore */ }
        throw new Error(msg);
      }
      await triggerBrowserDownload(response, `receipt-image-${details.id}.zip`);
      toast.success(archiveAfterExport ? 'Exported and archived.' : 'Exported successfully.');
      await mutate(); onUpdate?.();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Export failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsExportingImage(false);
    }
  };

  if (!receiptId) return null;

  const merchantName = details.companyName || 'Unknown Merchant';

  return (
    <>
      <div
        className="fixed inset-0 bg-base-300/70 backdrop-blur-sm flex justify-center items-center z-50 p-3 md:p-4"
        onClick={onClose}
      >
        <div
          className="bg-base-100 shadow-2xl w-full max-w-5xl max-h-[95vh] flex flex-col rounded-box border border-base-300 overflow-hidden"
          onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        >
          {/* Modal header */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 px-5 py-4 border-b border-base-300 shrink-0">
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                <h2 className="text-lg font-bold text-base-content truncate">{merchantName}</h2>
                <MatchStatusHeader receipt={details} />
                {details.compressionStatus === 'ACTIVE_OPTIMIZED' && (
                  <span className="badge badge-ghost badge-sm text-success">Optimized</span>
                )}
              </div>
              <button
                type="button"
                className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-base-content/50 font-mono mt-0.5 hover:text-primary transition-colors"
                onClick={handleCopyReceiptId}
                title="Click to copy"
              >
                <Copy size={11} />
                {details.id}
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
              {/* Primary action */}
              {canEdit && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  {!isMatched ? (
                    <button
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => setShowMatchModal(true)}
                      className="btn btn-primary btn-sm gap-1"
                    >
                      <GitMerge size={14} />
                      Find Match
                    </button>
                  ) : (
                    <button
                      type="button"
                      onClick={handleUpdateReceipt}
                      className="btn btn-primary btn-sm"
                      disabled={isUpdating}
                    >
                      {isUpdating ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Changes'}
                    </button>
                  )}

                  {/* Overflow menu */}
                  <div className="dropdown dropdown-end">
                    <label tabIndex={0} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm gap-1">
                      <MoreHorizontal size={16} />
                    </label>
                    <ul tabIndex={0} className="dropdown-content menu menu-sm p-2 shadow-lg bg-base-100 rounded-box w-52 z-[200]">
                      <li>
                        <button onClick={handleRunOcr} disabled={isRunningOcr}>
                          <RefreshCw size={13} className={isRunningOcr ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />
                          {isRunningOcr ? 'Running OCR...' : 'Run OCR'}
                        </button>
                      </li>
                      <li>
                        <button onClick={handleRerunLlmTag} disabled={isRetagging}>
                          <Sparkles size={13} />
                          {isRetagging ? 'Rerunning...' : 'Rerun LLM Tag'}
                        </button>
                      </li>
                      {currentImageUrl && (
                        <>
                          <li><button onClick={handleDownloadCurrentImage}><Download size={13} /> Download image</button></li>
                          <li><button onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImage(false)} disabled={isExportingImage}><Download size={13} /> Export ZIP</button></li>
                          <li><button onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImage(true)} disabled={isExportingImage}><Archive size={13} /> Export &amp; Archive</button></li>
                        </>
                      )}
                      {details.activeImageVariant === 'optimized' && details.originalImageRelativePath && (
                        <li>
                          <button onClick={handlePurgeOriginal} disabled={isPurgingOriginal} className="text-error">
                            {isPurgingOriginal ? 'Purging...' : `Purge original (${fmtBytes(details.originalImageSize)})`}
                          </button>
                        </li>
                      )}
                      <li className="divider my-0.5" />
                      <li><button onClick={handleDeleteReceipt} className="text-error">Delete receipt</button></li>
                    </ul>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              <button onClick={onClose} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle" aria-label="Close" type="button">
                <X size={18} />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Tab bar */}
          <div className="flex border-b border-base-300 shrink-0 px-5 gap-0 overflow-x-auto">
            {[
              { id: 'review', label: 'Review' },
              { id: 'image', label: 'Image Tools' },
              { id: 'ocr', label: 'OCR / Text' },
            ].map((tab) => (
              <button
                key={tab.id}
                type="button"
                className={`px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors whitespace-nowrap ${activeTab === tab.id ? 'border-primary text-primary' : 'border-transparent text-base-content/60 hover:text-base-content'}`}
                onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}
              >
                {tab.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* Body — scrollable */}
          <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto">

            {/* REVIEW TAB */}
            {activeTab === 'review' && (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 xl:grid-cols-[1fr_1.1fr] gap-0 divide-y xl:divide-y-0 xl:divide-x divide-base-300">

                {/* Left: image preview (compact) */}
                <div className="p-5 space-y-3">
                  {isTextSource ? (
                    <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4">
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold mb-2">Receipt Text (OCR)</div>
                      <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-base-content/80 font-sans max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto">{details.text || 'No receipt text available.'}</pre>
                    </div>
                  ) : currentImageUrl ? (
                    <div className="space-y-2">
                      <ReceiptImageViewport
                        imageUrl={currentImageUrl}
                        zoom={imageZoom}
                        rotation={imageRotation}
                        onZoomChange={setImageZoom}
                        onRotationChange={setImageRotation}
                        compact
                      />
                      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 justify-center">
                        {canEdit && (
                          <>
                            <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => runImageEdit('auto')} disabled={isImageEditing}><Wand2 size={13} /> Auto Fix</button>
                            <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => setShowCropEditor(true)} disabled={isImageEditing}>Crop</button>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {previewImgName && (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-center">
                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-primary btn-xs" onClick={handleSaveImageEdit} disabled={isImageEditing}>Save Preview</button>
                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs" onClick={handleDiscardImageEdit} disabled={isImageEditing}>Discard</button>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  ) : details.imgName ? (
                    <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-5 text-center space-y-2">
                      <ImageOff className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto text-base-content/40" />
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold">
                        {resolvedImageStatus === 'ARCHIVED' ? 'Image archived off-server' : 'Image not available'}
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60">
                        {resolvedImageStatus === 'ARCHIVED'
                          ? 'Use the Restore Images button in the receipts table to bring this image back.'
                          : 'The receipt record exists but the image file could not be found.'}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ) : null}
                </div>

                {/* Right: accounting review */}
                <div className="p-5 space-y-4">
                  {/* Receipt summary */}
                  <div>
                    <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Receipt Summary</div>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-x-4 gap-y-1 text-sm">
                      <div className="text-base-content/60">Merchant</div>
                      <div className="font-medium">{details.companyName || '—'}</div>
                      <div className="text-base-content/60">Date</div>
                      <div className="font-medium">
                        {fmtDate(details.date)}
                        {dateIssue && <span className="badge badge-warning badge-xs ml-2">{dateIssue}</span>}
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-base-content/60">Subtotal</div>
                      <div className="font-medium">{details.total != null ? fmt(details.total - (details.hst || 0)) : '—'}</div>
                      <div className="text-base-content/60">HST</div>
                      <div className="font-medium text-success">{details.hst != null ? fmt(details.hst) : '—'}</div>
                      <div className="text-base-content/60">Total</div>
                      <div className="font-bold text-base-content">{details.total != null ? fmt(details.total) : '—'}</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="divider my-0" />

                  {/* Bank match panel */}
                  <div>
                    <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Bank Match</div>

                    {details.bankTransactions && details.bankTransactions.length > 0 ? (
                      <div className="space-y-2">
                        {details.bankTransactions.map((txn) => (
                          <div key={txn.id} className="rounded-box border border-success/30 bg-success/5 px-4 py-3">
                            <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                              <div>
                                <div className="font-semibold text-sm text-base-content">{txn.description}</div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60 mt-0.5">
                                  {fmtDate(txn.date)}
                                  {txn.source?.name && ` · ${txn.source.name}`}
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <div className="text-sm font-bold text-success shrink-0">{fmt(Math.abs(txn.amount))}</div>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                        {canEdit && (
                          <button
                            type="button"
                            className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs text-base-content/50 gap-1"
                            onClick={() => setShowMatchModal(true)}
                          >
                            <GitMerge size={12} /> Change match
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    ) : details.paymentType === 'cash' ? (
                      <div className="rounded-box border border-warning/30 bg-warning/5 px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                        <Banknote size={16} className="text-warning shrink-0" />
                        <div>
                          <div className="text-sm font-semibold">Cash payment</div>
                          <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60">No bank transaction expected.</div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ) : canEdit ? (
                      <div className="space-y-3">
                        <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60">No bank match confirmed yet.</div>
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                          <button type="button" onClick={() => setShowMatchModal(true)} className="btn btn-primary btn-sm gap-1">
                            <GitMerge size={14} /> Match to Transaction
                          </button>
                          <button type="button" onClick={handleMarkReceiptAsCash} className="btn btn-warning btn-sm gap-1" disabled={isUpdating}>
                            <Banknote size={14} /> Mark as Cash
                          </button>
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs text-base-content/50">Owner paid personally</button>
                          <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs text-base-content/50">No bank match expected</button>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Not yet matched.</div>
                    )}
                  </div>

                  <div className="divider my-0" />

                  {/* Editable fields */}
                  {canEdit && (
                    <div className="space-y-3">
                      <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50">Edit Fields</div>
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                        <label className="form-control">
                          <span className="label-text text-xs">Date</span>
                          <input
                            type="date"
                            name="date"
                            value={details.date ? String(details.date).slice(0, 10) : ''}
                            onChange={handleDetailChange}
                            className={`input input-bordered input-sm ${dateIssue ? 'input-warning' : ''}`}
                          />
                          {dateIssue && <span className="label-text-alt text-warning">{dateIssue}</span>}
                        </label>
                        <label className="form-control">
                          <span className="label-text text-xs">Company Name</span>
                          <input type="text" name="companyName" value={details.companyName || ''} onChange={handleDetailChange} className="input input-bordered input-sm" />
                        </label>
                        <label className="form-control">
                          <span className="label-text text-xs">Total</span>
                          <input type="number" step="0.01" name="total" value={details.total ?? 0} onChange={handleDetailChange} className="input input-bordered input-sm" />
                        </label>
                        <label className="form-control">
                          <span className="label-text text-xs">HST</span>
                          <input type="number" step="0.01" name="hst" value={details.hst ?? 0} onChange={handleDetailChange} className="input input-bordered input-sm" />
                        </label>
                      </div>
                      <label className="form-control">
                        <span className="label-text text-xs">Notes</span>
                        <textarea name="notes" value={details.notes || ''} onChange={handleDetailChange} className="textarea textarea-bordered textarea-sm min-h-[80px]" />
                      </label>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* Technical details — collapsed by default */}
                  <CollapsibleSection title="Technical Details">
                    <div className="text-sm text-base-content/70 space-y-1.5">
                      <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Source:</span> {details.filePath || details.imageRelativePath || details.imgName || 'Manual / unknown'}</div>
                      <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Image Status:</span> {resolvedImageStatus}</div>
                      {details.compressionStatus && details.compressionStatus !== 'NOT_OPTIMIZED' && (
                        <div>
                          <span className="font-medium text-base-content">Compression:</span> {details.compressionStatus}
                          {details.compressionSavedBytes > 0 && <span className="ml-1 text-success">({fmtBytes(details.compressionSavedBytes)} saved)</span>}
                        </div>
                      )}
                      {details.updatedAt && <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Updated:</span> {new Date(details.updatedAt).toLocaleString()}</div>}
                      {details.createdAt && <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Created:</span> {new Date(details.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</div>}
                      {organization?.name && <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Organization:</span> {organization.name}</div>}
                    </div>
                  </CollapsibleSection>

                  {/* Items — collapsed by default */}
                  <CollapsibleSection title={`Line Items${items.length > 0 ? ` (${items.length})` : ''}`}>
                    <div className="space-y-2">
                      {items.map((item, index) => (
                        <div key={`${index}-${item.name || 'item'}`} className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 items-center">
                          <input type="text" placeholder="Item name" value={item.name} onChange={(e) => handleReceiptItemChange(index, 'name', e.target.value)} className="input input-xs input-bordered flex-1 min-w-[120px]" readOnly={!canEdit} disabled={!canEdit} />
                          <input type="number" placeholder="Qty" value={item.quantity} onChange={(e) => handleReceiptItemChange(index, 'quantity', e.target.value)} className="input input-xs input-bordered w-16" min="1" readOnly={!canEdit} disabled={!canEdit} />
                          <input type="number" placeholder="Price" value={item.price} onChange={(e) => handleReceiptItemChange(index, 'price', e.target.value)} className="input input-xs input-bordered w-20" step="0.01" min="0" readOnly={!canEdit} disabled={!canEdit} />
                          {canEdit && <button type="button" onClick={() => handleRemoveReceiptItem(index)} className="btn btn-xs btn-ghost text-error">×</button>}
                        </div>
                      ))}
                      {items.length === 0 && <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60">No line items.</div>}
                      {canEdit && <button type="button" onClick={handleAddReceiptItem} className="btn btn-xs btn-outline mt-1">+ Add Item</button>}
                    </div>
                  </CollapsibleSection>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* IMAGE TOOLS TAB */}
            {activeTab === 'image' && (
              <div className="p-5 space-y-4">
                {currentImageUrl ? (
                  <>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-[1fr_280px] gap-4">
                      <ReceiptImageViewport
                        imageUrl={currentImageUrl}
                        zoom={imageZoom}
                        rotation={imageRotation}
                        onZoomChange={setImageZoom}
                        onRotationChange={setImageRotation}
                      />
                      <div className="space-y-3">
                        <div>
                          <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">View Controls</div>
                          <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Drag the image to pan. Use the mouse wheel or buttons to zoom.</div>
                        </div>

                        {canEdit && (
                          <>
                            <div>
                              <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Image Editing</div>
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                                <button type="button" className="btn btn-outline btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => runImageEdit('auto')} disabled={isImageEditing}><Wand2 size={13} /> Auto Fix</button>
                                <button type="button" className="btn btn-outline btn-xs" onClick={() => setShowCropEditor(true)} disabled={isImageEditing}>Crop</button>
                              </div>
                              {previewImgName && (
                                <div className="flex gap-2 mt-2">
                                  <button type="button" className="btn btn-primary btn-xs" onClick={handleSaveImageEdit} disabled={isImageEditing}>Save Preview</button>
                                  <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs" onClick={handleDiscardImageEdit} disabled={isImageEditing}>Discard</button>
                                </div>
                              )}
                            </div>

                            <div>
                              <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Compression</div>
                              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1">
                                <button
                                  type="button"
                                  className="btn btn-outline btn-xs gap-1"
                                  onClick={handleRunOptimizationPreview}
                                  disabled={isOptimizing || isImageEditing}
                                >
                                  {isOptimizing ? <RefreshCw size={12} className="animate-spin" /> : <Scissors size={12} />}
                                  {isOptimizing ? 'Reviewing...' : 'Auto-Crop + Compress'}
                                </button>
                                <select
                                  className="select select-bordered select-xs"
                                  value={reviewMode}
                                  onChange={(e) => setReviewMode(e.target.value)}
                                  disabled={isOptimizing}
                                >
                                  <option value="ocr-only">OCR only</option>
                                  <option value="ocr-plus-llm">OCR + AI</option>
                                </select>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </>
                        )}

                        <div>
                          <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Export</div>
                          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                            <button type="button" className="btn btn-outline btn-xs gap-1" onClick={handleDownloadCurrentImage}><Download size={12} /> Download</button>
                            <button type="button" className="btn btn-outline btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImage(false)} disabled={isExportingImage}><Download size={12} /> Export ZIP</button>
                            <button type="button" className="btn btn-warning btn-xs gap-1" onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImage(true)} disabled={isExportingImage}><Archive size={12} /> Export &amp; Archive</button>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Optimization report */}
                    {optimizationReport && (
                      <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 p-4 space-y-3 bg-base-100">
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-2">
                          <div>
                            <div className="font-semibold text-sm">Compression Review</div>
                            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60">{optimizationReport.status} · {selectedOptimizationCandidate?.profile || 'No passing candidate'}</div>
                          </div>
                          {selectedOptimizationCandidate && (
                            <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-success">Saves {fmtBytes(selectedOptimizationCandidate.savedBytes)}</div>
                          )}
                        </div>

                        {selectedOptimizationCandidate ? (
                          <>
                            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                              <div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50 mb-1">Current</div>
                                <img src={currentImageUrl} alt="Current" className="w-full rounded-lg border border-base-300" />
                              </div>
                              <div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50 mb-1">Optimized Preview</div>
                                <img src={selectedOptimizationUrl} alt="Optimized" className="w-full rounded-lg border border-base-300" />
                              </div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-xs text-base-content/70">
                              <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">New Size:</span> {fmtBytes(selectedOptimizationCandidate.sizeBytes)}</div>
                              <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">OCR:</span> {Math.round((selectedOptimizationCandidate.legibility?.textSimilarity || 0) * 100)}%</div>
                              <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Numbers:</span> {Math.round((selectedOptimizationCandidate.legibility?.numericTokenRecall || 0) * 100)}%</div>
                              <div><span className="font-medium text-base-content">Crop:</span> {selectedOptimizationCandidate.autoCropApplied ? 'Applied' : 'No'}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex gap-2">
                              <button type="button" onClick={handleSaveOptimization} className="btn btn-sm btn-primary" disabled={isOptimizing}>Approve</button>
                              <button type="button" onClick={handleDiscardOptimization} className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" disabled={isOptimizing}>Discard</button>
                            </div>
                          </>
                        ) : (
                          <div className="space-y-2">
                            <div className="text-sm text-warning">No candidate passed OCR safety checks. Original image is unchanged.</div>
                            <button type="button" onClick={() => setOptimizationReport(null)} className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost">Close</button>
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-8 text-center space-y-2">
                    <ImageOff className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto text-base-content/30" />
                    <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60">No image available for this receipt.</div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* OCR / TEXT TAB */}
            {activeTab === 'ocr' && (
              <div className="p-5 space-y-4">
                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3">
                  <div>
                    <div className="font-semibold text-sm">Raw OCR & Extracted Text</div>
                    <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60">Text extracted by OCR and parsed by the LLM.</div>
                  </div>
                  {canEdit && (
                    <button type="button" onClick={handleRunOcr} disabled={isRunningOcr} className="btn btn-sm btn-primary gap-1">
                      {isRunningOcr ? <><RefreshCw size={14} className="animate-spin" />Running OCR...</> : <><RefreshCw size={14} />Run OCR</>}
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>

                <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-200/40 p-4">
                  {details.text ? (
                    <>
                      <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Extracted Text</div>
                      <pre className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-base-content/80 font-mono max-h-[400px] overflow-y-auto">{details.text}</pre>
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="text-sm text-base-content/60 text-center py-4">
                      No OCR text available. Run OCR to extract text from the receipt image.
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>

                {details.notes && (
                  <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 p-4">
                    <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50 mb-2">Processing Notes</div>
                    <div className="text-sm text-base-content/80 whitespace-pre-wrap">{details.notes}</div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Sticky footer */}
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 px-5 py-3 border-t border-base-300 shrink-0 bg-base-100">
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">
              <MatchStatusHeader receipt={details} />
              {details.updatedAt && <span className="ml-2">· Updated {new Date(details.updatedAt).toLocaleDateString()}</span>}
            </div>
            {canEdit && (
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <button type="button" onClick={onClose} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm">Close</button>
                <button type="button" onClick={handleUpdateReceipt} className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" disabled={isUpdating}>
                  {isUpdating ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Changes'}
                </button>
                {!isMatched && (
                  <button type="button" onClick={() => setShowMatchModal(true)} className="btn btn-success btn-sm gap-1">
                    <GitMerge size={14} /> Find Match
                  </button>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <ReceiptImageEditor
        isOpen={showCropEditor}
        imageUrl={currentImageUrl}
        onClose={() => setShowCropEditor(false)}
        onApply={(crop) => runImageEdit('manual-crop', crop)}
      />

      {showMatchModal && (
        <MatchReceiptModal
          receipt={details}
          onClose={() => setShowMatchModal(false)}
          onMatched={handleMatchingSuccess}
        />
      )}
    </>
  );
};

export default ReceiptsDetails;

```
