```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptsTable.jsx
'use client';
import React, { useState, useMemo, useCallback, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import {
  Trash,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  RefreshCw,
  Download,
  CheckCircle,
  Wand2,
  Receipt,
  Search,
  Filter,
  FileText,
  Eye,
  Sparkles,
  Archive,
  Upload,
  Scissors,
  MoreHorizontal,
  ChevronDown,
  GitMerge,
  X,
} from 'lucide-react';
import ReceiptsDetail from './ReceiptsDetails';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import MatchReceiptModal from './MatchReceiptModal';
import { isValid } from 'date-fns';
import { computeFiscalYearDates, getFiscalYearStartMonth } from '../../accounting/utils/fiscalYear';

const truncateId = (id) => {
  if (!id || id.length <= 10) return id || '';
  return `${id.slice(0, 6)}...${id.slice(-4)}`;
};

const parseDatePurchased = (dateStr) => {
  if (!dateStr) return null;
  const date = new Date(dateStr);
  if (!isValid(date)) return null;
  const utcDate = new Date(Date.UTC(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate()));
  return isValid(utcDate) ? utcDate : null;
};

const formatDatePurchased = (dateObj) => {
  if (!dateObj || !isValid(dateObj)) return 'Invalid Date';
  return dateObj.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    year: 'numeric', month: 'short', day: '2-digit', timeZone: 'UTC',
  });
};

const formatMoney = (value) => `$${Number(value || 0).toFixed(2)}`;
const RECEIPTS_FILTERS_STORAGE_KEY = 'receiptsTableFilters';

const triggerBlobDownload = async (response, fallbackName) => {
  const blob = await response.blob();
  const blobUrl = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const contentDisposition = response.headers.get('content-disposition') || '';
  const fileNameMatch = contentDisposition.match(/filename="?([^"]+)"?/i);
  const fileName = fileNameMatch?.[1] || fallbackName;
  const link = document.createElement('a');
  link.href = blobUrl;
  link.setAttribute('download', fileName);
  document.body.appendChild(link);
  link.click();
  link.remove();
  window.URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl);
};

const WORKFLOW_TABS = [
  { id: 'needs-matching', label: 'Needs Matching', preset: { matchStatus: 'unmatched', activeStatus: 'true', showDuplicates: false } },
  { id: 'matched', label: 'Matched', preset: { matchStatus: 'matched', activeStatus: 'true', showDuplicates: false } },
  { id: 'duplicates', label: 'Duplicates', preset: { matchStatus: 'all', activeStatus: 'all', showDuplicates: true } },
  { id: 'archived', label: 'Archived', preset: { matchStatus: 'all', activeStatus: 'false', showDuplicates: false } },
  { id: 'all', label: 'All Receipts', preset: { matchStatus: 'all', activeStatus: 'all', showDuplicates: false } },
];

const INITIAL_FILTERS = {
  receiptId: '', companyName: '', dateFrom: '', dateTo: '', timeframe: '',
  notes: '', showErrors: false, showDuplicates: false,
  activeStatus: 'true', matchStatus: 'unmatched', imageStatus: 'all',
};

const getInitialReceiptFilters = () => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return INITIAL_FILTERS;

  try {
    const saved = window.localStorage.getItem(RECEIPTS_FILTERS_STORAGE_KEY);
    if (!saved) return INITIAL_FILTERS;

    const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);
    return {
      ...INITIAL_FILTERS,
      companyName: parsed.companyName || '',
      dateFrom: parsed.dateFrom || '',
      dateTo: parsed.dateTo || '',
      receiptId: parsed.receiptId || '',
      notes: parsed.notes || '',
    };
  } catch {
    window.localStorage.removeItem(RECEIPTS_FILTERS_STORAGE_KEY);
    return INITIAL_FILTERS;
  }
};

const MatchStatusBadge = ({ receipt }) => {
  const isMatched = !!receipt.paymentType || (receipt.bankTransactions && receipt.bankTransactions.length > 0);
  if (!receipt.active) return <span className="badge badge-warning badge-sm">Inactive</span>;
  if (receipt.imageStorageStatus === 'ARCHIVED') return <span className="badge badge-info badge-sm">Img Archived</span>;
  if (isMatched) return <span className="badge badge-success badge-sm gap-1"><CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3" /> Matched</span>;
  return <span className="badge badge-ghost badge-sm">Unmatched</span>;
};

const ReceiptsTable = () => {
  const [receipts, setReceipts] = useState([]);
  const [totalPages, setTotalPages] = useState(0);
  const [totalReceiptsCount, setTotalReceiptsCount] = useState(0);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const [selectedReceipt, setSelectedReceipt] = useState(null);
  const [showMatchModal, setShowMatchModal] = useState(false);
  const [receiptToMatch, setReceiptToMatch] = useState(null);
  const [goToPageInput, setGoToPageInput] = useState('');
  const [taggingReceiptId, setTaggingReceiptId] = useState(null);
  const [retaggingReceiptId, setRetaggingReceiptId] = useState(null);
  const [enhancingId, setEnhancingId] = useState(null);
  const [pageSize, setPageSize] = useState(20);
  const [isRefreshing, setIsRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [isArchiveWorking, setIsArchiveWorking] = useState(false);
  const [isRestoring, setIsRestoring] = useState(false);
  const [selectedIds, setSelectedIds] = useState(new Set());
  const [batchProgress, setBatchProgress] = useState(null);
  const [workflowTab, setWorkflowTab] = useState('needs-matching');
  const [showAdvancedFilters, setShowAdvancedFilters] = useState(false);
  const [showAutoMatchModal, setShowAutoMatchModal] = useState(false);
  const zipRestoreInputRef = useRef(null);
  const folderRestoreInputRef = useRef(null);

  const [fyStartMonth, setFyStartMonth] = useState(null);
  const [filtersInput, setFiltersInput] = useState(getInitialReceiptFilters);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState(getInitialReceiptFilters);
  const [sortConfig, setSortConfig] = useState({ key: 'createdAt', direction: 'desc' });

  useEffect(() => { getFiscalYearStartMonth().then(setFyStartMonth).catch(() => {}); }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (folderRestoreInputRef.current) {
      folderRestoreInputRef.current.setAttribute('webkitdirectory', '');
      folderRestoreInputRef.current.setAttribute('directory', '');
    }
  }, []);

  const handleTabChange = useCallback((tabId) => {
    setWorkflowTab(tabId);
    const tab = WORKFLOW_TABS.find((t) => t.id === tabId);
    if (!tab) return;
    setFiltersInput((prev) => ({ ...prev, ...tab.preset }));
    setFilters((prev) => ({ ...prev, ...tab.preset }));
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const queryString = useMemo(() => {
    const params = new URLSearchParams();
    params.append('page', currentPage);
    params.append('limit', pageSize);
    if (filters.receiptId) params.append('id', filters.receiptId);
    if (filters.companyName) params.append('companyName', filters.companyName);
    if (filters.notes) params.append('notes', filters.notes);
    if (filters.dateFrom) params.append('dateFrom', filters.dateFrom);
    if (filters.dateTo) params.append('dateTo', filters.dateTo);
    if (filters.showErrors) params.append('showErrors', 'true');
    if (filters.showDuplicates) params.append('showDuplicates', 'true');
    if (filters.activeStatus && filters.activeStatus !== 'all') params.append('active', filters.activeStatus);
    if (filters.matchStatus && filters.matchStatus !== 'all') params.append('matchStatus', filters.matchStatus);
    if (filters.imageStatus && filters.imageStatus !== 'all') params.append('imageStatus', filters.imageStatus);
    params.append('sortKey', sortConfig.key);
    params.append('sortDirection', sortConfig.direction);
    return params.toString();
  }, [currentPage, pageSize, filters, sortConfig]);

  const fetchReceipts = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/list?${queryString}`);
      const data = await response.json();
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to load receipts.');
      setReceipts(data.receipts || []);
      setTotalPages(data.totalPages || 0);
      setTotalReceiptsCount(data.total || 0);
    } catch (err) {
      setError(err);
      toast.error(`Failed to load receipts: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [queryString]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchReceipts();
    setSelectedIds(new Set());
  }, [fetchReceipts]);

  const handleDownloadCSV = useCallback(() => {
    if (!receipts.length) { toast.info('No receipts to download.'); return; }
    const headers = ['ID', 'Date', 'Created At', 'Company Name', 'Total', 'HST', 'Notes'];
    const escape = (f) => {
      if (f == null) return '';
      const s = f.toString();
      return s.search(/("|,|\n)/g) >= 0 ? `"${s.replace(/"/g, '""')}"` : s;
    };
    const rows = [headers.join(','), ...receipts.map((r) => [r.id, r.date, r.createdAt, r.companyName, r.total, r.hst, r.notes].map(escape).join(','))];
    const blob = new Blob([rows.join('\n')], { type: 'text/csv' });
    const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.download = `receipts_page_${currentPage}.csv`;
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    document.body.removeChild(link);
  }, [receipts, currentPage]);

  const handlePageSizeChange = useCallback((e) => {
    setPageSize(parseInt(e.target.value, 10));
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, []);

  const requestSort = useCallback((key) => {
    let direction = 'asc';
    if (sortConfig.key === key && sortConfig.direction === 'asc') direction = 'desc';
    setSortConfig({ key, direction });
    setCurrentPage(1);
  }, [sortConfig]);

  const getSortIndicator = useCallback((key) => {
    if (sortConfig.key !== key) return null;
    return sortConfig.direction === 'asc' ? ' ▲' : ' ▼';
  }, [sortConfig]);

  const handleFilterInputChange = useCallback((e) => {
    const { name, value, type, checked } = e.target;
    setFiltersInput((prev) => ({ ...prev, [name]: type === 'checkbox' ? checked : value }));
  }, []);

  const handleTimeframeChange = useCallback((e) => {
    const timeframe = e.target.value;
    let start = ''; let end = '';
    const now = new Date();
    now.setUTCHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    if (timeframe === 'thisQuarter') {
      const qm = Math.floor(now.getUTCMonth() / 3) * 3;
      start = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear(), qm, 1));
      end = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear(), qm + 3, 0));
    } else if (timeframe === 'lastQuarter') {
      const cq = Math.floor(now.getUTCMonth() / 3);
      let pq = cq - 1; let y = now.getUTCFullYear();
      if (pq < 0) { pq = 3; y -= 1; }
      start = new Date(Date.UTC(y, pq * 3, 1));
      end = new Date(Date.UTC(y, pq * 3 + 3, 0));
    } else if (timeframe === 'thisYear') {
      start = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear(), 0, 1));
      end = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear(), 11, 31));
    } else if (timeframe === 'lastYear') {
      start = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear() - 1, 0, 1));
      end = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getUTCFullYear() - 1, 11, 31));
    } else if (timeframe === 'thisFiscalYear' && fyStartMonth) {
      const fy = computeFiscalYearDates(fyStartMonth, now);
      if (fy) { start = fy.from; end = fy.to; }
    } else if (timeframe === 'lastFiscalYear' && fyStartMonth) {
      const fy = computeFiscalYearDates(fyStartMonth, now);
      if (fy) {
        start = new Date(Date.UTC(fy.from.getFullYear() - 1, fy.from.getMonth(), fy.from.getDate()));
        end = new Date(Date.UTC(fy.to.getFullYear() - 1, fy.to.getMonth(), fy.to.getDate()));
      }
    }
    setFiltersInput((prev) => ({
      ...prev, timeframe,
      dateFrom: start ? start.toISOString().split('T')[0] : '',
      dateTo: end ? end.toISOString().split('T')[0] : '',
    }));
  }, []);

  const handleApplyFilters = useCallback(() => {
    setFilters(filtersInput);
    setCurrentPage(1);
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(RECEIPTS_FILTERS_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify({
        companyName: filtersInput.companyName, dateFrom: filtersInput.dateFrom,
        dateTo: filtersInput.dateTo, receiptId: filtersInput.receiptId, notes: filtersInput.notes,
      }));
    } catch { /* ignore */ }
  }, [filtersInput]);

  const handleResetFilters = useCallback(() => {
    const tab = WORKFLOW_TABS.find((t) => t.id === workflowTab);
    const reset = { ...INITIAL_FILTERS, ...(tab?.preset || {}) };
    setFiltersInput(reset);
    setFilters(reset);
    setCurrentPage(1);
    localStorage.removeItem(RECEIPTS_FILTERS_STORAGE_KEY);
  }, [workflowTab]);

  const handleOpenMatchModalForReceipt = useCallback((selected) => {
    const full = receipts.find((r) => r.id === selected.id) || selected;
    setReceiptToMatch(full);
    setShowMatchModal(true);
  }, [receipts]);

  const handleMatchSuccess = useCallback(() => {
    fetchReceipts();
    setShowMatchModal(false);
    setReceiptToMatch(null);
  }, [fetchReceipts]);

  const handleEnhance = useCallback(async (receipt) => {
    if (!receipt?.imgName) { toast.error('No image available to enhance.'); return; }
    setEnhancingId(receipt.id);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/enhance`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: receipt.id, action: 'preview', operation: 'auto' }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Enhancement failed');
      toast.success(data.message || 'Preview created. Open the receipt to save or revert it.');
      fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Enhance failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setEnhancingId(null);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts]);

  const handleRetagReceipt = useCallback(async (receipt) => {
    if (!receipt?.id) return;
    setRetaggingReceiptId(receipt.id);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/tagReceipt`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: receipt.id }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to rerun LLM tag.');
      toast.success(data.heicConverted ? 'LLM tag rerun. HEIC converted to JPEG.' : (data.message || 'LLM tag rerun successfully.'));
      await fetchReceipts();
      if (selectedReceipt?.id === receipt.id) setSelectedReceipt((prev) => ({ ...(prev || {}), ...data.receipt }));
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Rerun failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setRetaggingReceiptId(null);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts, selectedReceipt]);

  const handleDelete = useCallback(async (receipt) => {
    if (!receipt?.id) { toast.error('Invalid receipt data for deletion.'); return; }
    if (!window.confirm(`Archive receipt ID ${truncateId(receipt.id)}?`)) return;
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/delete`, {
        method: 'DELETE', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ id: receipt.id, imgName: receipt.imgName }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to archive receipt.');
      toast.success('Receipt archived successfully');
      fetchReceipts();
      if (selectedReceipt?.id === receipt.id) setSelectedReceipt(null);
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Error deleting receipt: ${err.message}`);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts, selectedReceipt]);

  const handleRefresh = useCallback(async () => {
    setIsRefreshing(true);
    try {
      await fetchReceipts();
    } finally {
      setIsRefreshing(false);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts]);

  const handleExportReceiptImages = useCallback(async (archiveAfterExport = false, explicitReceiptIds = null) => {
    const candidateIds = Array.isArray(explicitReceiptIds) && explicitReceiptIds.length
      ? explicitReceiptIds
      : receipts.filter((r) => r.imgName && r.imageStorageStatus !== 'ARCHIVED').map((r) => r.id);
    if (!candidateIds.length) { toast.info('No active receipt images available to export.'); return; }
    setIsArchiveWorking(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/archive/export`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: candidateIds, archiveAfterExport }),
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        let msg = 'Failed to export receipt images.';
        try { const d = await response.json(); msg = d.error || msg; } catch { /* ignore */ }
        throw new Error(msg);
      }
      await triggerBlobDownload(response, archiveAfterExport ? 'receipt-images-archived.zip' : 'receipt-images.zip');
      toast.success(archiveAfterExport ? 'Receipt images exported and archived.' : 'Receipt images exported.');
      await fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Export failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsArchiveWorking(false);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts, receipts]);

  const restoreFromFiles = useCallback(async (files) => {
    if (!files?.length) return;
    setIsRestoring(true);
    try {
      const formData = new FormData();
      Array.from(files).forEach((file) => formData.append('files', file, file.webkitRelativePath || file.name));
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/archive/restore`, { method: 'POST', body: formData });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to restore receipt images.');
      const r = data.report || {};
      toast.success(`Restore complete. Restored ${r.restoredCount || 0}, already present ${r.alreadyPresentCount || 0}, conflicts ${r.conflictCount || 0}.`);
      await fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Restore failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsRestoring(false);
      if (zipRestoreInputRef.current) zipRestoreInputRef.current.value = '';
      if (folderRestoreInputRef.current) folderRestoreInputRef.current.value = '';
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts]);

  const handleAutoMatchBatchReceipts = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = receipts.filter((r) => !r.paymentType && (!r.bankTransactions || r.bankTransactions.length === 0)).map((r) => r.id);
    if (!ids.length) { toast.info('No unmatched receipts on this page.'); return; }
    setIsRefreshing(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match/auto-match-batch`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: ids }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Failed to auto-match receipts.');
      const matched = data.matchedCount ?? data.matched?.length ?? 0;
      const failed = data.failedCount ?? data.errors?.length ?? 0;
      toast.success(`Auto-match complete. Matched ${matched}, failed ${failed}.`);
      fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Error auto-matching receipts: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setIsRefreshing(false);
    }
  }, [receipts, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleAutoMatchSingleReceipt = useCallback(async (receiptId) => {
    const receipt = receipts.find((r) => r.id === receiptId);
    if (!receipt) { toast.error('Receipt not found.'); return; }
    if (receipt.paymentType || (receipt.bankTransactions?.length > 0)) { toast.info('Already matched.'); return; }
    setTaggingReceiptId(receiptId);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match/auto-match-single`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (res.ok && data.success) {
        toast.success(data.message || 'Receipt matched automatically.');
        fetchReceipts();
      } else {
        toast.info(data.message || 'Automatic match failed. Please match manually.');
        const modalData = data.receipt ? { ...data.receipt, id: receiptId } : { id: receiptId };
        setReceiptToMatch(modalData);
        setShowMatchModal(true);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Automatic matching failed: ${err.message}`);
    } finally {
      setTaggingReceiptId(null);
    }
  }, [fetchReceipts, receipts]);

  const allPageIds = useMemo(() => receipts.map((r) => r.id), [receipts]);
  const allSelected = allPageIds.length > 0 && allPageIds.every((id) => selectedIds.has(id));
  const someSelected = allPageIds.some((id) => selectedIds.has(id));

  const toggleSelectAll = useCallback(() => {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (allSelected) allPageIds.forEach((id) => next.delete(id));
      else allPageIds.forEach((id) => next.add(id));
      return next;
    });
  }, [allSelected, allPageIds]);

  const toggleSelectOne = useCallback((id) => {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id); else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  }, []);

  const clearSelection = useCallback(() => setSelectedIds(new Set()), []);

  const handleBatchOcr = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds];
    if (!ids.length) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'OCR', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    for (let i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      try {
        await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/ocr`, {
          method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: ids[i] }),
        });
      } catch {
        setBatchProgress((prev) => prev ? { ...prev, errors: prev.errors + 1 } : null);
      }
      setBatchProgress((prev) => prev ? { ...prev, done: i + 1 } : null);
    }
    toast.success(`OCR queued for ${ids.length} receipt(s).`);
    setBatchProgress(null);
    fetchReceipts();
  }, [selectedIds, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleBatchLlmTag = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds];
    if (!ids.length) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'LLM Tag', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    for (let i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      try {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/tagReceipt`, {
          method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ receiptId: ids[i] }),
        });
        if (!res.ok) setBatchProgress((prev) => prev ? { ...prev, errors: prev.errors + 1 } : null);
      } catch {
        setBatchProgress((prev) => prev ? { ...prev, errors: prev.errors + 1 } : null);
      }
      setBatchProgress((prev) => prev ? { ...prev, done: i + 1 } : null);
    }
    toast.success(`LLM tagging complete for ${ids.length} receipt(s).`);
    setBatchProgress(null);
    fetchReceipts();
  }, [selectedIds, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleBatchAutoMatch = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds];
    if (!ids.length) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'Auto-Match', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/match/auto-match-batch`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: ids }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Auto-match failed.');
      const matched = data.matchedCount ?? data.matched?.length ?? 0;
      const failed = data.failedCount ?? data.errors?.length ?? 0;
      toast.success(`Auto-match complete. Matched ${matched}, failed ${failed}.`);
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Auto-match failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
    setBatchProgress(null);
    fetchReceipts();
  }, [selectedIds, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleBatchEstimate = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds];
    if (!ids.length) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'Estimating', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/bulk`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: ids, dryRun: true, autoCrop: true }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Savings estimate failed.');
      const passed = (data.results || []).filter((r) => r.status === 'PASSED').length;
      const savedKB = Math.round((data.totalEstimatedSavedBytes || 0) / 1024);
      if (passed > 0) toast.info(`${passed} of ${ids.length} receipts could save ~${savedKB} KB.`);
      else toast.warn('No receipts passed the compression safety check.');
      fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Savings estimate failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
    setBatchProgress(null);
  }, [selectedIds, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleBatchOptimize = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds];
    if (!ids.length) return;
    if (!window.confirm(`Compress optimized images for up to ${ids.length} selected receipt(s)? Originals are kept.`)) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'Batch Optimize', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/bulk`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: ids, dryRun: false, autoCrop: true }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Batch optimize failed.');
      const activated = data.activatedCount ?? 0;
      const savedKB = Math.round((data.totalEstimatedSavedBytes || 0) / 1024);
      if (activated > 0) toast.success(`${activated} of ${ids.length} receipts compressed. ~${savedKB} KB saved.`);
      else toast.warn('No receipts passed OCR safety checks — nothing was changed.');
      fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Batch optimize failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
    setBatchProgress(null);
  }, [selectedIds, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleBatchPurgeOriginals = useCallback(async () => {
    const ids = [...selectedIds].filter((id) => receipts.find((r) => r.id === id)?.activeImageVariant === 'optimized');
    if (!ids.length) { toast.info('None of the selected receipts have a purgeable original.'); return; }
    if (!window.confirm(`Permanently delete original images for ${ids.length} receipt(s)? This cannot be undone.`)) return;
    setBatchProgress({ action: 'Purging Originals', done: 0, total: ids.length, errors: 0 });
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/optimize/bulk-purge-original`, {
        method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ receiptIds: ids }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(data.error || 'Bulk purge failed.');
      const freedKB = Math.round((data.totalFreedBytes || 0) / 1024);
      toast.success(`Purged originals for ${data.purgedCount} receipt(s). Freed ~${freedKB} KB.`);
      fetchReceipts();
    } catch (err) {
      toast.error(`Bulk purge failed: ${err.message}`);
    }
    setBatchProgress(null);
  }, [selectedIds, receipts, fetchReceipts]);

  const handleGoToPageSubmit = useCallback(() => {
    const pageNumber = parseInt(goToPageInput, 10);
    if (Number.isNaN(pageNumber) || pageNumber < 1 || pageNumber > totalPages) {
      toast.error(`Page number must be between 1 and ${totalPages}.`); return;
    }
    setCurrentPage(pageNumber);
    setGoToPageInput('');
  }, [goToPageInput, totalPages]);

  const summary = useMemo(() => {
    const grandTotal = receipts.reduce((sum, r) => sum + (r.total || 0), 0);
    const totalHst = receipts.reduce((sum, r) => sum + (r.hst || 0), 0);
    const imageCount = receipts.filter((r) => !!r.imgName).length;
    const archivedImageCount = receipts.filter((r) => r.imageStorageStatus === 'ARCHIVED').length;
    const unmatchedCount = receipts.filter((r) => !r.paymentType && (!r.bankTransactions?.length)).length;
    return { grandTotal, totalHst, imageCount, archivedImageCount, unmatchedCount };
  }, [receipts]);

  const unmatchedOnPageCount = useMemo(
    () => receipts.filter((r) => !r.paymentType && (!r.bankTransactions || r.bankTransactions.length === 0)).length,
    [receipts]
  );

  const getPageNumbers = () => {
    const pages = [];
    const totalNumbers = 5;
    const half = Math.floor(totalNumbers / 2);
    if (totalPages <= totalNumbers) {
      for (let page = 1; page <= totalPages; page += 1) pages.push(page);
    } else {
      pages.push(1);
      let startPage = Math.max(2, currentPage - half);
      let endPage = Math.min(totalPages - 1, currentPage + half);
      if (currentPage <= half + 1) endPage = Math.min(totalPages - 1, totalNumbers - 1);
      if (currentPage >= totalPages - half) startPage = Math.max(2, totalPages - totalNumbers + 2);
      if (startPage > 2) pages.push('left-ellipsis');
      for (let page = startPage; page <= endPage; page += 1) pages.push(page);
      if (endPage < totalPages - 1) pages.push('right-ellipsis');
      if (totalPages > 1) pages.push(totalPages);
    }
    return pages;
  };

  return (
    <div className="card bg-base-100 shadow-xl border border-base-300 overflow-hidden">
      <div className="card-body p-4 md:p-6 space-y-4">

        {/* Page header */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 p-3">
            <Receipt className="w-5 h-5 text-primary" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-base-content">Receipts</h3>
            <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Review and match receipts to bank transactions.</p>
          </div>
          {error && <span className="text-sm text-error ml-2">Load error</span>}
        </div>

        {/* Workflow tabs */}
        <div role="tablist" className="tabs tabs-bordered overflow-x-auto flex-nowrap flex">
          {WORKFLOW_TABS.map((tab) => (
            <button
              key={tab.id}
              role="tab"
              type="button"
              className={`tab whitespace-nowrap ${workflowTab === tab.id ? 'tab-active font-semibold' : ''}`}
              onClick={() => handleTabChange(tab.id)}
            >
              {tab.label}
              {workflowTab === tab.id && totalReceiptsCount > 0 && (
                <span className="ml-2 badge badge-xs badge-primary">{totalReceiptsCount}</span>
              )}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Filter toolbar */}
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 items-end">
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-[180px] relative">
              <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-base-content/40 pointer-events-none" />
              <input
                type="text"
                name="companyName"
                value={filtersInput.companyName}
                onChange={handleFilterInputChange}
                placeholder="Search merchant..."
                className="input input-bordered input-sm w-full pl-9"
                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleApplyFilters()}
              />
            </div>
            <input
              type="date"
              name="dateFrom"
              value={filtersInput.dateFrom}
              onChange={handleFilterInputChange}
              className="input input-bordered input-sm"
              disabled={!!filtersInput.timeframe}
              title="Date from"
            />
            <span className="text-base-content/40 text-sm self-center">–</span>
            <input
              type="date"
              name="dateTo"
              value={filtersInput.dateTo}
              onChange={handleFilterInputChange}
              className="input input-bordered input-sm"
              disabled={!!filtersInput.timeframe}
              title="Date to"
            />
            <button
              type="button"
              className={`btn btn-sm btn-ghost gap-1 ${showAdvancedFilters ? 'btn-active' : ''}`}
              onClick={() => setShowAdvancedFilters((s) => !s)}
            >
              <Filter className="w-4 h-4" />
              Advanced
              <ChevronDown className={`w-3 h-3 transition-transform ${showAdvancedFilters ? 'rotate-180' : ''}`} />
            </button>
            <button type="button" onClick={handleApplyFilters} className="btn btn-sm btn-primary gap-1" disabled={loading}>
              <Search className="w-4 h-4" />Apply
            </button>
            <button type="button" onClick={handleResetFilters} className="btn btn-sm btn-ghost" disabled={loading}>Clear</button>
          </div>

          {showAdvancedFilters && (
            <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100/80 p-3 space-y-3">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
                <label className="form-control">
                  <span className="label-text text-xs">Receipt ID</span>
                  <input type="text" name="receiptId" value={filtersInput.receiptId} onChange={handleFilterInputChange} placeholder="Contains..." className="input input-bordered input-sm" />
                </label>
                <label className="form-control">
                  <span className="label-text text-xs">Notes</span>
                  <input type="text" name="notes" value={filtersInput.notes} onChange={handleFilterInputChange} placeholder="Contains..." className="input input-bordered input-sm" />
                </label>
                <label className="form-control">
                  <span className="label-text text-xs">Timeframe</span>
                  <select name="timeframe" value={filtersInput.timeframe} onChange={handleTimeframeChange} className="select select-bordered select-sm">
                    <option value="">Custom range</option>
                    <option value="thisQuarter">This Quarter</option>
                    <option value="lastQuarter">Last Quarter</option>
                    <option value="thisYear">This Year</option>
                    <option value="lastYear">Last Year</option>
                    {fyStartMonth && <option value="thisFiscalYear">This Fiscal Year</option>}
                    {fyStartMonth && <option value="lastFiscalYear">Last Fiscal Year</option>}
                  </select>
                </label>
                <label className="form-control">
                  <span className="label-text text-xs">Image Storage</span>
                  <select name="imageStatus" value={filtersInput.imageStatus} onChange={handleFilterInputChange} className="select select-bordered select-sm">
                    <option value="all">All</option>
                    <option value="active">On Server</option>
                    <option value="archived">Archived</option>
                    <option value="none">No Image</option>
                  </select>
                </label>
              </div>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-4">
                <label className="label cursor-pointer gap-2 p-0">
                  <input type="checkbox" name="showErrors" checked={filtersInput.showErrors} onChange={handleFilterInputChange} className="checkbox checkbox-sm" />
                  <span className="label-text text-sm">Errors only (total is $0)</span>
                </label>
                <label className="label cursor-pointer gap-2 p-0">
                  <input type="checkbox" name="showDuplicates" checked={filtersInput.showDuplicates} onChange={handleFilterInputChange} className="checkbox checkbox-sm" />
                  <span className="label-text text-sm">Duplicates only</span>
                </label>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Summary cards */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
          <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50">This Page</div>
            <div className="mt-1 text-lg font-semibold">{receipts.length} receipts</div>
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">{totalReceiptsCount} total filtered</div>
          </div>
          <div className={`rounded-box border px-4 py-3 ${summary.unmatchedCount > 0 ? 'border-warning/30 bg-warning/5' : 'border-base-300 bg-base-100'}`}>
            <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50">Unmatched</div>
            <div className={`mt-1 text-lg font-semibold ${summary.unmatchedCount > 0 ? 'text-warning' : 'text-base-content'}`}>{summary.unmatchedCount}</div>
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">on this page</div>
          </div>
          <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50">Page HST</div>
            <div className="mt-1 text-lg font-semibold text-success">{formatMoney(summary.totalHst)}</div>
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">tax recoverable</div>
          </div>
          <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-wider text-base-content/50">Page Total</div>
            <div className="mt-1 text-lg font-semibold">{formatMoney(summary.grandTotal)}</div>
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">all receipts</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Header actions row */}
        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <label htmlFor="pageSizeSelect" className="text-sm text-base-content/60">Show</label>
            <select id="pageSizeSelect" value={pageSize} onChange={handlePageSizeChange} className="select select-bordered select-sm" disabled={loading}>
              <option value={10}>10</option>
              <option value={20}>20</option>
              <option value={50}>50</option>
              <option value={100}>100</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
            {unmatchedOnPageCount > 0 && (
              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setShowAutoMatchModal(true)}
                className="btn btn-secondary btn-sm gap-1"
                disabled={isRefreshing || loading}
              >
                <GitMerge size={15} />
                Auto-Match ({unmatchedOnPageCount})
              </button>
            )}
            <div className="dropdown dropdown-end">
              <label tabIndex={0} className="btn btn-outline btn-sm gap-1">
                <Download size={15} />Export
                <ChevronDown size={13} />
              </label>
              <ul tabIndex={0} className="dropdown-content menu p-2 shadow bg-base-100 rounded-box w-52 z-50">
                <li><button onClick={handleDownloadCSV}><FileText size={13} /> Download CSV</button></li>
                <li><button onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImages(false)} disabled={isArchiveWorking || !summary.imageCount}><Download size={13} /> Export Images ZIP</button></li>
                <li><button onClick={() => handleExportReceiptImages(true)} disabled={isArchiveWorking || !summary.imageCount}><Archive size={13} /> Export &amp; Archive</button></li>
                <li className="divider my-0.5" />
                <li><button onClick={() => zipRestoreInputRef.current?.click()} disabled={isRestoring}><Upload size={13} /> Restore from ZIP</button></li>
                <li><button onClick={() => folderRestoreInputRef.current?.click()} disabled={isRestoring}><Upload size={13} /> Restore from Folder</button></li>
              </ul>
            </div>
            <button type="button" onClick={handleRefresh} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle" disabled={isRefreshing || loading} title="Refresh">
              <RefreshCw className={`w-4 h-4 ${isRefreshing || loading ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`} />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Selection batch bar */}
        {selectedIds.size > 0 && (
          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 rounded-box border border-primary/30 bg-primary/5 px-4 py-3">
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">{selectedIds.size} selected</span>
            {batchProgress ? (
              <span className="text-sm text-base-content/70">
                {batchProgress.action}: {batchProgress.done}/{batchProgress.total}
                {batchProgress.errors > 0 ? ` (${batchProgress.errors} errors)` : ''}
              </span>
            ) : (
              <>
                <button type="button" onClick={handleBatchOcr} className="btn btn-xs btn-primary gap-1"><RefreshCw size={12} /> OCR</button>
                <button type="button" onClick={handleBatchLlmTag} className="btn btn-xs btn-secondary gap-1"><Sparkles size={12} /> LLM Tag</button>
                <button type="button" onClick={handleBatchAutoMatch} className="btn btn-xs btn-success gap-1"><GitMerge size={12} /> Auto-Match</button>
                <div className="dropdown dropdown-end">
                  <label tabIndex={0} className="btn btn-xs btn-ghost gap-1"><MoreHorizontal size={12} /> More</label>
                  <ul tabIndex={0} className="dropdown-content menu menu-sm p-2 shadow bg-base-100 rounded-box w-48 z-50">
                    <li><button onClick={handleBatchEstimate}><Scissors size={12} /> Estimate Savings</button></li>
                    <li><button onClick={handleBatchOptimize}><Scissors size={12} /> Batch Optimize</button></li>
                    <li><button onClick={handleBatchPurgeOriginals} className="text-error"><Trash size={12} /> Purge Originals</button></li>
                  </ul>
                </div>
              </>
            )}
            <button type="button" onClick={clearSelection} className="btn btn-xs btn-ghost ml-auto" disabled={!!batchProgress}>Clear</button>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Desktop table */}
        <div className="hidden lg:block overflow-hidden rounded-box border border-base-300 shadow-sm">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="table table-sm w-full">
              <thead className="bg-base-200/80 sticky top-0 z-10">
                <tr>
                  <th className="w-10">
                    <input
                      type="checkbox"
                      className="checkbox checkbox-sm"
                      checked={allSelected}
                      ref={(el) => { if (el) el.indeterminate = someSelected && !allSelected; }}
                      onChange={toggleSelectAll}
                      disabled={loading || receipts.length === 0}
                    />
                  </th>
                  <th className="cursor-pointer" onClick={() => requestSort('companyName')}>Merchant{getSortIndicator('companyName')}</th>
                  <th className="cursor-pointer" onClick={() => requestSort('date')}>Date{getSortIndicator('date')}</th>
                  <th className="cursor-pointer text-right" onClick={() => requestSort('total')}>Amount{getSortIndicator('total')}</th>
                  <th>Status</th>
                  <th className="text-right w-28">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody>
                {loading ? (
                  <tr><td colSpan={6} className="py-12 text-center text-base-content/50"><RefreshCw className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin inline mr-2" />Loading receipts...</td></tr>
                ) : receipts.length === 0 ? (
                  <tr><td colSpan={6} className="py-10 text-center text-base-content/50">No receipts found.</td></tr>
                ) : (
                  receipts.map((receipt) => {
                    const parsedDate = parseDatePurchased(receipt.date);
                    const formattedDate = parsedDate ? formatDatePurchased(parsedDate) : 'N/A';
                    const formattedCreatedAt = receipt.createdAt ? new Date(receipt.createdAt).toLocaleDateString() : '';
                    const isMatched = !!receipt.paymentType || (receipt.bankTransactions?.length > 0);
                    const isImage = receipt.imgName && !receipt.imgName.endsWith('.pdf') && !receipt.imgName.endsWith('.txt');
                    const isArchivedImage = receipt.imageStorageStatus === 'ARCHIVED';
                    const isSelected = selectedIds.has(receipt.id);

                    return (
                      <tr
                        key={receipt.id}
                        className={`cursor-pointer ${receipt.active ? 'hover' : 'bg-warning/5'} ${isSelected ? 'bg-primary/5' : ''}`}
                        onClick={() => setSelectedReceipt(receipt)}
                      >
                        <td onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
                          <input type="checkbox" className="checkbox checkbox-sm" checked={isSelected} onChange={() => toggleSelectOne(receipt.id)} />
                        </td>
                        <td>
                          <div className="font-semibold text-sm text-base-content">{receipt.companyName || 'Unknown Merchant'}</div>
                          <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50 font-mono mt-0.5">{truncateId(receipt.id)}</div>
                          {receipt.compressionStatus === 'ACTIVE_OPTIMIZED' && (
                            <span className="badge badge-xs badge-ghost text-success mt-0.5">Optimized</span>
                          )}
                        </td>
                        <td>
                          <div className="text-sm font-medium text-base-content">{formattedDate}</div>
                          {formattedCreatedAt && <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">Added {formattedCreatedAt}</div>}
                        </td>
                        <td className="text-right">
                          <div className="font-semibold text-sm text-base-content">{formatMoney(receipt.total)}</div>
                          {receipt.hst > 0 && <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">HST {formatMoney(receipt.hst)}</div>}
                        </td>
                        <td onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
                          <MatchStatusBadge receipt={receipt} />
                        </td>
                        <td onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 justify-end">
                            {!isMatched ? (
                              <button
                                type="button"
                                className="btn btn-success btn-xs gap-1"
                                onClick={() => handleAutoMatchSingleReceipt(receipt.id)}
                                disabled={taggingReceiptId === receipt.id}
                                title="Auto-match this receipt"
                              >
                                {taggingReceiptId === receipt.id
                                  ? <RefreshCw size={11} className="animate-spin" />
                                  : <GitMerge size={11} />}
                                Match
                              </button>
                            ) : (
                              <button
                                type="button"
                                className="btn btn-outline btn-xs gap-1"
                                onClick={() => setSelectedReceipt(receipt)}
                              >
                                <Eye size={11} />View
                              </button>
                            )}
                            <div className="dropdown dropdown-end">
                              <label tabIndex={0} className="btn btn-ghost btn-xs btn-circle">
                                <MoreHorizontal size={14} />
                              </label>
                              <ul tabIndex={0} className="dropdown-content menu menu-sm p-2 shadow-lg bg-base-100 rounded-box w-48 z-[100]">
                                <li><button onClick={() => setSelectedReceipt(receipt)}><Eye size={13} /> View details</button></li>
                                {isImage && !isArchivedImage && (
                                  <li><button onClick={() => handleEnhance(receipt)} disabled={enhancingId === receipt.id}><Wand2 size={13} /> Preview fix</button></li>
                                )}
                                <li><button onClick={() => handleRetagReceipt(receipt)} disabled={retaggingReceiptId === receipt.id}><Sparkles size={13} /> Rerun LLM</button></li>
                                <li><button onClick={() => handleOpenMatchModalForReceipt(receipt)}><GitMerge size={13} /> Manual match</button></li>
                                <li><button onClick={() => handleDelete(receipt)} className="text-error"><Trash size={13} /> Archive</button></li>
                              </ul>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </td>
                      </tr>
                    );
                  })
                )}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Mobile cards */}
        <div className="lg:hidden space-y-3">
          {loading ? (
            <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 p-6 text-center text-base-content/50">
              <RefreshCw className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin inline mr-2" />Loading receipts...
            </div>
          ) : receipts.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 p-6 text-center text-base-content/50">
              No receipts found.
            </div>
          ) : (
            receipts.map((receipt) => {
              const parsedDate = parseDatePurchased(receipt.date);
              const formattedDate = parsedDate ? formatDatePurchased(parsedDate) : 'N/A';
              const isMatched = !!receipt.paymentType || (receipt.bankTransactions?.length > 0);
              const isSelected = selectedIds.has(receipt.id);

              return (
                <div
                  key={receipt.id}
                  className={`rounded-box border shadow-sm p-4 ${receipt.active ? 'border-base-300 bg-base-100' : 'border-warning/30 bg-warning/5'} ${isSelected ? 'border-primary/40 bg-primary/5' : ''}`}
                >
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
                      <input
                        type="checkbox"
                        className="checkbox checkbox-sm flex-shrink-0"
                        checked={isSelected}
                        onChange={() => toggleSelectOne(receipt.id)}
                        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
                      />
                      <button type="button" className="text-left min-w-0" onClick={() => setSelectedReceipt(receipt)}>
                        <div className="font-semibold text-sm truncate">{receipt.companyName || 'Unknown Merchant'}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50 mt-0.5">{formattedDate}</div>
                      </button>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                      <div className="font-semibold text-sm">{formatMoney(receipt.total)}</div>
                      {receipt.hst > 0 && <div className="text-xs text-base-content/50">HST {formatMoney(receipt.hst)}</div>}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-2 mt-3">
                    <MatchStatusBadge receipt={receipt} />
                    <div className="flex gap-1">
                      {!isMatched && (
                        <button
                          type="button"
                          className="btn btn-success btn-xs"
                          onClick={() => handleAutoMatchSingleReceipt(receipt.id)}
                          disabled={taggingReceiptId === receipt.id}
                        >
                          {taggingReceiptId === receipt.id ? <RefreshCw size={11} className="animate-spin" /> : 'Match'}
                        </button>
                      )}
                      <button type="button" className="btn btn-outline btn-xs" onClick={() => setSelectedReceipt(receipt)}>Open</button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              );
            })
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Pagination */}
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 rounded-box border border-base-300 bg-base-100 p-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => setCurrentPage((p) => Math.max(p - 1, 1))} disabled={currentPage === 1 || loading} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-square"><ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
            <span className="text-sm text-base-content/70">Page <span className="font-semibold text-base-content">{currentPage}</span> of <span className="font-semibold text-base-content">{totalPages || 1}</span></span>
            <button onClick={() => setCurrentPage((p) => Math.min(p + 1, totalPages || 1))} disabled={currentPage === totalPages || loading || totalPages === 0} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-square"><ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" /></button>
          </div>
          {totalPages > 1 && (
            <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-1">
              {getPageNumbers().map((page, i) =>
                typeof page === 'string' ? (
                  <span key={`${page}-${i}`} className="px-2 text-base-content/40">…</span>
                ) : (
                  <button key={page} onClick={() => setCurrentPage(page)} disabled={loading} className={`btn btn-sm ${page === currentPage ? 'btn-primary' : 'btn-ghost border border-base-300'}`}>{page}</button>
                )
              )}
            </div>
          )}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <input type="number" value={goToPageInput} onChange={(e) => setGoToPageInput(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') handleGoToPageSubmit(); }} className="input input-bordered input-sm w-20 text-center" placeholder="Page" min="1" max={totalPages} disabled={totalPages <= 1 || loading} />
            <button onClick={handleGoToPageSubmit} className="btn btn-primary btn-sm" disabled={!goToPageInput || loading}>Go</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Auto-match confirmation modal */}
      {showAutoMatchModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-base-300/60 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-50 p-4" onClick={() => setShowAutoMatchModal(false)}>
          <div className="card bg-base-100 shadow-2xl w-full max-w-sm border border-base-300" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div className="card-body gap-4">
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="font-bold text-lg">Auto-Match Receipts</h3>
                  <p className="text-sm text-base-content/60 mt-1">{unmatchedOnPageCount} unmatched receipts on this page</p>
                </div>
                <button onClick={() => setShowAutoMatchModal(false)} className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-circle"><X size={16} /></button>
              </div>
              <div className="rounded-box border border-info/30 bg-info/10 p-3 text-sm space-y-1">
                <div className="font-semibold text-base-content">Only high-confidence matches are applied</div>
                <div className="text-base-content/70">Receipts with exact amount, close date, and strong merchant match. Ambiguous matches are skipped and queued for manual review.</div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                <button type="button" className="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onClick={() => setShowAutoMatchModal(false)}>Cancel</button>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  className="btn btn-success btn-sm gap-2"
                  onClick={() => { setShowAutoMatchModal(false); handleAutoMatchBatchReceipts(); }}
                  disabled={isRefreshing}
                >
                  {isRefreshing ? <><RefreshCw size={14} className="animate-spin" />Running...</> : <><GitMerge size={14} />Run Auto-Match</>}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Receipt detail modal */}
      {selectedReceipt && (
        <ReceiptsDetail
          receipt={selectedReceipt}
          onClose={() => setSelectedReceipt(null)}
          onUpdate={() => fetchReceipts()}
        />
      )}

      {/* Match receipt modal */}
      {showMatchModal && receiptToMatch && (
        <MatchReceiptModal
          receipt={receiptToMatch}
          onClose={() => { setShowMatchModal(false); setReceiptToMatch(null); }}
          onMatched={handleMatchSuccess}
        />
      )}

      <input ref={zipRestoreInputRef} type="file" accept=".zip,application/zip" className="hidden" onChange={(e) => restoreFromFiles(e.target.files)} />
      <input ref={folderRestoreInputRef} type="file" multiple className="hidden" onChange={(e) => restoreFromFiles(e.target.files)} />
    </div>
  );
};

export default React.memo(ReceiptsTable);

```

FILE: client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptWidget.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/components/ReceiptWidget.jsx
import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import CameraPanel from './camera/CameraPanel';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import BaseWidget from '@/shared/components/BaseWidget';
import { FileText, ChartArea, SquareChartGantt } from 'lucide-react';
import Tooltip from '@/shared/components/Tooltip';

const ReceiptWidget = () => {
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user, organization } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const [recentReceipts, setRecentReceipts] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState(() => {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      return localStorage.getItem('receiptWidgetViewMode') || 'simple';
    }
    return 'simple';
  });
  const toggleViewMode = () => {
    const newMode = viewMode === "advanced" ? "simple" : "advanced";
    setViewMode(newMode);
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      localStorage.setItem('receiptWidgetViewMode', newMode);
    }
  };
  
  const headerActions = (
    <div className="flex space-x-2">
      <Tooltip content={viewMode === "advanced" ? "Switch to Simple View" : "Switch to Advanced View"}>
        <button onClick={toggleViewMode} className="btn btn-sm">
          {viewMode === "advanced" ? <ChartArea size={16} /> : <SquareChartGantt size={16} />}
        </button>
      </Tooltip>
    </div>
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (organization) {
      fetchRecentReceipts();
    }
  }, [organization]);

  const fetchRecentReceipts = async () => {
    try {
      const response = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/receipt/list`, {
        credentials: 'include',
      });
      if (response.ok) {
        const data = await response.json();
        setRecentReceipts(data.receipts.slice(0, 5));
      } else {
        throw new Error(`Error: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching receipts:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const simpleView = (
    <div className="p-4">
      <p className="text-sm">Receipt Management: View and manage your receipts.</p>
    </div>
  );

  const advancedView = (
    <div className="p-4">
      <div className="mb-6">
        <CameraPanel onUploadSuccess={fetchRecentReceipts} />
      </div>
      <div className="mt-4">
        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">Recent Receipts</h3>
        {loading ? (
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Loading...</p>
        ) : recentReceipts.length > 0 ? (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {recentReceipts.map(receipt => (
              <div 
                key={receipt.id}
                className="flex justify-between items-center text-sm py-2 border-b"
              >
                <span className="text-gray-600">{receipt.date || 'No date'}</span>
                <span className="text-gray-800">{receipt.companyName || 'Unknown'}</span>
                <span className="text-gray-900 font-medium">
                  ${receipt.total || '0.00'}
                </span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : (
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">No recent receipts</p>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <BaseWidget
      title="Receipt Management"
      path="/receipt"
      icon={<FileText />}
      headerActions={headerActions}
      viewMode={viewMode}
    >
      {viewMode === "simple" ? simpleView : advancedView}
    </BaseWidget>
  );
};

export default ReceiptWidget;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/receipt/schemas.js
//--- File: /home/luan_ngo/web/boss/services/receipt/schemas.js ---

import { z } from 'zod';

export const ReceiptItemSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string(),
  quantity: z.number().int(),
  price: z.number(), // Ensure this remains a number (Float)
});

export const ReceiptSchema = z.object({
  date: z.string().optional().refine(val => !val || !isNaN(Date.parse(val)), {
    message: "Invalid date format",
  }),
  companyName: z.string().optional(), 
  imgName: z.string(),
  id: z.string(),
  total: z.number().optional(), // Changed from z.string()
  hst: z.number().optional(),   // Changed from z.string()
  notes: z.string().optional(),
  items: z.array(ReceiptItemSchema).optional(),
});

export const ReceiptResponseSchema = {
  type: "object",
  properties: {
    date: { type: "string" },
    companyName: { type: "string" },
    total: { type: "string" },
    hst: { type: "string" },
    items: {
      type: "array",
      items: {
        type: "object",
        properties: {
          name: { type: "string" },
          quantity: { type: "number" },
          price: { type: "number" },
        },
        required: ["name", "quantity", "price"],
      },
    },
    notes: { type: "string" },
  },
  required: ["date", "companyName", "total", "hst", "items"],
};
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/archive.js
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/routes/api/receipt/archive.js
import express from 'express';
import multer from 'multer';
import os from 'os';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import fsp from 'fs/promises';
import { execFile } from 'child_process';
import { promisify } from 'util';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import AttachmentService from '#services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js';

const router = express.Router();
const upload = multer({
  storage: multer.memoryStorage(),
  limits: {
    files: 1000,
    fileSize: 200 * 1024 * 1024,
  },
});

const execFileAsync = promisify(execFile);
const attachmentService = new AttachmentService();

const sanitizeBatchToken = (value) =>
  String(value || '')
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/gi, '-')
    .replace(/-+/g, '-')
    .replace(/^-|-$/g, '')
    .toLowerCase();

const buildExportFilename = ({ archiveAfterExport = false } = {}) => {
  const stamp = sanitizeBatchToken(new Date().toISOString());
  return `receipt-images-${stamp}${archiveAfterExport ? '-archived' : ''}.zip`;
};

const normalizeUploadedRestoreName = (value = '') => {
  const normalized = String(value || '')
    .replace(/\\/g, '/')
    .trim()
    .replace(/^\/+/, '');

  if (!normalized) {
    return '';
  }

  const segments = normalized.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  const receiptsIndex = segments.indexOf('receipts');
  const trimmed = receiptsIndex >= 0 ? segments.slice(receiptsIndex) : segments;

  return trimmed
    .filter((segment) => segment !== '.' && segment !== '..')
    .join('/');
};

const walkFiles = async (rootDir) => {
  const results = [];

  const visit = async (currentDir) => {
    const entries = await fsp.readdir(currentDir, { withFileTypes: true });
    for (const entry of entries) {
      const absolutePath = path.join(currentDir, entry.name);
      if (entry.isDirectory()) {
        await visit(absolutePath);
      } else if (entry.isFile()) {
        results.push(absolutePath);
      }
    }
  };

  await visit(rootDir);
  return results;
};

router.post('/export', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const organizationId = req.user?.organizationId || null;
  const receiptIds = Array.isArray(req.body?.receiptIds)
    ? [...new Set(req.body.receiptIds.map((id) => String(id || '').trim()).filter(Boolean))]
    : [];
  const archiveAfterExport = Boolean(req.body?.archiveAfterExport);

  if (!organizationId) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing organization context.' });
  }

  if (!receiptIds.length) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'At least one receiptId is required.' });
  }

  const batchId = sanitizeBatchToken(`receipt-archive-${Date.now()}`);
  let workingDir = null;
  let zipPath = null;

  try {
    const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        id: { in: receiptIds },
        imgName: { not: null },
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        companyName: true,
        date: true,
        imgName: true,
        imageRelativePath: true,
        imageStorageStatus: true,
        imageArchivedAt: true,
        imageStorageChecksum: true,
        imageStorageSize: true,
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });

    const exportedReceipts = [];

    for (const receipt of receipts) {
      const relativePath = attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
      if (!relativePath) {
        continue;
      }

      const absolutePath = attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
        organizationId,
        relativePath,
        receipt.imgName
      );
      const metadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(absolutePath);

      if (!metadata.exists) {
        continue;
      }

      exportedReceipts.push({
        receiptId: receipt.id,
        companyName: receipt.companyName || null,
        date: receipt.date ? new Date(receipt.date).toISOString() : null,
        imgName: receipt.imgName,
        imageRelativePath: relativePath,
        imageStorageStatus: receipt.imageStorageStatus || 'ACTIVE',
        imageArchivedAt: receipt.imageArchivedAt ? new Date(receipt.imageArchivedAt).toISOString() : null,
        checksum: metadata.checksum,
        size: metadata.size,
        absolutePath,
      });
    }

    if (!exportedReceipts.length) {
      return res.status(404).json({
        error: 'No active receipt image files were found for the requested receipts.',
      });
    }

    workingDir = await fsp.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'receipt-export-'));
    const manifestPath = path.join(workingDir, 'manifest.json');

    for (const item of exportedReceipts) {
      const targetPath = path.join(workingDir, item.imageRelativePath);
      await fsp.mkdir(path.dirname(targetPath), { recursive: true });
      await fsp.copyFile(item.absolutePath, targetPath);
    }

    await fsp.writeFile(
      manifestPath,
      JSON.stringify(
        {
          version: 1,
          kind: 'receipt-image-archive',
          organizationId,
          batchId,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          archiveAfterExport,
          receipts: exportedReceipts.map(({ absolutePath, ...rest }) => rest),
        },
        null,
        2
      ),
      'utf8'
    );

    zipPath = path.join(os.tmpdir(), `${buildExportFilename({ archiveAfterExport })}`);
    await execFileAsync('zip', ['-qr', zipPath, '.'], { cwd: workingDir });

    if (archiveAfterExport) {
      for (const item of exportedReceipts) {
        await fsp.unlink(item.absolutePath).catch(() => {});
      }

      await Promise.all(
        exportedReceipts.map((item) =>
          prisma.receipt.update({
            where: { id: item.receiptId },
            data: {
              imageRelativePath: item.imageRelativePath,
              imageStorageStatus: 'ARCHIVED',
              imageArchivedAt: new Date(),
              imageArchiveBatchId: batchId,
              imageStorageChecksum: item.checksum,
              imageStorageSize: item.size,
            },
          })
        )
      );
    } else {
      await Promise.all(
        exportedReceipts.map((item) =>
          prisma.receipt.update({
            where: { id: item.receiptId },
            data: {
              imageRelativePath: item.imageRelativePath,
              imageStorageStatus: item.imageStorageStatus || 'ACTIVE',
              imageStorageChecksum: item.checksum,
              imageStorageSize: item.size,
            },
          })
        )
      );
    }

    const downloadName = buildExportFilename({ archiveAfterExport });

    res.download(zipPath, downloadName, async (error) => {
      if (error && !res.headersSent) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to download the exported receipt archive.' });
      }

      await Promise.allSettled([
        workingDir ? fsp.rm(workingDir, { recursive: true, force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
        zipPath ? fsp.rm(zipPath, { force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
      ]);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Receipt archive export error:', error);

    await Promise.allSettled([
      workingDir ? fsp.rm(workingDir, { recursive: true, force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
      zipPath ? fsp.rm(zipPath, { force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
    ]);

    return res.status(500).json({
      error: error.message || 'Failed to export receipt images.',
    });
  }
});

router.post('/restore', authenticate, upload.array('files'), async (req, res) => {
  const organizationId = req.user?.organizationId || null;
  let zipPath = null;
  let extractDir = null;

  if (!organizationId) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing organization context.' });
  }

  const incomingFiles = Array.isArray(req.files) ? req.files : [];
  if (!incomingFiles.length) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No files were uploaded for restore.' });
  }

  try {
    let manifest = null;
    let sourceEntries = [];

    const isZipUpload =
      incomingFiles.length === 1 && /\.zip$/i.test(incomingFiles[0]?.originalname || '');

    if (isZipUpload) {
      zipPath = path.join(os.tmpdir(), `receipt-restore-${Date.now()}.zip`);
      extractDir = await fsp.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'receipt-restore-'));
      await fsp.writeFile(zipPath, incomingFiles[0].buffer);

      await execFileAsync('unzip', ['-qo', zipPath, '-d', extractDir]);

      const extractedFiles = await walkFiles(extractDir);
      sourceEntries = extractedFiles
        .map((absolutePath) => {
          const relativeName = normalizeUploadedRestoreName(path.relative(extractDir, absolutePath));
          return {
            type: 'path',
            absolutePath,
            originalName: relativeName,
          };
        })
        .filter((entry) => entry.originalName && path.basename(entry.originalName) !== 'manifest.json');

      const manifestFile = extractedFiles.find((absolutePath) => path.basename(absolutePath) === 'manifest.json');
      if (manifestFile) {
        const manifestContent = await fsp.readFile(manifestFile, 'utf8');
        manifest = JSON.parse(manifestContent);
      }
    } else {
      sourceEntries = incomingFiles.map((file) => ({
        type: 'buffer',
        buffer: file.buffer,
        originalName: normalizeUploadedRestoreName(file.originalname),
      }));
    }

    const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        imgName: { not: null },
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        imgName: true,
        imageRelativePath: true,
        imageStorageStatus: true,
      },
    });

    const receiptsById = new Map(receipts.map((receipt) => [receipt.id, receipt]));
    const receiptsByRelativePath = new Map();
    const receiptsByImgName = new Map();

    for (const receipt of receipts) {
      const relativePath = attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
      if (relativePath) {
        receiptsByRelativePath.set(relativePath, receipt);
      }

      if (receipt.imgName && !receiptsByImgName.has(receipt.imgName)) {
        receiptsByImgName.set(receipt.imgName, receipt);
      }
    }

    const manifestEntries = Array.isArray(manifest?.receipts) ? manifest.receipts : [];
    const manifestByRelativePath = new Map(
      manifestEntries
        .map((entry) => [
          attachmentService.normalizeReceiptRelativePath(entry?.imageRelativePath, entry?.imgName),
          entry,
        ])
        .filter(([key]) => !!key)
    );

    const manifestByImgName = new Map(
      manifestEntries
        .map((entry) => [entry?.imgName ? path.basename(entry.imgName) : null, entry])
        .filter(([key]) => !!key)
    );

    const report = {
      restoredCount: 0,
      alreadyPresentCount: 0,
      conflictCount: 0,
      unmatchedCount: 0,
      restored: [],
      alreadyPresent: [],
      conflicts: [],
      unmatched: [],
    };

    for (const entry of sourceEntries) {
      const normalizedName = normalizeUploadedRestoreName(entry.originalName);
      const basename = path.basename(normalizedName);
      const manifestEntry =
        manifestByRelativePath.get(normalizedName) ||
        manifestByRelativePath.get(`receipts/${basename}`) ||
        manifestByImgName.get(basename) ||
        null;

      let receipt = manifestEntry?.receiptId ? receiptsById.get(manifestEntry.receiptId) : null;
      if (!receipt && normalizedName) {
        receipt = receiptsByRelativePath.get(normalizedName) || null;
      }
      if (!receipt && basename) {
        receipt = receiptsByImgName.get(basename) || null;
      }

      if (!receipt) {
        report.unmatchedCount += 1;
        report.unmatched.push(normalizedName || basename || 'unknown-file');
        continue;
      }

      const targetRelativePath =
        attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt) ||
        attachmentService.normalizeReceiptRelativePath(
          manifestEntry?.imageRelativePath,
          receipt.imgName
        );

      const incomingBuffer =
        entry.type === 'buffer' ? entry.buffer : await fsp.readFile(entry.absolutePath);
      const incomingChecksum = attachmentService.hashBuffer(incomingBuffer);
      const targetAbsolutePath = attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
        organizationId,
        targetRelativePath,
        receipt.imgName
      );
      const existingMetadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(targetAbsolutePath);

      if (existingMetadata.exists && existingMetadata.checksum !== incomingChecksum) {
        report.conflictCount += 1;
        report.conflicts.push({
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          imgName: receipt.imgName,
          targetRelativePath,
        });
        continue;
      }

      if (!existingMetadata.exists) {
        attachmentService.writeBufferToReceiptPath(
          incomingBuffer,
          organizationId,
          targetRelativePath,
          receipt.imgName
        );
        report.restoredCount += 1;
        report.restored.push({
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          imgName: receipt.imgName,
          targetRelativePath,
        });
      } else {
        report.alreadyPresentCount += 1;
        report.alreadyPresent.push({
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          imgName: receipt.imgName,
          targetRelativePath,
        });
      }

      const finalMetadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(targetAbsolutePath);

      await prisma.receipt.update({
        where: { id: receipt.id },
        data: {
          imageRelativePath: targetRelativePath,
          imageStorageStatus: 'ACTIVE',
          imageArchivedAt: null,
          imageArchiveBatchId: null,
          imageStorageChecksum: finalMetadata.checksum,
          imageStorageSize: finalMetadata.size,
        },
      });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Receipt image restore finished.',
      report,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Receipt archive restore error:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({
      error: error.message || 'Failed to restore receipt images.',
    });
  } finally {
    await Promise.allSettled([
      zipPath ? fsp.rm(zipPath, { force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
      extractDir ? fsp.rm(extractDir, { recursive: true, force: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
    ]);
  }
});

export default router;

```
