```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/autoMatch.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipts/autoMatch.js

import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';
import ReceiptsManager from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js';
import express from 'express'; 

const prisma = new PrismaClient();
const router = express.Router();

// POST /api/receipts/autoMatch
router.post('/', async (req, res) => {
  if (req.method !== 'POST') { 
    res.setHeader('Allow', ['POST']);
    return res.status(405).end(`Method ${req.method} Not Allowed`);
  }

  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }

    const userId = session.user.id;
    const organizationId = session.user.organizationId;

    const { receiptIds } = req.body; 

    let receiptsToMatch = [];

    if (Array.isArray(receiptIds) && receiptIds.length > 0) {
      // Fetch specific receipts to match
      receiptsToMatch = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
        where: {
          id: { in: receiptIds },
          organizationId,
          matchedBankTransactionId: null,
          paymentType: null,
        },
      });
    } else {
      // Fetch all unmatched receipts
      receiptsToMatch = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId,
          matchedBankTransactionId: null,
          paymentType: null,
        },
      });
    }

    if (receiptsToMatch.length === 0) {
      return res.status(200).json({ message: 'No unmatched receipts found to auto-match.' });
    }

    // Initialize ReceiptsManager
    const receiptsManager = new ReceiptsManager();

    // Extract receipt IDs for processing
    const receiptIdsToProcess = receiptsToMatch.map(receipt => receipt.id);

    // Perform auto-match
    const result = await receiptsManager.autoMatchReceipts(organizationId, receiptIdsToProcess);

    return res.status(200).json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Auto-Match Receipts Error:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to auto-match receipts.' });
  }
});

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/autoMatchReceipt.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipts/autoMatchReceipt.js
// called from receiptsTable
import express from 'express';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';
import ReceiptsManager from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js';

const prisma = new PrismaClient();
const router = express.Router();

// POST /api/receipts/autoMatchReceipt
router.post('/', async (req, res) => {
  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    res.setHeader('Allow', ['POST']);
    return res.status(405).end(`Method ${req.method} Not Allowed`);
  }

  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }

    const userId = session.user.id;
    const organizationId = session.user.organizationId;

    const { receiptId } = req.body;

    if (!receiptId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receiptId.' });
    }

    // Initialize ReceiptsManager
    const receiptsManager = ReceiptsManager;

    // Perform auto-match
    const result = await receiptsManager.autoMatchSingleReceipt(receiptId);

    return res.status(200).json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Auto-Match Receipt Error:', error.message);
    return res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
  }
});

export default router;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/checkDuplicate.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipt/checkDuplicate.js

import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';

const router = express.Router();

// A simple fuzzy match function that normalizes and checks if one string is contained in the other.
function isFuzzyMatch(str1, str2) {
  if (!str1 || !str2) return false;
  const normalize = (s) => s.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '');
  const normalized1 = normalize(str1);
  const normalized2 = normalize(str2);
  return normalized1.includes(normalized2) || normalized2.includes(normalized1);
}

router.post(
  '/',
  authenticate,
  withHandler({
    handler: async (req, res) => {
      const { companyName, total, date } = req.body;
      if (!companyName || total == null || !date) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing required fields.' });
      }
      const receiptDate = new Date(date);
      if (isNaN(receiptDate.getTime())) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid date format.' });
      }
      // For date matching, we check for receipts on the same day.
      const startOfDay = new Date(receiptDate);
      startOfDay.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
      const endOfDay = new Date(receiptDate);
      endOfDay.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

      // Query receipts with the same total and within the same day.
      const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId: req.user.organizationId,
          total: total,
          active:true,
          date: {
            gte: startOfDay,
            lte: endOfDay,
          },
        },
      });

      // Filter results by fuzzy matching the company name.
      const duplicates = receipts.filter((r) =>
        isFuzzyMatch(r.companyName, companyName)
      );

      return res.status(200).json({ duplicates });
    },
    allowedMethods: ['POST'],
    requiredRoles: [],
  })
);

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/delete.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipts/delete.js

import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';

const router = express.Router();

// DELETE /api/receipts/delete
router.delete('/', async (req, res) => {
  if (req.method !== 'DELETE') {
    return res.status(405).end(`Method ${req.method} Not Allowed`);
  }

  try {
    const { id, imgName } = req.body;
    if (!id) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receipt ID' });
    }

    const permissions = req.user?.permissions || [];
    if (!permissions.includes('receipt:edit') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:edit permission required.' });
    }

    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { organization: true },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    if (receipt.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: Access denied.' });
    }

    // Instead of deleting the receipt and its items, update active to false.
    const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id },
      data: { active: false },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Receipt marked as inactive successfully',
      receipt: updatedReceipt,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error marking receipt as inactive:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to mark receipt as inactive.' });
  }
});

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/deleteHeic.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';

const router = express.Router();

router.delete('/', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { receiptId, heicName } = req.body;

    if (!receiptId || !heicName) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receiptId or heicName.' });
    }

    // Verify receipt belongs to user's org
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      select: { organizationId: true },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    if (receipt.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden.' });
    }

    // Prevent path traversal — only allow a plain filename
    const safeName = path.basename(heicName);
    const heicPath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', receipt.organizationId, 'receipts', safeName);

    if (fs.existsSync(heicPath)) {
      await fs.promises.unlink(heicPath);
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Original HEIC deleted.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Delete HEIC error:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete original HEIC.' });
  }
});

export default router;

```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/enhance.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/enhance.js
import express from 'express';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import { processReceiptImageAdvanced } from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptImageProcessor.js';
import AttachmentService from '#services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js';

const router = express.Router();
const attachmentService = new AttachmentService();

function getUploadDir(organizationId) {
  return path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', organizationId, 'receipts');
}

function safeFilePath(organizationId, fileName) {
  const uploadDir = path.resolve(getUploadDir(organizationId));
  const candidate = path.resolve(path.join(uploadDir, fileName || ''));
  const uploadDirWithSep = `${uploadDir}${path.sep}`;

  if (candidate === uploadDir || !candidate.startsWith(uploadDirWithSep)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid file path.');
  }

  return candidate;
}

function noteForOperation(operation) {
  switch (operation) {
    case 'auto-crop':
      return '[Auto-Cropped]';
    case 'manual-crop':
      return '[Manual Crop Saved]';
    case 'compress':
      return '[Compressed]';
    case 'bw':
      return '[Converted to B&W]';
    case 'auto':
    default:
      return '[Auto Enhanced]';
  }
}

function buildPreviewPath(organizationId, currentImgName, operation) {
  const uploadDir = getUploadDir(organizationId);
  const base = path.basename(currentImgName, path.extname(currentImgName));
  const safeOp = String(operation || 'preview').replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/gi, '-').toLowerCase();
  return path.join(uploadDir, `${base}-${safeOp}-preview-${Date.now()}.jpg`);
}

function buildSavedPath(organizationId, currentImgName) {
  const uploadDir = getUploadDir(organizationId);
  const base = path.basename(currentImgName, path.extname(currentImgName));
  return path.join(uploadDir, `${base}-edited-${Date.now()}.jpg`);
}

function getCurrentImagePath(receipt) {
  const relativePath = attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
  return attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
    receipt.organizationId,
    relativePath,
    receipt.imgName
  );
}

const enhanceHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const {
    receiptId,
    action = 'preview',
    operation = 'auto',
    crop = null,
    previewImgName = null,
  } = req.body;

  const organizationId = req.user?.organizationId || null;
  const userId = req.user?.id || req.user?.userId || null;

  if (!organizationId || !userId) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });
  }

  if (!receiptId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Receipt ID required.' });
  }

  try {
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
    });

    if (!receipt || receipt.organizationId !== organizationId) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found or unauthorized.' });
    }

    if (!receipt.imgName) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No image to edit.' });
    }

    const currentPath = getCurrentImagePath(receipt);

    if (!fs.existsSync(currentPath)) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Current receipt image is missing.' });
    }

    if (action === 'preview') {
      const previewPath = buildPreviewPath(receipt.organizationId, receipt.imgName, operation);

      const result = await processReceiptImageAdvanced(currentPath, operation, {
        outputPath: previewPath,
        crop: operation === 'manual-crop' ? crop : null,
      });

      return res.status(200).json({
        message: 'Preview created.',
        previewImgName: path.basename(previewPath),
        previewUrl: `/uploads/${receipt.organizationId}/receipts/${path.basename(previewPath)}`,
        image: {
          currentSizeBytes: fs.statSync(currentPath).size,
          previewSizeBytes: result.processedSizeBytes,
        },
      });
    }

    if (action === 'discard') {
      if (!previewImgName) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'previewImgName is required to discard.' });
      }

      const previewPath = safeFilePath(receipt.organizationId, previewImgName);

      if (fs.existsSync(previewPath)) {
        fs.unlinkSync(previewPath);
      }

      return res.status(200).json({
        message: 'Preview discarded.',
      });
    }

    if (action === 'save') {
      if (!previewImgName) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'previewImgName is required to save.' });
      }

      const previewPath = safeFilePath(receipt.organizationId, previewImgName);

      if (!fs.existsSync(previewPath)) {
        return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Preview image not found.' });
      }

      const finalPath = buildSavedPath(receipt.organizationId, receipt.imgName);
      fs.renameSync(previewPath, finalPath);

      const oldCurrentPath = currentPath;
      if (fs.existsSync(oldCurrentPath) && path.resolve(oldCurrentPath) !== path.resolve(finalPath)) {
        fs.unlinkSync(oldCurrentPath);
      }

      const finalImgName = path.basename(finalPath);
      const finalRelativePath = `receipts/${finalImgName}`;
      const finalMetadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(finalPath);

      const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
        where: { id: receiptId },
        data: {
          imgName: finalImgName,
          imageRelativePath: finalRelativePath,
          imageStorageStatus: 'ACTIVE',
          imageStorageChecksum: finalMetadata.checksum,
          imageStorageSize: finalMetadata.size,
          activeImageVariant: 'edited',
          notes: receipt.notes
            ? `${receipt.notes}\n${noteForOperation(operation)}`
            : noteForOperation(operation),
          updatedAt: new Date(),
        },
      });

      return res.status(200).json({
        message: 'Image edit saved.',
        receipt: updatedReceipt,
      });
    }

    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid enhance action.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Image edit error:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
};

router.post(
  '/',
  authenticate,
  withHandler({
    handler: enhanceHandler,
    allowedMethods: ['POST'],
    requiredRoles: [],
  })
);

export default router;

```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/findDuplicates.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/findDuplicates.js
import express from 'express';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';

const router = express.Router();

const findDuplicatesHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }
    const organizationId = session.user.organizationId;

    // Group receipts by companyName and total (only if both are not null).
    const duplicatesRaw = await prisma.$queryRaw`
      SELECT companyName, total, COUNT(*) as count
      FROM "Receipt"
      WHERE "organizationId" = ${organizationId}
        AND companyName IS NOT NULL
        AND total IS NOT NULL
        AND active = true
      GROUP BY companyName, total
      HAVING COUNT(*) > 1
      ORDER BY companyName ASC
    `;

    const duplicateGroups = [];
    // For each group, fetch detailed receipt records.
    for (const group of duplicatesRaw) {
      const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId,
          companyName: group.companyName,
          total: group.total,
          active: true,
        },
        select: {
          id: true,
          date: true,
          companyName: true,
          total: true,
        },
        orderBy: { date: 'asc' },
      });

      duplicateGroups.push({
        companyName: group.companyName,
        total: group.total,
        count: Number(group.count), // Convert BigInt count to Number
        receipts,
      });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ groups: duplicateGroups });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error finding duplicates:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

router.get(
  '/',
  authenticate,
  withHandler({
    handler: findDuplicatesHandler,
    allowedMethods: ['GET'],
    requiredRoles: [],
  })
);

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/getById.js
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/routes/api/receipt/getById.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import { getReceiptImageInfo } from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptImageProcessor.js';
import AttachmentService from '#services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js';

const router = express.Router();
const attachmentService = new AttachmentService();

router.get('/:id', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const organizationId = req.user?.organizationId || null;

  if (!organizationId) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing organization context.' });
  }

  const permissions = req.user?.permissions || [];
  if (!permissions.includes('receipt:view') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:view permission required.' });
  }

  try {
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findFirst({
      where: {
        id,
        organizationId,
      },
      include: {
        items: true,
        bankTransactions: {
          include: {
            category: true,
            source: true,
          },
        },
        organization: {
          select: { name: true },
        },
        paymentSource: true,
        user: true,
      },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    const imageRelativePath = receipt.imgName
      ? attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt)
      : null;

    let imageInfo = null;
    let imageUrl = null;
    let imageAvailable = false;
    let resolvedImageStatus = receipt.imgName
      ? receipt.imageStorageStatus || 'ACTIVE'
      : 'NONE';

    if (imageRelativePath && resolvedImageStatus !== 'ARCHIVED') {
      const imagePath = attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
        receipt.organizationId,
        imageRelativePath,
        receipt.imgName
      );
      const fileMetadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(imagePath);

      if (fileMetadata.exists) {
        imageInfo = await getReceiptImageInfo(imagePath);
        imageUrl = `/uploads/${receipt.organizationId}/${imageRelativePath}`;
        imageAvailable = true;
      } else {
        resolvedImageStatus = 'MISSING';
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json({
      ...receipt,
      imageInfo,
      imageUrl,
      imageAvailable,
      imageRelativePath,
      resolvedImageStatus,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error fetching receipt:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
});

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/importFromEmail.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import ReceiptsManager from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js';

const router = express.Router();

async function importFromEmailHandler(req, res) {
  const { emailId } = req.body;

  if (!emailId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'emailId is required.' });
  }

  const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({
    where: { id: req.user.id },
    include: {
      organization: true,
    },
  });

  if (!user) {
    return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Authenticated user not found.' });
  }

  const organizationId = user.organizationId;
  const sessionId = `session-${Date.now()}`;

  try {
    const result = await ReceiptsManager.importReceiptFromEmail(
      emailId,
      sessionId,
      organizationId,
      user
    );
    return res.status(200).json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('importReceiptFromEmail Error:', error.message);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
}

router.post(
  '/importFromEmail',
  withHandler({
    handler: importFromEmailHandler,
    allowedMethods: ['POST'],
    requiresAuth: true,
  })
);

export default router;

```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/list.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/list.js
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/routes/api/receipt/list.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import AttachmentService from '#services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js';

const router = express.Router();
const attachmentService = new AttachmentService();

const RECEIPT_LIST_SELECT = {
  id: true,
  date: true,
  createdAt: true,
  updatedAt: true,
  companyName: true,
  imgName: true,
  total: true,
  hst: true,
  notes: true,
  paymentType: true,
  imageRelativePath: true,
  imageStorageStatus: true,
  activeImageVariant: true,
  compressionStatus: true,
  active: true,
  bankTransactions: {
    select: {
      id: true,
    },
    take: 1,
  },
};

const listReceiptsHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const {
    page = '1',
    limit = '100',
    id,
    companyName,
    dateFrom,
    dateTo,
    showErrors = 'false',
    showDuplicates = 'false',
    sortKey = 'createdAt',
    sortDirection = 'desc',
    active,
    matchStatus,
    amountMin,
    amountMax,
    notes,
    imageStatus,
  } = req.query;

  const authUser = req.user || {};
  const organizationId = authUser.organizationId || null;

  if (!organizationId) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing organization context.' });
  }

  const permissions = authUser.permissions || [];
  if (!permissions.includes('receipt:view') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:view permission required.' });
  }

  const allowedSortKeys = ['id', 'date', 'createdAt', 'companyName', 'total', 'hst'];
  if (!allowedSortKeys.includes(sortKey)) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: `Invalid sortKey. Allowed values are: ${allowedSortKeys.join(', ')}`,
    });
  }

  const sortDir = sortDirection.toLowerCase() === 'asc' ? 'asc' : 'desc';
  const take = Math.min(parseInt(limit, 10) || 100, 1000);
  const currentPage = Math.max(parseInt(page, 10) || 1, 1);
  const skip = (currentPage - 1) * take;

  const whereClause = {
    organizationId,
  };

  if (active && (active === 'true' || active === 'false')) {
    whereClause.active = active === 'true';
  } else {
    whereClause.active = true;
  }

  if (id) {
    whereClause.id = { contains: id };
  }

  if (notes) {
    whereClause.notes = { contains: notes };
  }

  if (companyName) {
    whereClause.companyName = { contains: companyName };
  }

  if (dateFrom || dateTo) {
    whereClause.date = {};
    if (dateFrom) {
      const parsedDateFrom = new Date(dateFrom);
      if (Number.isNaN(parsedDateFrom.getTime())) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid dateFrom format.' });
      }
      whereClause.date.gte = parsedDateFrom;
    }
    if (dateTo) {
      const parsedDateTo = new Date(dateTo);
      if (Number.isNaN(parsedDateTo.getTime())) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid dateTo format.' });
      }
      whereClause.date.lte = parsedDateTo;
    }
  }

  if (showErrors.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
    whereClause.OR = [{ total: null }, { total: 0 }, { total: 0.0 }];
  }

  if (matchStatus && matchStatus.toLowerCase() === 'matched') {
    whereClause.bankTransactions = { some: {} };
  } else if (matchStatus && matchStatus.toLowerCase() === 'unmatched') {
    whereClause.bankTransactions = { none: {} };
  }

  if (amountMin || amountMax) {
    whereClause.total = {};
    if (amountMin) {
      const parsedMin = parseFloat(amountMin);
      if (!Number.isNaN(parsedMin)) {
        whereClause.total.gte = parsedMin;
      }
    }
    if (amountMax) {
      const parsedMax = parseFloat(amountMax);
      if (!Number.isNaN(parsedMax)) {
        whereClause.total.lte = parsedMax;
      }
    }
  }

  if (imageStatus === 'archived') {
    whereClause.imgName = { not: null };
    whereClause.imageStorageStatus = 'ARCHIVED';
  } else if (imageStatus === 'active') {
    whereClause.imgName = { not: null };
    whereClause.NOT = [{ imageStorageStatus: 'ARCHIVED' }];
  } else if (imageStatus === 'none') {
    whereClause.imgName = null;
  }

  let duplicateKeys = [];
  if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
    const duplicates = await prisma.$queryRaw`
      SELECT date, total, COUNT(*) as count
      FROM Receipt
      WHERE organizationId = ${organizationId}
      GROUP BY date, total
      HAVING COUNT(*) > 1
    `;
    duplicateKeys = duplicates.map((row) => `${row.date}-${row.total}`);
  }

  const [receiptRows, totalCount] = await Promise.all([
    prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: whereClause,
      select: RECEIPT_LIST_SELECT,
      orderBy: { [sortKey]: sortDir },
      skip,
      take,
    }),
    prisma.receipt.count({ where: whereClause }),
  ]);

  let receipts = receiptRows;

  receipts = receipts.map((receipt) => {
    const imageRelativePath = receipt.imgName
      ? attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt)
      : null;

    const bankTransactionCount = receipt.bankTransactions?.length || 0;

    return {
      ...receipt,
      bankTransactionCount,
      imageRelativePath,
      imageStorageStatus: receipt.imgName
        ? receipt.imageStorageStatus || 'ACTIVE'
        : 'NONE',
    };
  });

  if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true' && duplicateKeys.length > 0) {
    receipts = receipts.filter((receipt) => {
      const key = `${receipt.date}-${receipt.total}`;
      return duplicateKeys.includes(key);
    });
  }

  let total = totalCount;
  if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
    total = duplicateKeys.length;
  }

  res.status(200).json({
    total,
    page: currentPage,
    totalPages: Math.ceil(total / take),
    receipts,
  });
};

export default router.use(
  withHandler({
    handler: listReceiptsHandler,
    allowedMethods: ['GET'],
    requiredRoles: [],
  })
);

```
