FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/match.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/match.js
import express from 'express';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';

const router = express.Router();

const RECEIPT_HINTS_OPEN = '[receipt_hints]';
const RECEIPT_HINTS_CLOSE = '[/receipt_hints]';
const DAY_MS = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;
const DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE = 0.05;
const MATCH_APPROACHES = {
  BALANCED: 'balanced',
  CLOSEST_DATE: 'closest-date',
  CLOSEST_AMOUNT: 'closest-amount',
  TRANSACTION_DETAILS: 'transaction-details',
  BROAD_REVIEW: 'broad-review',
};
const STOP_WORDS = new Set([
  'card', 'visa', 'mastercard', 'debit', 'credit', 'pos', 'purchase', 'payment', 'online',
  'transfer', 'etransfer', 'e', 'interac', 'withdrawal', 'deposit', 'bank', 'canada', 'inc',
  'ltd', 'limited', 'corp', 'corporation', 'store', 'shop', 'the', 'and', 'for', 'from', 'to',
  'fee', 'service', 'services', 'transaction', 'recurring', 'monthly', 'preauth', 'pending', 'ref',
  'auth', 'approval', 'completed', 'merchant', 'contactless', 'tap', 'sq', 'invoice', 'receipt'
]);

// Match status constants
const MATCH_STATUS = {
  UNMATCHED: 'UNMATCHED',
  CANDIDATES_FOUND: 'CANDIDATES_FOUND',
  MATCHED_AUTO: 'MATCHED_AUTO',
  MATCHED_APPROVED: 'MATCHED_APPROVED',
  NEEDS_REVIEW: 'NEEDS_REVIEW',
  CONFLICT: 'CONFLICT',
  NO_MATCH_EXPECTED: 'NO_MATCH_EXPECTED',
};

const CANDIDATE_STATUS = {
  CANDIDATE: 'CANDIDATE',
  AUTO_MATCHED: 'AUTO_MATCHED',
  APPROVED: 'APPROVED',
  REJECTED: 'REJECTED',
  SUPERSEDED: 'SUPERSEDED',
};

const normalizePositiveTax = (value) => {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return null;
  const numericValue = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(numericValue)) return null;
  return Math.abs(Number(numericValue.toFixed(2)));
};

const normalizeText = (value) =>
  String(value || '')
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s]/g, ' ')
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
    .trim();

const tokenize = (value) => {
  const normalized = normalizeText(value);
  return normalized ? normalized.split(' ').filter(Boolean) : [];
};

const tokensMatch = (left, right) => {
  if (!left || !right) return false;
  if (left === right) return true;
  if (left.length >= 4 && right.length >= 4 && (left.includes(right) || right.includes(left))) return true;
  if (left.length >= 5 && right.length >= 5) {
    const singularLeft = left.replace(/s$/, '');
    const singularRight = right.replace(/s$/, '');
    if (singularLeft === singularRight) return true;
  }
  return false;
};

const jaccardSimilarity = (left, right) => {
  const leftTokens = tokenize(left).filter((token) => !STOP_WORDS.has(token));
  const rightTokens = tokenize(right).filter((token) => !STOP_WORDS.has(token));

  if (!leftTokens.length || !rightTokens.length) return 0;

  let intersection = 0;
  for (const token of leftTokens) {
    if (rightTokens.some((candidate) => tokensMatch(token, candidate))) intersection += 1;
  }

  const union = Math.max(leftTokens.length, rightTokens.length);
  return union ? clamp(intersection / union) : 0;
};

const daysBetween = (left, right) => {
  const leftDate = new Date(left);
  const rightDate = new Date(right);

  if (Number.isNaN(leftDate.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(rightDate.getTime())) {
    return 9999;
  }

  const ms = Math.abs(leftDate.getTime() - rightDate.getTime());
  return Math.floor(ms / DAY_MS);
};

const clamp = (value, min = 0, max = 1) => Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));

const mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes = (existingNotes, hints) => {
  const base = String(existingNotes || '')
    .replace(/\[receipt_hints\][\s\S]*?\[\/receipt_hints\]/g, '')
    .trim();

  const serialized = JSON.stringify(hints);
  return `${base}${base ? '\n' : ''}${RECEIPT_HINTS_OPEN}${serialized}${RECEIPT_HINTS_CLOSE}`.trim();
};

const extractLikelyVendorKeywords = (...values) => {
  const seen = new Set();
  const keywords = [];

  values.forEach((value) => {
    tokenize(value).forEach((token) => {
      if (token.length < 3) return;
      if (/^\d+$/.test(token)) return;
      if (STOP_WORDS.has(token)) return;
      if (seen.has(token)) return;
      seen.add(token);
      keywords.push(token);
    });
  });

  return keywords.slice(0, 5);
};

const formatEmailSearchDate = (value) => {
  const parsed = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime())) return null;
  return parsed.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
};

const buildEmailSearchSuggestion = ({ transaction, company = '', date = '' }) => {
  const effectiveDate = date || transaction?.date;
  const baseDate = new Date(effectiveDate || transaction?.date || Date.now());
  const start = new Date(baseDate.getTime() - 7 * DAY_MS);
  const end = new Date(baseDate.getTime() + 7 * DAY_MS);
  const amountAbs = Math.abs(Number(transaction?.amount || 0));
  const keywords = extractLikelyVendorKeywords(company, transaction?.description, transaction?.notes);
  const keywordQuery = keywords.length ? `(${keywords.join(' OR ')})` : '';
  const amountQuery = amountAbs > 0 ? `("${amountAbs.toFixed(2)}" OR "${Math.round(amountAbs)}")` : '';
  const queryParts = [
    'has:attachment',
    '(receipt OR invoice OR order OR payment OR statement)',
    keywordQuery,
    amountQuery,
  ].filter(Boolean);

  return {
    query: queryParts.join(' '),
    startDate: formatEmailSearchDate(start),
    endDate: formatEmailSearchDate(end),
    keywords,
    reason: keywords.length
      ? 'Uses likely vendor keywords from the transaction description and a date window around the charge.'
      : 'Uses the amount and a date window around the charge.',
  };
};

const getConfidenceLabel = (score) => {
  if (score >= 0.92) return 'VERY_HIGH';
  if (score >= 0.80) return 'HIGH';
  if (score >= 0.65) return 'MEDIUM';
  return 'LOW';
};

const getConfidenceLabelDisplay = (score) => {
  if (score >= 0.92) return 'Very High';
  if (score >= 0.80) return 'High';
  if (score >= 0.65) return 'Medium';
  return 'Low';
};

const normalizeMatchApproach = (value) => {
  const normalized = String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  return Object.values(MATCH_APPROACHES).includes(normalized) ? normalized : MATCH_APPROACHES.BALANCED;
};

const getReceiptMatchApproachConfig = (approach, range, broadSearch) => {
  const tolerancePct = Math.max(Number(range || DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE), 0.005);
  const config = {
    dayWindow: broadSearch ? 30 : 14,
    tolerancePct: broadSearch ? Math.max(tolerancePct, 0.5) : tolerancePct,
    minimumTolerance: broadSearch ? 10 : 1.5,
    sortMode: MATCH_APPROACHES.BALANCED,
    label: 'Balanced',
  };

  switch (approach) {
    case MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_DATE:
      return {
        ...config,
        dayWindow: 4,
        tolerancePct: 1,
        minimumTolerance: 25,
        sortMode: MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_DATE,
        label: 'Closest date',
      };
    case MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_AMOUNT:
      return {
        ...config,
        dayWindow: 90,
        tolerancePct: Math.max(tolerancePct, 0.75),
        minimumTolerance: 25,
        sortMode: MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_AMOUNT,
        label: 'Closest amount',
      };
    case MATCH_APPROACHES.TRANSACTION_DETAILS:
      return {
        ...config,
        dayWindow: 60,
        tolerancePct: Math.max(tolerancePct, 0.75),
        minimumTolerance: 25,
        sortMode: MATCH_APPROACHES.TRANSACTION_DETAILS,
        label: 'Transaction details',
      };
    case MATCH_APPROACHES.BROAD_REVIEW:
      return {
        ...config,
        dayWindow: 90,
        tolerancePct: Math.max(tolerancePct, 1),
        minimumTolerance: 50,
        sortMode: MATCH_APPROACHES.BROAD_REVIEW,
        label: 'Broad review',
      };
    default:
      return config;
  }
};

const buildMatchReasons = ({ amountDelta, dateDeltaDays, vendorScore, descriptionScore, keywordScore, taxScore }) => {
  const reasons = [];
  if (amountDelta <= 0.01) reasons.push('Exact amount match');
  else if (amountDelta <= 1) reasons.push(`Amount is within $${amountDelta.toFixed(2)}`);
  if (dateDeltaDays <= 1) reasons.push('Date is within 1 day');
  else if (dateDeltaDays <= 3) reasons.push(`Date is within ${dateDeltaDays} days`);
  if (vendorScore >= 0.72) reasons.push('Vendor name closely matches the transaction description');
  if (descriptionScore >= 0.55) reasons.push('Receipt text lines up with the transaction description');
  if (keywordScore >= 0.55) reasons.push('Description keywords appear in the receipt');
  if (taxScore >= 0.9) reasons.push('Receipt tax looks consistent with the transaction');
  return reasons.slice(0, 4);
};

const buildReceiptHints = ({ receipt, transaction = null, matchConfidence = null, scoreBreakdown = null, needsReview = false }) => ({
  normalizedVendor: normalizeText(receipt?.companyName),
  extractedTax: normalizePositiveTax(receipt?.hst),
  taxConfidence: receipt?.hst != null ? 'RECEIPT_MATCHED' : 'UNKNOWN',
  suggestedExpenseAccount: transaction?.category?.code || null,
  suggestedStatementLine: transaction?.category?.statementLine || null,
  matchedReceiptId: receipt?.id || null,
  matchedTransactionId: transaction?.id || null,
  matchConfidence: matchConfidence == null ? null : Number(matchConfidence.toFixed(4)),
  needsReview,
  sourceType: transaction?.source?.type || null,
  scoreBreakdown,
});

async function countPriorVendorMatches(organizationId, vendorProbe) {
  if (!vendorProbe) return 0;
  try {
    return prisma.bankTransaction.count({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        receiptId: { not: null },
        OR: [
          { description: { contains: vendorProbe } },
          { notes: { contains: vendorProbe } },
        ],
      },
    });
  } catch {
    return 0;
  }
}

function scoreReceiptTransactionPair({ receipt, transaction, toleranceAmount = 1, priorVendorMatches = 0 }) {
  const receiptTotal = Math.abs(Number(receipt?.total || 0));
  const txAmount = Math.abs(Number(transaction?.amount || 0));
  const amountDelta = Math.abs(txAmount - receiptTotal);
  const dateDeltaDays = daysBetween(transaction?.date, receipt?.date);
  const exactAmount = amountDelta < 0.01;
  const nearAmount = amountDelta <= 1;
  const amountScore = exactAmount ? 1 : nearAmount ? 0.96 : clamp(1 - amountDelta / Math.max(toleranceAmount, 0.01));
  const dateScore = clamp(1 - dateDeltaDays / 14);

  const receiptNarrative = [receipt?.companyName, receipt?.text, receipt?.notes].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
  const transactionNarrative = [transaction?.description, transaction?.notes].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
  const vendorScore = jaccardSimilarity(receipt?.companyName, transactionNarrative);
  const descriptionScore = jaccardSimilarity(receiptNarrative, transaction?.description);

  const txKeywords = extractLikelyVendorKeywords(transaction?.description, transaction?.notes);
  const receiptKeywordScore = txKeywords.length
    ? txKeywords.filter((keyword) => normalizeText(receiptNarrative).includes(keyword)).length / txKeywords.length
    : 0;

  const txTax = normalizePositiveTax(transaction?.taxes);
  const receiptTax = normalizePositiveTax(receipt?.hst ?? receipt?.taxes);
  const taxScore = txTax == null || receiptTax == null
    ? 0.4
    : clamp(1 - Math.abs(txTax - receiptTax) / Math.max(Math.abs(txTax), 1));

  const sourceTypeScore = transaction?.source?.type ? 1 : 0.6;
  const priorMatchScore = priorVendorMatches > 0 ? 1 : 0;
  const exactDate = dateDeltaDays <= 2;

  const weightedScore = clamp(
    amountScore * 0.36 +
      dateScore * 0.16 +
      vendorScore * 0.2 +
      descriptionScore * 0.1 +
      receiptKeywordScore * 0.08 +
      taxScore * 0.05 +
      sourceTypeScore * 0.03 +
      priorMatchScore * 0.03 +
      (exactAmount ? 0.03 : 0) +
      (exactAmount && exactDate ? 0.03 : 0)
  );

  return {
    matchScore: Number(weightedScore.toFixed(4)),
    confidenceLabel: getConfidenceLabelDisplay(weightedScore),
    exactMatch: exactAmount && exactDate,
    matchReasons: buildMatchReasons({
      amountDelta,
      dateDeltaDays,
      vendorScore,
      descriptionScore,
      keywordScore: receiptKeywordScore,
      taxScore,
    }),
    scoreBreakdown: {
      amountScore: Number(amountScore.toFixed(4)),
      dateScore: Number(dateScore.toFixed(4)),
      vendorScore: Number(vendorScore.toFixed(4)),
      descriptionScore: Number(descriptionScore.toFixed(4)),
      keywordScore: Number(receiptKeywordScore.toFixed(4)),
      taxScore: Number(taxScore.toFixed(4)),
      sourceTypeScore: Number(sourceTypeScore.toFixed(4)),
      priorMatchScore: Number(priorMatchScore.toFixed(4)),
      amountDelta: Number(amountDelta.toFixed(2)),
      dateDeltaDays,
      exactAmount,
      exactDate,
    },
  };
}

async function findCandidateTransactionsForReceipt(organizationId, receipt, range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE, options = {}) {
  const receiptTotal = Math.abs(Number(receipt?.total || 0));
  const receiptDate = new Date(receipt?.date);

  if (!receiptTotal || Number.isNaN(receiptDate.getTime())) {
    return [];
  }

  const broadSearch = Boolean(options.broadSearch);
  const approach = normalizeMatchApproach(options.approach);
  const approachConfig = getReceiptMatchApproachConfig(approach, range, broadSearch);
  const dayWindow = approachConfig.dayWindow;
  const dateFrom = new Date(receiptDate.getTime() - dayWindow * DAY_MS);
  dateFrom.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const dateTo = new Date(receiptDate.getTime() + dayWindow * DAY_MS);
  dateTo.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

  const toleranceAmount = Math.max(receiptTotal * approachConfig.tolerancePct, approachConfig.minimumTolerance);
  const amountMin = receiptTotal - toleranceAmount;
  const amountMax = receiptTotal + toleranceAmount;

  const vendorProbe = extractLikelyVendorKeywords(receipt.companyName)[0] || null;
  const priorVendorMatches = await countPriorVendorMatches(organizationId, vendorProbe);

  const amountWhere = {
    lt: 0,
    gte: -amountMax,
  };
  if (amountMin > 0) {
    amountWhere.lte = -amountMin;
  }

  const matchingTransactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
    where: {
      organizationId,
      receiptId: null,
      amount: amountWhere,
      date: { gte: dateFrom, lte: dateTo },
    },
    include: {
      source: true,
      category: true,
      receipt: true,
    },
    orderBy: [{ date: 'asc' }, { amount: 'asc' }],
    take: 50,
  });

  const scored = matchingTransactions
    .map((transaction) => ({
      ...transaction,
      matchApproach: approach,
      matchApproachLabel: approachConfig.label,
      ...scoreReceiptTransactionPair({ receipt, transaction, toleranceAmount, priorVendorMatches }),
    }));

  return scored.sort((a, b) => {
    if (approachConfig.sortMode === MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_DATE) {
      const dateDiff = (b.scoreBreakdown?.dateScore || 0) - (a.scoreBreakdown?.dateScore || 0);
      if (dateDiff !== 0) return dateDiff;
      const amountDiff = (b.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0) - (a.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0);
      if (amountDiff !== 0) return amountDiff;
    }
    if (approachConfig.sortMode === MATCH_APPROACHES.CLOSEST_AMOUNT) {
      const amountDiff = (b.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0) - (a.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0);
      if (amountDiff !== 0) return amountDiff;
      const dateDiff = (b.scoreBreakdown?.dateScore || 0) - (a.scoreBreakdown?.dateScore || 0);
      if (dateDiff !== 0) return dateDiff;
    }
    if (approachConfig.sortMode === MATCH_APPROACHES.TRANSACTION_DETAILS) {
      const leftDetails = (a.scoreBreakdown?.vendorScore || 0) + (a.scoreBreakdown?.descriptionScore || 0) + (a.scoreBreakdown?.keywordScore || 0);
      const rightDetails = (b.scoreBreakdown?.vendorScore || 0) + (b.scoreBreakdown?.descriptionScore || 0) + (b.scoreBreakdown?.keywordScore || 0);
      if (rightDetails !== leftDetails) return rightDetails - leftDetails;
      const amountDiff = (b.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0) - (a.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore || 0);
      if (amountDiff !== 0) return amountDiff;
    }
    if (b.exactMatch !== a.exactMatch) return Number(b.exactMatch) - Number(a.exactMatch);
    if (b.matchScore !== a.matchScore) return b.matchScore - a.matchScore;
    return new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date);
  });
}

async function findCandidateReceiptsForTransaction(organizationId, transaction, options = {}) {
  const txAmount = Math.abs(Number(options.transactionAmount ?? transaction?.amount ?? 0));
  const txDate = new Date(options.transactionDate || transaction?.date);

  if (!txAmount || Number.isNaN(txDate.getTime())) {
    return [];
  }

  const broadSearch = Boolean(options.broadSearch);
  const dayWindow = broadSearch ? 30 : 14;
  const dateFrom = new Date(txDate.getTime() - dayWindow * DAY_MS);
  dateFrom.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  const dateTo = new Date(txDate.getTime() + dayWindow * DAY_MS);
  dateTo.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

  const tolerancePct = Math.max(Number(options.range || DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE), 0.005);
  const toleranceAmount = Math.max(txAmount * (broadSearch ? Math.max(tolerancePct, 0.5) : tolerancePct), broadSearch ? 10 : 1.5);
  const amountMin = txAmount - toleranceAmount;
  const amountMax = txAmount + toleranceAmount;

  const searchCompany = String(options.company || '').trim();
  const searchDate = options.date ? new Date(options.date) : null;
  const normalizedSearchVendor = normalizeText(searchCompany || transaction?.description);
  const vendorProbe = extractLikelyVendorKeywords(searchCompany, transaction?.description)[0] || null;
  const priorVendorMatches = await countPriorVendorMatches(organizationId, vendorProbe);

  const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
    where: {
      organizationId,
      paymentType: null,
      total: { gte: amountMin, lte: amountMax },
      date: {
        gte: searchDate && !Number.isNaN(searchDate.getTime()) ? new Date(searchDate.getTime() - (broadSearch ? 14 : 3) * DAY_MS) : dateFrom,
        lte: searchDate && !Number.isNaN(searchDate.getTime()) ? new Date(searchDate.getTime() + (broadSearch ? 14 : 3) * DAY_MS) : dateTo,
      },
      ...(searchCompany
        ? {
            OR: [
              { companyName: { contains: searchCompany } },
              { text: { contains: searchCompany } },
              { notes: { contains: searchCompany } },
            ],
          }
        : {}),
    },
    orderBy: [{ date: 'asc' }, { total: 'asc' }],
    take: 50,
  });

  const scored = receipts
    .map((receipt) => ({
      ...receipt,
      ...scoreReceiptTransactionPair({
        receipt,
        transaction: {
          ...transaction,
          amount: options.transactionAmount ?? transaction?.amount,
          date: options.transactionDate || transaction?.date,
          description: searchCompany || transaction?.description,
        },
        toleranceAmount,
        priorVendorMatches,
      }),
    }))
    .sort((a, b) => {
      if (b.exactMatch !== a.exactMatch) return Number(b.exactMatch) - Number(a.exactMatch);
      if (b.matchScore !== a.matchScore) return b.matchScore - a.matchScore;
      const aVendor = jaccardSimilarity(a.companyName, normalizedSearchVendor);
      const bVendor = jaccardSimilarity(b.companyName, normalizedSearchVendor);
      if (bVendor !== aVendor) return bVendor - aVendor;
      return new Date(a.date) - new Date(b.date);
    });

  return scored;
}

// Persist candidate records so the queue UI can show them without rescoring
async function storeCandidates({ organizationId, bankTransactionId, candidates }) {
  if (!candidates.length) return;

  // Remove stale CANDIDATE rows for this transaction (keep APPROVED/REJECTED)
  await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.deleteMany({
    where: {
      organizationId,
      bankTransactionId,
      status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE,
    },
  });

  await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.createMany({
    data: candidates.map((c) => ({
      organizationId,
      receiptId: c.id,
      bankTransactionId,
      status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE,
      confidence: c.matchScore,
      confidenceLabel: getConfidenceLabel(c.matchScore),
      amountScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.amountScore ?? 0,
      dateScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.dateScore ?? 0,
      vendorScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.vendorScore ?? 0,
      descriptionScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.descriptionScore ?? 0,
      keywordScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.keywordScore ?? 0,
      taxScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.taxScore ?? 0,
      sourceScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.sourceTypeScore ?? 0,
      priorMatchScore: c.scoreBreakdown?.priorMatchScore ?? 0,
      amountDelta: c.scoreBreakdown?.amountDelta ?? null,
      dateDeltaDays: c.scoreBreakdown?.dateDeltaDays ?? null,
      matchReasons: c.matchReasons ?? [],
    })),
    skipDuplicates: true,
  });
}

async function applyReceiptMatch({ organizationId, receiptId, transactionId, matchConfidence, scoreBreakdown, status = CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED, reviewedBy = null }) {
  const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({ where: { id: receiptId } });
  const transaction = await prisma.bankTransaction.findUnique({
    where: { id: Number(transactionId) },
    include: { source: true, category: true, receipt: true },
  });

  if (!receipt) throw new Error('Receipt not found.');
  if (!transaction) throw new Error('Transaction not found.');
  if (receipt.organizationId !== organizationId || transaction.organizationId !== organizationId) {
    throw new Error('Forbidden: Not your organization.');
  }

  const hints = buildReceiptHints({
    receipt,
    transaction,
    matchConfidence,
    scoreBreakdown,
    needsReview: matchConfidence < 0.9,
  });

  const txMatchStatus = status === CANDIDATE_STATUS.AUTO_MATCHED
    ? MATCH_STATUS.MATCHED_AUTO
    : MATCH_STATUS.MATCHED_APPROVED;

  const [updatedReceipt, updatedTransaction] = await prisma.$transaction([
    prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receipt.id },
      data: {
        paymentType: 'bank',
        notes: mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(receipt.notes, hints),
      },
    }),
    prisma.bankTransaction.update({
      where: { id: transaction.id },
      data: {
        receiptId: receipt.id,
        taxes: receipt.hst == null ? transaction.taxes : normalizePositiveTax(receipt.hst),
        notes: mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(transaction.notes, hints),
        receiptMatchStatus: txMatchStatus,
        receiptMatchConfidence: matchConfidence,
        receiptMatchReviewed: status === CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED,
        receiptMatchReviewedAt: status === CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED ? new Date() : null,
        receiptMatchReviewedBy: reviewedBy,
      },
      include: {
        receipt: true,
        source: true,
        category: true,
      },
    }),
  ]);

  // Update the winning candidate record and supersede the rest
  await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.updateMany({
    where: { organizationId, bankTransactionId: transaction.id, receiptId },
    data: {
      status,
      reviewedAt: new Date(),
      reviewedBy,
    },
  });
  await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.updateMany({
    where: {
      organizationId,
      bankTransactionId: transaction.id,
      receiptId: { not: receiptId },
      status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE,
    },
    data: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.SUPERSEDED },
  });

  return {
    message: 'Receipt matched successfully.',
    receipt: updatedReceipt,
    transaction: updatedTransaction,
    hints,
  };
}

// ---------- HTTP Handlers ----------

const fetchMatchingTransactionsHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }

    const {
      receiptId,
      transactionId,
      range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE,
      company = '',
      date = '',
      transactionDate = '',
      transactionAmount = null,
      broadSearch = false,
      approach = MATCH_APPROACHES.BALANCED,
    } = req.body || {};

    if (receiptId) {
      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
        where: { id: receiptId },
        select: {
          id: true, date: true, total: true, companyName: true, text: true, notes: true, hst: true, organizationId: true,
        },
      });

      if (!receipt) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
      if (receipt.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden.' });
      if (!receipt.date || receipt.total == null) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Receipt must have a valid date and total.' });

      const selectedApproach = normalizeMatchApproach(approach);
      const transactions = await findCandidateTransactionsForReceipt(session.user.organizationId, receipt, range, {
        broadSearch,
        approach: selectedApproach,
      });
      return res.status(200).json({
        mode: 'receiptToTransaction',
        approach: selectedApproach,
        transactions,
      });
    }

    if (transactionId) {
      const transaction = await prisma.bankTransaction.findFirst({
        where: { id: Number(transactionId), organizationId: session.user.organizationId },
        include: { source: true, category: true, receipt: true },
      });

      if (!transaction) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Transaction not found.' });

      const receipts = await findCandidateReceiptsForTransaction(session.user.organizationId, transaction, {
        range, company, date, transactionDate, transactionAmount, broadSearch,
      });

      // Persist candidates so the queue can show them
      if (receipts.length > 0 && !transaction.receiptId) {
        await storeCandidates({
          organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
          bankTransactionId: transaction.id,
          candidates: receipts.slice(0, 10),
        });
        const bestScore = receipts[0]?.matchScore ?? 0;
        const newStatus = receipts.length >= 2 && Math.abs(receipts[0].matchScore - receipts[1].matchScore) < 0.05
          ? MATCH_STATUS.CONFLICT
          : bestScore >= 0.85
            ? MATCH_STATUS.CANDIDATES_FOUND
            : MATCH_STATUS.NEEDS_REVIEW;

        await prisma.bankTransaction.update({
          where: { id: transaction.id },
          data: { receiptMatchStatus: newStatus },
        });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({
        mode: 'transactionToReceipt',
        receipts,
        emailSearchSuggestion: buildEmailSearchSuggestion({ transaction, company, date: transactionDate || date || transaction.date }),
      });
    }

    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Either receiptId or transactionId is required.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in fetchMatchingTransactionsHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

const matchReceiptToTransactionHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }

    const { receiptId, type, transactionId } = req.body;
    if (!receiptId || !type || (type === 'bank' && !transactionId)) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing required fields.' });
    }

    if (type === 'bank') {
      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
        where: { id: receiptId },
        select: { id: true, date: true, total: true, companyName: true, text: true, notes: true, hst: true, organizationId: true },
      });

      if (!receipt) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });

      const candidates = await findCandidateTransactionsForReceipt(session.user.organizationId, receipt, DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE);
      const selected = candidates.find((tx) => tx.id === Number(transactionId));

      const result = await applyReceiptMatch({
        organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
        receiptId,
        transactionId,
        matchConfidence: selected?.matchScore ?? 1,
        scoreBreakdown: selected?.scoreBreakdown ?? null,
        status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED,
        reviewedBy: session.user.id,
      });

      return res.status(200).json(result);
    }

    if (type === 'cash') {
      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({ where: { id: receiptId } });
      if (!receipt) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
      if (receipt.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden.' });

      const hints = buildReceiptHints({ receipt, transaction: null, matchConfidence: null, scoreBreakdown: null, needsReview: false });

      const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
        where: { id: receiptId },
        data: { paymentType: 'cash', notes: mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(receipt.notes, hints) },
      });

      return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Receipt marked as cash successfully.', receipt: updatedReceipt, hints });
    }

    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid type provided.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in matchReceiptToTransactionHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// Approve a stored candidate (from the queue UI)
const approveCandidateHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { candidateId } = req.body;
    if (!candidateId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing candidateId.' });

    const candidate = await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.findUnique({ where: { id: candidateId } });
    if (!candidate || candidate.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Candidate not found.' });
    }
    if (candidate.status === CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Candidate already approved.' });
    }

    const result = await applyReceiptMatch({
      organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
      receiptId: candidate.receiptId,
      transactionId: candidate.bankTransactionId,
      matchConfidence: candidate.confidence,
      scoreBreakdown: {
        amountScore: candidate.amountScore,
        dateScore: candidate.dateScore,
        vendorScore: candidate.vendorScore,
        descriptionScore: candidate.descriptionScore,
        keywordScore: candidate.keywordScore,
        taxScore: candidate.taxScore,
        sourceTypeScore: candidate.sourceScore,
        priorMatchScore: candidate.priorMatchScore,
        amountDelta: candidate.amountDelta,
        dateDeltaDays: candidate.dateDeltaDays,
      },
      status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED,
      reviewedBy: session.user.id,
    });

    return res.status(200).json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in approveCandidateHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: error.message || 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// Reject a candidate
const rejectCandidateHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { candidateId } = req.body;
    if (!candidateId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing candidateId.' });

    const candidate = await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.findUnique({ where: { id: candidateId } });
    if (!candidate || candidate.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Candidate not found.' });
    }

    await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.update({
      where: { id: candidateId },
      data: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.REJECTED, reviewedAt: new Date(), reviewedBy: session.user.id },
    });

    // If all candidates for this transaction are rejected, update status
    const remaining = await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.count({
      where: { bankTransactionId: candidate.bankTransactionId, status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE },
    });
    if (remaining === 0) {
      await prisma.bankTransaction.update({
        where: { id: candidate.bankTransactionId },
        data: { receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.UNMATCHED },
      });
    }

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Candidate rejected.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in rejectCandidateHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// Mark a transaction as not needing a receipt
const noReceiptRequiredHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { transactionId } = req.body;
    if (!transactionId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing transactionId.' });

    const tx = await prisma.bankTransaction.findFirst({
      where: { id: Number(transactionId), organizationId: session.user.organizationId },
    });
    if (!tx) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Transaction not found.' });

    await prisma.bankTransaction.update({
      where: { id: tx.id },
      data: {
        receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.NO_MATCH_EXPECTED,
        receiptMatchReviewed: true,
        receiptMatchReviewedAt: new Date(),
        receiptMatchReviewedBy: session.user.id,
      },
    });
    await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.updateMany({
      where: { bankTransactionId: tx.id, status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE },
      data: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.SUPERSEDED },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Transaction marked as no receipt required.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in noReceiptRequiredHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// Get the matching queue for the org
const getMatchQueueHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { organizationId } = session.user;
    const limit = Math.min(Number(req.query.limit) || 50, 200);

    // Transactions with stored candidates (CANDIDATES_FOUND / NEEDS_REVIEW / CONFLICT)
    const candidateTransactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        receiptId: null,
        receiptMatchStatus: { in: [MATCH_STATUS.CANDIDATES_FOUND, MATCH_STATUS.NEEDS_REVIEW, MATCH_STATUS.CONFLICT] },
      },
      include: {
        source: true,
        category: true,
        matchCandidates: {
          where: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE },
          include: { receipt: true },
          orderBy: { confidence: 'desc' },
          take: 3,
        },
      },
      orderBy: [{ receiptMatchConfidence: 'desc' }, { date: 'desc' }],
      take: limit,
    });

    // Unmatched expense transactions (amount < 0, no receipt, not explicitly excluded)
    const unmatchedTransactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        receiptId: null,
        amount: { lt: 0 },
        receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.UNMATCHED,
      },
      include: { source: true, category: true },
      orderBy: { date: 'desc' },
      take: limit,
    });

    // Unmatched receipts (active, no payment method, and not linked to a bank transaction)
    const unmatchedReceipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        active: true,
        paymentType: null,
        bankTransactions: { none: {} },
      },
      orderBy: { date: 'desc' },
      take: limit,
    });

    // High-confidence auto-matched (not yet user-reviewed)
    const autoMatched = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.MATCHED_AUTO,
        receiptMatchReviewed: false,
      },
      include: {
        source: true,
        category: true,
        receipt: true,
        matchCandidates: {
          where: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.AUTO_MATCHED },
          take: 1,
        },
      },
      orderBy: [{ receiptMatchConfidence: 'desc' }, { date: 'desc' }],
      take: limit,
    });

    // Conflicts
    const conflictTransactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: { organizationId, receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.CONFLICT, receiptId: null },
      include: {
        source: true,
        category: true,
        matchCandidates: {
          where: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE },
          include: { receipt: true },
          orderBy: { confidence: 'desc' },
          take: 5,
        },
      },
      orderBy: { date: 'desc' },
      take: limit,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({
      candidateTransactions,
      unmatchedTransactions,
      unmatchedReceipts,
      autoMatched,
      conflictTransactions,
      summary: {
        candidatesFound: candidateTransactions.length,
        unmatched: unmatchedTransactions.length,
        unmatchedReceipts: unmatchedReceipts.length,
        autoMatchedPendingReview: autoMatched.length,
        conflicts: conflictTransactions.length,
      },
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in getMatchQueueHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// Batch approve all CANDIDATE entries that are VERY_HIGH confidence
const batchApproveHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { organizationId } = session.user;

    const highConfidenceCandidates = await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE,
        confidenceLabel: 'VERY_HIGH',
      },
      orderBy: { confidence: 'desc' },
      take: 100,
    });

    const results = { approved: [], skipped: [], errors: [] };

    // Group by transaction so we only take the top candidate per tx
    const byTx = new Map();
    for (const c of highConfidenceCandidates) {
      if (!byTx.has(c.bankTransactionId)) byTx.set(c.bankTransactionId, c);
    }

    for (const [, candidate] of byTx) {
      try {
        // Skip if tx already matched
        const tx = await prisma.bankTransaction.findUnique({ where: { id: candidate.bankTransactionId } });
        if (!tx || tx.receiptId) {
          results.skipped.push({ candidateId: candidate.id, reason: 'Transaction already matched.' });
          continue;
        }

        const matched = await applyReceiptMatch({
          organizationId,
          receiptId: candidate.receiptId,
          transactionId: candidate.bankTransactionId,
          matchConfidence: candidate.confidence,
          scoreBreakdown: {
            amountScore: candidate.amountScore,
            dateScore: candidate.dateScore,
            vendorScore: candidate.vendorScore,
            descriptionScore: candidate.descriptionScore,
            keywordScore: candidate.keywordScore,
            taxScore: candidate.taxScore,
            sourceTypeScore: candidate.sourceScore,
            priorMatchScore: candidate.priorMatchScore,
            amountDelta: candidate.amountDelta,
            dateDeltaDays: candidate.dateDeltaDays,
          },
          status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.APPROVED,
          reviewedBy: session.user.id,
        });

        results.approved.push({
          candidateId: candidate.id,
          transactionId: candidate.bankTransactionId,
          receiptId: candidate.receiptId,
          confidence: candidate.confidence,
          transaction: matched.transaction,
        });
      } catch (err) {
        results.errors.push({ candidateId: candidate.id, error: err.message });
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json(results);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in batchApproveHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

const refreshCandidatesHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { transactionIds = [], range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE, broadSearch = false } = req.body || {};
    const ids = Array.isArray(transactionIds) ? transactionIds.map((id) => Number(id)).filter(Number.isFinite) : [];
    if (!ids.length) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'transactionIds must be a non-empty array.' });

    const transactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
        id: { in: ids },
        receiptId: null,
      },
      include: { source: true, category: true, receipt: true },
    });

    const results = { refreshed: [], skipped: [], errors: [] };

    for (const tx of transactions) {
      try {
        if (Number(tx.amount || 0) >= 0) {
          results.skipped.push({ transactionId: tx.id, reason: 'Only expense transactions are matched to receipts.' });
          continue;
        }

        const candidates = await findCandidateReceiptsForTransaction(session.user.organizationId, tx, { range, broadSearch });
        if (candidates.length > 0) {
          await storeCandidates({
            organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
            bankTransactionId: tx.id,
            candidates: candidates.slice(0, 10),
          });
        }

        const best = candidates[0];
        const newStatus = candidates.length === 0
          ? MATCH_STATUS.UNMATCHED
          : candidates.length >= 2 && Math.abs(candidates[0].matchScore - candidates[1].matchScore) < 0.05
            ? MATCH_STATUS.CONFLICT
            : best?.matchScore >= 0.85
              ? MATCH_STATUS.CANDIDATES_FOUND
              : MATCH_STATUS.NEEDS_REVIEW;

        await prisma.bankTransaction.update({
          where: { id: tx.id },
          data: { receiptMatchStatus: newStatus, receiptMatchConfidence: best?.matchScore ?? null },
        });

        results.refreshed.push({
          transactionId: tx.id,
          candidateCount: candidates.length,
          bestScore: best?.matchScore ?? null,
          status: newStatus,
          candidates: candidates.slice(0, 3).map((item) => ({
            id: item.id,
            companyName: item.companyName,
            total: item.total,
            date: item.date,
            matchScore: item.matchScore,
            confidenceLabel: item.confidenceLabel,
            matchReasons: item.matchReasons,
            scoreBreakdown: item.scoreBreakdown,
          })),
          emailSearchSuggestion: candidates.length ? null : buildEmailSearchSuggestion({ transaction: tx }),
        });
      } catch (err) {
        results.errors.push({ transactionId: tx.id, error: err.message });
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json(results);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in refreshCandidatesHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

const autoMatchSingleReceiptHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { receiptId, range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE } = req.body;
    if (!receiptId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receiptId.' });

    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      select: { id: true, date: true, total: true, companyName: true, text: true, notes: true, hst: true, organizationId: true, paymentType: true },
    });

    if (!receipt) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    if (receipt.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden.' });
    if (receipt.paymentType === 'bank') {
      return res.status(200).json({ matched: false, reason: 'Receipt is already matched to a bank transaction.' });
    }

    const candidates = await findCandidateTransactionsForReceipt(session.user.organizationId, receipt, range);
    const best = candidates[0];
    const second = candidates[1];

    const highConfidence =
      best &&
      (best.exactMatch ||
        (best.matchScore >= 0.93 &&
          best.scoreBreakdown.amountScore >= 0.95 &&
          (!second || best.matchScore - second.matchScore >= 0.15)));

    if (!highConfidence) {
      return res.status(200).json({ matched: false, reason: 'No high-confidence routine match found.', candidates: candidates.slice(0, 5) });
    }

    const result = await applyReceiptMatch({
      organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
      receiptId: receipt.id,
      transactionId: best.id,
      matchConfidence: best.matchScore,
      scoreBreakdown: best.scoreBreakdown,
      status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.AUTO_MATCHED,
      reviewedBy: null,
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ matched: true, ...result });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in autoMatchSingleReceiptHandler:', error);
    return res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
  }
};

const autoMatchBatchReceiptsHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { receiptIds = [], range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE } = req.body;
    const ids = Array.isArray(receiptIds) ? receiptIds : [];

    const receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
        ...(ids.length ? { id: { in: ids } } : { paymentType: null }),
      },
      select: { id: true, date: true, total: true, companyName: true, text: true, notes: true, hst: true, organizationId: true, paymentType: true },
      orderBy: { date: 'asc' },
    });

    const result = { matched: [], skipped: [], errors: [] };

    for (const receipt of receipts) {
      try {
        if (receipt.paymentType === 'bank') {
          result.skipped.push({ receiptId: receipt.id, reason: 'Already matched.' });
          continue;
        }

        const candidates = await findCandidateTransactionsForReceipt(session.user.organizationId, receipt, range);
        const best = candidates[0];
        const second = candidates[1];

        const highConfidence =
          best &&
          (best.exactMatch ||
            (best.matchScore >= 0.93 &&
              best.scoreBreakdown.amountScore >= 0.95 &&
              (!second || best.matchScore - second.matchScore >= 0.15)));

        if (!highConfidence) {
          result.skipped.push({
            receiptId: receipt.id,
            reason: 'No high-confidence routine match found.',
            candidates: candidates.slice(0, 3).map((item) => ({
              id: item.id, matchScore: item.matchScore, confidenceLabel: item.confidenceLabel, description: item.description, amount: item.amount, date: item.date,
            })),
          });
          continue;
        }

        const matched = await applyReceiptMatch({
          organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
          receiptId: receipt.id,
          transactionId: best.id,
          matchConfidence: best.matchScore,
          scoreBreakdown: best.scoreBreakdown,
          status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.AUTO_MATCHED,
        });

        result.matched.push({ receiptId: receipt.id, transactionId: best.id, matchScore: best.matchScore, receipt: matched.receipt, transaction: matched.transaction });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(`Failed to auto-match receipt ${receipt.id}`, err);
        result.errors.push({ receiptId: receipt.id, error: err.message });
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in autoMatchBatchReceiptsHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to auto-match receipts.' });
  }
};

async function autoMatchTransactionsHandler(req, res) {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { transactionIds, range = DEFAULT_SEARCH_RANGE } = req.body;
    if (!Array.isArray(transactionIds) || transactionIds.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'transactionIds must be a non-empty array.' });
    }

    const transactionsToMatch = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
        id: { in: transactionIds.map((id) => Number(id)) },
        receiptId: null,
      },
      include: { source: true, category: true, receipt: true },
    });

    const results = { matched: [], skipped: [], errors: [] };

    for (const tx of transactionsToMatch) {
      try {
        const candidates = await findCandidateReceiptsForTransaction(session.user.organizationId, tx, { range });
        const best = candidates[0];
        const second = candidates[1];

        if (candidates.length > 0) {
          await storeCandidates({ organizationId: session.user.organizationId, bankTransactionId: tx.id, candidates: candidates.slice(0, 5) });
        }

        const highConfidence =
          best &&
          (best.exactMatch ||
            (best.matchScore >= 0.93 &&
              best.scoreBreakdown.amountScore >= 0.95 &&
              (!second || best.matchScore - second.matchScore >= 0.15)));

        if (!highConfidence) {
          const newStatus = candidates.length === 0 ? MATCH_STATUS.UNMATCHED
            : candidates.length >= 2 && Math.abs(candidates[0].matchScore - candidates[1].matchScore) < 0.05 ? MATCH_STATUS.CONFLICT
              : best?.matchScore >= 0.85 ? MATCH_STATUS.CANDIDATES_FOUND : MATCH_STATUS.NEEDS_REVIEW;

          await prisma.bankTransaction.update({
            where: { id: tx.id },
            data: { receiptMatchStatus: newStatus, receiptMatchConfidence: best?.matchScore ?? null },
          });

          results.skipped.push({
            transactionId: tx.id,
            reason: 'No high-confidence routine receipt match found.',
            candidates: candidates.slice(0, 3).map((item) => ({
              id: item.id, companyName: item.companyName, total: item.total, date: item.date, matchScore: item.matchScore, confidenceLabel: item.confidenceLabel,
            })),
          });
          continue;
        }

        const matched = await applyReceiptMatch({
          organizationId: session.user.organizationId,
          receiptId: best.id,
          transactionId: tx.id,
          matchConfidence: best.matchScore,
          scoreBreakdown: best.scoreBreakdown,
          status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.AUTO_MATCHED,
        });

        results.matched.push({ transactionId: tx.id, receiptId: best.id, matchScore: best.matchScore, transaction: matched.transaction, receipt: matched.receipt });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(`Failed to match transaction ${tx.id}`, err);
        results.errors.push({ transactionId: tx.id, error: err.message });
      }
    }

    return res.status(200).json(results);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in autoMatchTransactionsHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
}

const unmatchReceiptHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized.' });

    const { transactionId } = req.params;
    if (!transactionId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing transactionId parameter.' });

    const tx = await prisma.bankTransaction.findUnique({
      where: { id: parseInt(transactionId, 10) },
      include: { receipt: true, source: true, category: true },
    });

    if (!tx) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Transaction not found.' });
    if (tx.organizationId !== session.user.organizationId) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden.' });
    if (!tx.receiptId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No receipt is matched to this transaction.' });

    const nextTxNotes = mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(tx.notes, {
      normalizedVendor: tx.receipt?.companyName ? normalizeText(tx.receipt.companyName) : null,
      extractedTax: tx.receipt?.hst == null ? null : normalizePositiveTax(tx.receipt.hst),
      taxConfidence: 'UNMATCHED',
      suggestedExpenseAccount: tx.category?.code || null,
      suggestedStatementLine: tx.category?.statementLine || null,
      matchedReceiptId: null,
      matchedTransactionId: tx.id,
      matchConfidence: 0,
      needsReview: true,
      sourceType: tx.source?.type || null,
      scoreBreakdown: null,
    });

    const nextReceiptNotes = mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(tx.receipt?.notes, {
      normalizedVendor: tx.receipt?.companyName ? normalizeText(tx.receipt.companyName) : null,
      extractedTax: tx.receipt?.hst == null ? null : normalizePositiveTax(tx.receipt.hst),
      taxConfidence: 'UNMATCHED',
      suggestedExpenseAccount: null,
      suggestedStatementLine: null,
      matchedReceiptId: tx.receiptId,
      matchedTransactionId: null,
      matchConfidence: 0,
      needsReview: true,
      sourceType: null,
      scoreBreakdown: null,
    });

    await prisma.$transaction([
      prisma.bankTransaction.update({
        where: { id: parseInt(transactionId, 10) },
        data: {
          receiptId: null,
          notes: nextTxNotes,
          receiptMatchStatus: MATCH_STATUS.UNMATCHED,
          receiptMatchConfidence: null,
          receiptMatchReviewed: false,
          receiptMatchReviewedAt: null,
          receiptMatchReviewedBy: null,
        },
      }),
      prisma.receipt.update({
        where: { id: tx.receiptId },
        data: { paymentType: null, notes: nextReceiptNotes },
      }),
    ]);

    // Reopen previously superseded candidates for this transaction
    await prisma.receiptMatchCandidate.updateMany({
      where: { bankTransactionId: parseInt(transactionId, 10), status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.SUPERSEDED },
      data: { status: CANDIDATE_STATUS.CANDIDATE },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ message: 'Receipt unmatched successfully.' });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in unmatchReceiptHandler:', error);
    return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

// ---------- Routes ----------

router.get('/queue', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: getMatchQueueHandler, allowedMethods: ['GET'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/approve-candidate', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: approveCandidateHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/reject-candidate', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: rejectCandidateHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/no-receipt-required', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: noReceiptRequiredHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/batch-approve', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: batchApproveHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/refresh-candidates', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: refreshCandidatesHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/auto-match-transactions', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: autoMatchTransactionsHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/transactions', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: fetchMatchingTransactionsHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: matchReceiptToTransactionHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));
```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/matchTransactions.js

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/matchTransactions.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipts/matchTransactions.js

import express from 'express';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';

const prisma = new PrismaClient();
const router = express.Router();

// POST /api/receipts/matchTransactions
router.post('/', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const session = await getSession(req);
    if (!session || !session.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
    }

    const userId = session.user.id;
    const organizationId = session.user.organizationId;

    const { receiptId } = req.body;

    if (!receiptId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receiptId.' });
    }

    // Fetch the receipt to ensure it exists
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      select: {
        date: true,
        total: true,
      },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    const { date, total } = receipt;

    if (!date || total === null || total === undefined) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Receipt must have a valid date and total.' });
    }

    // Define date range (+/- 1 day)
    const dateFrom = new Date(date);
    dateFrom.setDate(dateFrom.getDate() - 10);

    const dateTo = new Date(date);
    dateTo.setDate(dateTo.getDate() + 10);

    // Define amount range (+/- 10%)
    const amountMin = total * 0.9;
    const amountMax = total * 1.1;

    // Find matching transactions
    const matchingTransactions = await prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        date: {
          gte: dateFrom,
          lte: dateTo,
        },
        amount: {
          gte: -amountMax,
          lte: -amountMin,
        },
        receiptId: null, // Only unmatched transactions
      },
      orderBy: {
        date: 'asc',
      },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ transactions: matchingTransactions });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Error in matchTransactions:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
});

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/ocr.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import ReceiptOcrJobService from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptOcrJobService.js';

const router = express.Router();

const startOcrHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const { receiptId } = req.body;

  if (!receiptId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Receipt ID required.' });
  }

  const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
    where: { id: receiptId },
    select: {
      id: true,
      organizationId: true,
      imgName: true,
      text: true,
    },
  });

  if (!receipt || receipt.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId) {
    return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
  }

  if (!receipt.imgName && !receipt.text) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Nothing available to OCR on this receipt.' });
  }

  const status = ReceiptOcrJobService.startInBackground(receiptId);

  return res.status(202).json({
    message: status.isRunning ? 'OCR started in the background.' : 'OCR queued.',
    status,
  });
};

router.post(
  '/',
  authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: startOcrHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] })
);

router.get('/status', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const { receiptId } = req.query;
  if (!receiptId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId required.' });
  }
  const status = ReceiptOcrJobService.getStatus(receiptId);
  return res.status(200).json(status);
});

export default router;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/optimize.js
import express from 'express';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import ReceiptOptimizationService from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptOptimizationService.js';

const router = express.Router();

const ALLOWED_REVIEW_MODES = new Set(['ocr-only', 'ocr-plus-llm']);

function requireReceiptEdit(req, res) {
  const organizationId = req.user?.organizationId || null;
  const userId = req.user?.id || req.user?.userId || null;
  const permissions = req.user?.permissions || [];

  if (!organizationId || !userId) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing user or organization context.' });
    return null;
  }

  if (!permissions.includes('receipt:edit') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
    res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:edit permission required.' });
    return null;
  }

  return { organizationId, userId };
}

// POST /receipt/optimize/preview
const previewHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const {
    receiptId,
    autoCrop = true,
    compressionProfile = null,
    maxWidth = 1800,
    cropPadding = 18,
    reviewMode = 'ocr-only',
  } = req.body || {};

  if (!receiptId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId is required.' });

  if (!ALLOWED_REVIEW_MODES.has(reviewMode)) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: `Invalid reviewMode. Allowed values: ${[...ALLOWED_REVIEW_MODES].join(', ')}.`,
    });
  }

  const report = await ReceiptOptimizationService.preview(
    receiptId,
    context.organizationId,
    { autoCrop, compressionProfile, maxWidth, cropPadding, reviewMode }
  );

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: report.selected
      ? 'Optimization preview created.'
      : 'Optimization preview needs review.',
    report,
  });
};

// POST /receipt/optimize/save
const saveHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const { receiptId, previewRelativePath } = req.body || {};

  if (!receiptId || !previewRelativePath) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId and previewRelativePath are required.' });
  }

  const result = await ReceiptOptimizationService.save(
    receiptId,
    context.organizationId,
    context.userId,
    previewRelativePath
  );

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: 'Optimized image activated. Original image was retained.',
    ...result,
  });
};

// POST /receipt/optimize/discard
const discardHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const { receiptId, previewRelativePath } = req.body || {};

  if (!receiptId || !previewRelativePath) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId and previewRelativePath are required.' });
  }

  const result = await ReceiptOptimizationService.discard(
    receiptId,
    context.organizationId,
    previewRelativePath
  );

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: result.discarded ? 'Optimization preview discarded.' : 'No preview file found.',
    ...result,
  });
};

// GET /receipt/optimize/status?receiptId=...
const statusHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const { receiptId } = req.query || {};
  if (!receiptId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId is required.' });

  const report = await ReceiptOptimizationService.getReport(receiptId, context.organizationId);
  return res.status(200).json(report);
};

// GET /receipt/optimize/report/:receiptId
const reportHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const report = await ReceiptOptimizationService.getReport(
    req.params.receiptId,
    context.organizationId
  );
  return res.status(200).json(report);
};

// POST /receipt/optimize/bulk  — dry-run savings estimate or full preview for many receipts
const bulkHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const {
    receiptIds = [],
    dryRun = true,
    autoCrop = true,
    maxWidth = 1800,
    cropPadding = 18,
    compressionProfile = null,
    reviewMode = 'ocr-only',
  } = req.body || {};

  if (!Array.isArray(receiptIds) || receiptIds.length === 0) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptIds must be a non-empty array.' });
  }

  if (!ALLOWED_REVIEW_MODES.has(reviewMode)) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: `Invalid reviewMode. Allowed values: ${[...ALLOWED_REVIEW_MODES].join(', ')}.`,
    });
  }

  const results = [];

  for (const receiptId of receiptIds.slice(0, 50)) {
    try {
      const report = await ReceiptOptimizationService.preview(receiptId, context.organizationId, {
        autoCrop,
        maxWidth,
        cropPadding,
        compressionProfile,
        reviewMode,
      });

      const entry = {
        receiptId,
        status: report.status,
        selectedProfile: report.selectedProfile,
        savedBytes: report.selected?.savedBytes || 0,
        activated: false,
        dryRun,
      };

      if (!dryRun && report.selected?.previewRelativePath) {
        // Activate the best passing candidate.
        await ReceiptOptimizationService.save(
          receiptId,
          context.organizationId,
          context.userId,
          report.selected.previewRelativePath
        );
        entry.activated = true;
        entry.status = 'ACTIVE_OPTIMIZED';

        // Discard any non-selected preview files generated during this run.
        for (const candidate of report.candidates || []) {
          if (
            candidate?.previewRelativePath &&
            candidate.previewRelativePath !== report.selected.previewRelativePath
          ) {
            await ReceiptOptimizationService.discard(
              receiptId,
              context.organizationId,
              candidate.previewRelativePath
            ).catch(() => {});
          }
        }
      }

      results.push(entry);
    } catch (error) {
      results.push({ receiptId, status: 'FAILED', error: error.message, activated: false, dryRun });
    }
  }

  const activatedCount = results.filter((r) => r.activated).length;
  const totalSavedBytes = results.reduce((sum, r) => sum + (r.savedBytes || 0), 0);

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: dryRun
      ? `Savings estimate: ${results.filter((r) => r.status === 'PASSED').length} of ${results.length} receipts could be compressed.`
      : `Batch optimize complete: ${activatedCount} of ${results.length} receipts compressed and activated.`,
    dryRun,
    count: results.length,
    activatedCount,
    totalEstimatedSavedBytes: totalSavedBytes,
    results,
  });
};

// POST /receipt/optimize/purge-original  — Phase 5: permanently delete original file
const purgeOriginalHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const { receiptId } = req.body || {};
  if (!receiptId) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptId is required.' });

  const result = await ReceiptOptimizationService.purgeOriginal(
    receiptId,
    context.organizationId
  );

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: result.purged
      ? `Original image purged. Freed ${result.freedBytes} bytes.`
      : result.reason,
    ...result,
  });
};

// POST /receipt/optimize/bulk-purge-original  — Phase 5: bulk purge originals
const bulkPurgeOriginalHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const context = requireReceiptEdit(req, res);
  if (!context) return;

  const { receiptIds = [] } = req.body || {};

  if (!Array.isArray(receiptIds) || receiptIds.length === 0) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'receiptIds must be a non-empty array.' });
  }

  const results = [];
  let totalFreedBytes = 0;

  for (const receiptId of receiptIds.slice(0, 200)) {
    try {
      const result = await ReceiptOptimizationService.purgeOriginal(
        receiptId,
        context.organizationId
      );
      results.push({ receiptId, ...result });
      if (result.purged) totalFreedBytes += result.freedBytes || 0;
    } catch (error) {
      results.push({ receiptId, purged: false, error: error.message });
    }
  }

  const purgedCount = results.filter((r) => r.purged).length;

  return res.status(200).json({
    message: `Purged originals for ${purgedCount} of ${results.length} receipts.`,
    purgedCount,
    totalFreedBytes,
    results,
  });
};

router.post('/preview', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: previewHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/save', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: saveHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/discard', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: discardHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.get('/status', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: statusHandler, allowedMethods: ['GET'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.get('/report/:receiptId', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: reportHandler, allowedMethods: ['GET'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/bulk', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: bulkHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/purge-original', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: purgeOriginalHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

router.post('/bulk-purge-original', authenticate,
  withHandler({ handler: bulkPurgeOriginalHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/receipt.js
// /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/routes/api/receipt/receipt.js:

//--- File: pages/api/receipt/list.js ---
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';
import { getSession } from '#shared/utils/auth.js';

const prisma = new PrismaClient();

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  if (req.method === 'GET') {
    try {
      const session = await getSession(req);
      if (!session || !session.user) {
        return res
          .status(401)
          .json({ error: 'Unauthorized: No valid session found.' });
      }

      const { user } = session;

      const {
        page = '1',
        limit = '100',
        id, // receiptId filter
        companyName,
        dateFrom,
        dateTo,
        showErrors = 'false',
        showDuplicates = 'false',
        sortKey = 'createdAt', // allowed: id, date, createdAt, companyName, total, hst
        sortDirection = 'desc', // "asc" or "desc"
        active,       // new: active status filter (expected "true" or "false")
        matchStatus,   // new: "matched" or "unmatched"
        notes
      } = req.query;

      const sanitizedId = Array.isArray(id) ? id[0] : id;

      const allowedSortKeys = [
        'id',
        'date',
        'createdAt',
        'companyName',
        'total',
        'hst'
      ];
      if (!allowedSortKeys.includes(sortKey)) {
        return res
          .status(400)
          .json({
            error: `Invalid sortKey. Allowed values are: ${allowedSortKeys.join(', ')}`
          });
      }

      const sortDir = sortDirection.toLowerCase() === 'asc' ? 'asc' : 'desc';

      const take = Math.min(parseInt(limit, 10) || 100, 1000);
      const currentPage = Math.max(parseInt(page, 10) || 1, 1);
      const skip = (currentPage - 1) * take;

      const whereClause = {
        organizationId: user.organizationId
      };

      if (sanitizedId) {
        whereClause.id = {
          contains: sanitizedId
        };
      }

      if (companyName) {
        whereClause.companyName = {
          contains: companyName
        };
      }

     if (notes) {
        whereClause.notes = {
            contains: notes
        };
      }

      if (dateFrom || dateTo) {
        whereClause.date = {};
        if (dateFrom) {
          const parsedDateFrom = new Date(dateFrom);
          if (isNaN(parsedDateFrom)) {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid dateFrom format.' });
          }
          whereClause.date.gte = parsedDateFrom;
        }
        if (dateTo) {
          const parsedDateTo = new Date(dateTo);
          if (isNaN(parsedDateTo)) {
            return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid dateTo format.' });
          }
          whereClause.date.lte = parsedDateTo;
        }
      }

      if (showErrors.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
        whereClause.OR = [
          { total: null },
          { total: 0 },
          { total: 0.0 }
        ];
      }

      // Filter by active status if provided
      if (active && (active === 'true' || active === 'false')) {
        whereClause.active = active === 'true';
      }

      // Filter by bank transaction match status
      if (matchStatus && matchStatus.toLowerCase() === 'matched') {
        whereClause.matchedBankTransactionId = { not: null };
      } else if (matchStatus && matchStatus.toLowerCase() === 'unmatched') {
        whereClause.matchedBankTransactionId = null;
      }

      let duplicateKeys = [];
      if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
        const duplicates = await prisma.$queryRaw`
          SELECT date, total, COUNT(*) as count
          FROM Receipt
          WHERE organizationId = ${user.organizationId}
          GROUP BY date, total
          HAVING COUNT(*) > 1
        `;

        duplicateKeys = duplicates.map(row => `${row.date}-${row.total}`);
      }

      let receipts = await prisma.receipt.findMany({
        where: whereClause,
        include: {
          items: true,
          user: { select: { username: true } },
          matchedBankTransaction: {
            include: {
              category: true,
              source: true
            }
          },
          organization: {
            select: {
              name: true
            }
          }
        },
        orderBy: { [sortKey]: sortDir },
        skip,
        take
      });

      if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true' && duplicateKeys.length > 0) {
        receipts = receipts.filter(receipt => {
          const key = `${receipt.date}-${receipt.total}`;
          return duplicateKeys.includes(key);
        });
      }

      let total = await prisma.receipt.count({
        where: whereClause
      });

      if (showDuplicates.toLowerCase() === 'true') {
        total = duplicateKeys.length;
      }

      res.status(200).json({
        total,
        page: currentPage,
        totalPages: Math.ceil(total / take),
        receipts
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching receipts:', error);
      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
    }
  } else {
    res.setHeader('Allow', ['GET']);
    res.status(405).end(`Method ${req.method} Not Allowed`);
  }
}
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/revert.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipt/revert.js

import express from 'express';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';

const router = express.Router();

const revertHandler = async (req, res) => {
  const { receiptId } = req.body;
  const user = req.user?.id || req.user?.userId || null;

  try {
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({ where: { id: receiptId } });

    if (!receipt || receipt.organizationId !== user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    // Logic: Look for a filename that matches the current one but with "-original"
    // OR, if current is "xyz-processed.jpg", look for "xyz-original.jpg"
    
    let originalFilename = null;
    if (receipt.imgName.includes('-processed')) {
      originalFilename = receipt.imgName.replace('-processed', '-original');
    } else {
        // Fallback: maybe it was manually named? Try finding a -original version
        const base = receipt.imgName.replace(/(\.[\w\d_-]+)$/i, '');
        const ext = path.extname(receipt.imgName);
        originalFilename = `${base}-original${ext}`;
    }

    const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', receipt.organizationId, 'receipts');
    const originalPath = path.join(uploadDir, originalFilename);

    if (!fs.existsSync(originalPath)) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No backup original file found to revert to.' });
    }

    // Update DB to point back to original
    const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      data: {
        imgName: originalFilename,
        notes: receipt.notes ? `${receipt.notes}\n[Reverted to Original]` : '[Reverted to Original]',
        updatedAt: new Date(),
      },
    });

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Reverted to original image.',
      receipt: updatedReceipt,
    });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Revert error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
};

router.post('/', authenticate, withHandler({ handler: revertHandler, allowedMethods: ['POST'], requiredRoles: [] }));

export default router;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/tagReceipt.js
//--- File: server/src/routes/api/receipt/tagReceipt.js ---

import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import ReceiptsManager from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import { logError } from '../../../utils/logError.js';

const router = express.Router();

const tagReceiptHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { receiptId } = req.body;
    const userId = req.user?.id || req.user?.userId;
    const sessionId = req.session?.id || req.user?.sessionId || '';

    if (!receiptId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receiptId.' });
    }

    if (!userId) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: Missing authenticated user id.' });
    }

    // Fetch the receipt to get organizationId
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      include: { organization: true },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    // Use organizationId instead of organizationName
    const result = await ReceiptsManager.tagReceipt(
      receipt.id,
      userId,
      sessionId,
      receipt.organizationId
    );

    const { heicConverted, originalHeicName, ...taggedReceipt } = result;

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Receipt tagged successfully.',
      receipt: taggedReceipt,
      heicConverted: heicConverted || false,
      originalHeicName: originalHeicName || null,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    await logError(error);
    console.error('Tag Receipt Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

export default router.use(withHandler({
  handler: tagReceiptHandler,
  allowedMethods: ['POST'],
  requiredRoles: [], // Specify roles if needed
}));
```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/update.js
