```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/update.js
// server/src/routes/api/receipts/update.js

import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';

const router = express.Router();

// PUT /api/receipts/update
router.put('/', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { id, imgName, date, companyName, total, hst, notes, items = [], text } = req.body;

    if (!id) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing receipt ID' });
    }

    const permissions = req.user?.permissions || [];
    if (!permissions.includes('receipt:edit') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:edit permission required.' });
    }

    if (items && !Array.isArray(items)) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Items must be an array.' });
    }

    // Validate date format
    let parsedDate = null;
    if (date) {
      parsedDate = new Date(date);
      if (isNaN(parsedDate.getTime())) {
        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid date format. Expected YYYY-MM-DD.' });
      }
    }

    // Fetch the receipt to ensure it exists and belongs to the user
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { organization: true },
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Receipt not found.' });
    }

    if (receipt.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: Access denied.' });
    }

    // Clean items data
    const cleanItems = items.map(({ name, quantity, price }) => ({
      name,
      quantity,
      price,
    }));

    // Update the receipt
    const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        date: parsedDate,
        companyName,
        total,
        hst,
        notes,
        text,
        items: {
          deleteMany: {},
          create: cleanItems,
        },
      },
      include: { items: true },
    });

    res.status(200).json(updatedReceipt);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Update error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update receipt' });
  }
});

export default router;

```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/receipt/upload.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/receipt/upload.js
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/routes/api/receipt/upload.js
import express from 'express';
import multer from 'multer';
import path from 'path';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';
import ReceiptsManager from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import fs from 'fs';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';
import {
  processReceiptImageAdvanced,
  isHeicFile,
  convertHeicToJpeg,
  assertReadableImage,
} from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptImageProcessor.js';
import { extractRequestContext, logAndReportError } from '../../../utils/logError.js';
import AttachmentService from '#services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js';
import ReceiptOptimizationService from '#services/receipt/services/ReceiptOptimizationService.js';

const router = express.Router();
const attachmentService = new AttachmentService();

const storage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (req, file, cb) => {
    const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;
    const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', organizationId, 'receipts');

    fs.mkdir(uploadDir, { recursive: true }, (err) => {
      if (err) {
        console.error('Error creating upload directory:', err);
        return cb(err, uploadDir);
      }
      cb(null, uploadDir);
    });
  },
  filename: (req, file, cb) => {
    const uniqueName = `${uuidv4()}${path.extname(file.originalname)}`;
    cb(null, uniqueName);
  },
});

const upload = multer({
  storage,
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = [
      'image/jpeg',
      'image/png',
      'image/heic',
      'image/heif',
      'application/pdf',
      'text/csv',
      'text/plain',
    ];

    if (allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype)) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(
        new Error(
          'Invalid file type. Only JPEG, PNG, HEIC, PDF, CSV, and plain text are allowed.'
        )
      );
    }
  },
});

const uploadHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const files = req.files;
    const authUser = req.user || {};
    const userId = authUser.id || authUser.userId || null;
    const organizationId = authUser.organizationId || null;
    const sessionIdForTagging = authUser.sessionId || '';

    if (!userId || !organizationId) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Unauthorized: missing user or organization context.' });
    }

    const permissions = authUser.permissions || [];
    if (!permissions.includes('receipt:add') && !permissions.includes('permission:editAll')) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden: receipt:add permission required.' });
    }

    if (!files || files.length === 0) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No files uploaded.' });
    }

    const processedReceipts = [];

    for (const file of files) {
      let receiptData = {};
      let importNote = '';
      let uploadedPath = file.path;

      if (file.mimetype.startsWith('image/')) {
        let sourcePath = file.path;

        try {
          // Convert HEIC/HEIF to JPEG before any further processing
          if (isHeicFile(file.path) || file.mimetype === 'image/heic' || file.mimetype === 'image/heif') {
            console.log(`Converting HEIC upload to JPEG: ${file.filename}`);
            const jpegPath = await convertHeicToJpeg(file.path);
            fs.unlinkSync(file.path);
            sourcePath = jpegPath;
            uploadedPath = jpegPath;
          }

          await assertReadableImage(sourcePath);

          const bwOutputPath = path.join(
            path.dirname(sourcePath),
            `${path.basename(sourcePath, path.extname(sourcePath))}-bw.jpg`
          );

          const result = await processReceiptImageAdvanced(sourcePath, 'bw', {
            outputPath: bwOutputPath,
          });

          receiptData.imgName = path.basename(result.outputPath);
          importNote = '[Imported as Black & White]';

          if (fs.existsSync(sourcePath) && path.resolve(sourcePath) !== path.resolve(result.outputPath)) {
            fs.unlinkSync(sourcePath);
          }
        } catch (err) {
          if (err?.code === 'INVALID_IMAGE_UPLOAD') {
            if (fs.existsSync(uploadedPath)) {
              fs.unlinkSync(uploadedPath);
            }
            return res.status(400).json({
              error: 'The uploaded receipt photo could not be read as an image. Please retake it or choose it from your gallery.',
            });
          }

          console.error('B&W import processing failed:', err);
          receiptData.imgName = path.basename(sourcePath);
        }
      } else if (file.mimetype === 'application/pdf') {
        const buffer = fs.readFileSync(file.path);
        const extractedText = await ReceiptsManager.extractTextFromPDF(buffer);
        receiptData.text = extractedText;
        receiptData.filePath = `/uploads/${organizationId}/receipts/${file.filename}`;
      } else if (
        file.mimetype === 'text/csv' ||
        file.mimetype === 'text/plain'
      ) {
        const text = fs.readFileSync(file.path, 'utf-8');
        receiptData.text = text;
      } else {
        continue;
      }

      if (receiptData.imgName) {
        receiptData.imageRelativePath = `receipts/${receiptData.imgName}`;
        receiptData.imageStorageStatus = 'ACTIVE';

        const imageAbsolutePath = attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
          organizationId,
          receiptData.imageRelativePath,
          receiptData.imgName
        );
        const imageMetadata = attachmentService.getFileMetadata(imageAbsolutePath);

        receiptData.imageStorageSize = imageMetadata.size || 0;
        receiptData.imageStorageChecksum = imageMetadata.checksum || null;
      }

      if (importNote) {
        receiptData.notes = importNote;
      }

      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.create({
        data: {
          ...receiptData,
          user: { connect: { id: userId } },
          organization: { connect: { id: organizationId } },
        },
      });

      const taggedReceipt = await ReceiptsManager.tagReceipt(
        receipt.id,
        userId,
        sessionIdForTagging,
        organizationId
      );

      // Phase 4: auto-optimize image receipts in the background without blocking the response.
      if (receiptData.imgName) {
        ReceiptOptimizationService.autoOptimize(receipt.id, organizationId).catch(() => {});
      }

      processedReceipts.push(taggedReceipt);
    }

    res.status(200).json({
      message: 'Files uploaded and receipts processed successfully.',
      receipts: processedReceipts,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    await logAndReportError('Upload processing error:', error, extractRequestContext(req));

    if (error instanceof multer.MulterError) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
    }

    res
      .status(500)
      .json({ error: 'Internal server error while processing upload.' });
  }
};

router.post(
  '/',
  authenticate,
  upload.array('files'),
  withHandler({
    handler: uploadHandler,
    allowedMethods: ['POST'],
    requiredRoles: [],
  })
);

export default router;

```

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/schemas.js
import { z } from 'zod';

export const ReceiptItemSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string(),
  quantity: z.number().int(),
  price: z.number(),
});

export const ReceiptSchema = z.object({
  date: z.string().optional().refine((val) => !val || !isNaN(Date.parse(val)), {
    message: 'Invalid date format',
  }),
  companyName: z.string().optional(),
  imgName: z.string().optional(),
  id: z.string().optional(),
  total: z.number().optional(),
  hst: z.number().optional(),
  notes: z.string().optional(),
  items: z.array(ReceiptItemSchema).optional(),
});

export const ReceiptResponseSchema = {
  type: 'object',
  properties: {
    date: { type: ['string', 'null'] },
    companyName: { type: ['string', 'null'] },
    total: { type: ['string', 'number', 'null'] },
    hst: { type: ['string', 'number', 'null'] },
    items: {
      type: 'array',
      items: {
        type: 'object',
        properties: {
          name: { type: 'string' },
          quantity: { type: 'number' },
          price: { type: 'number' },
        },
        required: ['name', 'quantity', 'price'],
      },
    },
    notes: { type: ['string', 'null'] },
  },
  required: [],
};

FILE: server/src/services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js
// Full path: /home/luan_ngo/boss/server/src/services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js
// server/src/services/receipt/services/AttachmentService.js

import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import crypto from 'crypto';

const RECEIPTS_ROOT_SEGMENT = 'receipts';

class AttachmentService {
  getOrganizationUploadsRoot(organizationId) {
    if (!organizationId) {
      throw new Error('organizationId is required.');
    }

    return path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', organizationId);
  }

  getReceiptUploadsDir(organizationId) {
    return path.join(this.getOrganizationUploadsRoot(organizationId), RECEIPTS_ROOT_SEGMENT);
  }

  normalizeReceiptRelativePath(relativePath = '', fallbackFileName = '') {
    let candidate = String(relativePath || '')
      .replace(/\\/g, '/')
      .trim()
      .replace(/^\/+/, '');

    if (!candidate && fallbackFileName) {
      candidate = `${RECEIPTS_ROOT_SEGMENT}/${path.basename(fallbackFileName)}`;
    }

    if (!candidate) {
      return null;
    }

    const rawSegments = candidate.split('/').filter(Boolean);
    const safeSegments = [];

    for (const segment of rawSegments) {
      if (segment === '.' || segment === '..') {
        throw new Error('Invalid relative receipt path.');
      }

      safeSegments.push(
        String(segment)
          .replace(/[\0<>:"|?*]/g, '_')
          .trim()
      );
    }

    if (!safeSegments.length) {
      return null;
    }

    if (safeSegments[0] !== RECEIPTS_ROOT_SEGMENT) {
      safeSegments.unshift(RECEIPTS_ROOT_SEGMENT);
    }

    return safeSegments.join('/');
  }

  getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt = {}) {
    return this.normalizeReceiptRelativePath(receipt?.imageRelativePath, receipt?.imgName);
  }

  resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(organizationId, relativePath = '', fallbackFileName = '') {
    const normalizedRelativePath = this.normalizeReceiptRelativePath(relativePath, fallbackFileName);
    if (!normalizedRelativePath) {
      throw new Error('Receipt path is required.');
    }

    const uploadsRoot = this.getOrganizationUploadsRoot(organizationId);
    const absolutePath = path.resolve(path.join(uploadsRoot, normalizedRelativePath));
    const uploadsRootWithSep = `${path.resolve(uploadsRoot)}${path.sep}`;

    if (
      absolutePath !== path.resolve(uploadsRoot) &&
      !absolutePath.startsWith(uploadsRootWithSep)
    ) {
      throw new Error('Resolved receipt path is outside of the uploads directory.');
    }

    return absolutePath;
  }

  ensureReceiptDirectoryForPath(organizationId, relativePath = '', fallbackFileName = '') {
    const absolutePath = this.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(organizationId, relativePath, fallbackFileName);
    fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(absolutePath), { recursive: true });
    return absolutePath;
  }

  hashBuffer(buffer) {
    return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(buffer).digest('hex');
  }

  getFileMetadata(filePath) {
    if (!filePath || !fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
      return {
        exists: false,
        size: 0,
        checksum: null,
        modifiedAt: null,
      };
    }

    const stats = fs.statSync(filePath);
    if (!stats.isFile()) {
      return {
        exists: false,
        size: 0,
        checksum: null,
        modifiedAt: null,
      };
    }

    const buffer = fs.readFileSync(filePath);

    return {
      exists: true,
      size: stats.size,
      checksum: this.hashBuffer(buffer),
      modifiedAt: stats.mtime,
    };
  }

  saveAttachment(buffer, filename, organizationId, relativePath = null) {
    const sanitizedFilename = path.basename(filename);
    const targetPath = this.ensureReceiptDirectoryForPath(
      organizationId,
      relativePath,
      sanitizedFilename
    );

    fs.writeFileSync(targetPath, buffer);
    return targetPath;
  }

  writeBufferToReceiptPath(buffer, organizationId, relativePath = '', fallbackFileName = '') {
    const targetPath = this.ensureReceiptDirectoryForPath(
      organizationId,
      relativePath,
      fallbackFileName
    );

    fs.writeFileSync(targetPath, buffer);
    return targetPath;
  }

  copyFileToReceiptPath(sourcePath, organizationId, relativePath = '', fallbackFileName = '') {
    if (!sourcePath || !fs.existsSync(sourcePath)) {
      throw new Error('Source file does not exist.');
    }

    const targetPath = this.ensureReceiptDirectoryForPath(
      organizationId,
      relativePath,
      fallbackFileName
    );

    fs.copyFileSync(sourcePath, targetPath);
    return targetPath;
  }

  deleteAttachment(imgName, organizationId, relativePath = null) {
    if (!organizationId || (!imgName && !relativePath)) {
      return false;
    }

    try {
      const filePath = this.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(organizationId, relativePath, imgName);
      if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
        fs.unlinkSync(filePath);
        return true;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error deleting attachment:', error);
    }

    return false;
  }
}

export default AttachmentService;

```

FILE: server/src/services/receipt/services/LLMService.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/LLMService.js
import { llmClient } from '#integrations/ai/llm.js';
import { ReceiptResponseSchema } from '../schemas.js';
import GoogleApiService from '#integrations/google/services/googleApiService.js';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import SettingsService from '#services/settings/SettingsService.js';

const DEFAULT_RECEIPT_USER_PROMPT = `Extract structured receipt data from the receipt text below.

Rules:
- Use only the information explicitly present in the receipt text.
- Do not infer or invent values.
- If a value is missing or uncertain, return null for that field.
- If the text is a payment notification, bank alert, email wrapper, or upload instruction rather than a real receipt, do not treat wrapper text as receipt facts.
- Ignore boilerplate like greetings, signatures, upload links, and generic instructions.
- Prefer the actual merchant over the sender name.
- total must be the final receipt total actually charged on the receipt.
- hst should only be returned when tax is explicitly shown. Otherwise return null.
- items should only include real line items explicitly listed on the receipt. Otherwise return an empty array.
- notes should briefly describe any ambiguity, wrapper-content issue, or missing data that needs review.
- date should be ISO format YYYY-MM-DD when present, otherwise null.

Receipt text:
{receiptText}`;

const DEFAULT_RECEIPT_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You extract structured receipt data.
Return only the structured response.
Never guess.
When the source content is not a real receipt or is incomplete, leave unknown fields null, leave items empty, and explain the issue briefly in notes.`;

const parseMoney = (value) => {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return null;
  if (typeof value === 'number') {
    return Number.isFinite(value) ? Number(value.toFixed(2)) : null;
  }

  const cleaned = String(value).replace(/[^0-9.-]/g, '');
  if (!cleaned) return null;

  const parsed = parseFloat(cleaned);
  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? Number(parsed.toFixed(2)) : null;
};

const normalizeDate = (value) => {
  if (!value || typeof value !== 'string' || Number.isNaN(Date.parse(value))) {
    return null;
  }
  return value;
};

const normalizeItems = (items) => {
  if (!Array.isArray(items)) return [];

  return items
    .map((item) => ({
      name: String(item?.name || '').trim(),
      quantity: Number.isFinite(Number(item?.quantity)) ? Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(item.quantity))) : 1,
      price: Number.isFinite(Number(item?.price)) ? Number(Number(item.price).toFixed(2)) : 0,
    }))
    .filter((item) => item.name);
};

class LLMService {
  constructor() {
    this.llmClient = llmClient;
    this.googleApiService = new GoogleApiService();
    this.model = 'xiaomi/mimo-v2-flash';
  }

  async extractAndTagReceiptFromImage(imgPath, imgName, userId, sessionId, receiptId) {
    try {
      console.log(`Starting OCR for image: ${imgName}`);
      const receiptText = await this.ocrUsingGoogleVision(imgPath);
      console.log(`OCR Output for ${imgName}:`, receiptText);

      const taggedData = await this.extractAndTagReceipt(receiptText, receiptId, userId, sessionId);
      console.log(`LLM Tagging Output for ${imgName}:`, taggedData);
      taggedData.text = receiptText;
      return taggedData;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error in extractAndTagReceiptFromImage:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async extractAndTagReceipt(receiptText, receiptId, userId, sessionId) {
    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: userId } });
    if (!user) throw new Error('User not found for prompt fetching.');

    const promptTemplate =
      (await SettingsService.getPrompt(user.organizationId, 'receipt_extractAndTag_user')) ||
      DEFAULT_RECEIPT_USER_PROMPT;

    const systemPrompt =
      (await SettingsService.getPrompt(user.organizationId, 'receipt_extractAndTagReceipt_system')) ||
      DEFAULT_RECEIPT_SYSTEM_PROMPT;

    const prompt = String(promptTemplate).includes('{receiptText}')
      ? promptTemplate.replace('{receiptText}', receiptText || '')
      : `${promptTemplate}\n\nReceipt text:\n${receiptText || ''}`;

    try {
      const response = await this.llmClient.generateResponse(
        prompt,
        userId,
        sessionId,
        'STRUCTURED_OUTPUT',
        'deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash',
        ReceiptResponseSchema,
        'ReceiptResponse',
        systemPrompt
      );

      return {
        date: normalizeDate(response?.date),
        companyName: response?.companyName ? String(response.companyName).trim() : null,
        total: parseMoney(response?.total),
        hst: parseMoney(response?.hst),
        notes: response?.notes ? String(response.notes).trim() : null,
        items: normalizeItems(response?.items),
        text: receiptText,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error in extractAndTagReceipt:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async extractAndTagReceiptFromText(receiptText, receiptId, userId, sessionId) {
    try {
      console.log('Processing receipt text for receipt:', receiptId);
      const taggedData = await this.extractAndTagReceipt(receiptText, receiptId, userId, sessionId);
      console.log(`LLM Tagging Output for receipt text of ${receiptId}:`, taggedData);
      taggedData.text = receiptText;
      return taggedData;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error in extractAndTagReceiptFromText:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async ocrUsingGroqVision(imgPath) {
    try {
      return await this.llmClient.ocrUsingGroqVision(imgPath);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error in OCR using GroqVision:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async ocrUsingGoogleVision(imgPath) {
    try {
      return await this.googleApiService.performOcr(imgPath);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error in OCR using Google Vision:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

export default LLMService;

```

FILE: server/src/services/receipt/services/PDFService.js

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/PDFService.js
// server/src/services/receipt/services/PDFService.js
import { execSync } from "child_process";
import sharp from "sharp";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs";
import os from "os";
import { chromium } from "playwright";
import {
  PDFDocument,
  StandardFonts,
  rgb,
  PDFTextField,
  PDFCheckBox,
  PDFRadioGroup,
  PDFDropdown,
  PDFOptionList,
} from "pdf-lib";
import pdfParse from "pdf-parse";

function escapeXML(str) {
  if (typeof str !== "string") return str;
  return str
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
    .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
    .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
    .replace(/'/g, "&apos;");
}

function parseColor(input) {
  if (!input) return rgb(0, 0, 0);

  if (input.startsWith("#")) {
    const hex = input.replace("#", "");
    const normalized =
      hex.length === 3 ? hex.split("").map((c) => `${c}${c}`).join("") : hex;
    const n = parseInt(normalized, 16);
    const r = ((n >> 16) & 255) / 255;
    const g = ((n >> 8) & 255) / 255;
    const b = (n & 255) / 255;
    return rgb(r, g, b);
  }

  const match = input.match(/(\d+)[^\d]+(\d+)[^\d]+(\d+)/);
  if (match) {
    const r = Math.min(255, parseInt(match[1], 10)) / 255;
    const g = Math.min(255, parseInt(match[2], 10)) / 255;
    const b = Math.min(255, parseInt(match[3], 10)) / 255;
    return rgb(r, g, b);
  }

  return rgb(0, 0, 0);
}

function dataUrlToBuffer(dataUrl) {
  const match = String(dataUrl || "").match(/^data:(.+?);base64,(.*)$/);
  if (!match) return null;

  return {
    mimeType: match[1],
    buffer: Buffer.from(match[2], "base64"),
  };
}

function normalizeBoolean(value) {
  if (typeof value === "boolean") return value;
  if (typeof value === "number") return value !== 0;
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase();
    return ["true", "1", "yes", "on", "checked"].includes(normalized);
  }
  return !!value;
}

function wrapTextToLines(text, font, fontSize, maxWidth) {
  const normalizedText = String(text || "").replace(/\r/g, "");
  const paragraphs = normalizedText.split("\n");
  const lines = [];

  for (const paragraph of paragraphs) {
    const words = paragraph.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);

    if (words.length === 0) {
      lines.push("");
      continue;
    }

    let current = words[0];

    for (let i = 1; i < words.length; i += 1) {
      const candidate = `${current} ${words[i]}`;
      const width = font.widthOfTextAtSize(candidate, fontSize);

      if (width <= maxWidth) {
        current = candidate;
      } else {
        lines.push(current);
        current = words[i];
      }
    }

    lines.push(current);
  }

  return lines;
}

function resolvePathInsideOrg({ uploadsBase, orgId, folder = "", filename }) {
  if (!filename) return null;

  const orgRoot = path.normalize(path.join(uploadsBase, orgId));
  const candidate = path.normalize(path.join(orgRoot, folder || "", filename));
  const orgRootWithSep = `${orgRoot}${path.sep}`;

  if (candidate === orgRoot || candidate.startsWith(orgRootWithSep)) {
    return candidate;
  }

  return null;
}

function resolveFileManagerSourcePath(srcUrl, uploadsBase, orgId) {
  if (!srcUrl) return null;

  try {
    const url = new URL(srcUrl, "http://localhost");
    const pathname = url.pathname || "";

    if (
      pathname.endsWith("/filemanager/serve") ||
      pathname.endsWith("/filemanager/openPdf")
    ) {
      const folder = url.searchParams.get("folder") || "";
      const filename = url.searchParams.get("filename");
      return resolvePathInsideOrg({ uploadsBase, orgId, folder, filename });
    }

    const uploadsMarker = `${path.sep}uploads${path.sep}`;
    const normalizedPathname = path.normalize(pathname);

    if (normalizedPathname.includes(uploadsMarker)) {
      const idx = normalizedPathname.indexOf(uploadsMarker);
      const relativeFromUploads = normalizedPathname.slice(idx + uploadsMarker.length);
      const absolutePath = path.normalize(path.join(uploadsBase, relativeFromUploads));
      const orgRoot = path.normalize(path.join(uploadsBase, orgId));
      const orgRootWithSep = `${orgRoot}${path.sep}`;

      if (absolutePath === orgRoot || absolutePath.startsWith(orgRootWithSep)) {
        return absolutePath;
      }
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.warn("Could not resolve file manager image URL:", srcUrl, err.message);
  }

  return null;
}

function findAvailableChromiumExecutable() {
  const explicitPath = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_CHROMIUM_EXECUTABLE_PATH;
  if (explicitPath && fs.existsSync(explicitPath)) {
    return explicitPath;
  }

  const defaultPath = chromium.executablePath();
  if (defaultPath && fs.existsSync(defaultPath)) {
    return defaultPath;
  }

  const cacheRoot = process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH && process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH !== "0"
    ? process.env.PLAYWRIGHT_BROWSERS_PATH
    : path.join(os.homedir(), ".cache", "ms-playwright");

  if (!fs.existsSync(cacheRoot)) {
    return undefined;
  }

  const candidates = fs.readdirSync(cacheRoot)
    .filter((entry) => /^chromium(?:_headless_shell)?-\d+$/.test(entry))
    .sort((left, right) => {
      const leftVersion = Number(left.match(/-(\d+)$/)?.[1] || 0);
      const rightVersion = Number(right.match(/-(\d+)$/)?.[1] || 0);
      if (leftVersion !== rightVersion) return rightVersion - leftVersion;
      return Number(right.includes("_headless_shell")) - Number(left.includes("_headless_shell"));
    })
    .flatMap((entry) => [
      path.join(cacheRoot, entry, "chrome-headless-shell-linux64", "chrome-headless-shell"),
      path.join(cacheRoot, entry, "chrome-linux", "headless_shell"),
      path.join(cacheRoot, entry, "chrome-linux", "chrome"),
      path.join(cacheRoot, entry, "chrome-linux64", "headless_shell"),
      path.join(cacheRoot, entry, "chrome-linux64", "chrome"),
    ]);

  return candidates.find((candidate) => fs.existsSync(candidate));
}

async function resolveImageBytes(item, uploadsBase, orgId) {
  if (item.imageDataUrl) {
    const parsed = dataUrlToBuffer(item.imageDataUrl);
    if (!parsed?.buffer) return null;
    return {
      buffer: parsed.buffer,
      mimeType: parsed.mimeType || "",
      hint: parsed.mimeType || "",
    };
  }

  if (item.srcUrl) {
    const localPath = resolveFileManagerSourcePath(item.srcUrl, uploadsBase, orgId);
    if (localPath && fs.existsSync(localPath)) {
      return {
        buffer: fs.readFileSync(localPath),
        mimeType: "",
        hint: localPath,
      };
    }
  }

  return null;
}

async function embedImageForPdf(pdf, imageBuffer, hint = "") {
  const lowerHint = String(hint || "").toLowerCase();

  if (lowerHint.includes("image/png") || lowerHint.endsWith(".png")) {
    return pdf.embedPng(imageBuffer);
  }

  if (
    lowerHint.includes("image/jpeg") ||
    lowerHint.includes("image/jpg") ||
    lowerHint.endsWith(".jpg") ||
    lowerHint.endsWith(".jpeg")
  ) {
    return pdf.embedJpg(imageBuffer);
  }

  try {
    return await pdf.embedPng(imageBuffer);
  } catch {
    const converted = await sharp(imageBuffer).png().toBuffer();
    return pdf.embedPng(converted);
  }
}

class PDFService {
  constructor() {
    this.width = 2480;
  }

  async convertPDFToImage(pdfBuffer, metadata = {}, outputPath) {
    try {
      const dir = path.dirname(outputPath);
      if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });

      const metadataImage = await this.createMetadataHeader(metadata);
      const pageFiles = this.pdfToPngPages(pdfBuffer, dir);
      if (!pageFiles.length) throw new Error("No pages generated from PDF");

      const pageBuffers = [];
      for (const filePath of pageFiles) {
        const buf = await sharp(filePath).resize({ width: this.width }).png().toBuffer();
        pageBuffers.push(buf);
      }

      const allBuffers = [metadataImage, ...pageBuffers];
      const metas = await Promise.all(allBuffers.map((b) => sharp(b).metadata()));
      const totalHeight = metas.reduce((sum, m) => sum + m.height, 0);

      await sharp({
        create: {
          width: this.width,
          height: totalHeight,
          channels: 4,
          background: { r: 255, g: 255, b: 255, alpha: 1 },
        },
      })
        .composite(
          allBuffers.map((input, i) => ({
            input,
            top: metas.slice(0, i).reduce((acc, meta) => acc + meta.height, 0),
            left: 0,
          }))
        )
        .png()
        .toFile(outputPath);

      pageFiles.forEach((file) => fs.unlinkSync(file));
      return path.basename(outputPath);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error converting PDF to image:", error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  pdfToPngPages(pdfBuffer, outputDir) {
    const timeStamp = Date.now();
    const pdfPath = path.join(outputDir, `temp_${timeStamp}.pdf`);
    fs.writeFileSync(pdfPath, pdfBuffer);

    const outputPrefix = path.join(outputDir, `pdfpages_${timeStamp}`);
    execSync(`pdftoppm -png -r 200 "${pdfPath}" "${outputPrefix}"`);

    const allFiles = fs.readdirSync(outputDir);
    const pageFiles = allFiles
      .filter((f) => f.startsWith(path.basename(outputPrefix)) && f.endsWith(".png"))
      .map((f) => path.join(outputDir, f));

    fs.unlinkSync(pdfPath);
    return pageFiles;
  }

  async createMetadataHeader(metadata) {
    const height = 200;
    const from = escapeXML(metadata.from || "N/A");
    const to = escapeXML(metadata.to || "N/A");
    const date = escapeXML(metadata.date || "N/A");
    const subject = escapeXML(metadata.subject || "N/A");

    const svg = `
      <svg width="${this.width}" height="${height}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
        <rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="#f0f0f0"/>
        <text x="40" y="50" font-family="Arial" font-size="32">From: ${from}</text>
        <text x="40" y="90" font-family="Arial" font-size="32">To: ${to}</text>
        <text x="40" y="130" font-family="Arial" font-size="32">Date: ${date}</text>
        <text x="40" y="170" font-family="Arial" font-size="32">Subject: ${subject}</text>
      </svg>
    `;

    try {
      return await sharp(Buffer.from(svg)).png().toBuffer();
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error creating metadata header SVG:", err);
      throw err;
    }
  }

  async combineImagesVertically(imagePaths, metadata, finalOutputPath) {
    try {
      const metadataImage = await this.createMetadataHeader(metadata);
      const buffers = [metadataImage];

      for (const imgPath of imagePaths) {
        buffers.push(fs.readFileSync(imgPath));
      }

      const metas = await Promise.all(buffers.map((buf) => sharp(buf).metadata()));
      const totalHeight = metas.reduce((acc, meta) => acc + meta.height, 0);

      await sharp({
        create: {
          width: this.width,
          height: totalHeight,
          channels: 4,
          background: { r: 255, g: 255, b: 255, alpha: 1 },
        },
      })
        .composite(
          buffers.map((input, i) => ({
            input,
            top: metas.slice(0, i).reduce((sum, m) => sum + m.height, 0),
            left: 0,
          }))
        )
        .png()
        .toFile(finalOutputPath);

      return finalOutputPath;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error combining images vertically:", err);
      throw err;
    }
  }

  async convertAttachmentsToSingleImage(
    attachments,
    emailMetadata,
    organizationId,
    finalOutputPath,
    attachmentService
  ) {
    try {
      const convertedImagePaths = [];

      for (const att of attachments) {
        const uniqueName = `${Date.now()}_${att.filename}`;

        if (att.mimeType === "application/pdf") {
          const buffer = Buffer.from(att.data, "base64");
          const tempOutputPath = path.join(
            process.cwd(),
            "server",
            "uploads",
            organizationId,
            "receipts",
            `pdf_${uniqueName}.png`
          );
          await this.convertPDFToImage(buffer, emailMetadata, tempOutputPath);
          convertedImagePaths.push(tempOutputPath);
        } else if (att.mimeType.startsWith("image/")) {
          const buffer = Buffer.from(att.data, "base64");
          const savedPath = attachmentService.saveAttachment(buffer, att.filename, organizationId);
          convertedImagePaths.push(savedPath);
        }
      }

      if (!convertedImagePaths.length) {
        throw new Error("No valid PDF or image attachments to convert.");
      }

      await this.combineImagesVertically(
        convertedImagePaths,
        emailMetadata,
        finalOutputPath
      );

      return finalOutputPath;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error in convertAttachmentsToSingleImage:", error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async convertHtmlDocumentToPdf(htmlContent, outputPath, authCookie) {
    try {
      const PAGE_BREAK_MARKER = "<!--PAGE_BREAK-->";
      const pagesHtml = htmlContent
        .split(PAGE_BREAK_MARKER)
        .map((p) => p.trim())
        .filter(Boolean);

      if (!pagesHtml.length) {
        throw new Error("No valid pages found in HTML content.");
      }

      const API_URL = process.env.API_URL;
      const SERVER_PUBLIC_URL = process.env.SERVER_PUBLIC_URL;
      const baseURL = SERVER_PUBLIC_URL || API_URL || undefined;

      const injectedStyles = `
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="/global.css" />
        <style>
          @page { size: 8.5in 11in; margin: 48px; }
          .page-container { width: 8.5in; height: 11in; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background: #fff; }
          table { border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; }
          table, th, td { border: 0px dotted #e5e7eb; }
          img { max-width: 100%; height: auto; }
        </style>`;

      const executablePath = findAvailableChromiumExecutable();
      const browser = await chromium.launch({
        headless: true,
        ...(executablePath ? { executablePath } : {}),
        args: ["--no-sandbox", "--disable-setuid-sandbox"],
      });
      const context = await browser.newContext({
        viewport: { width: 816, height: 1056 },
        deviceScaleFactor: 1,
        baseURL,
        bypassCSP: true,
      });

      await context.setExtraHTTPHeaders({ "x-internal-request": "true" });

      await context.route("**/*", (route) => {
        const type = route.request().resourceType();
        const url = route.request().url();
        if (type === "font" || url.includes("analytics")) return route.abort();
        route.continue();
      });

      const pdfBuffers = [];

      for (const pageHtml of pagesHtml) {
        const fullHtml = `<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8">${injectedStyles}</head><body><div class="page-container">${pageHtml}</div></body></html>`;
        const page = await context.newPage();
        page.setDefaultNavigationTimeout(60_000);

        await page.setContent(fullHtml, {
          waitUntil: "networkidle",
          timeout: 60_000,
        });

        await page.evaluate(async () => {
          const imgs = Array.from(document.images || []);
          await Promise.all(
            imgs.map((img) => {
              if (img.complete) return Promise.resolve();
              return new Promise((resolve) => {
                img.onload = img.onerror = () => resolve();
              });
            })
          );
        });

        const pdfBuffer = await page.pdf({
          printBackground: true,
          preferCSSPageSize: true,
          scale: 1,
        });

        pdfBuffers.push(pdfBuffer);
        await page.close();
      }

      await context.close();
      await browser.close();

      const mergedPdf = await PDFDocument.create();
      for (const buf of pdfBuffers) {
        const pdf = await PDFDocument.load(buf);
        const copied = await mergedPdf.copyPages(pdf, pdf.getPageIndices());
        copied.forEach((cp) => mergedPdf.addPage(cp));
      }

      const mergedBytes = await mergedPdf.save();
      fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, mergedBytes);
      return outputPath;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Error converting HTML to PDF:", error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async extractTextFromPDF(buffer) {
    try {
      const data = await pdfParse(buffer);
      return data.text;
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error extracting text from PDF:", err);
      throw err;
    }
  }

  async applyEditsToPdf({ inputPath, outputPath, edits, uploadsBase, orgId }) {
    const inputBytes = fs.readFileSync(inputPath);
    const pdf = await PDFDocument.load(inputBytes, {
      ignoreEncryption: true,
      updateMetadata: false,
    });

    const helvetica = await pdf.embedFont(StandardFonts.Helvetica);

    const pageSizes = (edits.pageSizes || []).reduce((acc, page) => {
      acc[page.pageIndex] = page;
      return acc;
    }, {});

    const items = Array.isArray(edits.items) ? edits.items : [];
    const formValues = edits.formValues || {};
    const flattenForms = edits.flattenForms !== false;

    const pxToPt = (px, axis, pageIndex) => {
      const size = pageSizes[pageIndex];
      if (!size) return px;

      const scale =
        axis === "x"
          ? size.widthPt / size.widthPx
          : size.heightPt / size.heightPx;

      return px * scale;
    };

    try {
      const form = pdf.getForm();
      const fields = form.getFields();

      for (const field of fields) {
        const name = field.getName();

        if (!(name in formValues)) continue;

        const value = formValues[name];

        try {
          if (field instanceof PDFTextField) {
            field.setText(value == null ? "" : String(value));
          } else if (field instanceof PDFCheckBox) {
            if (normalizeBoolean(value)) {
              field.check();
            } else {
              field.uncheck();
            }
          } else if (field instanceof PDFRadioGroup) {
            if (value != null && String(value).trim()) {
              field.select(String(value));
            }
          } else if (field instanceof PDFDropdown) {
            if (value == null || String(value).trim() === "") {
              try {
                field.clear();
              } catch {}
            } else {
              field.select(String(value));
            }
          } else if (field instanceof PDFOptionList) {
            if (value == null || String(value).trim() === "") {
              try {
                field.clear();
              } catch {}
            } else {
              field.select(String(value));
            }
          }
        } catch (fieldErr) {
          console.warn(`Failed applying form value for field "${name}":`, fieldErr.message);
        }
      }

      try {
        form.updateFieldAppearances(helvetica);
      } catch (appearanceErr) {
        console.warn("Could not update field appearances:", appearanceErr.message);
      }

      if (flattenForms) {
        try {
          form.flatten();
        } catch (flattenErr) {
          console.warn("Could not flatten form:", flattenErr.message);
        }
      }
    } catch (formErr) {
      console.warn("No editable form found or form processing failed:", formErr.message);
    }

    for (const item of items) {
      const page = pdf.getPage(item.pageIndex);
      if (!page) continue;

      const size =
        pageSizes[item.pageIndex] || {
          widthPt: page.getWidth(),
          heightPt: page.getHeight(),
          widthPx: page.getWidth(),
          heightPx: page.getHeight(),
        };

      if (item.type === "rect") {
        const x = pxToPt(item.x, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const width = pxToPt(item.width, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const height = pxToPt(item.height, "y", item.pageIndex);
        const y = size.heightPt - pxToPt(item.y + item.height, "y", item.pageIndex);

        page.drawRectangle({
          x,
          y,
          width,
          height,
          color: parseColor(item.fill || "#FFFFFF"),
        });

        continue;
      }

      if (item.type === "text") {
        const boxX = pxToPt(item.x, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const boxWidth = pxToPt(item.width, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const boxHeight = pxToPt(item.height, "y", item.pageIndex);
        const boxTop = size.heightPt - pxToPt(item.y, "y", item.pageIndex);
        const boxBottom = boxTop - boxHeight;

        const paddingX = Math.max(1.5, pxToPt(6, "x", item.pageIndex));
        const paddingTop = Math.max(1.5, pxToPt(6, "y", item.pageIndex));
        const fontSize = Math.max(6, pxToPt(item.fontSizePx || 16, "y", item.pageIndex));
        const lineHeight = fontSize * 1.2;
        const maxTextWidth = Math.max(10, boxWidth - paddingX * 2);
        const lines = wrapTextToLines(item.text || "", helvetica, fontSize, maxTextWidth);
        const textColor = parseColor(item.color || "#000000");
        const align = item.align || "left";

        for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i += 1) {
          const line = lines[i];
          const textWidth = helvetica.widthOfTextAtSize(line, fontSize);
          const y = boxTop - paddingTop - fontSize - i * lineHeight;

          if (y < boxBottom + paddingTop) {
            break;
          }

          let x = boxX + paddingX;
          if (align === "center") {
            x = boxX + (boxWidth - textWidth) / 2;
          } else if (align === "right") {
            x = boxX + boxWidth - paddingX - textWidth;
          }

          page.drawText(line, {
            x,
            y,
            size: fontSize,
            font: helvetica,
            color: textColor,
          });
        }

        continue;
      }

      if (item.type === "image") {
        const resolved = await resolveImageBytes(item, uploadsBase, orgId);
        if (!resolved?.buffer) continue;

        const embedded = await embedImageForPdf(pdf, resolved.buffer, resolved.hint);

        const x = pxToPt(item.x, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const width = pxToPt(item.width, "x", item.pageIndex);
        const height = pxToPt(item.height, "y", item.pageIndex);
        const y = size.heightPt - pxToPt(item.y + item.height, "y", item.pageIndex);

        page.drawImage(embedded, {
          x,
          y,
          width,
          height,
        });
      }
    }

    const out = await pdf.save();
    fs.writeFileSync(outputPath, out);
    return outputPath;
  }
}

export default PDFService;

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptCRUDService.js
// server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptCRUDService.js

import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import { parseISO, isValid } from 'date-fns';

class ReceiptCRUDService {
  async listReceipts(userId) {
    return prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: { userId },
      include: { items: true },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async getReceiptById(receiptId) {
    return prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      include: { items: true },
    });
  }

  async addOrUpdateReceipt(data) {
    const { id, items, userId, organizationId, text, date, total, hst, ...rest } = data;

    const userConnect = userId ? { connect: { id: userId } } : undefined;
    const orgConnect = organizationId ? { connect: { id: organizationId } } : undefined;
    const itemsToCreate = { create: items || [] };

    let parsedDate = null;
    if (date) {
      parsedDate = parseISO(date);
      if (!isValid(parsedDate)) {
        parsedDate = null;
      }
    }

    if (id) {
      return prisma.receipt.update({
        where: { id },
        data: {
          ...rest,
          text,
          date: parsedDate,
          total,
          hst,
          user: userConnect,
          organization: orgConnect,
          items: {
            deleteMany: {},
            ...itemsToCreate,
          },
        },
        include: { items: true },
      });
    } else {
      return prisma.receipt.create({
        data: {
          ...rest,
          text,
          date: parsedDate,
          total,
          hst,
          user: userConnect,
          organization: orgConnect,
          items: itemsToCreate,
        },
        include: { items: true },
      });
    }
  }

  async removeReceiptById(id) {
    return prisma.receipt.delete({
      where: { id },
      include: { items: true },
    });
  }

  async removeReceiptByImg(imgName, userId) {
    return prisma.receipt.deleteMany({
      where: { imgName, userId },
    });
  }
}

export default ReceiptCRUDService;

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptImageProcessor.js
import sharp from 'sharp';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import heicConvert from 'heic-convert';

const HEIC_EXTENSIONS = new Set(['.heic', '.heif']);

export function isHeicFile(filePath) {
  return HEIC_EXTENSIONS.has(path.extname(filePath).toLowerCase());
}

export async function convertHeicToJpeg(inputPath) {
  const dir = path.dirname(inputPath);
  const base = path.basename(inputPath, path.extname(inputPath));
  const outputPath = path.join(dir, `${base}.jpg`);

  const inputBuffer = await fs.promises.readFile(inputPath);
  const jpegBuffer = await heicConvert({
    buffer: inputBuffer,
    format: 'JPEG',
    quality: 0.9,
  });
  await fs.promises.writeFile(outputPath, jpegBuffer);

  return outputPath;
}

export async function assertReadableImage(inputPath) {
  const resolvedPath = path.resolve(inputPath);

  if (!fs.existsSync(resolvedPath)) {
    throw new Error(`Input image not found: ${resolvedPath}`);
  }

  try {
    const metadata = await sharp(resolvedPath).metadata();
    if (!metadata?.format || !metadata?.width || !metadata?.height) {
      throw new Error('Image metadata is missing dimensions.');
    }
    return metadata;
  } catch (error) {
    const invalidImageError = new Error('Uploaded file could not be read as an image.');
    invalidImageError.cause = error;
    invalidImageError.code = 'INVALID_IMAGE_UPLOAD';
    throw invalidImageError;
  }
}

function buildOutputPath(inputPath, suffix) {
  const dir = path.dirname(inputPath);
  const ext = '.jpg';
  const base = path.basename(inputPath, path.extname(inputPath));
  return path.join(dir, `${base}-${suffix}-${Date.now()}${ext}`);
}

function clampInteger(value, min, max) {
  return Math.min(Math.max(Math.round(Number(value) || 0), min), max);
}

function normalizeMaxWidth(value) {
  const parsed = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(parsed) || parsed <= 0) return null;
  return Math.round(parsed);
}

function sanitizeCrop(crop, metadata) {
  if (!crop || typeof crop !== 'object') return null;

  const left = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(crop.left) || 0));
  const top = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(crop.top) || 0));
  const width = Math.round(Number(crop.width) || 0);
  const height = Math.round(Number(crop.height) || 0);

  if (!metadata?.width || !metadata?.height) return null;
  if (width <= 0 || height <= 0) return null;
  if (left >= metadata.width || top >= metadata.height) return null;

  const boundedWidth = Math.min(width, metadata.width - left);
  const boundedHeight = Math.min(height, metadata.height - top);

  if (boundedWidth <= 0 || boundedHeight <= 0) return null;

  return {
    left,
    top,
    width: boundedWidth,
    height: boundedHeight,
  };
}

function ensureDifferentPaths(inputPath, outputPath) {
  const normalizedInput = path.resolve(inputPath);
  const normalizedOutput = path.resolve(outputPath);

  if (normalizedInput === normalizedOutput) {
    throw new Error('Cannot use same file for input and output');
  }
}

export async function getReceiptImageInfo(imagePath) {
  const resolvedPath = path.resolve(imagePath);

  if (!fs.existsSync(resolvedPath)) {
    return null;
  }

  const stats = await fs.promises.stat(resolvedPath);
  const metadata = await sharp(resolvedPath).metadata();

  return {
    path: resolvedPath,
    sizeBytes: stats.size,
    sizeKB: Number((stats.size / 1024).toFixed(2)),
    width: metadata.width || null,
    height: metadata.height || null,
    format: metadata.format || null,
  };
}

export async function generateReceiptOptimizationCandidates(imagePath, options = {}) {
  const inputPath = path.resolve(imagePath);

  if (!fs.existsSync(inputPath)) {
    throw new Error(`Input image not found: ${inputPath}`);
  }

  const outputDir = path.resolve(options.outputDir || path.dirname(inputPath));
  await fs.promises.mkdir(outputDir, { recursive: true });

  const base = path.basename(inputPath, path.extname(inputPath)).replace(/[^a-z0-9._-]/gi, '-');
  const runId = options.runId || Date.now();
  const padding = clampInteger(options.cropPadding ?? 18, 0, 80);
  const maxWidth = normalizeMaxWidth(options.maxWidth || 1800);
  const originalStats = await fs.promises.stat(inputPath);
  const originalMetadata = await sharp(inputPath).metadata();

  const profileMap = {
    'jpeg-high': {
      cropped: false,
      quality: 82,
      grayscale: false,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 0.8,
      chromaSubsampling: '4:2:0',
    },
    'jpeg-medium': {
      cropped: false,
      quality: 68,
      grayscale: false,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 0.9,
      chromaSubsampling: '4:2:0',
    },
    'grayscale-sharp': {
      cropped: false,
      quality: 76,
      grayscale: true,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 1.1,
      chromaSubsampling: '4:4:4',
    },
    'bw-audit': {
      cropped: false,
      quality: 84,
      grayscale: true,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 1.25,
      linear: [1.05, -5],
      chromaSubsampling: '4:4:4',
    },
    'cropped-jpeg-medium': {
      cropped: true,
      quality: 70,
      grayscale: false,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 0.9,
      chromaSubsampling: '4:2:0',
    },
    'cropped-grayscale-sharp': {
      cropped: true,
      quality: 76,
      grayscale: true,
      normalise: true,
      sharpen: 1.1,
      chromaSubsampling: '4:4:4',
    },
  };

  const requestedProfiles = Array.isArray(options.profiles) && options.profiles.length
    ? options.profiles
    : Object.keys(profileMap);

  const candidates = [];

  for (const profile of requestedProfiles) {
    const config = profileMap[profile];
    if (!config) continue;

    const outputPath = path.join(outputDir, `${base}-${profile}-${runId}.jpg`);
    let pipeline = sharp(inputPath).rotate().flatten({ background: '#ffffff' });

    if (maxWidth) {
      pipeline = pipeline.resize({
        width: maxWidth,
        height: maxWidth * 3,
        fit: 'inside',
        withoutEnlargement: true,
      });
    }

    if (config.cropped) {
      pipeline = pipeline
        .trim({
          threshold: 24,
          background: { r: 255, g: 255, b: 255 },
        })
        .extend({
          top: padding,
          bottom: padding,
          left: padding,
          right: padding,
          background: '#ffffff',
        });
    }

    if (config.grayscale) {
      pipeline = pipeline.grayscale();
    }

    if (config.normalise) {
      pipeline = pipeline.normalise();
    }

    if (config.sharpen) {
      pipeline = pipeline.sharpen({ sigma: config.sharpen });
    }

    if (config.linear) {
      pipeline = pipeline.linear(config.linear[0], config.linear[1]);
    }

    await pipeline
      .jpeg({
        quality: config.quality,
        mozjpeg: true,
        chromaSubsampling: config.chromaSubsampling,
      })
      .toFile(outputPath);

    const stats = await fs.promises.stat(outputPath);
    const metadata = await sharp(outputPath).metadata();
    const areaRatio =
      originalMetadata.width && originalMetadata.height && metadata.width && metadata.height
        ? (metadata.width * metadata.height) / (originalMetadata.width * originalMetadata.height)
        : null;

    candidates.push({
      profile,
      outputPath,
      outputFilename: path.basename(outputPath),
      sizeBytes: stats.size,
      savedBytes: originalStats.size - stats.size,
      width: metadata.width || null,
      height: metadata.height || null,
      format: metadata.format || 'jpeg',
      autoCropApplied: config.cropped,
      cropReport: config.cropped
        ? {
            method: 'sharp-trim-white-background',
            padding,
            areaRatio,
            rejectedByGeometry:
              areaRatio !== null && (areaRatio < 0.2 || areaRatio > 1.2),
          }
        : null,
    });
  }

  return candidates;
}

export async function processReceiptImageAdvanced(imagePath, operation = 'auto', options = {}) {
  const inputPath = path.resolve(imagePath);

  if (!fs.existsSync(inputPath)) {
    throw new Error(`Input image not found: ${inputPath}`);
  }

  const outputPath = path.resolve(
    options.outputPath || buildOutputPath(inputPath, operation.replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/gi, '-'))
  );

  ensureDifferentPaths(inputPath, outputPath);
  await fs.promises.mkdir(path.dirname(outputPath), { recursive: true });

  const originalStats = await fs.promises.stat(inputPath);
  const originalSizeBytes = originalStats.size;

  const metadata = await sharp(inputPath).metadata();
  const crop = sanitizeCrop(options.crop, metadata);

  let pipeline = sharp(inputPath).rotate();

  if (crop) {
    pipeline = pipeline.extract(crop);
  } else if (operation === 'auto-crop') {
    pipeline = pipeline.trim({
      threshold: 18,
      background: { r: 255, g: 255, b: 255 },
    });
  }

  switch (operation) {
    case 'manual-crop':
    case 'auto-crop': {
      pipeline = pipeline
        .flatten({ background: '#ffffff' })
        .jpeg({
          quality: 90,
          mozjpeg: true,
          chromaSubsampling: '4:4:4',
        });
      break;
    }

    case 'compress': {
      pipeline = pipeline
        .flatten({ background: '#ffffff' })
        .jpeg({
          quality: 65,
          mozjpeg: true,
          chromaSubsampling: '4:2:0',
        });
      break;
    }

    case 'bw': {
      pipeline = pipeline
        .flatten({ background: '#ffffff' })
        .grayscale()
        .normalise()
        .sharpen({ sigma: 1.2 })
        .linear(1.05, -5)
        .jpeg({
          quality: 82,
          mozjpeg: true,
          chromaSubsampling: '4:4:4',
        });
      break;
    }

    case 'auto':
    default: {
      pipeline = pipeline
        .flatten({ background: '#ffffff' })
        .normalise()
        .sharpen({ sigma: 1.1 })
        .jpeg({
          quality: 78,
          mozjpeg: true,
          chromaSubsampling: '4:2:0',
        });
      break;
    }
  }

  await pipeline.toFile(outputPath);

  const processedStats = await fs.promises.stat(outputPath);
  const processedMetadata = await sharp(outputPath).metadata();

  return {
    success: true,
    operation,
    outputPath,
    outputFilename: path.basename(outputPath),
    originalSizeBytes,
    processedSizeBytes: processedStats.size,
    cropApplied: !!crop,
    width: processedMetadata.width || null,
    height: processedMetadata.height || null,
    format: processedMetadata.format || 'jpeg',
  };
}

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptImageVariantService.js
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import AttachmentService from './AttachmentService.js';

class ReceiptImageVariantService {
  constructor() {
    this.attachmentService = new AttachmentService();
  }

  getVariantDir(organizationId, variantType = 'previews') {
    return path.join(
      this.attachmentService.getReceiptUploadsDir(organizationId),
      variantType
    );
  }

  getVariantRelativePath(variantType, fileName) {
    return `receipts/${variantType}/${path.basename(fileName)}`;
  }

  ensureVariantDir(organizationId, variantType = 'previews') {
    const dir = this.getVariantDir(organizationId, variantType);
    fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
    return dir;
  }

  resolveReceiptPath(receipt) {
    const relativePath = this.attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
    return this.attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
      receipt.organizationId,
      relativePath,
      receipt.imgName
    );
  }

  getMetadata(filePath) {
    return this.attachmentService.getFileMetadata(filePath);
  }

  async promotePreviewToOptimized(receipt, previewRelativePath) {
    const previewPath = this.attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
      receipt.organizationId,
      previewRelativePath
    );

    if (!fs.existsSync(previewPath)) {
      throw new Error('Optimization preview image not found.');
    }

    const previewsDir = path.resolve(this.getVariantDir(receipt.organizationId, 'previews'));
    if (!path.resolve(previewPath).startsWith(`${previewsDir}${path.sep}`)) {
      throw new Error('Only receipt optimization previews can be promoted.');
    }

    const optimizedDir = this.ensureVariantDir(receipt.organizationId, 'optimized');
    const optimizedPath = path.join(optimizedDir, path.basename(previewPath));

    if (path.resolve(previewPath) !== path.resolve(optimizedPath)) {
      await fs.promises.rename(previewPath, optimizedPath);
    }

    return {
      absolutePath: optimizedPath,
      relativePath: this.getVariantRelativePath('optimized', path.basename(optimizedPath)),
      imgName: path.basename(optimizedPath),
      metadata: this.getMetadata(optimizedPath),
    };
  }

  discardPreview(receipt, previewRelativePath) {
    const previewPath = this.attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
      receipt.organizationId,
      previewRelativePath
    );

    const previewsDir = path.resolve(this.getVariantDir(receipt.organizationId, 'previews'));
    const previewPathResolved = path.resolve(previewPath);

    if (!previewPathResolved.startsWith(`${previewsDir}${path.sep}`)) {
      throw new Error('Only receipt optimization previews can be discarded.');
    }

    if (fs.existsSync(previewPathResolved)) {
      fs.unlinkSync(previewPathResolved);
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }
}

export default ReceiptImageVariantService;

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptImportService.js
import EmailService from "#services/email/services/EmailService.js";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs";
import AttachmentService from "./AttachmentService.js";
import EmailAttachmentService from "#services/email/services/AttachmentService.js";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import moment from 'moment';

const RECEIPT_HINTS_OPEN = '[receipt_hints]';
const RECEIPT_HINTS_CLOSE = '[/receipt_hints]';

class ReceiptImportService {
  constructor(dependencies = {}) {
    const {
      pdfService = null,
      llmService = null,
      receiptCRUDService = null,
      textConverter = null,
    } = dependencies || {};

    this.prisma = prisma;
    this.pdfService = pdfService;
    this.llmService = llmService;
    this.receiptCRUDService = receiptCRUDService;
    this.textConverter = textConverter;
    this.attachmentService = new AttachmentService();
  }

  assertImportDependencies() {
    const missing = [];
    if (!this.pdfService) missing.push('pdfService');
    if (!this.llmService) missing.push('llmService');
    if (!this.receiptCRUDService) missing.push('receiptCRUDService');
    if (!this.textConverter) missing.push('textConverter');

    if (missing.length > 0) {
      throw new Error(
        `ReceiptImportService is missing required dependencies for importReceiptFromEmail: ${missing.join(', ')}`
      );
    }
  }

  normalizePositiveTax(value) {
    if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return null;
    const numericValue = Number(value);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numericValue)) return null;
    return Math.abs(Number(numericValue.toFixed(2)));
  }

  normalizeMoney(value) {
    if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return null;
    const numericValue = Number(value);
    if (!Number.isFinite(numericValue)) return null;
    return Number(numericValue.toFixed(2));
  }

  normalizeVendor(value) {
    return String(value || '')
      .toLowerCase()
      .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, ' ')
      .trim();
  }

  mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(existingNotes, hints) {
    const base = String(existingNotes || '')
      .replace(/\[receipt_hints\][\s\S]*?\[\/receipt_hints\]/g, '')
      .trim();

    const serialized = JSON.stringify(hints);
    return `${base}${base ? '\n' : ''}${RECEIPT_HINTS_OPEN}${serialized}${RECEIPT_HINTS_CLOSE}`.trim();
  }

  buildReceiptBackedHints({ extracted, contentSource, fileName }) {
    return {
      normalizedVendor: this.normalizeVendor(extracted?.companyName),
      extractedTax: this.normalizePositiveTax(extracted?.hst),
      taxConfidence: extracted?.hst != null ? 'RECEIPT_IMPORTED' : 'UNKNOWN',
      suggestedExpenseAccount: null,
      suggestedStatementLine: null,
      matchConfidence: null,
      needsReview: true,
      contentSource,
      fileName,
    };
  }

  async importReceiptFromEmail(emailId, sessionId, organizationId, user) {
    try {
      this.assertImportDependencies();

      if (!emailId) {
        throw new Error("Email ID is required.");
      }
      if (!user || !user.id) {
        throw new Error("User information is missing or invalid.");
      }

      const email = await this.prisma.email.findUnique({
        where: { id: emailId },
        include: {
          account: {
            include: {
              user: { include: { organization: true } }
            }
          }
        }
      });

      if (!email) {
        throw new Error("Email not found.");
      }

      const messageId = email.providerId;

      const [emailData, attachments] = await Promise.all([
        EmailService.fetchEmailContent({
          emailAccountId: email.account.id,
          messageId,
          rawOnly: true
        }),
        EmailService.getAttachments(email.account.id, messageId)
      ]);

      const emailContent = emailData.body;
      let fileName = null;
      let contentSource = "unknown";
      let extracted;

      const emailMetadata = {
        from: email.sender,
        to: email.recipients,
        date: email.date.toISOString(),
        subject: email.subject
      };

      if (attachments?.length) {
        const att = attachments[0];
        let rawAttachment;

        try {
          rawAttachment = await EmailAttachmentService.getAttachmentByFilename(
            email.account.id,
            messageId,
            att.filename
          );
        } catch (err) {
          console.warn(
            `[importReceiptFromEmail] Failed to fetch attachment by filename (${att.filename}). Falling back to attachment ID. Error: ${err.message}`
          );
          rawAttachment = await EmailService.getAttachment(
            email.account.id,
            messageId,
            att.attachmentId
          );
        }

        const attBuffer = Buffer.from(rawAttachment.data, "base64");
        const fileExt = att.filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();

        if (
          att.mimeType === "application/pdf" ||
          (att.mimeType === "application/octet-stream" && fileExt === "pdf")
        ) {
          const savedPdfPath = this.attachmentService.saveAttachment(
            attBuffer,
            att.filename,
            organizationId
          );
          fileName = path.basename(savedPdfPath);
          const filePath = `/uploads/${organizationId}/receipts/${fileName}`;
          contentSource = "attachment-pdf";

          const pdfText = await this.pdfService.extractTextFromPDF(attBuffer);
          extracted = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromText(
            pdfText,
            fileName,
            user.id,
            sessionId
          );
          extracted.filePath = filePath;
        } else if (
          att.mimeType === "text/plain" ||
          (att.mimeType === "application/octet-stream" && fileExt === "txt")
        ) {
          const savedTextPath = this.attachmentService.saveAttachment(
            attBuffer,
            att.filename,
            organizationId
          );
          fileName = path.basename(savedTextPath);
          const filePath = `/uploads/${organizationId}/receipts/${fileName}`;
          contentSource = "attachment-text";

          const plainText = attBuffer.toString("utf-8");
          extracted = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromText(
            plainText,
            fileName,
            user.id,
            sessionId
          );
          extracted.filePath = filePath;
        } else if (
          att.mimeType.startsWith("image/") ||
          (att.mimeType === "application/octet-stream" &&
            ["jpg", "jpeg", "png", "bmp", "gif"].includes(fileExt))
        ) {
          const savedImagePath = this.attachmentService.saveAttachment(
            attBuffer,
            att.filename,
            organizationId
          );
          fileName = path.basename(savedImagePath);
          contentSource = "attachment-image";
          extracted = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromImage(
            savedImagePath,
            fileName,
            user.id,
            sessionId
          );
        } else if (att.mimeType === "application/octet-stream") {
          throw new Error(
            `Unsupported attachment MIME type: ${att.mimeType} for file ${att.filename}`
          );
        } else {
          throw new Error(`Unsupported attachment MIME type: ${att.mimeType}`);
        }
      } else if (emailContent) {
        const filename = `receipt_text_${Date.now()}.txt`;
        const uploadDir = path.join(
          process.cwd(),
          "uploads",
          organizationId,
          "receipts"
        );

        if (!fs.existsSync(uploadDir)) {
          fs.mkdirSync(uploadDir, { recursive: true });
        }

        const outputPath = path.join(uploadDir, filename);
        let generatedFileName;

        if (emailContent.htmlText && emailContent.htmlText.trim()) {
          generatedFileName = await this.textConverter.convertHtmlToImage(
            emailContent.htmlText,
            emailMetadata,
            outputPath
          );
          contentSource = "html";
        } else if (emailContent.plainText && emailContent.plainText.trim()) {
          generatedFileName = await this.textConverter.convertTextToImage(
            emailContent.plainText,
            emailMetadata,
            outputPath
          );
          contentSource = "text";
        } else {
          throw new Error("No valid content found in email");
        }

        fileName = generatedFileName;
        const filePath = `/uploads/${organizationId}/receipts/${generatedFileName}`;

        const receiptFilePath = path.join(
          process.cwd(),
          "uploads",
          organizationId,
          "receipts",
          fileName
        );

        extracted = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromImage(
          receiptFilePath,
          fileName,
          user.id,
          sessionId
        );
        extracted.filePath = filePath;
      }

      if (!fileName) {
        throw new Error("Failed to create receipt file");
      }

      if (
        !extracted.date ||
        (typeof extracted.date === "string" &&
          (extracted.date.trim().toLowerCase() === "na" || extracted.date.trim().toLowerCase() === "n/a"))
      ) {
        extracted.date = email.date;
      }

      const parsedDate = moment(extracted.date, "MM/DD/YYYY", true);
      if (!parsedDate.isValid()) {
        extracted.date = moment(email.date).toISOString();
      } else {
        extracted.date = parsedDate.toISOString();
      }

      extracted.total = this.normalizeMoney(extracted.total);
      extracted.hst = this.normalizePositiveTax(
        extracted.hst ?? extracted.tax ?? extracted.taxes
      );
      extracted.companyName = String(extracted.companyName || '').trim();

      const receiptHints = this.buildReceiptBackedHints({
        extracted,
        contentSource,
        fileName,
      });

      const metaNotes = `${extracted.notes || ""}\nImported from email: ${emailMetadata.subject}\nSource: ${contentSource}`.trim();
      extracted.notes = this.mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(metaNotes, receiptHints);

      const savedReceipt = await this.receiptCRUDService.addOrUpdateReceipt({
        date: extracted.date,
        companyName: extracted.companyName,
        total: extracted.total,
        hst: extracted.hst,
        notes: extracted.notes,
        items: extracted.items || [],
        userId: user.id,
        organizationId: user.organization.id,
        ...(contentSource === "attachment-pdf" ||
        contentSource === "attachment-text" ||
        contentSource === "html" ||
        contentSource === "text"
          ? { filePath: extracted.filePath }
          : { imgName: fileName }),
        text: extracted.text
      });

      try {
        const { default: ReceiptMatchingService } = await import('#services/receipt/services/ReceiptMatchingService.js');
        const receiptMatchingService = new ReceiptMatchingService(this.receiptCRUDService);
        const matchResult = await receiptMatchingService.autoMatchSingleReceipt(savedReceipt.id);
        console.log(`Auto-match result for receipt ${savedReceipt.id}:`, matchResult);
        savedReceipt.autoMatch = matchResult;
      } catch (autoMatchError) {
        console.warn(`Auto-match failed for receipt ${savedReceipt.id}: ${autoMatchError.message}`);
        savedReceipt.autoMatch = { error: autoMatchError.message };
      }

      savedReceipt.receiptBackedHints = receiptHints;
      return savedReceipt;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("importReceiptFromEmail Error:", {
        emailId,
        organizationId,
        error: error.message,
        stack: error.stack
      });
      throw new Error(`Failed to import receipt: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }
}

export default ReceiptImportService;

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService.js
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import OpenRouterProvider from '#integrations/ai/providers/openrouter.js';

const SYSTEM_PROMPT = `You are an audit-receipt image reviewer.
You are given a compressed or cropped receipt image and the original OCR text extracted before compression.
Your only job: judge whether the compressed image is still legible for accounting audit purposes.
Focus on merchant name, date, total amount, and tax amount.
Return raw JSON only — no markdown, no explanation.`;

function buildPrompt(originalOcrText, receipt) {
  const known = [];
  if (receipt.companyName) known.push(`Merchant: ${receipt.companyName}`);
  if (receipt.total != null) known.push(`Total: ${receipt.total}`);
  if (receipt.hst != null) known.push(`Tax/HST: ${receipt.hst}`);
  if (receipt.date) known.push(`Date: ${String(receipt.date).slice(0, 10)}`);

  return `Examine this compressed receipt image for audit legibility.

Known audit fields extracted from the original:
${known.length ? known.join('\n') : '(no structured data extracted yet)'}

Original OCR text (first 2000 chars):
${String(originalOcrText || '').slice(0, 2000)}

Can each audit-critical field still be read in this compressed image?

Return exactly this JSON shape and nothing else:
{
  "pass": true,
  "confidence": 0.92,
  "criticalIssues": [],
  "readableFields": {
    "merchant": true,
    "date": true,
    "total": true,
    "tax": true
  },
  "summary": "All audit fields remain clearly legible after compression."
}

Valid criticalIssues codes: merchant_missing, date_missing, total_missing, tax_missing, image_too_dark, image_blurry, text_unreadable.
Set pass to false if any audit-critical field cannot be confirmed readable.`;
}

function parseJson(text) {
  const clean = String(text || '')
    .trim()
    .replace(/^```[a-z]*\s*/i, '')
    .replace(/\s*```$/i, '')
    .trim();

  try {
    return JSON.parse(clean);
  } catch {
    const match = clean.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
    if (match) {
      try {
        return JSON.parse(match[0]);
      } catch {
        // fall through
      }
    }
    return {};
  }
}

class ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService {
  constructor() {
    const apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
    this.provider = apiKey
      ? new OpenRouterProvider({
          apiKey,
          model: process.env.RECEIPT_LEGIBILITY_REVIEW_MODEL || 'google/gemini-2.0-flash-001',
          httpReferer: process.env.OPENROUTER_HTTP_REFERER || null,
          xTitle: process.env.OPENROUTER_X_TITLE || null,
        })
      : null;
  }

  isAvailable() {
    return !!this.provider;
  }

  async reviewCandidate(candidateImagePath, originalOcrText, receipt = {}) {
    if (!this.provider) {
      return { skipped: true, reason: 'OPENROUTER_API_KEY not configured.' };
    }

    if (!fs.existsSync(candidateImagePath)) {
      return { skipped: true, reason: 'Candidate image file not found.' };
    }

    const imageBuffer = fs.readFileSync(candidateImagePath);
    const base64Image = imageBuffer.toString('base64');
    const ext = path.extname(candidateImagePath).toLowerCase();
    const mimeType = ext === '.png' ? 'image/png' : 'image/jpeg';

    try {
      const result = await this.provider.generate(
        { text: buildPrompt(originalOcrText, receipt), image: base64Image, mimeType },
        SYSTEM_PROMPT,
        'VISION_CHAT',
        null,
        { maxTokens: 512 }
      );

      const parsed = parseJson(result?.content || '');

      return {
        skipped: false,
        pass: parsed.pass === true,
        confidence: typeof parsed.confidence === 'number' ? parsed.confidence : null,
        criticalIssues: Array.isArray(parsed.criticalIssues) ? parsed.criticalIssues : [],
        readableFields: parsed.readableFields && typeof parsed.readableFields === 'object'
          ? parsed.readableFields
          : {},
        summary: typeof parsed.summary === 'string' ? parsed.summary : '',
      };
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('[ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService] Review failed:', error.message);
      return { skipped: true, reason: error.message };
    }
  }
}

export default ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService;

```
