```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptLegibilityService.js
import LLMService from './LLMService.js';

function normalizeText(value) {
  return String(value || '')
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}.]+/gu, ' ')
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
    .trim();
}

function tokenize(value) {
  const normalized = normalizeText(value);
  return normalized ? normalized.split(' ').filter(Boolean) : [];
}

function numericTokens(value) {
  return String(value || '').match(/\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?/g) || [];
}

function tokenRecall(originalTokens, candidateTokens) {
  if (!originalTokens.length) return 1;
  const candidateSet = new Set(candidateTokens);
  const retained = originalTokens.filter((token) => candidateSet.has(token));
  return retained.length / originalTokens.length;
}

function containsApproximate(text, value) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return true;
  const normalizedText = normalizeText(text);
  const normalizedValue = normalizeText(value);
  if (!normalizedValue) return true;
  return normalizedText.includes(normalizedValue);
}

function containsMoney(text, value) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return true;
  const amount = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(amount)) return true;
  const fixed = amount.toFixed(2);
  const loose = fixed.replace('.', '[.,]');
  return new RegExp(`(^|[^0-9])${loose}([^0-9]|$)`).test(String(text || ''));
}

const MONTH_NAMES = [
  'january', 'february', 'march', 'april', 'may', 'june',
  'july', 'august', 'september', 'october', 'november', 'december',
];
const MONTH_ABBR = ['jan', 'feb', 'mar', 'apr', 'may', 'jun', 'jul', 'aug', 'sep', 'oct', 'nov', 'dec'];

function containsDate(text, dateValue) {
  if (!dateValue) return true;
  const date = new Date(dateValue);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return true;

  // Use local-time parts so single-digit day/month match what's printed on the receipt
  const yyyy = String(date.getFullYear());
  const month0 = date.getMonth(); // 0-based
  const d = date.getDate();
  const mm = String(month0 + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const dd = String(d).padStart(2, '0');
  const raw = String(text || '');
  const lower = raw.toLowerCase();

  // Numeric patterns: yyyy-mm-dd, mm/dd/yyyy, dd/mm/yyyy, mm/dd/yy, dd/mm/yy, mm-dd-yyyy, dd-mm-yyyy
  if (
    raw.includes(`${yyyy}-${mm}-${dd}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${mm}/${dd}/${yyyy}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${dd}/${mm}/${yyyy}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${mm}/${dd}/${yyyy.slice(2)}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${dd}/${mm}/${yyyy.slice(2)}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${mm}-${dd}-${yyyy}`) ||
    raw.includes(`${dd}-${mm}-${yyyy}`)
  ) return true;

  // Written month patterns: "Apr 2, 2024" / "April 2, 2024" / "2 Apr 2024" / "2 April 2024"
  const monthFull = MONTH_NAMES[month0];
  const monthAbbr = MONTH_ABBR[month0];
  const dayStr = String(d); // no leading zero for written formats

  return (
    lower.includes(`${monthFull} ${dayStr},`) ||
    lower.includes(`${monthAbbr} ${dayStr},`) ||
    lower.includes(`${monthFull} ${dayStr} `) ||
    lower.includes(`${monthAbbr} ${dayStr} `) ||
    lower.includes(`${dayStr} ${monthFull}`) ||
    lower.includes(`${dayStr} ${monthAbbr}`)
  );
}

class ReceiptLegibilityService {
  constructor() {
    this.llmService = new LLMService();
  }

  async extractText(imagePath) {
    return this.llmService.ocrUsingGoogleVision(imagePath);
  }

  compareText(originalText, candidateText, receipt = {}, thresholds = {}) {
    const normalizedOriginal = normalizeText(originalText);
    const normalizedCandidate = normalizeText(candidateText);
    const originalTokens = tokenize(normalizedOriginal);
    const candidateTokens = tokenize(normalizedCandidate);
    const originalNumeric = numericTokens(originalText);
    const candidateNumeric = numericTokens(candidateText);

    const textSimilarity = tokenRecall(originalTokens, candidateTokens);
    const numericTokenRecall = tokenRecall(originalNumeric, candidateNumeric);

    const readableFields = {
      merchant: containsApproximate(candidateText, receipt.companyName),
      total: containsMoney(candidateText, receipt.total),
      tax: containsMoney(candidateText, receipt.hst),
      date: containsDate(candidateText, receipt.date),
    };

    const criticalIssues = [];
    if (!readableFields.merchant) criticalIssues.push('merchant_missing');
    if (!readableFields.total) criticalIssues.push('total_missing');
    if (!readableFields.tax) criticalIssues.push('tax_missing');
    if (!readableFields.date) criticalIssues.push('date_missing');

    const similarityThreshold = thresholds.textSimilarity ?? 0.9;
    const numericThreshold = thresholds.numericTokenRecall ?? 0.95;
    const pass =
      textSimilarity >= similarityThreshold &&
      numericTokenRecall >= numericThreshold &&
      criticalIssues.length === 0;

    const reviewRequired =
      !pass &&
      criticalIssues.length === 0 &&
      textSimilarity >= similarityThreshold - 0.08 &&
      numericTokenRecall >= numericThreshold - 0.05;

    return {
      pass,
      status: pass ? 'PASSED' : reviewRequired ? 'REVIEW_REQUIRED' : 'FAILED_LEGIBILITY',
      textSimilarity,
      numericTokenRecall,
      readableFields,
      criticalIssues,
      originalLineCount: String(originalText || '').split(/\r?\n/).filter(Boolean).length,
      candidateLineCount: String(candidateText || '').split(/\r?\n/).filter(Boolean).length,
    };
  }
}

export default ReceiptLegibilityService;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptMatchingService.js
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import AccountingService from '#services/accounting/services/AccountingService.js';
import ReceiptImportService from './ReceiptImportService.js';

const DAY_MS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
const HIGH_CONFIDENCE_AUTO_MATCH_SCORE = 0.97;
const MIN_CONFIDENCE_SCORE = 0.55;

const clamp01 = (value) => Math.max(0, Math.min(1, value));

const normalizePositiveTax = (value) => {
  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === '') return null;
  const numericValue = Number(value);
  if (!Number.isFinite(numericValue)) return null;
  return Math.abs(Number(numericValue.toFixed(2)));
};

class ReceiptMatchingService {
  constructor() {
    this.prisma = prisma;
    this.accountingService = new AccountingService();
    this.receiptImportService = new ReceiptImportService();
  }

  normalizeVendor(value) {
    return String(value || '')
      .toLowerCase()
      .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, ' ')
      .trim();
  }

  tokenize(value) {
    return this.normalizeVendor(value).split(' ').filter(Boolean);
  }

  similarity(a, b) {
    const aTokens = new Set(this.tokenize(a));
    const bTokens = new Set(this.tokenize(b));
    if (!aTokens.size || !bTokens.size) return 0;

    let overlap = 0;
    for (const token of aTokens) {
      if (bTokens.has(token)) overlap += 1;
    }

    return overlap / new Set([...aTokens, ...bTokens]).size;
  }

  scoreReceiptMatch({ transaction, receipt, priorVendorMatched = false }) {
    const absAmount = Math.abs(Number(transaction?.amount || 0));
    const receiptTotal = Math.abs(Number(receipt?.total || 0));
    const amountDelta = Math.abs(absAmount - receiptTotal);
    const amountTolerance = Math.max(2, absAmount * 0.05);
    const amountScore = clamp01(1 - amountDelta / amountTolerance);

    const txDate = new Date(transaction?.date);
    const receiptDate = new Date(receipt?.date);
    const dateDeltaDays = Math.abs(txDate - receiptDate) / DAY_MS;
    const dateScore = clamp01(1 - dateDeltaDays / 14);

    const vendorScore = this.similarity(receipt?.companyName, transaction?.description);
    const descriptionScore = this.similarity(receipt?.companyName, transaction?.notes || transaction?.description);
    const sourceTypeScore = String(transaction?.source?.type || '').includes('CREDIT_CARD') ? 0.9 : 1;
    const priorVendorScore = priorVendorMatched ? 1 : 0;

    const score = (
      amountScore * 0.35 +
      dateScore * 0.2 +
      vendorScore * 0.2 +
      descriptionScore * 0.1 +
      sourceTypeScore * 0.05 +
      priorVendorScore * 0.1
    );

    return {
      score: Number(score.toFixed(4)),
      breakdown: {
        amountScore: Number(amountScore.toFixed(4)),
        dateScore: Number(dateScore.toFixed(4)),
        vendorScore: Number(vendorScore.toFixed(4)),
        descriptionScore: Number(descriptionScore.toFixed(4)),
        sourceTypeScore: Number(sourceTypeScore.toFixed(4)),
        priorVendorScore: Number(priorVendorScore.toFixed(4)),
      },
    };
  }

  async getPriorVendorAccount({ organizationId, normalizedVendor, excludeTransactionId = null }) {
    const recentMatched = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        receiptId: { not: null },
        categoryId: { not: null },
        ...(excludeTransactionId ? { NOT: { id: excludeTransactionId } } : {}),
      },
      include: {
        category: true,
        receipt: true,
      },
      orderBy: { date: 'desc' },
      take: 50,
    });

    return recentMatched.find((item) => this.normalizeVendor(item.receipt?.companyName) === normalizedVendor)?.category || null;
  }

  async getCandidateReceipts({ organizationId, transaction, limit = 10 }) {
    const txDate = new Date(transaction.date);
    const from = new Date(txDate.getTime() - 14 * DAY_MS);
    const to = new Date(txDate.getTime() + 14 * DAY_MS);
    const absAmount = Math.abs(Number(transaction.amount || 0));

    const receipts = await this.prisma.receipt.findMany({
      where: {
        organizationId,
        date: { gte: from, lte: to },
        total: { gte: Math.max(0, absAmount * 0.75), lte: absAmount * 1.25 + 5 },
      },
      orderBy: { date: 'desc' },
      take: limit,
    });

    const normalizedVendor = this.normalizeVendor(transaction.description);
    const priorVendorAccount = await this.getPriorVendorAccount({
      organizationId,
      normalizedVendor,
      excludeTransactionId: transaction.id,
    });

    const scored = receipts
      .map((receipt) => {
        const priorVendorMatched = this.normalizeVendor(receipt.companyName) === normalizedVendor && Boolean(priorVendorAccount);
        const scoring = this.scoreReceiptMatch({ transaction, receipt, priorVendorMatched });
        return {
          ...receipt,
          scoring,
          suggestedExpenseAccount: priorVendorAccount,
        };
      })
      .filter((receipt) => receipt.scoring.score >= MIN_CONFIDENCE_SCORE)
      .sort((a, b) => b.scoring.score - a.scoring.score);

    return scored;
  }

  async matchTransactionToReceipt({ organizationId, transactionId, receiptId, userId }) {
    const transaction = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.findFirst({
      where: { id: transactionId, organizationId },
      include: {
        category: true,
        source: true,
        receipt: true,
      },
    });
    if (!transaction) throw new Error('Transaction not found.');

    const receipt = await this.prisma.receipt.findFirst({
      where: { id: receiptId, organizationId },
    });
    if (!receipt) throw new Error('Receipt not found.');

    const normalizedVendor = this.normalizeVendor(receipt.companyName);
    const priorVendorAccount = await this.getPriorVendorAccount({
      organizationId,
      normalizedVendor,
      excludeTransactionId: transaction.id,
    });
    const scoring = this.scoreReceiptMatch({
      transaction,
      receipt,
      priorVendorMatched: Boolean(priorVendorAccount),
    });

    const suggestedExpenseAccount = transaction.category || priorVendorAccount || null;
    const hints = this.receiptImportService.buildReceiptBackedHints({
      receipt,
      suggestedExpenseAccount: suggestedExpenseAccount
        ? {
            id: suggestedExpenseAccount.id,
            code: suggestedExpenseAccount.code,
            description: suggestedExpenseAccount.description,
          }
        : null,
      suggestedStatementLine: suggestedExpenseAccount?.statementLine || null,
      matchConfidence: scoring.score,
      needsReview: scoring.score < HIGH_CONFIDENCE_AUTO_MATCH_SCORE,
    });
    hints.scoring = scoring.breakdown;

    const updated = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.update({
      where: { id: transaction.id },
      data: {
        receiptId: receipt.id,
        matchedReceiptId: receipt.id,
        taxes: normalizePositiveTax(receipt.taxes ?? transaction.taxes),
        notes: this.accountingService.mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(transaction.notes, hints),
      },
      include: {
        receipt: true,
        category: true,
        source: true,
      },
    });

    await this.accountingService.syncJournalWithBankTx(transaction.id, userId);

    return {
      transaction: {
        ...updated,
        receiptHints: hints,
        needsReview: Boolean(hints.needsReview),
      },
      receipt: updated.receipt,
      receiptHints: hints,
    };
  }

  async unmatchTransaction({ organizationId, transactionId, userId }) {
    const transaction = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.findFirst({
      where: { id: transactionId, organizationId },
      include: { receipt: true },
    });
    if (!transaction) throw new Error('Transaction not found.');

    const updated = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.update({
      where: { id: transactionId },
      data: {
        receiptId: null,
        matchedReceiptId: null,
        notes: this.accountingService.stripReceiptHintsFromNotes(transaction.notes),
      },
      include: {
        receipt: true,
        category: true,
        source: true,
      },
    });

    await this.accountingService.syncJournalWithBankTx(transaction.id, userId);
    return updated;
  }

  async autoMatchTransactions({ organizationId, transactionIds = [], userId }) {
    const matched = [];
    const skipped = [];
    const errors = [];

    for (const transactionId of transactionIds) {
      try {
        const transaction = await this.prisma.bankTransaction.findFirst({
          where: { id: Number(transactionId), organizationId },
          include: { category: true, source: true, receipt: true },
        });

        if (!transaction) {
          skipped.push({ transactionId, reason: 'Transaction not found.' });
          continue;
        }
        if (transaction.receiptId) {
          skipped.push({ transactionId, reason: 'Transaction already matched.' });
          continue;
        }
        if (Number(transaction.amount || 0) >= 0) {
          skipped.push({ transactionId, reason: 'Only expense transactions are auto-matched.' });
          continue;
        }

        const candidates = await this.getCandidateReceipts({ organizationId, transaction, limit: 5 });
        if (!candidates.length) {
          skipped.push({ transactionId, reason: 'No candidate receipts found.' });
          continue;
        }

        const [topCandidate, secondCandidate] = candidates;
        const hasClearWinner = !secondCandidate || topCandidate.scoring.score - secondCandidate.scoring.score >= 0.08;

        if (topCandidate.scoring.score >= HIGH_CONFIDENCE_AUTO_MATCH_SCORE && hasClearWinner) {
          const result = await this.matchTransactionToReceipt({
            organizationId,
            transactionId: transaction.id,
            receiptId: topCandidate.id,
            userId,
          });
          matched.push({ transactionId, receiptId: topCandidate.id, score: topCandidate.scoring.score, transaction: result.transaction });
          continue;
        }

        const hints = this.receiptImportService.buildReceiptBackedHints({
          receipt: topCandidate,
          suggestedExpenseAccount: topCandidate.suggestedExpenseAccount
            ? {
                id: topCandidate.suggestedExpenseAccount.id,
                code: topCandidate.suggestedExpenseAccount.code,
                description: topCandidate.suggestedExpenseAccount.description,
              }
            : null,
          suggestedStatementLine: topCandidate.suggestedExpenseAccount?.statementLine || null,
          matchConfidence: topCandidate.scoring.score,
          needsReview: true,
        });
        hints.scoring = topCandidate.scoring.breakdown;

        await this.prisma.bankTransaction.update({
          where: { id: transaction.id },
          data: {
            notes: this.accountingService.mergeReceiptHintsIntoNotes(transaction.notes, hints),
          },
        });

        skipped.push({
          transactionId,
          reason: 'Candidate scored below auto-match threshold. Stored review hints instead.',
          score: topCandidate.scoring.score,
          suggestedReceiptId: topCandidate.id,
        });
      } catch (error) {
        errors.push({ transactionId, error: error.message });
      }
    }

    return { matched, skipped, errors };
  }
}

export default ReceiptMatchingService;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptOcrJobService.js
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import ReceiptTaggingService from './ReceiptTaggingService.js';

class ReceiptOcrJobService {
  constructor() {
    this.jobs = new Map();
    this.taggingService = new ReceiptTaggingService();
  }

  getStatus(receiptId) {
    const state = this.jobs.get(receiptId);
    return {
      isRunning: !!state?.isRunning,
      lastStartedAt: state?.lastStartedAt || null,
      lastFinishedAt: state?.lastFinishedAt || null,
      lastError: state?.lastError || null,
      heicConverted: state?.heicConverted || false,
      originalHeicName: state?.originalHeicName || null,
    };
  }

  async runReceiptOcr(receiptId) {
    const existing = this.jobs.get(receiptId) || {};
    this.jobs.set(receiptId, {
      ...existing,
      isRunning: true,
      lastStartedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      lastError: null,
    });

    try {
      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findUnique({
        where: { id: receiptId },
        select: {
          id: true,
          userId: true,
          organizationId: true,
        },
      });

      if (!receipt) {
        throw new Error('Receipt not found.');
      }

      const result = await this.taggingService.tagReceipt(
        receipt.id,
        receipt.userId,
        `ocr-${Date.now()}`,
        receipt.organizationId
      );

      this.jobs.set(receiptId, {
        isRunning: false,
        lastStartedAt: this.jobs.get(receiptId)?.lastStartedAt || new Date().toISOString(),
        lastFinishedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        lastError: null,
        heicConverted: result?.heicConverted || false,
        originalHeicName: result?.originalHeicName || null,
      });
    } catch (error) {
      this.jobs.set(receiptId, {
        isRunning: false,
        lastStartedAt: this.jobs.get(receiptId)?.lastStartedAt || new Date().toISOString(),
        lastFinishedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        lastError: error.message,
      });
      console.error(`Background OCR failed for receipt ${receiptId}:`, error);
    }
  }

  startInBackground(receiptId) {
    const current = this.getStatus(receiptId);
    if (current.isRunning) {
      return current;
    }

    setTimeout(() => {
      this.runReceiptOcr(receiptId).catch((error) => {
        console.error(`Unexpected OCR worker error for receipt ${receiptId}:`, error);
      });
    }, 0);

    const startedState = {
      isRunning: true,
      lastStartedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      lastFinishedAt: current.lastFinishedAt,
      lastError: null,
    };

    this.jobs.set(receiptId, startedState);
    return startedState;
  }
}

export default new ReceiptOcrJobService();
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptOptimizationService.js
import fs from 'fs';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import {
  generateReceiptOptimizationCandidates,
  getReceiptImageInfo,
} from './ReceiptImageProcessor.js';
import ReceiptImageVariantService from './ReceiptImageVariantService.js';
import ReceiptLegibilityService from './ReceiptLegibilityService.js';
import ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService from './ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService.js';

// Minimum bytes saved before auto-activation kicks in (20 KB).
const AUTO_MIN_SAVED_BYTES = 20 * 1024;

// Tighter OCR thresholds for unattended auto-activation.
const AUTO_TEXT_THRESHOLD = 0.95;
const AUTO_NUMERIC_THRESHOLD = 0.96;

// Profiles used for auto-optimization on upload (limits OCR calls to 1).
const AUTO_PROFILES = ['grayscale-sharp', 'cropped-grayscale-sharp'];

class ReceiptOptimizationService {
  constructor() {
    this.variantService = new ReceiptImageVariantService();
    this.legibilityService = new ReceiptLegibilityService();
    this.openRouterReviewService = new ReceiptLegibilityOpenRouterService();
  }

  async getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId) {
    const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findFirst({
      where: { id: receiptId, organizationId },
    });

    if (!receipt) throw new Error('Receipt not found.');
    if (!receipt.imgName) throw new Error('Receipt has no image to optimize.');
    return receipt;
  }

  // ─── Preview ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  async preview(receiptId, organizationId, options = {}) {
    const receipt = await this.getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId);
    const originalPath = this.variantService.resolveReceiptPath(receipt);

    if (!fs.existsSync(originalPath)) throw new Error('Receipt image is missing.');

    const originalMetadata = this.variantService.getMetadata(originalPath);
    const previewDir = this.variantService.ensureVariantDir(organizationId, 'previews');
    const runId = `${receipt.id}-${Date.now()}`;
    const originalText = receipt.text || await this.legibilityService.extractText(originalPath);

    const defaultProfiles = options.autoCrop === false
      ? ['jpeg-high', 'jpeg-medium', 'grayscale-sharp', 'bw-audit']
      : null;

    const candidates = await generateReceiptOptimizationCandidates(originalPath, {
      outputDir: previewDir,
      runId,
      maxWidth: options.maxWidth,
      cropPadding: options.cropPadding,
      profiles: options.compressionProfile
        ? [options.compressionProfile]
        : (options.profiles || defaultProfiles),
    });

    const reviewMode = options.reviewMode || 'ocr-only';
    const evaluated = [];

    for (const candidate of candidates) {
      const previewRelativePath = this.variantService.getVariantRelativePath(
        'previews',
        candidate.outputFilename
      );
      const previewUrl = `/uploads/${organizationId}/receipts/previews/${candidate.outputFilename}`;

      if (candidate.cropReport?.rejectedByGeometry) {
        evaluated.push({
          ...candidate,
          previewRelativePath,
          previewUrl,
          legibility: {
            pass: false,
            status: 'FAILED_LEGIBILITY',
            criticalIssues: ['suspicious_crop_geometry'],
          },
        });
        continue;
      }

      const candidateText = await this.legibilityService.extractText(candidate.outputPath);
      let legibility = this.legibilityService.compareText(
        originalText,
        candidateText,
        receipt,
        {
          textSimilarity: options.textSimilarityThreshold,
          numericTokenRecall: options.numericTokenThreshold,
        }
      );

      // Phase 3: LLM secondary review for borderline cases.
      if (reviewMode === 'ocr-plus-llm' && legibility.status === 'REVIEW_REQUIRED') {
        const llmReview = await this.openRouterReviewService.reviewCandidate(
          candidate.outputPath,
          originalText,
          receipt
        );

        if (!llmReview.skipped) {
          // LLM can rescue a borderline candidate only when numeric recall is still strong.
          const rescuable =
            llmReview.pass &&
            llmReview.criticalIssues.length === 0 &&
            legibility.numericTokenRecall >= 0.93;

          legibility = {
            ...legibility,
            pass: rescuable,
            status: rescuable ? 'PASSED' : 'FAILED_LEGIBILITY',
            llmReview,
          };
        }
      }

      evaluated.push({ ...candidate, previewRelativePath, previewUrl, legibility });
    }

    const passingCandidates = evaluated
      .filter((c) => c.legibility?.pass && c.savedBytes > 0)
      .sort((a, b) => a.sizeBytes - b.sizeBytes);

    const selected = passingCandidates[0] || null;
    const status = selected
      ? 'PASSED'
      : evaluated.some((c) => c.legibility?.status === 'REVIEW_REQUIRED')
        ? 'REVIEW_REQUIRED'
        : 'FAILED_LEGIBILITY';

    const serializeCandidate = (c) =>
      c
        ? {
            profile: c.profile,
            previewRelativePath: c.previewRelativePath,
            previewUrl: c.previewUrl,
            sizeBytes: c.sizeBytes,
            savedBytes: c.savedBytes,
            width: c.width,
            height: c.height,
            autoCropApplied: c.autoCropApplied,
            cropReport: c.cropReport,
            legibility: c.legibility,
          }
        : null;

    const report = {
      receiptId: receipt.id,
      status,
      selectedProfile: selected?.profile || null,
      reviewMode,
      original: {
        relativePath: this.variantService.attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt),
        sizeBytes: originalMetadata.size || 0,
        checksum: originalMetadata.checksum || null,
        imageInfo: await getReceiptImageInfo(originalPath),
      },
      selected: serializeCandidate(selected),
      candidates: evaluated.map(serializeCandidate),
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receipt.id },
      data: {
        compressionStatus: status,
        compressionProfile: selected?.profile || null,
        compressionScore: selected?.legibility?.textSimilarity || null,
        compressionSavedBytes: selected?.savedBytes || 0,
        legibilityStatus: selected?.legibility?.status || status,
        legibilityCheckedAt: new Date(),
        legibilityReportJson: report,
        autoCropApplied: !!selected?.autoCropApplied,
        autoCropReportJson: selected?.cropReport || null,
      },
    });

    return report;
  }

  // ─── Save ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  async save(receiptId, organizationId, userId, previewRelativePath) {
    const receipt = await this.getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId);
    const originalPath = this.variantService.resolveReceiptPath(receipt);
    const originalRelativePath =
      this.variantService.attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
    const originalMetadata = this.variantService.getMetadata(originalPath);
    const promoted = await this.variantService.promotePreviewToOptimized(
      receipt,
      previewRelativePath
    );
    const imageInfo = await getReceiptImageInfo(promoted.absolutePath);

    const updatedReceipt = await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receipt.id },
      data: {
        imgName: promoted.imgName,
        imageRelativePath: promoted.relativePath,
        imageStorageStatus: 'ACTIVE',
        imageStorageChecksum: promoted.metadata.checksum,
        imageStorageSize: promoted.metadata.size,
        originalImageRelativePath:
          receipt.originalImageRelativePath || originalRelativePath,
        originalImageChecksum:
          receipt.originalImageChecksum || originalMetadata.checksum,
        originalImageSize: receipt.originalImageSize || originalMetadata.size,
        compressedImageRelativePath: promoted.relativePath,
        compressedImageChecksum: promoted.metadata.checksum,
        compressedImageSize: promoted.metadata.size,
        activeImageVariant: 'optimized',
        compressionStatus: 'ACTIVE_OPTIMIZED',
        compressionSavedBytes: Math.max(
          0,
          (originalMetadata.size || 0) - (promoted.metadata.size || 0)
        ),
        optimizedAt: new Date(),
        optimizedByUserId: userId || null,
      },
    });

    return {
      receipt: updatedReceipt,
      imageUrl: `/uploads/${organizationId}/${promoted.relativePath}`,
      imageInfo,
    };
  }

  // ─── Discard ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  async discard(receiptId, organizationId, previewRelativePath) {
    const receipt = await this.getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId);
    const discarded = this.variantService.discardPreview(receipt, previewRelativePath);
    return { discarded };
  }

  // ─── Report ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  async getReport(receiptId, organizationId) {
    const receipt = await this.getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId);
    return {
      receiptId: receipt.id,
      compressionStatus: receipt.compressionStatus,
      compressionProfile: receipt.compressionProfile,
      compressionScore: receipt.compressionScore,
      compressionSavedBytes: receipt.compressionSavedBytes,
      legibilityStatus: receipt.legibilityStatus,
      legibilityCheckedAt: receipt.legibilityCheckedAt,
      legibilityReportJson: receipt.legibilityReportJson,
      autoCropApplied: receipt.autoCropApplied,
      autoCropReportJson: receipt.autoCropReportJson,
      optimizedAt: receipt.optimizedAt,
      originalImageRelativePath: receipt.originalImageRelativePath,
      originalImageSize: receipt.originalImageSize,
      activeImageVariant: receipt.activeImageVariant,
    };
  }

  // ─── Phase 4: Auto-optimize on upload ─────────────────────────────────────────
  //
  // Called fire-and-forget from the upload route after tagging completes.
  // Uses tighter thresholds and a minimal profile set to limit OCR calls to 1.
  // Cleans up all preview files regardless of outcome.

  async autoOptimize(receiptId, organizationId) {
    try {
      const receipt = await prisma.receipt.findFirst({
        where: { id: receiptId, organizationId },
      });

      if (!receipt || !receipt.imgName) return;
      if (receipt.compressionStatus === 'ACTIVE_OPTIMIZED') return;

      const originalPath = this.variantService.resolveReceiptPath(receipt);
      if (!fs.existsSync(originalPath)) return;

      const previewDir = this.variantService.ensureVariantDir(organizationId, 'previews');
      const runId = `auto-${receipt.id}-${Date.now()}`;
      const originalText =
        receipt.text || await this.legibilityService.extractText(originalPath);

      // Generate a small candidate set — avoids running OCR on 6 images.
      const candidates = await generateReceiptOptimizationCandidates(originalPath, {
        outputDir: previewDir,
        runId,
        profiles: AUTO_PROFILES,
      });

      // Sort ascending by output size; OCR the smallest first.
      const viable = candidates
        .filter((c) => !c.cropReport?.rejectedByGeometry && c.savedBytes >= AUTO_MIN_SAVED_BYTES)
        .sort((a, b) => a.sizeBytes - b.sizeBytes);

      let activated = null;

      for (const candidate of viable) {
        const candidateText = await this.legibilityService.extractText(candidate.outputPath);
        const legibility = this.legibilityService.compareText(
          originalText,
          candidateText,
          receipt,
          { textSimilarity: AUTO_TEXT_THRESHOLD, numericTokenRecall: AUTO_NUMERIC_THRESHOLD }
        );

        if (legibility.pass) {
          const previewRelativePath = this.variantService.getVariantRelativePath(
            'previews',
            candidate.outputFilename
          );
          await this.save(receiptId, organizationId, null, previewRelativePath);
          activated = candidate;
          break;
        }
      }

      // Clean up preview files that were not activated.
      for (const candidate of candidates) {
        if (candidate === activated) continue;
        try {
          if (fs.existsSync(candidate.outputPath)) fs.unlinkSync(candidate.outputPath);
        } catch {
          // best-effort cleanup
        }
      }

      // If no candidate was auto-activated, update status so admin knows to review.
      if (!activated) {
        const allPassed = false;
        const anyReview = viable.length > 0;
        await prisma.receipt.update({
          where: { id: receiptId },
          data: {
            compressionStatus: anyReview ? 'REVIEW_REQUIRED' : 'NOT_OPTIMIZED',
            legibilityCheckedAt: new Date(),
          },
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(
        `[ReceiptOptimizationService.autoOptimize] Receipt ${receiptId}: ${error.message}`
      );
    }
  }

  // ─── Phase 5: Purge original file ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  //
  // Permanently removes the original pre-optimization image from disk.
  // Only allowed when the optimized variant is the active image.

  async purgeOriginal(receiptId, organizationId) {
    const receipt = await this.getReceipt(receiptId, organizationId);

    if (receipt.activeImageVariant !== 'optimized') {
      throw new Error(
        'Original can only be purged when the optimized image is the active variant.'
      );
    }

    if (!receipt.originalImageRelativePath) {
      return { purged: false, reason: 'No original image path recorded on this receipt.' };
    }

    // Safety check: original path must not equal the current active image path.
    const currentRelativePath =
      this.variantService.attachmentService.getReceiptRelativePathFromRecord(receipt);
    if (receipt.originalImageRelativePath === currentRelativePath) {
      throw new Error(
        'Original path matches active image path — refusing to delete the active image.'
      );
    }

    let deleted = false;
    try {
      const originalAbsPath =
        this.variantService.attachmentService.resolveReceiptAbsolutePath(
          organizationId,
          receipt.originalImageRelativePath
        );

      if (fs.existsSync(originalAbsPath)) {
        fs.unlinkSync(originalAbsPath);
        deleted = true;
      }
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error(`Could not delete original image: ${error.message}`);
    }

    await prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receipt.id },
      data: {
        originalImageRelativePath: null,
        originalImageChecksum: null,
        originalImageSize: null,
      },
    });

    return {
      purged: true,
      deleted,
      freedBytes: receipt.originalImageSize || 0,
    };
  }
}

export default new ReceiptOptimizationService();

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js
// server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptsManager.js

import ReceiptCRUDService from "./ReceiptCRUDService.js";
import ReceiptMatchingService from "./ReceiptMatchingService.js";
import ReceiptTaggingService from "./ReceiptTaggingService.js";
import ReceiptImportService from "./ReceiptImportService.js";
import AttachmentService from "./AttachmentService.js";
import PDFService from "./PDFService.js";  // <<== This is our merged file
import TextToImageConverter from "./TextToImageConverter.js";
import LLMService from "./LLMService.js";

class ReceiptsManager {
  constructor() {
    this.crudService = new ReceiptCRUDService();
    this.matchingService = new ReceiptMatchingService(this.crudService);
    this.taggingService = new ReceiptTaggingService();
    this.attachmentService = new AttachmentService();
    this.pdfService = new PDFService(); // Our merged PDFService with all methods
    this.textConverter = new TextToImageConverter();
    this.llmService = new LLMService();

    // Pass pdfService in as "pdfService"
    this.importService = new ReceiptImportService({
      pdfService: this.pdfService,
      llmService: this.llmService,
      receiptCRUDService: this.crudService,
      textConverter: this.textConverter
    });
  }

  listReceipts = (userId) => this.crudService.listReceipts(userId);
  addOrUpdateReceipt = (data) => this.crudService.addOrUpdateReceipt(data);
  removeReceiptById = (id) => this.crudService.removeReceiptById(id);
  getReceiptById = (receiptId) => this.crudService.getReceiptById(receiptId);

  autoMatchSingleReceipt = async (receiptId) =>
    await this.matchingService.autoMatchSingleReceipt(receiptId);

  autoMatchReceipts = async (organizationId, receiptIds = []) =>
    await this.matchingService.autoMatchReceipts(organizationId, receiptIds);

  matchReceipt = async (receiptId, transactionId,receipt) =>
    await this.matchingService.matchReceipt(receiptId, transactionId,receipt);

  tagReceipt = (receiptId, userId, sessionId, organizationId) =>
    this.taggingService.tagReceipt(
      receiptId,
      userId,
      sessionId,
      organizationId
    );

  // Just call our importService
  importReceiptFromEmail = (emailId, sessionId, organizationId, userId) =>
    this.importService.importReceiptFromEmail(emailId, sessionId, organizationId,userId);

  saveAttachment = (buffer, filename, organizationId) =>
    this.attachmentService.saveAttachment(buffer, filename, organizationId);

  extractTextFromPDF = (buffer) => this.pdfService.extractTextFromPDF(buffer);
  convertPDFToImage = (buffer, emailMetadata, outputPath) =>
    this.pdfService.convertPDFToImage(buffer, emailMetadata, outputPath);

  generateUniqueFilename = () =>
    `receipt_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;

  removeReceiptByImg = async (imgName, userId, organizationId) => {
    await this.attachmentService.deleteAttachment(imgName, organizationId);
    return this.crudService.removeReceiptByImg(imgName, userId);
  };
}

export default new ReceiptsManager();
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptTaggingService.js
//--- File: server/src/services/receipt/services/ReceiptTaggingService.js ---

import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import LLMService from "./LLMService.js";
import { parseISO, isValid } from "date-fns";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs";
import { isHeicFile, convertHeicToJpeg } from "./ReceiptImageProcessor.js";

class ReceiptTaggingService {
  constructor() {
    this.prisma = prisma;
    this.llmService = new LLMService();
  }

  async tagReceipt(receiptId, userId, sessionId, organizationId) {
    const receipt = await this.prisma.receipt.findUnique({
      where: { id: receiptId },
      include: { organization: true }
    });

    if (!receipt) {
      throw new Error("Receipt not found.");
    }

    let imgPath = "";
    let currentImgName = receipt.imgName;
    let heicConverted = false;
    let originalHeicName = null;
    let originalHeicPath = null;
    if (currentImgName) {
      imgPath = path.join(
        process.cwd(),
        "/uploads",
        organizationId,
        "receipts",
        currentImgName
      );
      if (!fs.existsSync(imgPath)) {
        throw new Error("Receipt image does not exist on the server.");
      }

      // HEIC files aren't supported by Google Vision or browsers — convert to JPEG first
      if (isHeicFile(imgPath)) {
        console.log(`Converting HEIC to JPEG for receipt ${receipt.id}: ${currentImgName}`);
        try {
          originalHeicPath = imgPath;
          const jpegPath = await convertHeicToJpeg(originalHeicPath);
          originalHeicName = currentImgName;
          imgPath = jpegPath;
          currentImgName = path.basename(jpegPath);
          heicConverted = true;
          await this.prisma.receipt.update({
            where: { id: receipt.id },
            data: { imgName: currentImgName },
          });
          console.log(`HEIC converted and saved as: ${currentImgName}`);
        } catch (convErr) {
          console.error(`HEIC conversion failed for receipt ${receipt.id}:`, convErr);
          throw new Error(`Failed to convert HEIC image: ${convErr.message}`);
        }
      }
    }

    let extractedData;
    if (currentImgName) {
      extractedData = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromImage(
        imgPath,
        currentImgName,
        userId,
        sessionId,
        receipt.id
      );
    } else if (receipt.text) {
      extractedData = await this.llmService.extractAndTagReceiptFromText(
        receipt.text,
        receipt.id,
        userId,
        sessionId
      );
    } else {
      throw new Error("No image or text found to tag the receipt.");
    }

    console.log(`Tagging Receipt ID: ${receipt.id}`, extractedData);

    const validatedData = {
      date:
        extractedData.date && isValid(new Date(extractedData.date))
          ? extractedData.date
          : null,
      companyName: extractedData.companyName || null,
      total:
        extractedData.total !== undefined && !isNaN(extractedData.total)
          ? extractedData.total
          : null,
      hst:
        extractedData.hst !== undefined && !isNaN(extractedData.hst)
          ? extractedData.hst
          : null,
      notes: extractedData.notes || null,
      text: extractedData.text || null,
      items: extractedData.items || []
    };

    const updatedReceipt = await this.prisma.receipt.update({
      where: { id: receipt.id },
      data: {
        date: validatedData.date ? new Date(validatedData.date) : null,
        companyName: validatedData.companyName,
        total: validatedData.total,
        hst: validatedData.hst,
        notes: validatedData.notes,
        text: validatedData.text,
        items: {
          deleteMany: {},
          create: validatedData.items.map((item) => ({
            name: item.name || "Unnamed Item",
            quantity: item.quantity || 1,
            price: item.price || 0.0
          }))
        }
      },
      include: { items: true }
    });

    // Auto-delete the original HEIC file once OCR succeeded and text was extracted
    if (heicConverted && originalHeicPath && validatedData.text) {
      try {
        await fs.promises.unlink(originalHeicPath);
        console.log(`Deleted original HEIC file after successful OCR: ${originalHeicPath}`);
      } catch (unlinkErr) {
        console.warn(`Could not delete original HEIC file ${originalHeicPath}:`, unlinkErr.message);
      }
    }

    return { ...updatedReceipt, heicConverted, originalHeicName };
  }
}

export default ReceiptTaggingService;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/services/receipt/services/TextToImageConverter.js
import sharp from 'sharp';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';
import { chromium } from 'playwright';

class TextToImageConverter {
  constructor() {
    this.width = 2480; // A4 width at 300dpi
    this.fontSize = 40;
    this.lineHeight = 1.5;
  }

  async convertTextToImage(content, metadata = {}, outputPath) {
    // Prepare text content with metadata
    const lines = this.prepareText(content, metadata);

    // Create SVG with the text content
    const svg = this.createSVG(lines);

    // Convert SVG to PNG using sharp
    await sharp(Buffer.from(svg))
      .png()
      .toFile(outputPath);

    return path.basename(outputPath);
  }
  async convertHtmlToImage(htmlContent, metadata = {}, outputPath) {
    try {
        // Launch browser
        const browser = await chromium.launch();
        const context = await browser.newContext({
            javaScriptEnabled: false,
        });
        const page = await context.newPage();

        // Remove all image elements
        htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/<img\b[^>]*>/gi, '');

        // Clean up HTML
        htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/[\n\t]/g, '');
        
        // Set content
        await page.setContent(htmlContent);
        await page.setViewportSize({ width: this.width, height: 800 });

        // Get the full height
        const bodyHandle = await page.$('body');
        const { height } = await bodyHandle.boundingBox();
        await bodyHandle.dispose();

        // Update viewport and take screenshot
        await page.setViewportSize({ width: this.width, height: Math.ceil(height) });
        await page.screenshot({
            path: outputPath,
            fullPage: true,
            type: 'png'
        });

        await browser.close();
        return path.basename(outputPath);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error converting HTML to image:', error);
        throw error;
    }
}

  prepareText(content, metadata) {
    const lines = [];

    // Add metadata header
    if (metadata.from) lines.push(`From: ${metadata.from}`);
    if (metadata.to) lines.push(`To: ${metadata.to}`);
    if (metadata.date) lines.push(`Date: ${metadata.date}`);
    if (metadata.subject) lines.push(`Subject: ${metadata.subject}`);
    lines.push(''); // Empty line after metadata

    // Split content into lines (basic word wrap)
    const words = content.split(/\s+/);
    let currentLine = '';
    const maxCharsPerLine = Math.floor(this.width / (this.fontSize * 0.6)); // Approximate characters per line

    words.forEach(word => {
      if ((currentLine + ' ' + word).length <= maxCharsPerLine) {
        currentLine = currentLine ? `${currentLine} ${word}` : word;
      } else {
        if (currentLine) lines.push(currentLine);
        currentLine = word;
      }
    });
    if (currentLine) lines.push(currentLine);

    return lines;
  }

  createSVG(lines) {
    // Calculate total height based on number of lines
    const height = Math.max(800, (lines.length * this.fontSize * this.lineHeight) + 100);

    // Create the SVG content
    const textElements = lines.map((line, index) => {
      const y = 60 + (index * this.fontSize * this.lineHeight);
      return `<text x="40" y="${y}" font-family="Arial" font-size="${this.fontSize}px">${this.escapeXml(line)}</text>`;
    }).join('\n');

    // Add background for metadata
    const metadataHeight = 200;
    const metadataRect = `<rect x="0" y="0" width="${this.width}" height="${metadataHeight}" fill="#f0f0f0"/>`;

    return `<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" standalone="no"?>
      <svg width="${this.width}" height="${height}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
        <rect width="100%" height="100%" fill="white"/>
        ${metadataRect}
        ${textElements}
      </svg>`;
  }

  escapeXml(unsafe) {
    return unsafe.replace(/[<>&'"]/g, c => {
      switch (c) {
        case '<': return '&lt;';
        case '>': return '&gt;';
        case '&': return '&amp;';
        case '\'': return '&apos;';
        case '"': return '&quot;';
        default: return c;
      }
    });
  }
}

export default TextToImageConverter;
```
